[p.3] / āryamañjuśriye kumārabhūtāya namaḥ /
# # / / rgya gar skad du / / ma dhyan nta bi bham ga t'i k'a / / bod skad du / / dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i 'grel bshad /
uttamajano hi prāyaśo guruṃ śraddhādevatāṃ cābhyarcyakarmasu pravartata / ityayamapyahamuttamajananayamanuvartī madhyāntavibhāgasūtrabhāṣyaṃ
# 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo / / ya rabs dag ni phal cher bla ma dang dad pa'i lha la mchod nas las rnams la 'jug ste / / dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i mdo rnam par bshad par 'dod pas /
cikīrṣustatpraṇeturvaktuś ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā tadarthavibhāgāya prayukta / iti pratipādayannāha - / śāstrasyā'sya praṇetāram
# bdag la yang 'di ni ya rabs kyi tshul can no zhes shes par bya ba'i phyir / / de mdzad pa dang 'chad pa la mchod nas / / de'i don rnam par dbye bar zhugs so zhes rab tu bstan pa'i phyir / / bstan bcos 'di ni rab mdzad pa /
ityādi / / evaṃ kṛtvā ko guṇaḥ prāpyate ?
# zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so / / de ltar byas na yon tan ci zhig thob ce na /
guṇavato hitakāriṇaś ca pūjayatāmeṣāṃ puṇyamupacīyate /
# yon tan dang ldan pa dang phan 'dogs 'dogs pa la mchod na bsod nams 'phel bar 'gyur ro /
puṇya upacite samārambhād vighnavināyakairanupahatānalpena prayāsena / samāpayantīti /
# bsod nams 'phel na yang dag par rtsom pa la bar chad dang bgegs kyis mi tshugs par tshogs chung ngu rdzogs par 'gyur ro /
athavā praṇetṛpraṇeyapravacanāt sūtrapraṇetṛvaktṛvṛttīṣu / gauravotpādanārthamāha- / śāstrasyā'sya praṇetāram / iti sarvam /
# yang na mdzad pas gsungs pa dang 'chad pas bshad pa yang dag par byin par bsnyad pas / / mdzad pa dang 'chad pa dang mdo dang 'brel ba la gus pa bskyed par bya ba'i phyir / / bstan bcos 'di ni rab mdzad pa /
tatra praṇetṛvacanāt sūtre gauravam utpadyate /
# zhes bya ba thams cad smos so / / de la mdzad pas bshad par bstan pas mdo la gus pa skye ste /
yasyā'sya kārikāśāstrasyāryamaitreyaḥ praṇetā /
# 'di ltar bstan bcos tshig le'ur byas pa'i mdzad pa po ni 'phags pa byams pa ste /
sa caikajātipratibandhāt sarvabodhisattvābhijñādhāraṇīpratisaṃvit / samādhīndriyakṣāntivimokṣaiḥ paramaṃ pāraṃ gataḥ sarvāsu / bodhisattvabhūmiṣu [p.4] / niḥśeṣam api prahīṇāvaraṇaḥ /
# de yang skye ba gcig gis thogs pa'i phyir / / byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa dang gzungs dang so so yang dag par rig pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang dbang dang bzod pa dang rnam par thar pa thams cad kyi dam pa'i pha rol tu son pa / / byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad la sgrib pa yang ma lus par spangs pa'o /
vaktṛsamādānadvāreṇa vṛttau gauravam utpadyate /
# 'chad pas yang dag par byin pa'i sgo nas 'grel pa la gus pa skye bar 'gyur te /
vaktā punar atrācāryā'saṅgaḥ tasmācchrutvācāryambhadantavasubandhuḥ / tad bhāṣyam akarot /
# 'di la 'chad pa ni slob dpon thogs med do / / de las slob dpon btsun pa dbyig gnyen gyis gsan nas 'di'i 'grel pa mdzad de /
tayor uttaram aprajñāvator abhrānti prativedhadhāraṇopadeśasāmarthyād / atra sūtrārtho'bhrāntam upadiṣṭa iti vṛttau gauravam utpadyate /
# de gnyis kyang shes rab mchog dang ldan pas ma nor bar rtogs pa dang bzung ba dang ston nus pas 'dir mdo'i don ma nor ba bstan to zhes 'grel pa la gus pa skye ste /
evaṃ ye pudgalaṃ pramāṇīkurvanti teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyo gauravotpattiḥ /
# de ltar gang dag gang zag tshad mar byed pa de dag ni / / mdo dang 'grel pa la gus pa skye'o /
ye ca dharmānusāriṇas teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyoḥ śubhārthā'vabodhaḥ /
# gang yang chos la ston pa de dag ni mdo dang 'grel pa'i don bzang po khong du chud de /
jāte ca niścaye iyaṃ praṇeturvaktuś ca pratītyā prabhāvanā na tu
# nges pa skyes na 'di mdzad pa dang 'chad pa yang rtogs pas rab tu phye ba yin gyis /
tarkāgamamātreṇa prabhāvaneti praṇetṛvaktṛgauravotpattiḥ /
# rtog ge dang lung tsam gyis rab tu phye bar ni zad do zhes mdzad pa dang 'chad pa la gus pa skye'o /
idam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ - / kīdṛśaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ / / śāstraṃ kim iti cet nāma-pada-vyañjanakāyaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ
# da ni bstan bcos kyi rang bzhin ci 'dra ba dang ci'i phyir bstan bcos zhes bya ba 'di bshad par bya'o / / ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs su snang ba'i rnam par rig pa rnams ni bstan bcos so /
śāstraṃ / / atha vā lokottara-jñānaprāpakaśabdaviśeṣaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ / śāstraṃ / / kathaṃ vijñaptayaḥ praṇīyanta ucyante vā ?/
# yang na 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes thob par byed pa'i sgra'i khyad par du snang ba'i rnam par rig pa rnams bstan bcos so / / rnam par rig pa rnams ji ltar mdzad cing brjod ce na /
praṇetṛ-vijñaptiprabhatvat prajñaptīnāṃ nātra doṣaḥ / / śiṣyadhārmiko hi śīlasamādhiprajñāviśeṣotpādāt
# mdzad pa dang 'chad pa'i rnam par rig pa las nyan pa'i rnam par rig pa rnams skye bas 'di la nyes pa med do / / slob ma 'chos pa'i phyir bstan bcos te / / slob ma'i 'chos pa ni tshul khrims dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi khyad par bskyed pa'i phyir /
kāyavāṅmanasāṃbhārānutpatīkarmaṇo nivartate sambhārotpattikarmāṇi / ca pravartate /
# lus dang ngag dang yid tshogs par mi 'byung ba'i las las bzlog pa dang tshogs par 'byung ba'i las la 'jug pa'o /
atha vā śāstralakṣaṇasya śāsanācchāstraṃ /
# yang na bstan bcos kyi mtshan nyid du 'thad pa'i phyir bstan bcos te /
svalakṣaṇaṃ yad upadeśo bhāsamānasarva kleśaprahāṇāya / nirantaradīrghavividhatīvraduḥkhabhītyāś ca durgater bhavāc ca
# lung mnos pa goms par byas pas bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa spong bar 'gyur ba dang bar chad med pa yun ring ba'i sdug bsngal drag po sna tshogs kyis 'jigs pa'i ngan song rnams dang srid pa las skyob pa gang yin pa de ni bstan bcos kyi mtshan nyid do /
santrāyate / / tasmāt kleśaripuśāsanād bhavadurgatisantārāc ca śāstralakṣaṇaṃ /
# de'i phyir nyon mongs pa'i dgra 'chos pa dang ngan 'gro dang srid pa las skyob pas bstan bcos kyi mtshan nyid de /
etac ca dvayam api sarvasmin mahāyāne sarvasmiṃś ca tad vyākhyāne / vidyate nānyatreti / / ata etac chāstraṃ / / āha ca - / yacchāsti ca kleśaripūn aśeṣān
# de gnyis kyang theg pa chen po thams cad dang de bshad pa thams cad la yod kyi gzhan la med de de'i phyir 'di ni bstan bcos so / / de la smras pa / / nyon mongs dgra rnams ma lus 'chos pa dang /
santrāyate durgatito bhavāc ca /
# ngan 'gro srid las skyob pa gang yin pa /
tacchāsanā (tttrāṇa-) guṇāc ca śāstraṃ
# chos skyob yon tan phyir na bstan bcos te /
etad dvayaṃ cānyamateṣu nāsti // / asyeti /
# gnyis po 'di dag gzhan gyi lugs la med / / 'di ni zhes bya ba ni /
kriyānadvāreṇa saptavastusaṅgrahasya
# theg pa gsum gyi sgo nas dngos po bdun du bsdus pa /
kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaprāpakasya madhyāntavibhāgakārikāśāstrasya / hṛdi sthitatvād asyeti pratyakṣopadeśaḥ /
# nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa spong ba thob pa dang bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa 'di ni sems la gnas pa'i phyir dang 'di zhes mngon sum du bstan to /
praṇetārm iti kartāraṃ /
# rab mdzad pa zhes bya ba ni byed pa po'o /
yadyapy ayaṃ dhātuḥ prāpaṇārthas tathāpi pra-śabdasaṃyogāt / viśeṣārthako draṣṭavyaḥ / / uktaṃ hi - [p.5] / upasargeṇa dhātvartho balād anyaḥ pratīyate /
# skad kyi dbyings 'di thob par byed pa yin mod kyi / / 'on kyang rab kyi sgra dang sgrogs na byed par lta ste / / skad dbyings don gyi stobs ldan yang / / nye bar bsgyur bas zil non 'gyur /
gaṅgāsalilamādhuryaṃ sāgareṇa yathāmbhasā //
# gang g'a'i chu ni mngar mod kyi / / rgya mtsho'i chu ni ji bzhin no / / zhes bshad do /
sugatātmajam iti /
# bde gshegs nyid skyes zhes bya ba ni /
suṣṭhu gataḥ savāsana kleśāvaraṇāj jñeyāvaraṇāc cāpratiṣṭhitaṃ / virvāṇam iti sugataḥ /
# bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa las mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das par shin tu gshegs pas bde bar gshegs pa'o /
sa ca sarvavāsanāvaraṇaprahīṇaḥ sarvathā sarvadharmāvabodhasvarūpaḥ
# de yang bag chags kyi sgrib pa thams cad spangs pa / / chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad du thugs su chud pa'i rang gi ngo bo 'byor ba thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pa /
sarvavibhūtyāśrayabhūta-ṇiratnavad acintyaprabhāvavigrahaḥ / sarvasattvānāmanābhogena sarvārtha raṇasamartho
# yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che ltar bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mthu mnga' ste / / sems can thams cad kyi don thams cad lhun gyis grub par mdzad par spyod pa /
nirvikalpakajñānaviśeṣātmakaḥ sugataḥ taj janitatvān nirvikalpasya / jñānasya / / tasmāt tasmin vā jātaḥ sugatātmajaḥ /
# rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi khyad par gyi bdag nyid ni bde bar gshegs pa'o / / de'i bdag nyid ni rnam par dag pa'i deb zhin nyid de / / de las rnam bar mi rtog pa'i ye shes rab tu byung ba'i phyir de las sam / / der skye bas na bde gshegs nyid skyes so /
athavā sugatātmanā jāta iti sugatātmajaḥ /
# yang na bde bar gshegs pa nyid du skyes pas / / bde gshegs nyid skyes te /
yathoktaṃ sūtrāntare -jāto bhavati tathāgatavaṃśe tadātmakavstu / pratilābhād iti /
# mdo gzhan las de'i bdag nyid kyi chos rab tu rnyed pas / / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung du skyes pa yin no zhes ji skad gsungs pa lta bu'o /
evaṃ sati bodhisattvasya daśamyāṃ bhūmau pratiṣṭhitasya sarvākāraṃ / jñeyaṃ vastu karatalastham ivāmalakaṃ / tattvaṃśukāvacchāditalocanasyevābhāsamāyāti /
# de lta bas na byang chub sems dpa' sa bcu pa la rab tu gnas pa ni / / shes bya'i dngos po'i rnam pa thams cad sgyu ru ra lag mthil du gzhag pa / / dar lva srab mos gyogs pa'i mig la snang ba bzhin no /
bhagavataḥ punar apanītalocanāvaraṇasyevetyayaṃ viśeṣaḥ /
# bcom ldan 'das kyi ni mig gi sgrib pa bsal ba bzhin te / / 'di ni khyad par ro /
atra hi sugatātmajasya śāstrapraṇetur avabodhasampat pradarśitā / lābhasatkāranirapekṣasya śāstrapraṇetṛtvena karuṇāsampat
# 'dir ni bde bar gshegs pa'i bdag nyid las skyes pas / / bstan bcos mdzad pa de kho na thugs su chud pa phun sum tshogs par bstan pa dang rnyed pa dang bkur sti la mi lta bar bstan bcos mdzad pas /
prajñāsampacca / / vaktāram iti vyākhyānasya kartāraṃ / / abhyarhyeti sambadhyate / / sugatātmajamityapītyapare / / sa punar āryā'saṅgaḥ / / tasya hīdaṃ śāstram abhivyaktaṃ ākhyātaṃ cāryamaitreyādhiṣṭhānāt / dharmasantānena / / ceti samuccaye pādapūraṇe'dhikavacane vā / / anyān api buddhabodhisattvānarcayitvā na kevalaṃ praṇetāraṃ / vaktārañceti / / kebhyo vaktāraṃ / / asmad ādibhya iti / / vayam ādir yeṣāṃ te'samadādayas tebhyo'smadādibhyaḥ / / anenātmana upadeśasyāmṛṣātvaṃ vyajyate / / abhyarhyeti abhyarcya /
# thugs rje phun sum tshogs pa dang shes rab phun sum tshogs par bstan pa'o / / 'chad pa ni bshad par byed pa ste / / mngon par mchod ces bya ba dang sbyar ro / / kha cig na re bde gshegs nyid las skyes pa zhes kyang bya'o zhe'o / / de ni 'phags pa thogs med do / / de la ni 'phags pa byams pa'i byin rlabs kyis na / / chos kyi rgyun gyis bstan bcos 'di mngon du gyur cing bshad do / / su la 'chad pa zhe na / / bdag sogs la zhes bya ba ste / / bdag thog mar byas pa gang yin pa de dag ni bdag la sogs pa ste / / 'di ni bdag nyid kyi mi slu ba las lung mnos par ston to / / yang zhes bya ba ni bsdu ba'am / / rtsa ba bskangs pa'am / / lhag pa'i tshig ste / / mdzad pa dang 'chad pa nyi tshe la ma yin gyi / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' gang yang rung ba dag la mchod par bya'o / / mngon mchod ces bya ba ni rjed pa'o /
abhitaḥ purataḥ sākṣād iva sthitaṃ /
# mngon par zhes bya ba ni mdun nam mngon sum dang 'dra bar gnas pa'o /
arhitvā arcayitvā kāyavāṅmanobhiḥ /
# mchod pa ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyis rjed pa'o /
śāstrasya praṇetāraṃ vaktāraṃ cābhyarcya kiṃ kariṣyasītyāha - / yatīṣye'rthavivecane // iti / / yatnamārapsye arthavivecane arthavivareṇe pṛthagbhāvakaraṇe vā / / iyaṃ ca nimittārthā saptamī / / arthavivecananimittam ityarthaḥ // [p.6] / arthaḥ punar atra śāstraśarīram iti / / ete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyanta iti vacanāt / / kim artham idaṃ śāstraṃ praṇītaṃ /
# bstan bcos mdzad pa dang 'chad pa la mngon par mchod nas ci zhig bya zhe na / / don rnams dbye phyir 'bad par bya / / zhes bya ba smos so / / don dbye ba'i phyir ram; don dgrol ba'i phyir ram / / so sor dbye ba'i phyir bsgrim par bya ba'i phyir zhes bya ba 'di ni rgyu'i don te / / don rnam par dbye ba'i rgyur zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / don ni 'dir bstan bcos kyi lus yin te zhes bya ba don bdun po 'di dag bstan bcos 'di las 'chad do zhes 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ samyag nirvikalpa-jñānotpādanārthaṃ / / dharmanairātmyadeśanatayā nirvikalpajñānotpādāt tadabhyāsāc ca / niḥśeṣasavāsana kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇam avāpyate / / ayaṃ punardharmanairātbhyasyavirodhavādo yat sarvadharmarahitatā
# ci'i phyir bstan bcos 'di bshad ce na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes bskyed pa'i phyir te / / chos la bdag med pa bstan pas rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes bskyed pa dang de goms pas bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa ma lus par spangs pa thob par 'gyur ro /
dharmanairātmyam/ / antarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā ca dharmanairātmyam ityatas tat pratiṣedhena
# chos la bdag med pa yang chos thams cad med pa nyid chos la bdag med pa dang nang na byed pa'i skyes bu med pa nyid chos rnams la bdag med pa'o zhes mi mthun par smra ba de dag bkag pas /
tathābhūtanairātmyapratipādanārthaṃ śāstrārambhaḥ /
# chos la bdag med pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du bstan par bya ba'i phyir bstan bcos brtsam mo /
lakṣaṇāvaraṇādiṣv apratipannavipratipannānāṃ samyag avabodhotpādanād / apratipattivipratipattyapanayanārtham ity anye / / atha vā pañcākārajñeyaṃ lokadhātusattvadharmavineyopāyadhātvātmake
# gzhan dag na re mtshan nyid dang sgrib pa la sogs pa ma rtogs pa dang log par rtogs pa rnams yang dag par rtogs pa skyed pas ma rtogs pa rnams dang log par rtogs pa bsal ba'i phyir ro zhe'o / / yang na 'jig rten gyi khams dang sems can dang chos dang 'dul ba dang thabs kyi bdag nyid de /
pratyekam anantaprabhedatvād durvijñeyam iti bodhisattvānāṃ
# shes bya rnam lnga re re la yang rab tu dbye ba mtha' yas pa'i phyir shes par bya dka'o snyam du /
yaścittasaṅkocas tad apanayanārtham āha -
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems zhum pa gang yin pa de bstsal ba'i phyir /
lakṣaṇaṃ hyāvṛtis tattvaṃ / iti /
# mtshan nyid dang sgrib pa dang de kho na zhes bya ba dag smos so /
tatrāditaḥ śāstraśarīraṃ vyavasthāpyata iti /
# de la thog ma kho nar bstan bcos kyi lus rnam par gzhag ste zhes bya ba la /
tatreti śāstrasyārthavivecane śāstre [p.7] / vā / / ādita iti prathamata iti / / śāstraṃ vivaraṇaṃ /
# de la zhes bya ba ni bstan bcos kyi don rnam par 'byed pa de la'am / / bstan bcos la'o / / thog ma kho nar zhes bya ba ni / / dang po kho nar ro / / bstan bcos ni bshad par zad do /
taccharīraṃ saṃkṣepaḥ piṇḍārtho vāśrayārthena vā śarīraṃ /
# de'i lus ni mdor bsdus pa'am / / don bsdus pa'o / / gnas kyi don ni lus so /
yathā hi bāhyādhyātmikāyatanāśrayaḥ kāyaḥ śarīram ity ucyate evaṃ
# dper na phyi dang nang gi skye mched kyi gnas ni khog pa ste / / lus zhes bya ba de bzhin du /
yānarthān niścitya śāstraṃ pravartate te'rthās tasya śarīraṃ / / te ca saptyārthā lakṣaṇādayaḥ / / vyavasthāpyata iti prajñāpyate ākhyāyata ityarthaḥ /
# don gang dag la gnas te / / bstan bcos la 'jug pa'i don de rnams ni de'i lus so / / de dag kyang don bdun po dag ste / / mtshan nyid la sogs pa dag go / / rnam par gzhag ces bya ba ni bcas pa ste /
nanu śāstrāvabhodhenaiva taccharīraṃ vijñāsyata iti nirarthakam ādau / tad vyavasthāpanaṃ /
# bshad ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / bstan bcos khong du chud pa nyid kyis de'i lus shes par mi 'gyur ram / / de bas na thog ma de rnam par gzhag pa ni don med do /
na nirarthakaṃ śiṣyā'nugrahārthatvāt /
# slob ma rnams la phan gdags pa'i phyir don med pa ma yin no /
gatārtho hi śiṣyaḥ sukhaṃ vistaram ucyamānaṃ pratipādyate / / dṛṣṭā bhūmir niḥśaṅkam aśvavāhaneneva nānyathā / / ityete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyante /
# slob mas don khong du chud na rgyas par brjod kyang bde blag tu khong du chud par 'gyur te dkyus kyis bstan pa'i rta thags thogs med par rgyug pa bzhin te / / gzhan du ma yin no zhes bya ba don bdun po 'di dag bstan bcos 'di las 'chad do zhes bya ba la zhes bya ba ni /
itiḥ śāstraśarīrasamāptyarthaḥ / / eta iti ye lakṣaṇādaya uddiṣṭāḥ / / sapteti saṃkhyāparyantādhigamārtham upādānaṃ / / arthyanta ityarthā adhigamyanta iti yāvat /
# bstan bcos kyi lus rdzogs so zhes bya ba ni tha tshig go / / shes par bya ba yin pas don de khong du chud par bya ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / bdun po zhes bya ba ni grangs so / / 'di dag ces bya ba ni mtshan nyid la sogs pa smos pa gang yin pa rnams so /
asmin śāstra iti madhyāntavibhāgasaṃjñake /
# bstan bcos 'di las zhes bya ba ni dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya'o /
upadiśyanta ityākhyāyante viniściyante vā / / yad uta iti tathā'rthapratipādananipātaḥ / / lakṣaṇam iti / / lakṣyante'neneti lakṣaṇaṃ /
# 'chad ces bya ba ni bstan pa'am gtan la 'bebs pa'o / / 'di lta ste zhes bya ba ni de'i don khong du chud par byed pa'i tshig gi phrad do / / mtshan nyid ces bya ba ni / / 'dis mtshon par byed pas mtshan nyid do /
tac ca dvividhaṃ saṅkleśalakṣaṇaṃ vyavadānalakṣaṇāñca /
# de yang rnam pa gnyis te / / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid do /
tatra saṅkleśalakṣaṇaṃ navavidhaṃ /
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid ni rnam pa dgu ste /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti / ityārabhya yāvat / saptadhā'bhūtakalpanāt iti / / śeṣeṇārdhena vyavadānalakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ / / yadi lakṣyante'neneti laksaṇam ityevaṃ sati lakṣaṇasya
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya ba nas bzung ste / / rnam bdun yang dag min rtog las / / zhes bya ba'i bar du'o / / lhag ma ni rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid du bstan to / / gal te 'dis mtshon par byed pas mtshan nyid ces bya na /
saṅkleśavyavadānabhedo bhaved iti naitad evaṃ / / svabhāva eva hi bhāvānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ /
# de lta na ni mtshan nyid kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang tha dad par 'gyur ro zhe na / / de ni de lta ma yin te dngos po rnams kyi rang bzhin nyid mtshan nyid de /
tad yathā pṛthivīdhātuḥ kharalakṣaṇo na ca kharatvāt pṛthivīdhātuḥ / pṛthagastīti / / atha vā lakṣyate tad iti lakṣaṇaṃ /
# dper na sa'i khams kyi mtshan nyid ni sra ba ste / / sra ba nyid las sa'i khams gud na med pa lta bu'o; / / yang na des mtshon par bya bas mtshan nyid de /
evaṃ hi saṅkleśo vyavadānañca saṅkleśavyavadānātmatvena lakṣyata iti / lakṣaṇaṃ /
# de ltar kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba yang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i bdag nyid kyis mtshon par bya bas mtshan nyid du 'gyur ro /
atha vā dvayoḥ saṅkleśavyavadānayor lakṣaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ svalakṣaṇañca / sāmānyalakṣaṇañca / / āvaraṇam iti / / āvṛṇoti kuśalān dharmānāvriyante'nena kuśaladharmā utpattivibandhāt / ityāvaraṇaṃ / / tat punas tripañcāśat prakāraṃ / / tattvam iti /
# yang na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba gnyis las mtshan nyid rnam pa gnyis te / / rang gi mtshan nyid dang spyi'i mtshan nyid do / / sgrib pa zhes bya ba ni dge ba'i chos rnams la sgrib par byed pa'am / / 'dis dge ba'i chos rnams bsgrib pas sgrib pa ste / / skye ba la bgegs byed pa'i phyir sgrib pa'o / / de yang lnga bcu rtsa gsum mo /
tadevedaṃ tat tasya bhāvas tattvam aviparyāsa ityarthaḥ /
# de kho na zhes bya ba ni 'di nyid de yin pas de'o / / de'i dngos po ni de kho na ste / / phyin ci ma log ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tac ca daśa prakāraṃ / [p.8] / vipakṣaprahāṇārthaḥ pakṣaḥ pratipakṣaḥ / / sa sārgaḥ / / tadabhyāso bhāvanā /
# de yang rnam pa bcu'o / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs spangs pa'i phyir / / phyogs ni gnyen po ste de ni lam mo / / de goms par bya ba ni bsgom pa'o; /
avasthā tasyaiva santānenotpattiviśeṣaḥ /
# gnas skabs ni de nyid rgyun gyis skye ba'i khyad par ro /
sā punar ekānnaviṃśatiprakārā gotrāvasthādikā /
# de yang rnam par bcu dgu ste / / rigs kyi gnas la sogs pa'o /
phalasya lābhaḥ phalaprāptiḥ /
# 'bras bu thob pa ni 'bras bu rnyed pa'o /
tat punaḥ pañcadaśaprakāraṃ vipākaphalādi / / yānānuttartham iti / / gamyate'neneti yānaṃ / / yānac ca tadānuttaryañceti yānānuttaryaṃ /
# de yang rnam pa bco lnga ste / / rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu la sogs pa'o / / theg pa bla na med pa zhes bya ba ni 'dis 'gro bas theg pa ste / / de ni theg pa yang yin la bla na med pa yang yin pas theg pa bla na med pa'o /
tat punastrividhaṃ pratipattyānuttaryādi /
# de yang rnam pa gsum ste / / bsgrub pa bla na med pa la sogs pa'o /
saptamo'rtha iti niyamārtham anukramārthañcāha / / etāvanta evārthā nirdiśyante nāto'nya iti /
# don bdun pa zhes bya ba ni / / nges pa'i don dang go rims kyi don du smos pa ste / / don 'di rnams 'dir bshad kyi de las gzhan ma yin no /
anukramaḥ punar ayaṃ lokottarajñānānukūlyārthaḥ /
# yang go rims 'di ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes dang mthun pa'i phyir te /
tathā hi bodhisattvenādhimukticaryābhūmisthitena śīlapratiṣṭhitena
# 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' mos pas spyod pa la gnas pa / / tshul khrims la rab tu gnas pas /
prathamaṃ saṅkleśavyavadānakuśalena bhavitavyaṃ /
# thog mar kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba la mkhas par bya'o /
tataḥ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yasya yad āvaraṇaṃ tasya taj jñeyaṃ /
# de'i 'og tu dge ba'i chos rnams kyi gang gis sgrib pa gang yin pa de shes par bya ste /
tasyāprahāṇād vimukter asambhavād avijñānañca prahātuṃ na śakyate / doṣadarśanāt /
# de ma spangs na rnam par grol mi srid la / / rnam par mi shes na yang nyes pa ma mthong bas spong mi nus so /
tatas tadāvaraṇād yenālambanena cittaṃ vimucyate tatttvaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# de'i 'og tu sgrib pa de las dmigs pa gang gis sems rnam par grol bar 'gyur ba de ni de kho na yin par khong du chud par bya'o /
tatastenālambhanenatadāvaraṇasya yena prayogena kṣayo bhavati sā
# de'i 'og tu dmigs pa des sgrib pa de sbyor ba gang gis zad par 'gyur ba de gnyen po bsgom par shes par bya'o /
pratipakṣabhāvanā jñeyā/ / tatas tasyāṃ pratipakṣabhāvāyāṃ vipakṣahānyā pratipakṣavṛddhyā / cā'vasthā jñeyā gotrāvasthādikā /
# de'i 'og tu gnyen po bsgom pa ni de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs 'bri ba dang gnyen po 'phel ba la gnas skabs su shes par bya ste / / rigs kyi gnas skabs la sogs pa'o /
tato lokottaradharmābhimukhīkaraṇaṃ phalāni srota apatti phalādīni / veditavyāni /
# de'i 'og tu 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos mngon du gyur pa ni 'bras bu rnams te / / rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la sogs par shes par bya'o /
sarvam apyetat srottaratvācchrāvakādibhiḥ sādhāraṇaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ / / yathoktaṃ sūtre -
# de dag thams cad kyang bla ma dang bcas pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang nyan thos la sogs pa dang thun mong ste / / mdo las ji skad du /
sa pravrajitaḥ śrāvakaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate
# rab tu byung ba de nyan thos kyi bslab pa dang cho ga dang spyod yul dang yang dag par spyod pa la yang slob po /
pratyekabuddhaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate
# rang sangs rgyas kyi bslab pa dang cho ga dang spyod yul dang yang dag par spyod pa la slob po /
bodhisattvaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate /
# byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa dang cho ga dang spyod yul dang yang dag par spyod pa la yang slob po zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o /
bodhisattvānāṃ tvānuttaryam asādhāraṇaṃ / / saptamo'rtha ānuttaryaṃ /
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ni bla na med pa thun mong ma yin pa ste don bdun pa bla na med pa'o /
anyastvāha / / saṅkleśavyavadānalakṣaṇe kauśalotpādanārtham ādau laksaṇaṃ /
# gzhan na re kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid la mkhas par bya ba bskyed pa'i phyir thog mar mtshan nyid do /
tatra yaḥ saṅkleśas tadāvaraṇaṃ /
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa gang yin pa de ni / / sgrib pa'o /
yad vyavadānaṃ tat tattvaṃ /
# rnam par byang ba gang yin pa de ni de kho na'o /
āvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ ca tattvādhigamād bhavatītyata āvaraṇatattvaṃ /
# de kho na nyid khong du chud pas sgrib pa spong bar 'gyur te / / de'i phyir sgrib pa dang de kho na'o /
tat prahāṇopāyapradarśanārthaṃ tataḥ saparivāraḥ pratipakṣo mārgaḥ /
# de spang ba'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir / / de'i 'og tu gnyen po 'khor dang bcas pa ni lam mo /
tasya mārgasyādimadhyānteṣu mṛdumadhyādhimātraprabhedapradarśanārthaṃ
# lam de'i thog ma dang bar ma dang tha mal chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen po rab tu dbye bar bstan pa'i phyir de'i gnas skabs so /
tatrāvasthā / / avasthānurūpaṃ phalamāvahatīti tad anantaraṃ phalaṃ /
# gnas skabs dang mthun pa'i 'bras bu thob par byed pas / / de'i 'og tu 'bras bu'o /
etac ca sarvaṃ bodhisattvasya śrāvakādisādhāraṇam ity
# de dag thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos la sogs pa dang thun mong ste /
asādhāraṇa-mahāyānanayaprakāśanārthaṃ yānānuttaryam iti / / apare punar āhuḥ /
# de bas na thun mong ma yin pa dang theg pa chen po'i tshul rab tu bstan pa'i phyir bla na med pa zhes bya'o zer ro /
sadasal lakṣaṇajñāpanārthaṃ prathamato lakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ /
# gzhan dag na re yod pa dang med pa'i mtshan nyid shes par bya ba'i phyir thog mar mtshan nyid bshad do /
lakṣaṇaṃ jñātvāvaraṇaṃ prahātavyaṃ tattvaṃ ca sākṣāt kartavyam iti tad / anantaram āvaraṇatattvaṃ / [p.9]
# mtshan nyid shes nas sgrib pa spang bar bya ba dang de kho na mngon sum du bya bas de'i 'og tu sgrib pa dang de kho na'o /
tayoś ca prahāṇasākṣātkaraṇayor ayam upāya iti pratipakṣabhāvanā /
# de gnyis spang ba dang mngon du bya ba'i thabs ni 'di yin te / / gnyen po bsgom pa'o /
tasyāś ca tāratamyam avasthāviśeṣaḥ /
# de'i 'bring dang mchog ni gnas skabs kyi khyad par ro /
tat kṛtañca prahāṇaṃ phalaṃ /
# des spang bar bya ba ni 'bras bu'o /
tad anantaraṃ yānānuttaryam iti prakāśanārtham ayam anukrama iti /
# de'i 'og tu theg pa bla na med pa'o zhes bya bar rab tu bstan pa'i phyir 'di ni go rims so zhes zer ro /
anyacca sattvasya sadasad dharmasaṃmohāpavādasamāropaprahāṇārthaṃ / lakṣaṇanirdeśaḥ /
# gzhan yang sems pa yod pa dang med pa'i chos la rmongs nas / / skur pa 'debs pa dang sgro 'dogs pa spang ba'i phyir mtshan nyid bshad do /
prahīṇasaṃmohasyāvaraṇakauśalārtham āvaraṇaṃ /
# rmongs pa spangs nas sgrib pa la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir sgrib pa'o /
tenāvṛtaṃ tattvam iti tattvakauśalārthaṃ tad anantaraṃ tattvaṃ /
# des de kho na bsgribs pas de kho na la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir de'i 'og tu de kho na'o /
tattvapratividdhabhāvanayāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ bhavatīti tattvānantaraṃ / pratipakṣabhāvanā /
# de kho na rab tu rtogs pa bsgoms pas sgrib pa spong bar 'gyur bas de kho na'i 'og tu gnyen po bsgom pa'o /
tat prabhedakauśalārtham avasthā /
# de'i dbye ba la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir gnas skabs so /
avasthayāṃ phalaṃ prabhāvitavyam ityavasthānantaraṃ phalaṃ tat / kauśalotpādanārthaṃ /
# gnas skabs kyis 'bras bu rab tu phye bas de la mkhas par bya ba bskyed pa'i phyir gnas skabs kyi 'og tu 'bras bu'o /
sarvam etan mahāyānamāgamyeti yānānuttaryam ante nirdiṣṭaṃ //1-1// / tatra lakṣaṇam ārabhyāha -
# de dag thams cad kyang theg pa chen po la brten pas theg pa bla na med pa tha mar bshad do snyam mo / / de la mtshan nyid las brtsams nas /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate / / śūnyatā vidyate tv atra tasyām api sa vidyate // iti /
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / de la gnyis po yod ma yin / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod / / de la yang ni de yod do /
tatreti lakṣaṇāvaraṇādisaptārtheṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu lakṣaṇam adhikṛtyoddiśyāha / abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti / / yathoddiśas tathā nirdeśa iti kṛtvā / / lakṣaṇañca prāg uddiṣṭamatastasyaiva śeṣebhyo nirdeśaḥ prāgārabhyate / / kecit virundhanti sarvadharmāḥ sarvathā niḥsvabhāvāḥ śaśaviśāṇavad
# zhes bya bar gsungs so zhes bya ba la / / de la zhes bya ba ni mtshan nyid dang sgrib pa la sogs pa dngos po bdun smos pa dag gi nang nas mtshan nyid las brtsams nas de'i dbang du mdzad de / / de'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so / / ji ltar bstan pa de bzhin du bshad de / / thog mar mtshan nyid bstan pas de'i phyir lhag ma rnams pas de nyid bshad pa sngar brtsam mo / / la la dag chos thams cad ri bong gi rva ltar rang bzhin ye med do /
ityataḥ sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārthamāha -
# snyam du sems pa de'i phyir thams cad la skur ba dgag pa'i don du /
abhūtaparikalpo'stīti /
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya bar gsungs te /
svabhāvata iti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
# rang bzhin gyi zhes bya ba tshig gi lhag ma'o /
nanv evaṃ sūtravirodhaḥ - sarvadharmāḥ śūnyā iti śāstre vacanāt / / nāsti virodhaḥ yasmāt -
# de ltar na mdo las chos thams cad stong pa'o zhes bshad pas / / mdo dang mi 'gal lam zhe na / / mi 'gal te 'di ltar /
dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate / / abhūtaparikalpo hi grāhyagrāhakasvarūparahitaḥ śūnya ucyate na tu / sarvathā niḥsvabhāvaḥ /
# de la gnyis po yod ma yin / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i ngo bo dang bral bas stong pa zhes bya ba'i rang bzhin ye med pa ni ma yin te /
ato na sūtravirodhaḥ /
# de'i phyir mdo dang mi 'gal lo /
yadyevaṃ dvayaṃ śaśaviṣāṇavat sarvathā nāsti /
# gal te de ltar gnyis po ni ri bong gi rva ltar ye med la /
abhūtaparikalpaś ca paramārthataḥ svabhāvato'styevaṃ / śūnyatā'bhāvaprasaṅgaḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa ni / / don dam par rang bzhin gyis yod na / / de lta na ni stong pa nyid med par 'gyur ro zhe na /
naitad evaṃ yasmāt - [p.10] / śūnyatā vidyate tvatra / iyam eva hi -śūnyatā yā grāhagrāhakarahitatā'bhūtaparikalpasyeti na / śūnyatāyā nāstitvaṃ bhavati /
# de ni de lta ma yin te 'di ltar / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod / / yang dag ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa nyid gang yin pa de stong pa nyid yin pas stong pa nyid med par mi 'gyur ro /
yadyadvayā śūnyatā sā cābhūtaparikalpe'sti kasmād vayamamuktāḥ /
# gal te gnyis po med pa stong pa nyid yin la / / de yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa la yod na / / ci'i phyir bdag cag ma grol /
vidyamānā ca kasmān na gṛhyata iti saṃśayāpanayanārthaṃ - / tasyām api sa vidyate / / ityāha /
# yod na yang ci'i phyir ma rtogs snyam pa'i dogs pa bsal ba'i phyir / / de la yang ni de yod do / / zhes bya ba gsungs te /
yasmācchūnyatāyām apyabhūtaparikalpo vidyate tasmād bhavanto na / muktāḥ / / ata eva ca samalatvān na prasannābdhātavad gṛhyate / / atha vā cittacaittebhyo'nyatra rūpādayo dravyatvena santīti yad darśanaṃ / tat pratiṣedhārtham āha -
# 'di ltar stong pa nyid la yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod pas de'i phyir khyed ma grol lo / / de bas na dri ma dang bcas pas chu'i khams dangs pa bzhin rtogs par mi rung ngo / / yang na sems can dang sems las byung ba rnams dang gzugs dang rdzas nyid du yod par gang dag lta ba de dgag pa'i phyir /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod /
dravyataḥ / / nāsti rūpaṃ tad vyatiriktaṃ dravyata iti / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ? / yasmāt - / dvayaṃtatra na vidyate /
# ces gsungs te de nyid rdzas su yod do / / gzugs ni de las logs shig na yang med la / / rdzas su yang med do / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
na hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kasyacid grāhako nāpi kenacit gṛhyate /
# 'di ltar de la gnyis po yod ma yin / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni ci la yang 'dzin pa ma yin / / sus kyang gzung bar bya ba ma yin gyi /
kiṃ tarhi grāhyagrāhakatvaṃ bhāvamātram eva /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba'i dngos po tsam nyid de /
yato vijñānād bahī rūpādayo na gṛhyante / / svapnāadivad vijñānaṃ rūpādyābhāsam utapdyate / / na ca yad yasya kāraṇaṃ tad abhāve tasyotpattir yujyate /
# 'di ltar rnam par shes pa las phyi rol na gzugs la sogs pa gzung ba med par rmi lam la sogs pa bzhin du / / gzugs la sogs par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ngo / / gal te rgyu yin na de med par de 'byung bar mi rung ngo /
tasmān nirālambanam eva svapnādāviva /
# de'i phyir dmigs pa med pa nyid de / / da rmi lam la sogs pa bzhin no /
anyatrāpi svabījaparipākād arthābhāsaṃ vijñānam utpadyate ity / avaseyaṃ /
# gzhan la yang rang gi sa bon yongs su smin pa las don du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa 'byung bar shes par bya'o /
grāhyābhāve grāhakasyābhāvād grāhye'sati grāhako bhavituṃ na
# gzung ba med na 'dzin pa med par 'gyur bas gzung ba med na 'dzin pa yod par mi rung ste /
yujyate / / tasmān na rūpam abhūtaparikalpāt pṛthag asti /
# de bas na gzugs ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa las gud na yod pa ma yin no /
yadi tarhi grāhyabhāvastena viśuddhyālambanābhāvān mokṣābhāvaḥ /
# gal te gzung ba med na de'i phyir rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa med pas thar pa yang med par 'gyur ro zhe na /
naitad evaṃ yasmāt - / śūnyatā vidyate tvatra / tu śabdo yasmād arthaḥ /
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / 'di ltar / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod / / ni zhes bya ba'i sgra ni gang gi phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
śūnyatā hi vuśuddhyālambanā /
# stong pa nyid ni rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa ste /
sā ca grāhyagrāhakarahitatā 'bhūtapraikalpe'stīti na mokṣābhāvaḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba nyid de / / de yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la yod pas thar pa med par mi 'gyur ro /
yady abhūtaparikalpe'sti sā vidyamānā kimarthaṃ na gṛhyate /
# gal te yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog pa la yod na / / de yod pas ci'i phyir mi rtogs she na /
abhūtaparikalpāvṛtatvān na gṛhyata ākāśanairmalyavat na tu asattvād / iti pratipādayann āha -
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pas bsgribs pas nam mkha' dri ma med pa bzhin du rtogs par mi rung gi med pa ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir; de la yang ni de yod do zhes bya ba gsungs so /
tasyām api sa vidyata iti / / atha vā sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārtham āha - [p.11] / abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti / / na sarvam asat nāpi sadātmakaṃ vijñānapariṇāmāatmanā'stīti kṛtvā /
# yang na thams cad la skur ba 'debs pa dgag pa'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya ba gsungs te / / rnam par shes pa gyur ba'i bdag nyid yod pas / / thams cad med pa yang ma yin bdag nyid yod pa yang ma yin no /
ye tu manyante yathaiva rūpādayaḥ prakhyāyante tathiavābhūtaparikalpāt / svabhāvataḥ pṛthag vidyanta iti tān pratyāha
# gang dag sems pa gzugs la sogs pa ji ltar snang ba de ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa las logs shig na rang bzhin du yod do zhes /
abhūtasamāropapratiṣedhārthaṃ -
# yod pa ma yin pa la sgro 'dogs pa dgag pa'i don du de'i phyir /
dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate / iti /
# de la gnyis po yod ma yin /
abhūtaparikalpamātraṃ vidyata ityabhiprāyaḥ /
# zhes bya ba gsungs so / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam yod par dgongs pa'o /
kenacit dvayor abhāvo vo vnadhyāputravat cheda rūpo gṛhyate / / anyair antarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā dharmāṇāṃ śūnyate'tyucyate / / ataḥ śūnyatāpavādapratiṣedhārthaṃ bhūtanairātmyakhyāpanārthañcāha
# kha cig gnyis po med pa ni mo gsham gyi bu bzhin du dngos po med de zhes chad pa'i dngos po'i ngo bor 'dzin pa dang gzhan dag nang na byed pa'i skyes bu med pa nyid ni / / chos rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes smra ba de'i phyir / / stong pa nyid du skur pa 'debs pa dgag pa'i don dang bdag med pa yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir /
śūnyatā vidyate tvatra iti /
# stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod ces bya ba gsungs so /
yadyabhūtaparikalpe śūnyatāstyevaṃ sati sarvaprāṇinām aprayatnena / mokṣaprasaṅgaḥ / / nāsyetad yasmāt - / tasyām api sa vidyate / / na hyaviśodhitāyāṃ śūnyatāyāṃ mokṣo'sti saṅkliṣṭā ca mahatā yatnena / viśodhyata iti nāsty ayatnena mokṣaḥ /
# gal te yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la stong pa nyid yod na de lta na ni / / bsgrim mi dgos par srog chags thams cad thar bar 'gyur ro zhe na / / de lta ma yin te 'di ltar / / de la yang ni de yod do / / stong pa nyid kyang rnam par ma sbyangs kyi bar du thar pa med pa'i phyir te / / kun nas nyon mongs par gyur pa ni / / 'bad pa chen pos rnam par sbyang dgos pas 'bad pa ma byas par thar pa med do /
atha vā lakṣaṇaṃ saṅkleśavyavadānābhidhānād anyan nāstītyataḥ / saṅkleśavyavadānalakṣaṇapradarśanārthamāha -
# yang na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dag gi mtshan nyid brjod pa las gzhan med pas de'i phyir kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid bstan pa'i don du /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti / iti vistaraḥ / / abhūtaparikalpasvabhāvaḥ saṃkleśo bhrāntilakṣaṇatvāt /
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces rgya cher gsungs so / / 'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i rang bzhin ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'o /
katham etaj jñātavyaṃ bhrāntilakṣaṇam iti ?
# 'di 'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid du ji ltar shes par bya zhe na /
yena - / dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate
# 'di ltar de la gnyis po yod ma yin /
svātmanyavidhyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa pratyānād / bhrāntisvarūpeṇa jñayate/
# bdag nyid du med par gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang bas 'khrul ba'i ngo bo nyid du mngon ngo /
edāniṃ vyavadānasvarūpapradarṣana arthamāḥ - / śūnyatā vidyate tvatra / iti/ / śūnyatāsvabhāvo hi vyavadānaṃ dvayābhāvasvabhāvatvāt / / atra ca śūnyatāprabhāvitatvāt mārganirodhayor api grahaṇamṃ veditavyaṃ
# da ni rnam par byang ba'i ngo bo brtag pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod / / ces bya ba gsungs so / / gnyis po med pa'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin ni rnam pa byang ba'o / / stong pa nyid kyis rab tu phye bas lam dang 'gog pa dag kyang 'dir bsdu bar rig par bya'o /
saṅkleśapakṣād eva vyavadānapakṣo mārgayitavyo na punaḥ pṛthaktvam / asyāstīti pradarśanārtham āha atreti /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs nyid las rnam par byang ba'i phyogs nyid btsal bar bya ba'i rang gi rgyud gud na med par rab tu bstan pa'i phyir 'di la zhes bya ba gsungs so /
yadi dvayaṃ nāsti kathaṃ tasyāṃ vidyamānāyāṃ loko bhrānta ityāha - / tasyām api sa vidyate iti /
# gal te gnyis po med na ci'i phyir de yod par 'jig rten 'khrul bar gyur zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir de la yang ni de yod do zhes bya ba gsungs te /
grāhyagrāhakavikalpo hastyādyākāraśūnyamāyāyām iva / hastyākārādayaḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o / / sgyu ma ni gang po che la sogs pas stong yang / / glang po che la sogs par snang ba lta bu'o /
abhūtam asmin dvayaṃ parikalpyate'nena vetyabhūtaparikalpaḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa gnyis po de la'am / / des yongs su rtog pas yang dag pa ma yin pa gnyis por yongs su rtog pas yang dag ma yin kun rtog pa'o /
abhūtavacanena ca yathā'yaṃ parikalpyate grāhyagrāhakatvena tathā / nāstīti pradarśayati / / parikalpavacanena tvartho yathā parikalpyate tathārtho na vidhyate iti / pradarṣayati/ / evam asya grāhyagrāhakavinirmuktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati / / kaḥ punar asau ?
# yang dag pa ma yin pa'i tshig gis ni / / ji ltar 'di la gzung ba dang 'dzin par kun rtog pa de bzhin du med par ston to / / kun rtog pa'i tshig gis ni don ji lta bur kun rtog pa don de lta bur yod pa ma yin zhes ston te / / de ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa las rnam par grol ba de'i mtshan nyid bshad pa yin no /
atītānāgatavartamānā hetuphalabhūtās traidhātukā anādikālikā / nirvāṇaparyavasānāḥ saṃsārānurūpāścittacaittā
# de yang gang yin zhe na sems dang sems las byung ba 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi dang rgyu dang 'bras bur gyur pa dang khams gsum pa dang thog ma med pa'i dus can dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i mthar thug pa dan / / 'khor ba'i rjes su mthun pa dag ni /
aviśeṣeṇābhūtaparikalpaḥ / / viśeṣeṇa [p.12] / tu grāhyagrāhakavikalpaḥ /
# khyad par med par yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'o / / khyad par ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa rnam par rtog pa'o /
tatra grāhyavikalpo'rthasattvapratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ /
# de la gzung bar rnam par rtog pa ni; don dang sems can du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'o /
grāhakavikalpa ātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ /
# 'dzin par rnam par rtog pa ni bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba'o /
dvayaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañceti / / tatra grāhyaṃ rūpādi /
# gnyis po ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba de la gzung ba ni gzugs la sogs pa'o /
grāhakaṃ cakṣūr vijñānādi /
# 'dzin pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa'o /
grāhyagrāhakabhāvena virahitatā viviktatā hyabhūtaparikalpasya / śanyatā / / na tv abhūtaparikalpo'pyabhāvaḥ yathā śūnyā rajjuḥ sarpasvabhāvenātat / svabhāvatvāt sarvakālaṃ śūnyā na tu rajju svabhāvena tathehāpi /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po dang bral ba nyid de / / dben pa nyid ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i stong pa nyid yin gyi / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yang med pa ni ma yin te / / dper na thag pa ni sprul pa'i dngos po stong ste / / de'i rang bzhin ma yin pas dus thams cad du stong pa nyid yin gyi / / thag pa'i dngos po ni ma yin te / / 'dir yang de bzhin no /
tasyām api sa vidyata iti abhūtaparikalpaḥ /
# de la yang ni de yod do zhes bya ba ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ste /
evaṃ hy āgantukāvaraṇopakliṣṭatvāt tad agrahaṇam uktam abdhātvādivad  iti /
# de ltar glo bur gyi sgrib pas nyon mongs pa'i phyir / / de chu khams la sogs pa bzhin du rtogs par mi rung ngo zhes bstan pa yin no /
evaṃ yad yatra nāsti tat tena śūnyam iti yathābhūtaṃ samanupaśyatīti /
# de ltar gang na gang med pa de ni / / des stong par yang dag par rjes su mthong ngo zhes bya ba la /
kiṃ kutra nāsti ?
# ci zhig gang na med ce na /
abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis po ste /
ato'bhūtaparikalpaṃ dvayena śūnyaṃ paśyati /
# de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis kyis stong par mthong ngo /
yat punar atrā'vaśiṣṭaṃ tat sat / / kiṃ punar ihāvaśiṣṭaṃ ?
# 'di la lhag ma gang yin pa de ni yod pa de 'di la lhag ma gang yin zhe na /
abhūtaparikalpaḥ śūnyatā ca / / tad ubhayam ihāstītyanādhyāropānapavādena paśyan yathābhūtaṃ
# yang dag ma yin pa kun rtog pa stong pa nyid dang de gnyi ga yang 'dir yod par ma skur ba dang sgro btags pa med par mthong na yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so /
prajānāti / / tatrābhūtaparikalpe'dvayadarśanād anadhyāropaḥ /
# de la yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis po med par mthong ba'i phyir sgro mi 'dogs so /
abhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatāścāstitvadarśanād anapavādaḥ / / aviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇam udbhāvitaṃ bhavati / / yac chūnyaṃ tasya sad bhāvāt yena śūnyaṃ tasya tatrābhāvāt / / sarvabhāve sarvābhāve vā nāviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ / / śūnyatāyā evābhāvaprasaṅgāt / / na śūnyasaṃjñā'satyāṃ śūunyatāyāṃ yujyate / / dharmatāyā hi bhāvāyāt tattvād anityatvādivat / / dvayam astīti śūnyatābhāvaḥ / / yadi śaśaviṣāṇakalpanena dvayaṃ kathaṃ tenābhūtaparikalpasya / śūnyatāsambhavaḥ ? / anyena hy anyasya śūunyatā dṛṣṭā yathā bhikṣubhir vihārasya / / naitad evaṃ / / yathā rajjur māyā vā svātmany avidyamānena sarpākāreṇa puruṣādinā / prabhāsate /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa dang stong pa nyid yod par mthong ba'i phyir te / / skur pa mi 'debs te / / stong pa nyid gang yin pa de yod pa dang gang gis stong pa de de la med pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid phyin ci ma log par bstan pa yin no / / thams cad med pa'am thams cad yod pa ni stong pa nyid kyang mtshan nyid phyin ci log yin te / / stong pa nyid med par 'gyur ro / / stong pa zhes bya ba med na stong pa nyid du mi rung ste / / chos nyid ni dngos po la rag lus pa'i phyir mi rtag pa nyid la sogs pa bzhin no / / gnyis po yod do zhe na / / stong pa nyid med par 'gyur ro / / gal te gnyis po ni ri bong gi ra dang 'dren yang ji ltar des yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa stong ste /
tatra kasyacid grāhanirvartanārthaṃ sarpapuruṣādibhiś ca śūnyety ucyate / evam abhūtaparikalpo'pi svātmany avidyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa / prakhyāyamāno bālānāṃ tad grāhābhiniveśaty ājanārthaṃ dvayena / śūnyam ity ucyate //1-2// [p.13] / na śūnyaṃ nā'pi cā'śūnyaṃ iti / / kim artham asau śloka ārabdha iti ?
# dper na dge slong rnams kyis gtsug lag khang bzhin du gzhan gyis gzhan stong par mthong zhe na; dper na thag pa la'am sgyu ma la bdag nyid kyis med par sbrul gyi rnam pa dang skyes bu la sogs pa lta bur snang ba de la kha cig 'dzin pa bzlog pa'i phyir / / sbrul dang skyes bu la sogs pas stong ngo zhes brjod pa de bzhin du / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog pa la yang bdag nyid kyis med par gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang ba de la byis pa rnams 'dzin cing mngon par zhen pa dor bar bya ba'i phyir gnyis kyis ston zhes bshad do / / stong pa ma yin mi stong min / / zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di ci'i phyir brtsams she na /
sarvasya saṃskṛtasyāsaṃskṛtasya ca dvayarahitatājñāpanārthaṃ /
# 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas thams cad gnyis dang bral ba nyid du shes par bya ba'i phyir ro /
evaṃ ca hyekāntapratikṣepeṇa sarvam idaṃ na śūnyaṃ nāśūnyam iti / prajñāpāramitāpāṭhābhiprāyatāviṣkṛtā bhavati / / anyathā pūrvāparaviruddham etat syāt /
# de ltar mtha' gcig bkag pas 'di thams cad stong pa yang ma yin mi stong pa yang ma yin pa zhes shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i nang nas bshad pa'i dgongs pa bstan pa yin no / / gzhan du na ltag 'og 'gal bar 'gyur ro /
kiñca madhyamāpratipat prakāśanārthaṃ /
# gzhan yang dbu ma'i lam rab tu bstan pa'i phyir te /
anyathaikāntikaśūnyataivāśanyānto vā syāt /
# gzhan du na ni gcig tu stong pa kho na'am / / mi stong pa'i mthar 'gyur ro /
apavādasamāropapratiṣedhopasaṃhārārthaṃ vā'syārambhaḥ /
# yang na skur pa 'debs pa dang sgro 'dogs pa dgag pa bshad ma thag pa mjug bsdu ba'i don du de brtsams so /
hetupratyayapratibaddhātmalābhād abhūtaparikalpaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ /
# rgyu dang rkyen dang 'brel pa las skyes pa'i phyir / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni 'dus byas te /
śūnyatā punas tan nirapekṣatvād asaṃskṛtaṃ /
# de la mi ltos pa'i phyir stong pa nyid ni 'dus ma byas so /
vidhīyate prajñāpāramitādimadhye paṭhyate /
# bshad pa ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa'i nang nas 'byung ba'o /
sattvād abhūtaparikalpasya na saṃskṛtaṃ śūnyam abhūtaparikalpātmatvena / asatvād dvayasya / / grāhyagrāhakātmanā śūnyaṃ /
# yod pas zhes bya ba ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ste / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i bdag nyid kyis 'dus byas stong pa ma yin no / / med pas zhes bya ba ni gnyis po ste / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyis stong pa'o /
śūnyātāyās tu sarvam abhūtaparikalpe tad dharmateti kṛtvā /
# stong pa nyid ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la de'i chos nyid du yod de /
śūnyatāyām apy abhūtaparikalpo dharmirūpeṇa vidyate /
# stong pa nyid la yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa chos can gyi ngo bor yod do /
evam asaṃskṛtam api dharmatārūpeṇa na śūnyaṃ /
# de ltar 'dus ma byas kyang chos nyid kyi ngo bos stong pa ma yin te /
abhāvasaṃjñakena dvayena svarūpaśūnyaṃ /
# dngos po med ces bya ba gnyis kyi ngo bos stong pa'o /
sā ca madhyamā pratipad iti ratnakūṭādimadhye'stīti kāśyapāyam / eko'ntaḥ / / nāstītyayaṃ dvitīyo'ntaḥ / / yadetayor dvayor antayor madhyamiyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipad / dharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣeti sā madhyamā pratipadevam anulomitā / / sarvam iti saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtañca /
# de ni dbu ma'i lam yin no zhes bya ba ni dkon mchog brtsegs pa la sogs pa'i nang nas / / 'od srungs yod ces bya ba 'di ni mtha' gcig go / / med ces bya ba 'di ni mtha' gnyis te / / 'od srungs mtha' gnyis po 'di dag gi dbus gang yin pa 'di ni chos rnams la yang dag par so sor rtog pa'o zhes 'byung ba gang yin pa ste / / de ltar dbu ma'i lam de dang mthun par byas pa yin no / / thams cad ces bya ba ni 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas so /
naikāntena śūnyam ity abhūtaparikalpasya tac chūnyatāyāś ca [p.14] / sadbhāvāt /
# gcig tu stong pa yang ma yin zhes bya ba ni / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog dang de la stong pa nyid kyang yod pa'i phyir ro /
nāpyekāntenāśūnyaṃ dvayasyābhāvāt /
# gcig tu mi stong pa yang ma yin pa ni gnyis po med pa'i phyir ro /
sarvanāstitvaṃ sarvāstitvaṃ vā'nta eva syāt / / na madhyamā pratipad //1-3//
# thams cad yod pa'am thams cad med pa ni mtha' nyid du 'gyur gyi / / dbu ma'i lam ma yin no /
evam abhūtaparikalpasya sal lakṣaṇam asallakṣaṇañca khyāpayitveti /
# de ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i yod pa'i mtshan nyid dang med pa'i mtshan nyid brjod nas zhes bya ba 'di /
idaṃ sattvena lakṣyata iti sattvam eva sallakṣaṇaṃ /
# yod par nye bar mtshon pas yod pa nyid / / yod pa'i mtshan nyid de /
abhūtaparikalpo vidyata ity anenābhūtaparikalpasya sattvaṃ / pradarśayatīty arthaḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod ces bya ba des yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod par ston zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
evam asattvena lakṣyata iti asatvam evāsal lakṣaṇāt / / tat punar yad grāhyagrāhakabhāvenāsattvaṃ /
# de bzhin du med par nye bar mtshon pas med pa nyid med pa'i mtshan nyid de / / de yang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po med pa ste /
yasmād abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ nāsti tasmād abhūtaparikalpo'pi / dvayātmanā nāstīty uktaṃ bhavati /
# 'di ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis po med pas de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yang gnyis kyi bdag nyid kyis yod pa ma yin no zhes bstan pa yin no /
svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti / / ko viśeṣo'sti sallakṣaṇasvalakṣaṇayoḥ ? / sallakṣaṇaṃ hi sāmānyaṃ / / svalakṣaṇam tu viśeṣaḥ /
# rang gi mtshan nyid brjod de zhes bya ba la yod pa'i mtshan nyid dang rang gi mtshan nyid gnyis khyad par ci yod ce na / / yod pa'i mtshan nyid ni spyi'i'o / / rang gi mtshan nyid ni bye brag yin no /
yadi svalakṣaṇam anākhyātamatra kiṃ syāt ?
# gal te rang gi mtshan nyid ma bshad na ci zhig tu 'gyur zhe na /
śarīram abhūtaparikalpasya noktaṃ syāt /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i lus ma bshad par 'gyur te /
atas tac charīrapratipādanārtham ucyate -
# de bas na de'i lus khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir /
arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ prajāyate / / vijñānaṃ nāsti cā'syārthas tadabhāvāt tadapyasat // iti /
# don dang sems can bdag rnam rig / / snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni / / rab tu skye'o de'i don med / / de med pas na de yang med /
atha vā grāhyagrāhakarahitatā'bhūtaparikalpamātrate'ty ucciṣṭaṃ / / tasyām abhūtaparikalpamātratāyām indriyaviṣayavijñānaṃ yathā
# ces bya ba gsungs so / / yang na gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa'i yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam nyid yod do zhes bstan pa yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam de la /
vyavasthitaṃ na jñāyata / / abhūtaparikalpapratibhāsabhedena tad vyavasthitajñāpanārtham
# dbang po dang yul dang rnam par shes pa ji ltar rnam par gzhag pa mi shes pas yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i snang ba tha dad pa de la rnam par gzhag go zhes shes par bya ba'i phyir /
abhūtaparikalpasya svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati - / arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ / / iti vistaraḥ / [p.15]
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i rang gi mtshan nyid bshad de / / don dang sems can bdag rnam rig / / snang ba'i zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o; /
atha vā 'bhūtaparikalpo'stītyanena tat sattvamātraṃ jñāyate na tu / tat svabhāvaḥ / / dvayābhāve'pi yad grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśakāraṇaṃ na vijñāyate dvayaṃ / ca nāstīti yataḥ pratīyate tad api noktam ityatas tat pratipādanārtham
# yang na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod ces bya ba des de yod pa tsam du shes par byed kyi / / de'i rang bzhin ni ma yin pa dang gnyis po med par yang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa'i rgyu gang yin pa rnam par mi shes pa dang gang gi phyir gnyis po med par yid ches par bya ba de yang ma bshad pas de bstan pa'i phyir /
āha - / arthasattvātmavijñapti pratibhāsaṃ
# don dang sems can bdag rnam rig / / snang ba'i zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
iti vistaraḥ / / tatra vijñānasvabhāvo'bhūtaparikalpaḥ /
# de la yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin no /
tac ca vijñānaṃ sasamprayogam abhipretaṃ /
# rnam par shes pa de yang 'dir mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas par dgongs te /
pradhānena tu vijñānaṃ gṛhītaṃ /
# gtso bor ni rnam par shes pa gzung ngo /
sa eva grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśo'rthasattvādipratibhāsanibandhanaḥ / / nāsti cāsyārthas tadabhāvāt tad apyasat / iti / / dvayābhāvakāraṇaṃ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa de nyid kyi rgyu ni don dang sems can la sogs par snang ba'o / / de'i don med de med pas na de yang med ces bya ba ni gnyis po med pa'i rgyu'o /
tatrārthasattvapratibhāsamālayavijñānaṃ sasamprayogaṃ /
# de la don dang sems can du snang ba'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa ste /
tac ca vipākatvād avyākṛtam eva /
# de yang rnam par smin pa'i phyir lung du ma bstan pa nyid do /
ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ sasaṃprayogaṃ /
# bdag tu snang ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi yid mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'o /
tac ca nivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ kleśasaṃprayuktatvād uktaṃ /
# de yang bsgribs la lung du ma bstan pa ste / / nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir bstan pa'o /
vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtaṃ sasamprayigañcakṣur / vijñānādi ṣaṭkaṃ /
# rnam par rig par snang ba ni / / mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa la sogs pa drug po mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'o /
tadetānyarthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsānyaṣṭau vijñānāni / sasamprayogāṇi samudayasatyasaṅgṛhītāt sahakāripratyayāpekṣād / ālayavijñānāt yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pañcagatiṣu prabhavanti / / kaścit
# don dang sems can dang bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba rnam par shes pa brgyad po mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa de dag ni kun 'byung ba'i bden par bsdus pa / / lhan cig byed pa'i rkyen la ltos pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las ji ltar mthun mthun du 'gro ba lnga rnams su rab tu 'byung ngo /
kuśalā'kuśala-avyākṛtadharma-vāsanāpariṇāmaviśeṣo'sty-ālayavijñānasya
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos kyis bag chags 'gyur ba'i khyad par 'ga' zhig yod de /
yadādhipatyena parasparabhinnābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prajāyate /
# de dbang gis phan tshun tha dad par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa rab tu skye'o /
katham asatyarthādau vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam utpadyate ? / na hi puruṣe'sati sthāṇuḥ puruṣābhāso bhavatīti / / naiṣa doṣaḥ /
# don la sogs pa med pa der snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ji ltar skye ste / / mi med na sdong po mi snang bar mi 'gyur ba lta ba'o zhe na /
arthādyābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ bālā vijñānāt pṛthag / arthāstitvenā'bhiniviśante taimirikasya keśoṇḍukādivat /
# de ni nyes pa ma yin te / / don la sogs par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa la byas pa rnam par shes pa las don gud na yod par mngon par zhen te / / rab rib can la skra shad 'dzings pa la sogs pa bzhin no /
tasmāt tadabhiniveśatyājanārtham ucyate - / vijñānam evedam arthādyābhāsam utpadyate taimirikāṇām iva
# de'i phyir de la mngon par zhen pa spangs pa'i phyir / / rnam par shes pa 'di nyid don la sogs par snang bar 'byung ste /
keśoṇḍukādyābhāsaṃ vināpyarthasattvādineti /
# rab rib can la skra shad 'dzings pa la sogs pa snang ba de bzhin du med par yang don dang sems can la sogs par snang ngo zhes brjod do /
evaṃ cāṣṭavijñānavastukaḥ paratantro'bhūtaparikalpa ity uktaṃ bhavati /
# de ltar na rnam par shes pa brgyad kyi dngos po can / / gzhan gyi dbang ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog par bshad pa yin no /
rūpādabhāveneti rūpa-śabda-gandha-rasa-spraṣṭavya dharmasvarūpeṇa / pratibhāsaṃ tadākāreṇotpannatvāt /
# gzugs la sogs pa'i dngos por zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg pa dang chos kyi ngo bor snang ba ni de'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
sattvapratibhāsaṃ yat pañcendriyatvena svaparasantānayoḥ / / pratibhāsa ity adhikṛtaṃ / / adhikasaktisthānatvāt pañcasv indriyeṣu sattvākhyā / / tais teṣu vā sajjata iti sattvaḥ / / tadākārotpattitām upādāya vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam iti / / ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ ātmamohādisamprayogād iti kliṣṭasya
# sems can du snang ba'i dbang po lngar bdag dang gzhan gyi rgyud la gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni / / snang ba zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro / / dbang po lnga la sems can zhes bya bar lhag par chags pa'i gnas su gyur pa ste / / de dag gis sam / / de dag la chags pas sems can te / / de'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir / / de snang ba'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o /
manasa ātmamohenātmadṛṣṭyā ātmatṛṣṇāyā'smimānena ca nityaṃ / samprayuktatvāt [p.16] / teṣāñcātmālambanatvādy uktam ātmapratibhāsatvaṃ kliṣṭasya manasaḥ / / vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ ṣaḍ vijñānānīti /
# bdag tu snang ba zhes bya ba dang bdag tu snang ba ni bdag tu rmongs pa la sogs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir / / nyon mongs pa can gyi yid do zhes bya ba la nyon mongs pa can gyi yid ni bdag tu rmongs pa dang bdag tu lta ba dang bdag la chags pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang rtag tu mtshungs par ldan pa dang de dag kyang bdag tu dmigs pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa can gyi yid ni bdag tu snang bar rigs so /
viṣamagrāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānāt tadākārotpattitām upādāya / vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ / / nāsti cāsyārtha iti catuṣṭayasyākārasyeti /
# rnam par rig par snang ba ni rnam par shes pa drug rnams so zhes bya ba ni yul 'dzin pa'i ngo bor snang bas de'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir rnam par rig pa snang ngo / / de'i don med ces bya ba ni rnam pa bzhi char gyi'o /
arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca / vitathapratibhāsatvād iti arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt / ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca vitathapratibhāsatvād iti / arthasattvapratibhāsayor grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānād / vitathapratibhāsatvāsambhavād anākāratvam evārthābhāve kāraṇaṃ / / na tv anyayor grāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānād anākāraḥ / / vitathapratibhāsatvem evārthābhāve kāraṇam uktaṃ / / ākāro hyālambanasyānityādirūpeṇa grahaṇaprakāraḥ / / sa cānayor nāsti grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānāt / / ato'nākāratvād agrāhakatvād ityarthaḥ / / ālambanasamvedanaṃ vākāraḥ / / tac ca tayor nāstīty upalabdhyabhāvād anākāraḥ / / yadyubhayam apy anākāraṃ parasparabhinnasvarūpac ca rūpādivac
# don dang sems can du snang ba rnam pa med pa dang bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba ni log par snang ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni don dang sems can du snang ba gnyis gzung ba'i ngo bor snang bas / / log par snang ba mi srid pa'i phyir / / rnam pa med pa nyid ni don med pa'i rgyu'o / / gzhan dag ni 'dzin pa'i ngo bor snang bas rnam pa med pa ma yin te / / log par snang ba nyid ni don med pa'i rgyu'o zhes bshad do / / rnam pa ni dmigs pa la mi rtag pa la sogs pa'i ngo bor 'dzin pa'i rnam pa yin na / / de yang de dag la med de / / gzung ba'i ngo bor snang bas de'i phyir rnam pa med pa ni 'dzin pa ma yin no zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / yang na dmigs pa yang dag par tshor ba la rnam pa zhes bya ste / / de yang de dag la med pas dmigs pa med pa'i phyir rnam pa med do / / gal te gnyis ka yang rnam pa med pa dang phan tshun tha dad pa'i ngo bo yin te / / gzugs la sogs pa dang mig la sogs pa bzhin no /
cakṣurādivac ca evaṃ sati lokaśāstraprasiddhebhyo / rūpādibhyaścakṣurādibhyaś ca vijñānasya ko'sāvātmātiśayo yatas tān / nirākritya tair abhinnarūpaṃ vijñānaṃ gṛhyate tad / avyatiriktasyārthasyāsambhavāt ? / etad evaṃ vyavasthāpyate - / yasmād bhinnarthasvarūpamasannapicittāsantānapratiniyamena svabījāt
# de lta yin na ni 'jig rten dang bstan bcos las grags pa'i gzugs la sogs pa dang mig la sogs pa las rnam par shes pa rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa ci yod na / / 'di ltar de dag ni gsal la / / de dag dang tha dad pa med pa'i ngo bo rnam par shes pa ni yongs su bzung zhe na / / de las lhag pa'i don mi srid pa'i phyir ro / / de ni 'di ltar rnam par gzhag ste / / 'di ltar tha dad pa'i don gyi ngo bo med kyang sems kyi rgyud so sor nges pas /
pratyekātmagrahītaṃ bhinnārthādipratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prasūyate /
# rnam par shes pa nyid so sos zin pa tha dad pa'i don la sogs par snang bar rang gi sa bon las rab tu 'byung ste /
tathāhi pretā apaḥ pūyapurīṣamūtrādipūrṇā dhṛtadaṇḍapāṇibhir / ubhayataḥ purusaiḥ saṃrakṣyamāṇāḥ paśyanti manuṣYādayaḥ punaḥ / svacchaśītalodakaparipūrṇā nirvibandhā ity upalabhante / / yoginaścāśubhamanasikārādy abhyastā nirantaraṃ pṛthivīṃ / kaṅkālapūrṇāṃ paśyanti /
# 'di ltar yi dags rnams kyis chu rnag dang phyi sa dang gcin la sogs pas gang ba dang skyes bu la gan dbyig pa thogs pa rnams kyis dogs gnyis bsrung bar mthong la / / mi la sogs pas ni chu dang ba dang bsil ba dang bkrur rung ba dang btung du rung ba dang 'jug tu rung bas gang zhig bgegs byed pa med par shes so / / rnal 'byor pa mi sdug pa yid la byed pa la sogs pa goms pas ni / / rgyun mi 'chad par sa la keng rus kyis gang bar mthong ngo /
tathā pṛthivyādi kṛtsneṣu sarvaṃ pṛthivayādibhir vyāptaṃ paśyati /
# de bzhin du sa la sogs pa zad par la thams cad sa la sogs pas khyab par mthong ngo /
na cārthapratibuddhātmalābhasya-arthamantareṇa-arthasvarūpād vā / bhinnākārasya vijñānāsya prasūtir yuktā /
# don la rag las te bdag nyid thob pa ni don med par ram / / don gyi rang gi ngo bo tha dad pa'i rnam pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung bar mi rigs so /
tasmāt tad arthamantareṇa sarvam arthasattvādinirbhāsaṃ vijñānam eva / prasūyata iti niścīyate /
# de bas na don med par yang don dang sems can la sogs pa thams cad du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa nyid rab tu 'byung ngo zhes bya bar nges so /
grāhyābhāve dvayor ātmavijñaptipratibhāsayor grāhakākāreṇa / prakhyānāt vitathapratibhāsatvaṃ /
# gzung ba med par bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba gnyis 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang bas log par snang ba nyid do /
atha vā yathā vijñānenārthaḥ parikalpyate tathārthasyābhāvo / vyāghrādiśrutyādiṣv iva vitathālambanatvād vitathapratibhāsatā /
# yang na ji ltar rnam par shes pas don yongs su brtags pa de bzhin du bdag dang rnam par rig par don med de stag la sogs pa thob pa ltar / / log par dmigs pa'i phyir /
tathā hi vijñaptir api vijñapty antaraparikalpitenātmanā śūnyeti / siddhāntaḥ /
# log par snang ba nyid do / / 'di ltar rnam par rig pa yang rnam par rig pa gzhan gyis kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid kyis stong ngo zhes grub pa'i mtha' las 'byung ngo /
ataścārthasattvavijñānasyevātmavijñaptipratibhāsasyāpyarthābhāvaḥ /
# de'i phyir don dang sems can du snang ba bzhin du / / bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba'i don yang med do /
arthābhāvāt tad vijñānam asat / / vijānātīti vijñānaṃ grāhyābhāve vijānanāpy ayuktaṃ /
# don med pas rnam par shes pa de yang med do / / rnam par rig pas na rnam par shes pa ste / / de yang gzung ba med na rnam par shes pa por mi rigs te /
tasmād arthābhāvād vijñātṛtvena vijñānam asad na [p.17] / tv arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsatayā /
# de lta bas na don med pa'i phyir rnam par shes pa kho nar rnam par shes pa med kyi don dang sems can dang bdag dang rnam par rig par snang bas na med pa ma yin no /
tad asattve hi sarvathā'bhāvaprasaṅgaḥ / / tad avyatirekeṇa vijñānasvabhāvānirdeśāt / / tad bhinnasvabhāve sati tad vijñānaṃ kathaṃ yujyeta kathaṃ parasparaṃ / bhinnaṃ bhavet ? //1-4//
# de med du zin na de ma gtogs par rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin ma bstan pa'i phyir ye med par thal bar 'gyur ro / / de dang tha dad pa'i rang bzhin yin na ni de ji ltar rnam par shes par rung / / ji ltar phan tshun tha dad par 'gyur /
evaṃgrāhyagrāhakābhāvāt tat pratibhāsavijñānasadbhāvāc ca yat / pūrvaṃ pratijñātaṃ - / abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate / / iti tat prasiddham iti pradarśayann āha - / abhūtaparikalpatvaṃ siddham asya bhavatyataḥ / / abhūtaparikalpatvañca teṣāñcaturṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ siddhaṃ /
# de ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa ni med la de snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni yod pas / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni yod / / gnyis po ni de na yod pa ma yin par sngar dam bcas pa de grub po zhes rab tu bstan pa'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog pa / / de ni de phyir grub pa yin / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / rnam par shes pa bzhi po de yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog pa grub pa yin no /
ata ity anantaroktād hetorarthābhāvāt tad apy asad iti punar apy
# de phyir zhes bya ba ni bshad ma thag pa'i rgyu de'i phyir te / / don med pas na de yang med ces bya'o /
abhūtaparikalpāstitvaprasādhanārthaṃ dvayābhāvaprasādhanārthañcāha / na tathā sarvathā'bhāvāt / ityādi / / atha vā ata iti vakṣyamāṇādvetoḥ / / tameva pradarṣayannāh / na tathā sarvathā'bhāvāt / iti/ / na tathā'stitvān na ca sarvathā nāstitvāt tad
# yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod par bsgrub pa dang gnyis po med par rab tu bsgrub pa'i phyir / / de bzhin ma yin ye med min / / zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so / / yang na de'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'og nas 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / de nyid rab tu bstan pa'i phyir / / de bzhin ma yin ye med min / / zhes bya ba gsungs te / / de bzhin du yod pa ma yin pa dang ye med pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsam utpadyate /
# gang gi phyir gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba de skye ba ste /
tatra catuḥprakāre'py anākāratvād vitathākāratvāc ca yathāsambhavaṃ / grāhakatvābhāvaḥ /
# de la rnam pa bzhi po de yang rnam pa med pa dang log par snang ba'i phyir ji ltar mthun par 'dzin pa nyid du med do /
vijñaptyantaraparikalpitena cātmanā sarvasya śūnyatvād / grāhyatvābhāvaḥ /
# rnam par rig pa gzhan gyis kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid kyis thams cad stong bas gzung ba nyid du med do /
na ca sarvathā'bhāvo bhrāntimātrasyotpādād ityātmatvenābhāvo na tu
# 'khrul pa tsam 'byung ba'i phyir ye med pa yang ma yin no zhes bya ba ni bdag nyid kyis med kyang /
yadākāreṇa pratibhāsate tena bhrāntir ucyare māyāvat /
# rnam par snang ba gang yin pa de ni 'khrul pa zhes bya ste / / sgyu ma bzhin no /
mātra- śabdas tadadhikavyavacchedārthaḥ / / etad uktaṃ bhavati -
# tsam zhes bya ba'i sgra ni de las lhag ma rnam bar gcad pa'i tha tshig ste /
bhrāntivijñānasya sadbhāvān na sarvathā'bhāva iti /
# de ni 'di skad du 'khrul pa'i rnam par shes pa yod do /
kimartha punas tasya bhrāntivijñānasyā'bhāva eva neṣyate / grāhyagrāhakābhāvavat ? / na hi kenacit tasyāstitvaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyate / sarvāvijñānaviṣayātikrāntatvād ity abhipretam iti cet / / yasmāt -
# ye med pa ma yin no zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / 'khrul pa'i rnam par shes pa de gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa bzhin du med pa nyid du ci'i phyir mi 'dod / / rnam par shes pa thams cad kyi yul las 'das pa'i phyir / / sus kyang de yod pa nyid du brtag par mi nus so zhes bsams pa'o zhe na 'di ltar /
tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate /
# de zad nas ni grol bar 'dod /
ato'syābhāva eva neṣyate / / kiṃ tarhi saṅkleśavyavadānapakṣasāmarthāt tad astitvam anumīyate / [p.18]
# de'i phyir de med pa nyid du mi 'dod do / / de ji lta zhe na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i phyogs kyi mthus de yod par rjes su dpag go /
anyatheti yadi tasya sarvathābhāva eveṣyate na bandho na mokṣa iti /
# gzhan du na zhes bya ba ni gal te ye med pa nyid du 'dod na ni bcings pa yang med ces bya ste /
bhrāntimātre'py asati saṅkleśābhāvād bandho'pi nāsti /
# 'khrul pa tsam yang med du zin na / / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pas bcings pa yang med do /
pūrvaṃ baddho mucyata iti kṛtvā muktir api na syāt / / atha vā kathaṃ na yathā prakhyāti tathā bhāveneṣyate sarvathā
# sngar bcings pa las grol lo zhes bya na grol ba yang med par 'gyur / / yang na de ji ltar snang ba de bzhin du yod pa'am /
vā'bhāva iti parābhiprāyavyudāsārtham āha -
# yang na ye med par ci'i phyir mi 'dod ces gzhan de snyam du sems pa bsal ba'i phyir /
tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate / / tasmiṃścāparikṣīṇe bandha ityarthād uktaṃ bhavati /
# de zad nas ni grol bar 'dod / / ces gsungs te / / de ma zad na bcings pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
anyathā hi na bandho na mokṣa iti saṅkleśavyavadānāpavādadoṣaḥ syāt /
# de gzhan du na bcings pa dang grol ba med do zhes de skad bshad par 'gyur te / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang mya ngan las 'das pa la skur ba 'debs pa'i nyes par 'gyur ro /
yathā grāhyagrāhakatvena bhrāntir udbhāsitā'pi yadi tathā syāt / paramārthata evaṃ sati nityaḥ saṅkleśaḥ syāt /
# gal te ji ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa nyid du phyugs yan chad la snang ba yang gal te de bzhin du don dam par 'gyur na ni / / de ltar yin du zin na rtag par kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur te /
tathā ca nirvāṇābhāvaḥ / / evaṃ ca bhrāntimātrasyāpy abhāve saṅkleśābhāvo nityañca vyavadānaṃ / prasajyeta /
# de ltar na mya ngan las 'das pa yang med par 'gyur ro / / de ltar 'khrul pa tsam med na yang kun nas nyon mongs pa med par 'gyur te / / rtag tu rnam par byang bar 'gyur ro /
evaṃ cobhayathāpi mokṣārthināṃ vyartho yatnaḥ syāt / / ato'vaśyam abhūtaparikalpabhāvo'bhyupagantavyo dvayābhāvaś ca //1-5//
# de ltar na gnyi gar yang thar pa tshol ba rnams kyi 'bad pa don med par 'gyur bas de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod pa dang gnyis po med par gdon mi za bar khas blang bar bya'o /
saṅgrahalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti saṅgraha eva lakṣaṇaṃ /
# bsdu ba'i mtshan nyid ston te zhes bya ba ni / / bsdu ba nyid mtshan nyid do /
atha vā yena saṅgraho lakṣyate tat saṅgrahalakṣaṇaṃ / / tac ca kim artham uktaṃ ?
# yang na gang gis bsdu bar mtshon pa de bsdu ba'i mtshan nyid do / / de yang ci'i phyir bshad ce na /
atra hi grāhyagrāhakarahitam abhūtaparikalpamātramevāstīty ayuktaṃ /
# 'dir ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang brla ba yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam nyid yod do zhes smras la /
sūtrāntareṣu punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ paṭhyante / / ataḥ sūtrāntarair avirodhapradarśanārthaṃ teṣām iha saṅgraha ucyate / / ata eva vṛttikāra āha -
# mdo gzhan dag las ni / / ngo bo nyid gsum gsungs pas mdo dag dang mi 'gal bar rab tu bstan pa'i phyir de dag 'dir bsdu bar brjod de / / de lta bas na 'grel pa mdzad pas /
abhūtaparikalpamātre satīti vistareṇa -
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam du zad na zhes bya ba rgya cher smos so /
kalpitaḥ paratantraś ca pariniṣpanna eva ca /
# brtag pa dang ni gzhan dbang dang / / yongs su grub pa nyid kyang ngo /
arthād abhūtakalpāc ca dvayābhāvāc ca deśitaḥ // iti /
# don phyir yang dag min rtog phyir / / gnyis po med pa'i phyir bshad do / / zhes bya ba ni /
grāhyaṃ grāhakaṃ ca svabhāvaśūnyatvād abhūtam apy astitvena / parikalpyata iti [p.19] / parikalpita ucyate / / sa punar dravyato'sannapi vyavahārato'stīti svabhāva ucyate / / paratantraḥ paravaśaḥ hetupratyayapratibaddhajanmakatvāt / / āha ca -
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa rang bzhin gyis stong pa las yang dag pa ma yin par yang yod par yongs su rtog pas kun brtags pa zhes bya'o / / de ni rdzas su med kyang tha snyad du yod pas ngo bo nyid ces bya'o / / gzhan gyi dbang ni rgyu dang rkyen la rag las te skye bas gzhan gyi kha na las pa'o / / smras pa /
akalpitaḥ pratyayaco'nabhilāpyaś ca sarvathā /
# brtags min rkyen las skyes pa dang / / rnam pa kun tu brjod med pa /
paratantrasvabhāvo hi śuddhalaukikagocaraḥ //
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid / / 'jig rten pa yi spyod yul lo /
yā'bhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā sa pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ / tasyā'saṃskṛtatvāt nirvikāratvena pariniṣpannatvāt / / āha ca - / kalpitena svabhāvena tasya yā'tyantaśūnyatā /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa nyid gnyis dang bral ba nyid gang yin pa de ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid de / / de ni 'dus ma byas pas mi 'gyur bar yongs su grub pa'o / / brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis te / / shin tu stong nyid gang yin pa /
svabhāvaḥ pariniṣpanno 'vikalpajñānagocaraḥ // / arthād ityarthādhipatyād uktaṃ /
# yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo ste / / mi rtog ye shes spyod yul lo / / don phyir zhes bya ba ni don gyi dbang du mdzad nas bshad pa ste /
evam abhūtaparikalpād dvayābhāvācceti vaktavyaṃ /
# de ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i phyir dang gnyis po med pa'i phyir ro zhes brjod par bya'o /
arthaḥ parikalpitaḥ svabhāva ityartho'tra rūpādayaścakṣurādaya ātmā / vijñaptayaś ca /
# don ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid do zhes bya la / / don ni 'dir gzugs la sogs pa dang mig la sogs pa dang bdag dang rnam par rig pa rnams te /
sa ca kalpitena svabhāvenābhūtaparikalpe nāstīty asan parikalpitaḥ / svabhāva ucyate / / āha ca -
# de yang rnam par brtags pa'i rang bzhin du yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la med pas / / med pa la kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bya'o / / yang smras pa /
akalpito vikalpo hi vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ / / svabhāvo nāstyasau tasya vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ //
# rnam rtog rnam par mi rtog ni / / rnam rtog gzhan gyis brtags pa ste / / rnam rtog gzhan gyis brtags de yi / / rang bzhin de ni yod ma yin /
abhūtaparikalpaḥ paratantraḥ svabhāva iti / / parair hetupratyayais tantryate janyate na tu svayambhavatīti paratantraḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid do zhes bya ba la rgyu dang rkyen gzhan dag gi dbang byed pa dang skyed pa ste / / rang mi 'byung bas gzhan gyi dbang ngo /
grāhyagrāhakābhāvaḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva iti / / nirvikārapariniṣpattyā'viparītapariniṣpattyā ca parniṣpannatvāt / pariniṣpanna ucyate /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bya ba ni mi 'gyur bar yongs su grub pa dang phyin ci ma log par yongs su grub pas yongs su grub pa'i phyir / / yongs su grub pa pa'o zhes bya'o /
atra hy abhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā grāhyagrāhakābhāva uktaḥ /
# 'dir ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa gnyis dang bral ba nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med par bstan pa yin gyi /
na tu dvayasyābhāvamātraṃ /
# gnyis po med pa tsam gyis ni ma yin no /
evañcābhūtaparikalpa eva hetupratyapāratantryāt paratantraḥ /
# de ltar na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa nyid rgyu dang rkyen gzhan gyi kha na las pas gzhan gyi dbang ngo /
sa eva grāhyagrāhakarūpeṇa svātmany avidyamānena prakhyānāt / parikalpitaḥ /
# de nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i ngo bor bdag nyid kyis med kyang snang ba'i phyir kun brtags pa'o /
sa eva grāhyagrāhakarahitatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ /
# de nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba'i phyir yongs su grub pa'o /
evam abhūtaparikalpe trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ saṅgrahītāḥ /
# de ltar na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la ngo bo nyid gsum 'dus so /
etenā'bhūtaparikalpam anūdya parijñeyaṃ parijñāya prahātavyaṃ / parijñāya sākṣāt kartavyañca vastu sandarśitaṃ bhavati //1-6// [p.20]
# de ltar byas na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yongs su shes par bya ba dang spang bar bya ba dang yongs su shes par bya ba mngon du bya ba'i dngos po yang bstan pa yin no /
aparijñātāsal lakṣaṇo hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kleśakarmajanmasaṅkleśāya / sampravartate /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa med pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su ma shes pa'i phyir / / nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs par gyur to /
ato'sallakṣaṇaparijñānārtham upāyaṃ pradarśayann āha -
# de lta bas na med pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su shes par bya ba dang de'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir /
upalabdhiṃ samāśritya / iti vistaraḥ / / abhūtaparikalpe tad upalakṣaṇam abhūtaparikalpo veti / / grāhyagrāhakayor asattvam evā'sallakṣaṇaṃ /
# dmigs pa la ni brten nas su / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog pa la de mtshon pa'am / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'o / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis med pa nyid ni med pa'i mtshan nyid do /
tatrānupraveśas tad avabodhaḥ /
# de la 'jug pa ni de khong du chud pa'o /
tasyopāyo yatas tad asallakṣaṇam anupraviśati /
# de'i thabs ni thabs gang gis de'i med pa'i mtshan nyid kyis rjes su 'jug pa'o /
sa punar dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthapratibodhaprayoganiśraya viśeṣaḥ / kuśalo dvividhaḥ /
# de yang chos kyi dbyings kun tu 'gro ba'i don rab tu rtog par bya bar sbyor ba ni / / gnas kyi khyad par mkhas par rnam pa gnyis so /
tad upalakṣyā'yaṃ śloka uktaḥ /
# de nye bar mtshon pa'i don du tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so /
vijñaptimātropalabdhiṃ niśrityā'rthā'nupalabdhir jāyata iti / / idaṃ vijñaptimātram ālambanārtharahitaṃ svabījaparipākād
# rnam par rig pa tsam du dmigs pa la brten nas don mi dmigs pa skye'o zhes bya ba ni / / dmigs pa'i don dang bral ba 'di ni rnam par rig pa tsam nyid de /
rūpādyābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ pravartate na tu rūpādiko'rtho'stītyevaṃ
# rang gi sa bon yongs su smin pa las gzugs la sogs par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa skye ba yin gyi /
grāhakopalabdhiṃ niśritya grāhyānupalabdhiṃ praviśati / / evaṃ hy anena vicārayitavyaṃ -
# gzugs la sogs pa'i don ni yod pa ma yin no zhes de ltar 'dzin pa dmigs pa la gnas te / / gzung ba mi dmigs par rab tu 'jug go / / des 'di ltar brtags par bya ste /
utpadyamānam anutpannaṃ vā vijñānaṃ viṣayamālambeta /
# rnam par shes pa skye ba'i tshe'am / / skye sa zin pas yul la dmigs par 'gyur grang na /
tatrotpadyamānaṃ viṣayaṃ nālambate utpadyamānasyāsattvāt /
# de la skye ba'i tshe ni med pas skye ba'i tshe yul la dmigs par mi rung ngo /
notpannam api viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpannatvāt /
# yul du snang ba'i bdag nyid du skyes pa'i phyir / / skyes pas kyang ma yin te /
na ca viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpattim uktvā vijñānasyānyā kriyā'sti / yāṃ kriyāṃ kurvat vijñānaṃ viṣayam ālambana ity ucyate /
# yul du snang ba'i bdag nyid du skye ba ma gtogs par / / gang byed na rnam par shes pa yul la dmigs pa'o zhes bya'o zhes bya ba'i rnam par shes pa'i bya ba gzhan med do /
yadi vālambanasya vartamāna eva vijñāne vyāpāro notpadyamāne evam / ālambanapratyayo na vijṇyānotpādakaḥ / / tat parikalpanaṃ nirarthakaṃ /
# gal te yang da ltar gyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyi dmigs pa byed pa yin gyi / / skye ba'i tshe ni ma yin no zhe na / / de lta na ni dmigs pa'i rkyen rnam par shes pa'i skye ba ma yin te / / der yongs su rtog pa don med do /
vartamānālambanagrahaṇe kṣaṇabhedadoṣo bhavati /
# da ltar gyi dmigs pa 'dzin na ni skad cig pa 'jig pa'i gnod par 'gyur ro /
na cātmātiśayabhāve pūrvavad vijñānenālambanagrahaṇaṃ yujyate /
# rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa yang med pas snga ma bzhin te / / rnam par shes pas dmigs pa 'dzin par mi rung ngo /
athālambanagrahaṇakāle tasyātmātiśaya iṣyate evam apy / ātmātiśayasyānyata eva darśanād anyadevotpannam ālambanaṃ gṛhṇātīti / prasajyate / / anyo manyate -
# 'on te dmigs pa 'dzin pa'i dus na / / de la rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur par 'dod na / / de lta na yang rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa gzhan nyid du snang bas / / byung ba gzhan nyid kyis dmigs pa 'dzin par thal bar 'gyur ro /
nirudhyamāno'rtha evotpadyamānasya vijñānasyālambanapratyayaḥ /
# gzhan ni 'gag pa'i tshe'i don nyid skye ba'i tshe'i rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa'i rkyen nyid yin te /
sa ca svākārapratibhāsa jñānakāraṇatvena śeṣebhyaḥ pratyayebhyo / viśiṣyata / [p.21]
# de yang rang gi rnam par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'i rgyu yin pas rkyen lhag ma rnams las khyad par can no snyam du sems te /
iti / / tenāpi rūpādiparamāṇavastat samūho vālambanatvena parikalpyate / / ubhayathāpi cālambanābhāvaḥ /
# des kyang gzugs la sogs pa'i rdul phra rab bam / / de 'dus pa la dmigs pa kho nar kun tu brtag grang na / / de gnyi ga yang dmigs par mi 'gyur te /
sarvam eva hi vijñānaṃ ghaṭapaṭādipratibhāsam utpadyate na tu / paramāṇupratibhāsaṃ /
# rnam par shes pa thams cad ni bum pa dang snam bu la sogs par snang ba 'byung gi / / rdul phra rab tu snang ba ni ma yin no /
na cā'rthākārasyā'nyanirbhāsasya vijñānasyānyad ālambanaṃ /
# don gyi rnam pa gzhan du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa ni gzhan ma yin te /
cakṣurādīnām apy ālambanatvaprasaṅga iti /
# mig la sogs pa yang dmigs pa nyid du thal bar 'gyur ta re /
yo'pi manyate samuditāḥ paramāṇava ālambanaṃ na pratyekaṃ tasyāpy ayam / aparihāraḥ /
# gang gzhan yang rdul phra rab sil bu so so la dmigs pa yin pa snyam du sems pa de'i 'di yang lan du mi rung ste /
samuditā api hi te pratyekam evālambanatveneṣYante na tat samudāyena /
# sil bu de ni de dag so so nyid la dmigs par 'dod kyi /
tatra paramāṇūnāṃ pratyekapratibhāsaṃ jñānaṃ notpadyate nāpi tat
# de dag gi 'dus pa la ni ma yin no / / der rdul phra rab so sor snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni mi 'byung gi /
samudāyapratibhāsaṃ /
# 'di ltar de dag gi 'dus par snang ba ste /
tasmān na paramāṇūnām ālambanatvaṃ sambhavati /
# de bas na rdul phra rab rnams la dmigs pa mi srid do /
nāpi paramāṇusamūha ālambanaṃ prajñaptisataḥ kāraṇatvāsambhavāt /
# brtags par yod pa ni rgyur mi srid pa'i phyir / / rdul phra rab 'dus pa yang dmigs pa ma yin na /
vijñānakāraṇaṃ hi samanantarādipratyayavad ālambanapratyayo'pīṣyate /
# de ma thag pa la sogs pa'i rkyen ltar dmigs pa'i rkyen yang dag par shes pa'i rgyur 'dod de /
tasmān na nirudhyamāno'pyālambanaṃ /
# de'i phyir 'gag pa'i tshe yang dmigs pa'i rkyen du mi srid do /
atha ca niruddha ālambanaṃ evaṃ satyātītānāgataṃ viṣayaḥ syāt / / svapnādau tu vijñānam anālambanam iti siddhaṃ /
# ji ste yang 'gag pa nyid dmigs pa yin na / / de lta na ni 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa yul du 'gyur pa dang rmi lam la sogs pa la yang rnam par shes pa dmigs pa med par grub po /
nā'nālambanaṃ svapnādivijñānaṃ nimittālambanatvād iti kecit /
# la lan re rmi lam la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa yang mtshan ma la dmigs pa'i phyir dmigs pa med pa ma yin no /
nimittaṃ punar arthapratibimbaṃ viprayuktasaṃskārasvabhāvaṃ /
# mtshan ma ni don gyi gzugs brnyan te ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed kyi rang bzhin no zhe'o /
na hi svapnādāvasatyarthe tannimittaṃ yujyate mukhādyabhāve tat / pratibimbavat /
# rmi lam la sogs pa don med pa la de'i mtshan ma mi rung ste / / bzhin la sogs pa med par de'i gzugs brnyan mi 'grub pa bzhin no /
utpadyamānam utpannaṃ vālambanaṃ vijñānanimittam abhāvān nirodhāc / ceti pūrvam uktaṃ /
# 'byung ba'i tshe'am byung zin pa'i rnam par shes pas kyang mtshan ma la dmigs pa ma yin te / / med pa dang dgag pa sngar bstan pa'i phyir ro /
vijñānameva arthapratibhāsatvād arthapratibimbaṃ / / ato na viprayuktasaṃskārātmakaṃ nimittaṃ yujyate /
# de'i phyir ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed kyi rang bzhin mtshan mar mi rung bas / / rnam par shes ba nyid don du snang ba don gyi gzugs brnyan te /
avaśyaṃ cārthākāraṃ vijñānam abhyupagantavyaṃ /
# rnam par shes pa nyid don gyi rnam par gdon mi za bar khas blang dgos so /
anākāre hi tasmin grāhyagrāhakaniyama eva na syāt /
# rnam pa med na ni de la gzung ba dang 'dzin pa nges pa nyid du mi 'gyur ro /
anyastvapratighaṃ rūpameva svapne yogināṃ cāśubhādāvālambanaṃ manyate / tasyāpi varṇasaṃsthānādyātmakatvād apratighatvaṃ
# gzhan ni thogs pa med pa'i gzugs nyid rmi lam dang rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi mi sdug pa la sogs par dmigs pa'o snyam du sems te / / de'i yang kha dog dang dbyibs la sogs pa'i bdag nyid yin pas /
manomātraviṣayatvañca virudhyate /
# thogs pa med pa nyid dang yid 'ba' zhig gi yul du 'gal lo /
na cāvijñaptimātrād anyad apratighaṃ rūpaṃ śāstre varṇyate /
# rnam par rig byed ma yin pa tsam ma gtogs par yang thogs pa med pa'i gzugs gzhan bstan bcos las mi bshad pas /
tasmāt kalpanāmātram eva /
