# de'i phyir de nyid kyang rtog pa tsam nyid do /
aparastv anubhūtārtham eva svapne vijñānaviṣayatvenecchati jātyandhena / svapne nīlādirūpāgrahaṇāt /
# gzhan dag ni dmus long gi rmi lam na sngon po la sogs pa'i gzugs mi 'dzin pa'i phyir / / don myong ba ni rmi lam gyi rnam par shes pa'i yul nyid du 'dod do /
na jātyandhaḥ svapne rūpaṃ na gṛhṇāti /
# dmus long gi rmi lam na gzugs mi 'dzin pa yin te /
avyutpannasaṅketatvāt tu nāmato na jānāty ato nānyasyācaṣṭe /
# brda mi shes pas ming rnam par mi shes pa'i phyir gzhan la bsnyad mi nus so /
yadi cānubhūtasyaiva svapne darśanam evaṃ jātyandhasyāpi rūpadarśanaṃ / kiṃ neṣyate ?
# gal te yang myong ba nyid rmi lam du mthong na de lta na dmus long gis kyang gzugs mthong bar ci'i phyir mi 'dod /
tenāpi pūrvajanmasu rūpam upalabdham eva /
# des kyang tshe rabs snga ma dag la gzugs dmigs pa nyid do /
na ca [p.22] / vartamānajanmany upalabdham eva svapne pratibhāsate /
# de ltar gyi tshe la dmigs pa nyid rmi lam du snang ba yang ma yin te /
na hy atītānāgatavartamānānubhave suptasya jāgrataś ca kaścid / viśeṣo'sti /
# 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi 'dzin par yang rmi lam dang gnyid kyis ma log par khyad par med do /
tasmāt parikalpamātram evaitad anubhūtārthaviṣayaṃ svapne vijñānam iti
# de lta bas na don myong ba de ni rmi lam gyi rnam par shes pa'i yul lo zhes bya ba ni kun rtog pa tsam nyid do /
/  atītasya cābhāvān nirviṣayaṃ vijñānam eva svapne'rthābhāsam / utpadyata iti niścayaḥ / / evaṃ vijñaptimātratvenopalambhād arthā'nupalabdhir bhāvyeti /
# 'das pa yang med par yul med par rnam par shes pa nyid rmi lam du don du snang ba 'byung bar nges so / / de ltar rnam par rig pa tsam du dmigs pas yul mi dmigs par bsgom mo /
ya / arthā'nupalabdhiṃ niścitya vijṇaptimātrasyāpyanupalabdhirjāyata iti/
# don mi dmigs pa la brten nas / / rnam par rig pa tsam yang mi dmigs pa skye ste zhes bya ba ni /
yatha na vijṇyanād bahiḥ parikalpitaṃ grāhyamastīti / vijñaptimātratābalena manogrāhyābhāvaṃ praviśati tathā / grāhyabhāvabalena vijñaptimātrasyāpy abhāvaṃ pratipadyate / / na grāhyābhāve grāhakatvaṃ yujyate / / grāhyam apekṣya tad grāhakasya vyavasthāpanāt / / evam asallakṣaṇaṃ grāhyagrāhakayoḥ parikalpitarūpayoḥ praviśati / nābhūtaparikalpasyeti darśanaṃ bhavati / / kim arthaṃ punaḥ prathamata eva vijñaptimātrasyaivābhāvaṃ na / vibhāvayati ? / grāhyapratibaddhatvāddhi grāhakasyopalabhyārthābhāve sukhaṃ praveśaḥ
# ji ltar rnam par shes pa las phyi rol na kun brtags pa'i gzung ba med pas rnam par rig pa tsam nyid kyi stobs kyis gzung ba med par 'jug pa de ltar gzung ba med pa'i stobs kyis rnam par rig pa tsam yang med par khong du chud do / / gzung ba nyid la ltos te de 'dzin par rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir / / gzung ba med na 'dzin par mi rung ngo / / de ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa kun brtags pa'i rang gi ngo bo dag gi med pa'i mtshan nyid la 'jug gi / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa yin no / / ci'i phyir thog ma nyid du rnam par rig pa tsam nyid med par rnam par mi gzhag ce na / / 'dzin pa ni gzung ba la rag las pa'i phyir dmigs par bya ba'i don med na /
syād ālambanasvabhāvavināśāt / / anyathā bhāvāpavādam eva kuryāt / / grāhyagrāhakayoḥ parasparanirapekṣatvāt /
# dmigs pa'i ngo bo'i dngos po 'jig pas bde blag tu 'jug par 'gyur gyi / / gzhan du na gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis phan tshun ltos pa med pa'i phyir /
imāñca grāhyagrāhakavikalpātītāṃ jñānabhūmiṃ saṃbhāreṣu / nirantaraṃ pravartamānaḥ prathamakalpāsaṃkhyeyaparisamāptau praviṣati /
# dngos po la skur pa 'debs pa nyid du 'gyur ro / / rgyun mi 'chad par tshogs rnams la zhugs te / / bskal pa grangs med pa dang po yongs su rdzogs na; gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par rtog pa las 'das pa'i ye shes kyis 'dir chud de /
tathā hi vijñaptimātram idaṃ niśritya rūpānupalambhānukūlo / lokottaramārge prathama uṣmagatākhyaḥ saparivāraḥ samādhirāmukhī / bhavati / / tasyānantaraṃ mūrdhākhyaḥ /
# 'di ltar rnam par rig pa tsam 'di la brten nas / / gzugs la sogs pa med par bsgom pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi thog ma'i rang bzhin dro bar gyur pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin 'khor dang bcas pa mngon du 'gyur ro / / de'i 'og tu rtse mo zhes bya ba'o /
tasyānantaram aśeṣagrāhyānupalambhād grāhakānupalabhānukūlaḥ / kṣāntyākhyaḥ samādhiḥ / / tasyānantaram arthānupalabdhiṃ niśritya vijñaptimātrasyāpy anupalabdhiṃ / bhāvayan laukikāgryadharmākhyaḥ prajñādisahitaḥ saparivāraḥ samādhir / āmukhībhavati / / tad anantaraṃ darśanamārgaḥ /
# de'i 'og tu gzung ba ma lus par mi dmigs pas 'dzin pa mi dmigs pa dang mthun pa bzod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to / / de'i 'og tu don mi dmigs pa la brten te / / rnam par shes pa tsam yang mi dmigs par bsgom zhing 'jig rten gyi chos kyi mchog ces bya ba shes rab la sogs pa dang bcas pa'i ting nge 'dzin 'khor dang bcas pa mngon du 'gyur ro /
tatraiva ca sarvatragadharmadhātvadhigamāt prathamāṃ bhūmiṃ praviśatīti / ayaṃ ca tattvamanaskāro nāvimuktimanaskāro'pramāṇādivat //1-7// / upalabdhir upalabdhitvenā'siddhā / / abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ityucyate'nupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi / satī / [p.23] / upalabdher anupalabdhisvabhāvatvam iti pradarśayann āha - / upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabdhisvabhāvatā / iti /
# de'i 'og tu mthong ba'i lam ste / / de nyid la yang chos kyi dbyings kun tu 'gro bar rtog pas sa dang po la 'jug ces bya'o / / 'di ni de kho na yid la byed pa yin gyi / / tshad med pa la sogs pa bzhin du mos pa yid la byed pa ni ma yin te / / dmigs pa mi dmigs pa'i rang bzhin gyi phyir ro zhes rab tu bstan pa'i phyir / / de yi phyir na dmigs pa ni / / mi dmigs ngo bo nyid du grub / / ces bya ba gsungs so / / yang na rnam pa 'dis so so rang gis rig pa'i phyir /
atha vā yat pūrvaṃ pratijñātam abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ nāstīti tad / anenākāreṇa pratyātmavedyatvāt siddham iti pradarśayann āha - / upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabhisvabhāvatā / iti / / tata iti - / upalabhyārthābhāve upālabdhyabhāvāt /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis med do zhes gang sngar dam bcas pa de grub po zhes rab tu bstan pa'i phyir / / de yi phyir na dmigs pa ni / / mi dmigs ngo bo nyid du grub / / ces bya ba gsungs so / / de'i phyir zhes bya ba ni / / dmigs par bya ba'i don gyi dngos po med pa'i phyir ro /
upalabdhir iti bhāvakartṛkaraṇānām anyatamat parikalpyate / / etat tritayam apy abhāvān na yujyate / / upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabdhisvabhāvatā / / ata eva vṛttikāra āha - / upalabhyārthābhāva upalabdhyayogād iti / / tasmāc ca samatā jñeyā nopalambhopalambhayoḥ /
# dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni dngos po dang byed pa po dang byed pa gang yang rung ba zhig tu brtag grang na / / las med pas de gsum char yang mi rung ste / / de'i phyir dmigs pa mi dmigs pa'i ngo bo nyid du grub po / / de nyid kyi phyir 'grel pa mdzad pas dmigs par bya ba'i don med na dmigs par mi rung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / de lta bas na dmigs pa dang mi dmigs pa mnyam par shes par bya /
yasmād upalabdhir anupalabdhisvabhāvā tasmāt samatā tulyatā jñeyā /
# 'di ltar dmigs pa ni mi dmigs pa'i ngo bo nyid du gyur te / / de'i phyir mnyam mo /
arthānupalambhasya vijñaptimātratopalambhasya cāsattvād aviśeṣataḥ / / upalabdhyanupalabdhiśabdayoḥ parasparaviruddhatvāpanaya nārthamāha - / abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ity ucyate / / na tu tayā kiñcid upalabhyte'rthābhāvād iti / / ataḥ paramārthato 'nupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi satīti nāsti virodhaḥ / / apara āha -
# don mi dmigs pa dang rnam par rig pa tsam du dmigs pa yang med par bye brag med pa'i phyir mtshungs pa nyid du shes par bya'o / / dmigs pa dang mi dmigs pa'i sgra dag phan tshun 'gal ba bsal ba'i phyir / / yang dag pa ma yin pa'i don du snang bas dmigs pa zhes bya'o zhes bya ba smos te / / don med pas 'dis ni ci yang mi dmigs so / / de'i phyir don dam par mi dmigs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyang yin pas 'gal ba med do /
yaś ca bālānām asatyārthe'rthopalambho yaścāryāṇām arthānupalambhas / tayor dvayos tulyalakṣaṇatvāt samatā jñeyā sarpabhrānty anupalabdhivat / ata eva bravīti - abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ity / ucyate'nupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi satīti sarpabhrānty anupalabdhivyapadeśavad  iti / / anyaḥ punar āha -
# gzhan dag na re byis pa rnams don med pa la don du dmigs pa gang yin pa dang 'phags pa rnams don mi dmigs pa gang yin pa de gnyis mtshan nyid mtshungs pas mnyam par shes par bya ste / / sbrul du 'khrul pa mi dmigs pa bzhin no / / de nyid kyi phyir sbrul du 'khrul pa mi dmigs par bshad pa bzhin du / / mi dmigs pa'i ngo bo nyid yin yang / / yang dag pa ma yin pa'i don du snang ba'i phyir dmigs pa zhes bshad do zhes zer ro /
yaś ca bālānāṃ grāhakopalambho yaścāryāṇām arthābhāvād / grāhakānupalambhas tayor dvayor upalambhānupalambhayor ubahyato'pi
# gzhan dag na re byis pa rnams kyis 'dzin par dmigs pa gang yin pa dang don med pa'i phyir 'phags pa rnams kyis 'dzin pa mi dmigs pa gang yin pa dang dmigs pa dang mi dmigs pa de gnyis ni gnyi ga yang gzung ba med na /
samatā jñeyā grāhye'sati grāhakābhāvāviśeṣāt / / ata evāha - abhūtārthapratibhāsatayeti vistaraḥ /
# 'dzin pa med par bye brag med pa'i phyir mnyam par shes par bya ste / / de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa'i don du snang bas zhes rgya cher smos so zhe'o /
kecitu manyante samāropā'pavādapratipakṣeṇāha - / tasmāc ca samtā jñeyā nopalambhopalambhayoḥ / iti / / arthābhāvād upalabdher upalabdhisvarūpatvenā'bhāvāt svarūpeṇa tad / abhāva ucyate /
# yang kha cig sems pa sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i gnyen por de lta bas na dmigs pa dang mi dmigs mnyam par shes par bya / / zhes gsungs so snyam ste / / don med pa'i phyir dmigs pa ni dmigs pa'i rang bzhin du med pas / / ngo bo nyid kyis de med pa zhes bya ste /
upalambha upalabdhisvabhāvo nāpanīyate nāpyanupalabdhisvabhāvaḥ / prakṣipyate / / kiṃ tarhi samam etad ubhayaṃ nirvikalpatayā /
# dmigs pa la dmigs pa'i rang bzhin bsal bar bya ba'am / / mi dmigs pa'i rang bzhin yang gzhag par bya ba med de / / de gnyis ka yang rnam par brtag tu med pas mnyam pa nyid do; /
tasmānnopalambhopalambhayoḥ samāropāpavādanirapekṣeṇa pratyātmasamatā / jñeyeti /
# de lta bas na sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa la mi ltos par dmigs pa dang mi dmigs pa gnyis so so rang gis mnyam pa nyid du shes par bya'o / / smras pa /
āha ca - / nāpaneyam ataḥ kiñcit prakṣeptavyaṃ na kiñcana /
# 'di las bsal bya gang yang med / / gzhag par bya ba'ang ci yang med /
draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtato bhūtaṃ bhūtadarśī vimucyate // [p.24] / yadyevaṃ kathaṃ vijñaptir upalabdhir ity ucyate /
# yang dag nyid la yang ngag lta / / yang dag mthong ba rnam par grol / / gal te de lta na ci'i phyir rnam par rig pa tsam la dmigs pa zhes bya zhe na / / mi dmigs pa'i rang bzhin yin yang /
abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā loke śāstre ca tathā pratītatvād / anupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi satīti //1-8//
# yang dag pa ma yin pa'i don du snang bas / / 'jig rten dang bstan bcos las kyang de bzhin du grags pa'i phyir ro /
prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati
# rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid ston te zhes bya ba la /
kāmarūpārūpyadhātvātmakamabhūtaparikalpasya prabhedo / nānāprakāratā / / prabheda eva lakṣaṇamiti prabhedalakṣaṇam, anena / prabhedenā'bhūtaparikalpasya lakṣaṇāt /
# 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams kyi bdag nyid ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i rab tu dbye ba ste / / rnam pa tha dad pa nyid do / / rab tu dbye ba nyid mtshan nyid yin pas / / rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid de / / rab tu dbye ba 'dis yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa mtshon pa'i phyir ro /
prabhedalakṣaṇañca kimarthaṃ khyāpyate?
# rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid kyang ci'i phyir bshad ce na /
abhūtaparikalpamātre kāmarūpadhātvorayogāt /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam la 'dod pa dang gzugs kyi khams mi rigs te /
yo'yaṃ dhātubhāvena vipakṣapratipakṣabhedādāryapudgalādibhedaḥ sa na / prāpnotīti mahān śāsanopaplavaḥ prasajyata ityāśaṅkyudāsārthaṃ / prabhedalakṣaṇamākhyātam / / atha vā yatra vitarkavicāraustastatraivā'bhūtaparikalpo'sti na
# khams tha dad pas mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po tha dad pa'i phyir 'phags pa'i gang zag la sogs par tha dad pa gang yin pa de thob par mi 'gyur te / / de bas na bstan pa la nyes pa chen por 'gyur ro snyam pa'i dogs ba bsal ba'i phyir rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid bshad do / / yang na / / gang rtog pa dang dpyod pa yod pa de nyid na /
tvanyatreti yo manyate tadapanayanārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇamucyate / / abhūtaparikalpastu cittacaittāstridhātukāḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod kyi gzhan ni ma yin no snyam ste / / de bas na de bsal ba'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog ni / / sems dang sems byung khams gsum pa / / zhes rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid brjod de gang na rtog pa dang dpyod pa yod pa nyi tshe la ni ma yin no /
na tu yatraiva vitarkavicārāviti / / yathā rūpaṃ bhūtāni bhautikañca, evamabhūtaparikalpo'pi cittaṃ / caittāś ca, na kevalaṃ cittameva /
# dper na gzugs ni 'byung ba rnams dang 'byung ba las gyur pa yin pa bzhin du / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yang sems dang sems las byung ba yin gyi / / sems 'ba' zhig ni ma yin no /
te ca tridhātukasvabhāvāḥ /
# de dag kyang khams gsum pa'i ngo bo nyid de /
kāmarūpākhyāvacarabhedena tridhātukaḥ /
# 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa tha dad pas khams gsum pa rnams so /
tatra ye tasmād abhūtaparikalpānnarakādyākārā viṃśatiprakārāḥ / pravartante sa kāmadhātuḥ /
# de la yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa de las sems can dmyal ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa nyi shu gang dag 'byung ba de ni 'dod pa'i khams so /
ye saptadaśaprakārā brāhkamāyikādyākārāste rūpadhātuḥ /
# tshangs rigs la sogs pa'i rnam pa bcu bdun gang yin pa de dag ni gzugs kyi khams so /
ya ākāśānantyāyatanādyākārāścatuḥprakārāste ārūpyadhātuḥ / / anyaḥ punarāha - aprahīṇakāmarāgā avibhūtārūpyasaṃjñāś ca / kāmāvacaraḥ kāmadhātuḥ / / prahīṇakāmarāgā avibhūtārūpyasaṃjñāś ca rūpāvacaro rūpadhātuḥ / / prahīṇakāmarūparāgā vibhūtā rūpyasaṃjñāścārūpyāvacara / ārūpyadhātuḥ / / kāmarāgānuśayitāḥ kāmadhātuḥ /
# nam mkha' mtha' yas la sogs pa'i rnam pa bzhi po gang yin pa de dag ni gzugs med pa'i khams so / / gzhan na re 'dod pa la 'dod chags ma spangs pa dang gzugs kyi 'du shes dang ma bral ba rnams ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'o / / 'dod pa la 'dod chags spangs la gzugs kyi 'du shes dang ma bral ba rnams ni gzugs kyi khams so / / 'dod pa dang gzugs la 'dod chags spangs shing gzugs kyi 'du shes dang yang bral ba rnams ni gzugs med pa na spyod pa'o zhes zer ro / / gzhan dag ni 'dod pa la 'dod chags rgyas par gyur pa rnams ni 'dod pa'i khams so /
rūparāgānuśayitā rūpadhātuḥ /
# gzugs la 'dod chags rgyas par gyur pa rnams ni gzugs kyi khams so /
ārūpyarāgānuśayitā ārūpyadhāturityanye / [p.25]
# gzugs med pa la 'dod chags rgyas par gyur pa rnams ni / / gzugs med pa'i khams so zhes smra'o /
satatacikṣepakakścaitasikaduḥkhaprakārāḥ kāmadhātuḥ /
# kha cig ni rtag tu gyeng ba dang sems las byung ba'i sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa'i gnas su gyur pa rnams ni 'dod pa'i khams so /
samāhitā vigatacaitasikaduḥkhaprakārā rūpadhātuḥ / / samāhitāḥ prahīṇamukhaduḥkhaprakārā ārūpadhāturityapare /
# mnyam par gzhag pa la sems las byung ba'i sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa dang bral ba rnams ni gzugs kyi khams so / / mnyam par gzhag la bde ba dang sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa spangs pa rnams ni / / gzugs med pa'i khams so zhes smra'o /
aprahīṇagandharasatadvijñānābnhāsāḥ kāmadhātuḥ /
# kha cig ni dri dang ro dang de dag tu snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ma spangs pa rnams ni 'dod pa'i khams so /
prahīṇagandharasatadvijñānābhāsā rūpadhātuḥ /
# dri dang ro dang de dag tu snang ba'i rnam par shes pa spangs pa rnams ni gzugs kyi khams so /
prahīṇapañcadaśadhātvābhāsā ārūpyadhāturityapare /
# khams bco lngar snang ba spangs pa rnams ni gzugs med pa'i khams so zhes smra'o /
teṣu sarveṣu vyākhyāneṣu katame ta ityavaśyaṃ pūrvavyākhyānoktā eva / vaktavyā iti sākāṅkṣāṇyevaitāni vyākhyānāni / / abhūtaparikalpādhikāre
# bshad pa de dag thams cad la de dag gang yin zhe na / / thog mar bshad pa las brjod pa nyid bshad par bya ba ste / / de ltar na bshad pa 'di dag ni ltos pa dang bcas pa nyid do / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i skabs yin bzhin du yang /
punarabhūtaparikalpagrahaṇamanupalabdhyantaritatvād iti / / paryāyalakṣaṇañceti /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa smos pa ni mi dmigs pas bar du bcad pa'i phyir ro / / rnam grangs kyi mtshan nyid kyang ston te zhes bya ba ni /
cittacaittānāṃ prabhedaṃ khyāpayitvā'bhūtaparikalpasya paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ / khyāpayati / / kathaṃ kṛtvā ?
# sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi bye brag rab tu bstan pas / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i rnam grangs kyi mtshan nyid kyang ston to / / ji lta zhe na /
abhūparikalpyavastunaḥ svabhāvaviśeṣaparikalpanayā cittacaittānāṃ / pravṛttatvāt /
# sems dang sems las byung ba rnams yang dag pa ma yi pa kun rtog pa'i dngos po'i rang bzhin dang khyad par la rtog par zhugs pa'i phyir ro /
arthasvarūpaviśeṣadṛṣṭiścittacaittā abhūtaparikalpaśceti / paryāyāntarbhūtāḥ /
# don gyi rang gi ngo bo dang bye brag mthong ba sems dang sems las byung ba rnams dang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa zhes bya ba ni rnam grangs su gtogs pa ste; don la ni khyad par med do /
tatrārthamātre dṛṣṭir vijñānam iti / / mātraśabdo viśeṣanirāsārthaḥ /
# de la don tsam mthong ba ni rnam par shes pa'o zhes bya ba la tsam zhes bya ba'i sgra ni /
tenāgṛhītaviśeṣā vastusvarūpamātropalabdhir ityarthaḥ /
# khyad par sel ba'i phyir te khyad par mi 'dzin gyi dngos po'i rang gi ngo bo tsam dmigs so zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
arthaviśeṣe dṛṣṭiścaitasā vedanādaya iti / / tena tena viśeṣarūpeṇa tatrātipravṛtteḥ /
# don gyi khyad par mthong ba ni sems las byung ba rnams te tshor ba la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni khyad par gyi ngo bo de dang des der mngon par 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
tatrāhlādakaparitāpakatvaviśeṣo yas tasya bhāvasya yat / saumanasyādisthānaṃ tad grahaṇaṃ vedanā /
# de la gang dngos po de'i khyad par sim pa dang gdung ba nyid yid bde ba la sogs pa'i gnas pa gang yin pa de 'dzin pa ni tshor ba'o /
strīpuruṣādivyavahāralakṣaṇo yo'rthaviśeṣas tad grahaṇaṃ saṃjñā /
# bud med dang skyes pa la sogs par tha snyad gdags pa'i mtshan ma don gyi khyad par gang yin pa de 'dzin pa ni 'du shes so /
evam anye'pi yathāyogaṃ yojyāḥ /
# de bzhin du gzhan yang ci rigs su sbyar bar bya'o /
evaṃ caiṣāmāśrayālambanakāladravyasamatābhiḥ samprayuktatvaṃ na
# de ltar de dag kyang gnas pa dang dmigs pa dang dus dang rdzas mtshungs pa nyid kyis mtshungs par ldan pa yin gyi /
tvākārasamatayāpi vijñānāviśeṣaprasaṅgāt / / cittaviśeṣā eva caitasā ihābhipretā iti kecijjānanti /
# rnam par shes pa dang khyad par med par thal bar 'gyur bas rnam par mtshungs pas ni ma yin no / / kha cig ni 'dir sems kyi bye brag nyid sems las byung bar dgongs par shes te /
tedeva vijñānaṃ tādṛśasvarūpādinā vicitrapratibhāsam utpadyate / mayūracandrikavat / / katham ekaṃ vicitrañca ?
# rma bya'i mdongs ltar rnam par shes pa de nyid / / de lta bu'i ngo bo la sogs par snang ba sna tshogs su 'byung ngo zhe'o / / ji ltar na gcig pu yang yin la sna tshogs kyang yin / / gcig pu du ma'i ngo bo nyid du 'gyur du 'ong zhes /
naikaṃ hi lakṣaṇaṃ loke vicitram iṣyate / / mā bhūd ekam anekasvabhāvam iti syād eṣa [p.26] / doṣo yadi dharmasvabhāvaḥ syāt / / bhrāntimātre tu naiṣa doṣaḥ / / kva tathā sarvathā bhāvāt / iti vacanāt /
# 'jig rten ni gcig la mi mthun pa'i mtshan nyid sna tshogs su mi 'dod do zhe na / / gal te chos kyi ngo bo nyid yongs su grub par gyur na ni / / 'di yang nyes par 'gyur ro / / nor pa tsam la ni nyes pa 'di med de / / de bzhin ma yin ye med min / / zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro /
naitad evaṃ sūtravacanavirodhāt / / yā vedanā yā saṃjñā yac cittaṃ yad vijñānañca saṃsṛṣṭvā amī / dharmā na visaṃsṛṣṭā iti / / saṃsargaś ca nāma satāṃ yugapac ca bhavatīti /
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / mdo las tshor ba gang yin pa dang 'du shes gang yin pa dang sems gang yin pa dang rnam par shes pa gang yin pa ste chos 'di rnams ni 'dres pa ste / / ma yin no zhes 'byung ba dang 'gal ba'i phyir ro / / 'dres pa zhes bya ba ni yod pa rnams cig car phrad par 'gyur ba la bya'o /
yo hi dharmasvabhāvam apariniṣpannam icchati tasyaitat sūtram / asminnarthe'jñāpakam iti //1-9//
# gang chos kyi ngo bo nyid yongs su ma grub par 'dod pa de la / / mdo de ni don 'dir khungs su mi rung ngo /
abhūtaparikalpamātre'nyasya cābhāve hetuphalaprabhedaṃ na vijñāyata / iti tat pratipādanārthaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇañca khyāpayati / / anena hetuphalabhāvenā'bhūtaparikalpa iti lakṣaṇaṃ / / pravṛttir eva lakṣaṇaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ / / pravṛttiḥ punar divdhā - kṣaṇaparamparāpravṛttir yadādipatyena
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam du zad la gzhan yang med pas rgyu dang 'bras bu rab tu dbye ba rnam par mi shes pas de rab tu bstan pa'i phyir 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid kyang ston te / / 'dis yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos por mtshon pa'o / / 'jug pa nyid mtshan nyid yin pas 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid de / / 'jug pa yang rnam pa gnyis so / / skad cig brgyud mar 'jug pa ste /
pratyutpanna upabhogasaṅkleśaḥ janmāntarapravṛttiś ca
# de'i dbang gis da ltar byung ba'i nye bar spyod pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa dang tshe rabs gzhan du 'jug ste /
yadādhipatyenāyatyāṃ kleśakarmajanmasaṅkleśaḥ /
# de'i dbang gis tshe phyi ma'i nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa'o /
iha kṣaṇaparamparāpravṛttiḥ pravṛttilakṣaṇam uktaṃ /
# 'dir ni skad cig brgyud mar 'jug pa 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid du bshad pa'o /
janmāntarapravṛttiṃ saṅkleśalakṣaṇatvena khyāpayiṣyati /
# tshe rabs gzhan du 'jug pa ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid du 'og nas 'chad do /
ekaṃ pratyayavijñānaṃ
# gcig ni rkyen gyi rnam par shes /
iti vistaraḥ / / tatraikam ityālayavijñānaṃ śeṣāṇāṃ saptānāṃ vijñānānāṃ
# zhes rgya cher 'byung ba de la / / gcig ces bya ba de ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ste /
hetupratyayabhāvena hetur iti pratyayavijñānaṃ / / dvitīyam aupabhogikaṃ / iti /
# rnam par shes pa lhag ma bdun rnams kyi rgyu'i rkyen gyi dngos po'i rgyu yin pas rkyen gyi rnam par shes pa'o / / gnyis pa nye bar spyod pa can zhes bya ba ni /
vijñānam ity anuvartate /
# rnam par shes pa zhes bya bar snyegs te /
tat phalam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
# de'i 'bras bu zhes bya ba tshig gi lhag ma'o /
tat punaḥ saptavidhaṃ pravṛttivijñānam upabhogaprayojakatvād aupabhogikaṃ
# de yang rnam pa bdun no / / nye bar spyod pa ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa'i dgos pa yin pas nye bar spyod pa can no /
upabhogaparicchedaprerakās tatra caitasāḥ // iti / / tatra vijñāne ye caitasās te'pi tat phalam iti sambandhaḥ /
# rnam par shes pa de la sems las byung ba nye bar spyod pa dang yongs su gcod pa dang 'jug par byed pa gang yin pa dag kyang de'i 'bras bu zhes bya bar sbyar te /
vijñānatvād ekayogakṣematvāc ca /
# rnam par shes pa dang grub pa dang bde ba gcig pa'i phyir ro /
ālayavijñānam anyeṣāṃ vijñānānāṃ pratyayatvāt pratyayavijñānam  iti /
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni rnam par shes pa gzhan dag ni rgyu'i rkyen yin pas rkyen gyi rnam par shes pa'o zhes bya ba la /
ālīyante sarve sāsravā dharmās tatra phalabhāvena tac ca teṣu
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad der 'bras bu'i dngos por sbyor ba dang de yang de dag la rgyu'i dngos por sbyor bas kun gzhi'o /
hetubhāvenetyālayaḥ / [p.27] / sattvabhājanaloka-vijñā-anāt tannirbhāsatayā vijñānaṃ / / tac caikāntavipākatvād avyākṛtaṃ /
# sems can dang snod kyi 'jig rten de ltar snang bas rnam par rig par byed pa'i phyir rnam par shes pa'o / / de yang cig tu rnam par smin pas lung du ma bstan pa nyid do /
sarveṣāṃ sāsravāṇāṃ dharmāṇāṃ bījam anubadhnāti anyeṣāñca / pravṛttivijñānānāṃ hetupratyayo bhavatīti pratyayavijñānaṃ /
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad kyi sa bon rjes su 'brel ba dang 'jug pa ni rnam par shes pa gzhan dag gi rgyu'i rkyen yin pas rkyen gyi rnam par shes pa'o /
tat pratyayaṃ pravṛttijñānamoupabhogikam iti /
# de las byung ba 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni nye bar spyod pa can no zhes bya ba ni /
tasmād ālayavijñānāt pratyetīti tat pratyayam utpadyata ityarthaḥ / / katham utpadyate ?
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa de las byung ba ste / / de'i rkyen gyis skye zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / ji ltar 'byung zhe na /
pravṛttivijñānaṃ hy ālayavijñānāt pravartamānam anutpannasya taj / jātīyasya pravṛttivijñānasyotpādakaṃ bījam ālayavijñāne
# 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ba na de dang rigs gcig pa 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ma byung ba 'byung bar byed pa'i sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la brtas par byed de /
paripuṣṇāti / / tasmāt paripuṣṭabījāt pariṇāmaviśeṣaprāptāt punas taj jātīyaṃ / pravṛttivijñānam utpadyata ityevaṃ tat pratyayaṃ pravṛttivijñānaṃ / bhavati / / nanv ālayavijñānam apy aupabhogikaṃ pravṛttivijñānañca
# sa bon brtas nas 'gyur ba'i bye brag rnyed pa de las yang de dang rigs gcig la 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ste / / de ltar na de'i rkyen gyis 'jug pa'i rnam par shes par 'gyur ro / / bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal ba yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba'i nye bar spyod pa'i gnas su gyur pa dang kun kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la bag chags bsgo ba'i phyir / / kun gzhi'i rnam par shes pa yang nye bar spyod pa can du 'gyur la /
pratyayavijñānaṃ prasajyate aduḥkhāsukhavedanopabhogāśrayatvāt / ālayavijñāne ca vāsanābhāvanāt / / na pratyayabhāvavyatirekeṇānyā vāsanābhāvanā'sti / / yathoktam abhidharmasūtragāthāyāṃ - / sarvadharmā hi ālīnā vijñāne teṣu tat tathā / / anyonyaṃ phalabhāvena hetubhāvena sarvadā // iti / / na prasajyate tad vedanāyā durupalakṣYatvāt /
# 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa yang rkyen gyi rnam par shes par 'gyur bar thal bar mi 'gyur ram / / rkyen gyi dngos po ma gtogs par bag chags bsgo ba gzhan med de / / chos mngon pa'i mdo las tshigs su bcad pa las ji skad du / / phan tshun 'bras bu'i dngos po dang / / rgyu yi dngos por rtog tu yang / / rnam par shes la chos kun sbyor / / de yang de bzhin de dag la'o / / zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o zhe na / / thal bar mi 'gyur te ci'i phyir zhe na / / de'i tshor ba shes par dka' bas 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa bzhin du nye bar spyod pa can du mi shes sos /
na tadaupabhogikatvena lakṣyate pravṛttivijñānavat / / prakarṣagataṃ vā jñeyaṃ sūryavat / / tathā hy upabhogatrividhavedanāśrayatvaṃ pravṛttivijñānasyaiva na / tvālayavijñānasyeti / / hetupratyayaścātra vivakṣito na pratyayamātraṃ / / tathā hi kuśalākuśaladharmādhipatyād ālayavijñānaṃ / vipākaniṣyandaphalavāsanāṃ parigṛhṇāti / / avyākṛtadharmādhipatyāc ca niṣyandaphalavāsanām eveti / / ata ālayavijñānaṃ niravaśeṣāṇāṃ sāsravadharmāṇāṃ hetupratyayaḥ / / pravṛttivijñānaṃ tu ālayavijñānasyādhipatipratyaya iti nāsti / pravṛttivijñānasya pratyayatvaprasaṅgaḥ / / upabhogo vedaneti / / triprakārāpy upabhukṣyata ity upabhogaḥ anubhūyata ity arthaḥ / / bhavarasasārasarūpā vedanā / / tasmā bālās tat saṃvedanārthaṃ viṣayam abhiniviśante / / na kevalaṃ vedanā arthopalabdhir apy upabhoga ityanye / / tac ca na upabhogo vedaneti bhāṣyavirodhāt / / arthopalabdhiś ca na vijñānād anyeti na tasyāścaitasatvaṃ prayujyate / / veditaparicchedaḥ saṃjñā sukhādiviśeṣodgrahaṇātmakatvāt / / upabhoge saṃjñāyāñ ca prerakāḥ saṃskārā vijñānasya / cetanāmanaskārādayaḥ / [p.28]
# yang na nyi ma ltar khyad zhugs par shes par bya ste / / 'di ltar nyes par spyod pa tshor ba rna pa gsum po'i gnas ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa nyid yin gyi / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni ma yin no; / / 'dir ni rgyu'i rkyen du 'dod kyi rkyen tsam du ni ma yin te / / 'di ltar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'i chos kyi dbang gis rnam par smin pa dang rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu'i bag chags dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos kyi dbang gis rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu'i bag chags yongs su 'dzin to / / de'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos ma lus pa rnams kyi rgyu'i rkyen to / / 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i bdag po'i rkyen te / / rgyu'i rkyen ma yin pas 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa'i rkyen du thal bar 'gyur ba med do / / nye bar spyod pa ni tshor ba'o zhes bya ba la / / rnam pa gsum char yang nye bar spyod pas nye bar spyod pa ste / / myong bar byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / srid pa'i ro bro ba'i snying po 'dra ba ni tshor ba ste / / de'i phyir byis pa rnams de kun tu myong bar bya ba'i phyir yul rnams la chags so / / kha cig na re tshor ba 'ba' zhig tu ma zad kyi don la dmigs pa yang nye bar spyod pa zhes bya'o zhes zer te /
atha vā / / upabhogo vedaneti yathāsvamālambanānubhāvāt / sukhādivedanīyakarmānubhavanāc ca / / evaṃ viṣayakarmaṇor upabhuktir vedanety upabhogaḥ / / viṣayacihnaṃ vyavahāranimittaṃ paricchinnaṃ karotīti paricchedaḥ saṃjñā / vijñānāntarālambana ābhogaḥ saṃskārāḥ / / tataścetanādyādhipatyād vijñānam ālambanānantaraṃ bhajate / / ādiśabdena chandhādayo gṛhyante / / uktaṃ yato yādṛśo yad arthā ca pravṛttir iti //1-10// / tatra chādanād avidyayā yathābhūtadarśanāvabandhanāt / / ropaṇāt saṃskārair vijñāne karmavāsanāyāḥ pratiṣṭhāpanāt / / nayanād vijñānenopapattisthānasaṃprāpaṇāt / / samparigrahaṇān nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvasya / / pūraṇāt ṣaḍāyatanena / / triparicchedāt sparśena / / upabhogād vedanayā / / karṣaṇāt tṛṣṇayā karmākṣiptasya punar bhavasya / / nibandhanād upādānair vijñānasyotpatyanukūleṣu kāmādiṣu / / ābhimukhyād bhavena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ puarnbhave / vipākadānāyābhimukhīkaraṇāt /
# bshad pa las nye bar spyod pa ni tshor ba zhes 'byung ba dang 'gal bas de ni ma yin no / / don la dmigs pa ni rnam par shes pa las gzhan ma yin pas de sems las byung bar mi rung ngo / / bde ba la sogs pa'i bye brag 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyi phyir tshor ba yongs su spyod pa ni 'du shes nye bar spyod pa dang 'du shes la rnam par shes pa 'jug par byed pa dag ni 'du byed rnams te / / sems pa dang yid la byed pa la sogs pa'o / / yang na nye bar spyod pa ni tshor ba'o zhes bya ba ni / / rang gi dmigs pa ji lta ba bzhin du myong ba'am / / bde ba la sogs pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i las myong ba'i phyir ro / / de ltar yul dang las la spyod pa ni tshor ba ste / / de'i phyir nye bar spyod pa zhes bya'o / / yul gyi don rtags tha snyad kyi mtshan ma yongs su gcod par byed pas yongs gcod ni 'du shes so / / rnam par shes pa dmigs pa gzhan la 'jug par byed pa dag ni 'du byed rnams te / / de ltar na sems pa la sogs pa'i dbang gis rnam par shes pa dmigs pa gzhan la brten to / / sogs pa'i sgras ni 'dun pa la sogs pa bsdu'o / / gang nas ci 'dra gang gi phyir 'jug pa ni bshad zin to /
duḥKhanā jantyā jarāmaraṇena ca parikliśyate jagat / / saṅkleśalakṣaṇañca khyāpayatīti kleśakarmajanmasaṅkleśā yathā
# kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid kyang ston to zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa rnams ji ltar 'byung ba na /
pravartamānā jagataḥ parikleśāya bhavanti tat saṅkleśalakṣaṇaṃ /
# 'gro ba yongs su nyon mongs par 'gyur ba de ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid do /
tathācā'satyapyātmaninabhūtaparikalpamātrāt saṃsāraḥ prajāyate iti / pradarśanāthaṃ khyāpyate / / chādanādropaṇāc caiva nayanāt samparigrahāt / / iti vistaraḥ / / so'yaṃ pravṛttipakṣamadhi dvādaśāṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādo darśitaḥ / / tatra chādanāt /
# de ni bdag med par yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam las 'khor ba rgyas par 'gyur ba / / rab tu bstan pa'i phyir bshad de / / sgrib pa'i phyir dang 'debs pa'i phyir / / khrid pa'i phyir dang kun 'dzin phyir / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yan lag bcu gnyis pa 'di yang 'jug pa'i phyogs kyi dbang du mdzad do / / de la sgrib pa'i phyir te /
kliśyate jagad ityantavacanaṃ sarveṇa sambadhyate /
# 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do zhes tha mar smos pa ni thams cad dang sbyar ro /
kena chādanāt kathaṃ vā chādanāt kliśyata iti ?
# gang gis sgrib pa ji ltar sgrib pa'i phyir nyon mongs par byed ce na /
ata āha - / avidyayā yathābhūtadarśanavibandhād iti /
# de'i phyir ma rig pas yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mthong ba la bgegs byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
avidyayā hy adarśanātmakatvād bhūtadarśanaviṣaye pracchādite
# ma rig pa ni mi mthong ba'i bdag nyid yin pas yang dag pa mthong ba'i yul la rab tu sgrib pa'i phyir /
bhūtadarśanaṃ notpadyate'to bhūtadarśanotpattivibandhanād avidyā / bhūtadarśanavibandhaḥ / / bhūtadarśanaṃ punaḥ prādhānyena lokottaraprajñā tat pṛṣṭhodbhavatvāt
# yang dag pa mthong ba mi skye ste / / de'i phyir yang dag pa mthong ba skye ba la bgegs byed pas ma rig pa ni yang dag pa mthong ba la bgegs byed pa'o / / yang dag pa mthong ba yang dngos su ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab po /
tat pṛṣṭhalābhāt tad avagamāc ca tat prayoga iti / śrutacintābhāvanāmayī bhūtadarśanam ity ucyate /
# de'i rjes las byung ba'i phyir de'i rjes las thob pa dang de'i rtogs pa'i phyir de sbyong bar byed pa thos pa dang sems pa dang bsgom pa las byung ba yang yang dag pa mthong ba zhes bya'o /
bhūtadarśanavibandhād avidyā saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya ityevaṃ chādanād
# yang dag pa mthong ba'i bgegs su gyur pas / / ma rig pa ni 'du byed rnams kyi rkyen zhes bya ste /
avidyayā kliśyate jagad iti / [p.29]
# de ltar sgrib pa'i phyir ma rig pas 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do /
ropaṇāt kliśyate jagad iti sambadhyate /
# 'debs pa'i phyir zhes bya ba yang 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed ces bya ba dang sbyar ro /
kena ropaṇāt kva kasya vetyata āha saṃskārair vijñāne karmavāsanāyā  iti /
# gang gis gang du ci 'dabs she na; de'i phyir 'du byed rnams kyis rnam par shes pa la las kyi bag chags zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra saṃskārā yat kāyikaṃ karma vācikaṃ mānasaṃ ca / puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyasvarūpaṃ tat punar bhavam abhisaṃskarotīti saṃskāraḥ / / apraṇihitaṃ rohayatītyarthaḥ /
# de la 'du byed rnams ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i ngo bo nyid gang yin pa'o / / de ni yang srid pa mngon par 'du byed pas 'du byed de / / ma btab pa 'debs zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tadeva ca saṃskāraśabdenocyate na tu sarvaṃ / / taccābidyādhipatyāt punar bhavam ākṣeptuṃ samarthaṃ bhavati na
# de nyid du 'du byed kyi sgrar bshad kyi thams cad ni ma yin no / / de yang ma rig pa'i dbang gis yang srid pa 'debs nus par 'gyur gyi /
sattāmātreṇetyavidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ity ucyate / / tathāhi tāny anutpannavidyasya punarbhavaṃ saṃskurvanti notpannavidyasya /
# yod pa tsam gyis ni ma yin pas / / ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ste / / 'di ltar ma rig pa ma skyes na de dag yang srid pa 'du byed kyi /
na cādhipatyamātreṇaivāvidyā saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya ucyate sāmānyena / sā samutthānapratyayopi / / avidhyā hi samprayuktvādhyathā sarvakleṣānāṃ sāmānyena / samutyānapratyayastayā tatsamuttyā nāṃ cetanānām api /
# rig pa skyes na ni ma yin no / / bdag po tsam gyis ni ma rig pa 'du byed kyi rkyen zhes mi bya'i / / spyi'i rkyen yin pas kun nas 'byung ba na yang yin te / / 'di ltar ma rig pa ni nyon mongs pa thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir / / ji ltar nyon mongs pa kun nas 'byung ba rnams kyi spyi'i rkyen yin pa de bzhin du de las byung ba'i sems pa rnams kyi yang yin no /
api saṃskārāṇāṃ bhavabhogabhedaprārthanānvayānāṃ samutthāne tat
# bsod nams kyi 'du byed srid pa dang longs spyod bye brag can la smon pa'i rjes su 'gro ba rnams kyi yang yin te /
sahabhūtā'vidyā sāmānyapratyayaḥ /
# kun nas 'byung ba ni de dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i ma rig pa ni spyi'i rkyen yin no /
āniñjyānām api tad bhūminiḥsaranadṛṣṭisamutthānānāṃ tat / sahabhūtā'vidyā sāmānyapratyaya iti saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya uktaḥ /
# mi gyo ba de la nges par 'byung bar lta ba kun 'byung ba rnams kyi yang yin te / / de dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i ma rig pa ni spyi'i rkyen yin pas / / 'du byed kyi rkyen zhes bshad do /
vijñāna iti atrālayavijñānam abhipretaṃ na tu pravṛttivijñānaṃ /
# rnam par shes pa la zhes bya ba ni / / 'dir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la dgongs pa yin gyi / / 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni ma yin te /
vyuparatapravṛttivijñānasyotpattisthānanayanā'sambhavāt kuśalakliṣṭayoś / ca samavadhānābhāvāt saṃskārais tatra karmavāsanāyāḥ / pratiṣṭhāpanābhāvāt /
# rgyun chad pa dang 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pas skye ba'i gnas su khrid mi srid pa dang dge ba dang nyon mongs pa can gnyis 'grogs mi srid pas / / 'du byed rnams kyis de la las kyi bag chags gzhom mi srid pa'i phyir ro /
karmavāsanāyā iti / / kā punar iyaṃ karmavāsanā nāma ?
# las kyi bag chags zhes bya ba la las kyi bag chags zhes bya ba 'di gang yin zhe na /
anāgatasya janmano bījaṃ hetubhāvaḥ /
# ma 'ongs pa'i sa bon te rgyu'i dngos po'o /
tad yathā brīhiphalaṃ bhūmibhasmapurīṣādipratyayaviśeṣam apekṣya
# dper na 'bru'i 'bras bu sa dang thal ba dang lung la sogs pa rkyen gyi bye brag la ltos te /
pariṇamad aṅkurotpattau hetubhūtaṃ bījam iti /
# 'gyur ba las myu gu 'byung ba'i rgyu'i dngos po ni sa bon zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
pratiṣṭhāpanād iti ropaṇam eva paryāyāntareṇācaṣṭe /
# 'jog pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'debs pa nyid kyi rnam grangs gzhan bshad pa'o /
pratiṣṭhāpanaṃ punaratra vijñānasantāne tat prathamatas tad bījasyāpy
# 'jog pa yang rnam par shes pa'i rgyud 'di la des thog ma kho na'i sa bon de rgyas par byed pa yin te /
āyanaṃ / / nahi kasyacit sāsravasya dharmasyānāsravasyevāpūrvaṃ bījam ādhīyate
# zag pa med pa'i ltar zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos ni 'ga' tsam gyis kyang sa bon sngon ma bskyed pa med de /
evaṃ saṃskārair vijñāne punarbhāvabījādhānāj jagat kliśyate / / nayanāj jagat kliśyata iti / / kena nayanāt kva kasya veti na vijñāyata ityāha vijñānenotpatti
# 'di ltar 'du byed rnams kyis rnam par shes pa la yang srid pa'i sa bon skyed pa'i phyir 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do / / khrid pa'i phyir 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do zhes bya ba gang gis gang du gang khrid pa mi shes nas /
sthānasaṃpreṣaṇād iti / / karmaparibhāvitena vijñānena santānavṛttyā cyutisthānād
# de'i phyir rnam par shes pas skye ba'i gnas su phyin par byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / las kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i rnam par shes pa rgyun chags su 'jug pas 'chi'o /
upapattisthāne punar bhavabījabhūtāyā vāsanāyāḥ prāpaṇaṃ nayanaṃ /
# gnas nas skye ba'i gnas su yang srid pa'i sa bon du gyur ba'i bag chags phyin par byed / / khrid par byed do /
tathā ca sati na pratisandhivijñānaṃ saṃskārapratyayaṃ
# de ltar byas na nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes pa'i rkyen ni 'du byed ma yin gyi /
pūrvakālabhavavijñānam eva [p.30] / saṃskārapratyayam iti pradarśitaṃ bhavati /
# sngon gyi dus kyi srid pa'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyi rkyen 'du byed yin par rab tu bstan pa yin te /
nahi vinaṣṭāt kāraṇāt kāryotpattir yujyate /
# rgyu zhig pa las 'bras bu 'byung bar mi rung ngo /
ārūpyasamāpatīlābhino hi yatraiva cyavante tatraivotpadyanta iti katham / ārūpyeṣūpapattisthānaprāpaṇam iti tad yathāyogaṃ veditavyaṃ / nāmarūpavat / / samparigrahāj jagat kliśyata iti / / kena samparigrahāt kasya vetyata āha - / nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvasyeti / / nāmarūpaṃ hi pañcaskandhāḥ /
# gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnyed pa rnams ni gang shi ba de nyid du skye bas gzugs med pa rnams su ji ltar skye ba'i gnas su phyin par byed ce na / / de ni ci rigs par shes par bya ste / / ming dang gzugs bzhin no / / kun 'dzin phyir 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do zhes bya ba gang gis gang du gang yongs su 'dzin zhe na / / de'i phyir ming dang gzugs kyi lus so zhes bya ba smos te / / ming dang gzugs ni phung po lnga'o /
te ca pratisaṇdhim upādāya kalalārbudapeśīghanapraśākhāvasthā / anutpannaṣaḍāyatanā vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam iti /
# de dag kyang nying mtshams sbyor ba nas bzung ste / / nur nur po dang mer mer po dang nar nar po dang gor gor po dang rkang lag 'gyus pa'i dus dang skye mched drug ma dod kyi bar du rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs zhes bya ste /
tad bhāvitaviśeṣeṇa hy anatareṣu nikāyasabhāgeṣu tad viśiṣṭatvaṃ sidhyati
# 'di ltar de la bsgos pa'i bye brag gis rigs mthun pa gzhan dag tu de bye brag can du grub po /
tasmiṃścotpanne manuṣya-tiryagādinikāyasabhāgabedād ātmabhāvo bhidyata / iti nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvaḥ parigṛhīta ity ucyate / / atha vā''maraṇāt sarvam evātmabhāvaṃ parigṛhṇāti tat prathamataḥ / sarvasya hetubhāvena vyavasthānād iti / / atha vā'bhinne'pi nāmarūpeṇāti tat prathamataḥ sarvasya hetubhāvena / vyavasthānād iti / / atha vā'bhinne'pi nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvo yathā parigṛhyeta tat pṛthaktvena
# de skyes nas kyang mi dang dud 'gro la sogs pa'i rigs mthun pa tha dad pa'i phyir lus kyang tha dad pas ming dang gzugs kyis lus yongs su 'dzin zhes bya'o / / yang na 'chi ba la thug gi bar du lus thams cad yongs su 'dzin pa ste / / de thog ma kho nar thams cad kyi rgyu'i dngos por rnam par gnas pa'i phyir / / yang na dbyer med kyang ming gzugs kyis lus yongs su 'dzin to zhes 'di tha dad par ston to /
darśayati yathā sarvaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ pañcabhiḥ skandhaiḥ saṅgṛhītam iti / / aupapādukānāṃ tu vijñānapratyayaṃ ṣaḍāyatanam evetyato / vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpaṃ yathāsambhavaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# dper na 'dus byas thams cad phung po lnga rnams kyis kun bsdus so zhes bya ba lta bu'o / / rdzus te skye ba rnams ni rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis skye mched drug nyid do / / de'i phyir rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs ci rigs par shes par bya'o /
pūraṇāt kliśyata iti / / kena pūraṇāt kasya veti / / ṣaḍāyatanena / / nāmarūpasaṅgṛhītaṃ śarīraṃ / / nāmarūpāvasthāyāṃ hi śarīram aparipūrṇam ucyate cakṣurādy / āyatanābhāvāt /
# rdzogs byed phyir 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do zhes bya ba gang gis gang du gang rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir zhe na / / skye mched drug gis ming dang gzugs su bsdus pa'i lus te 'di ltar ming dang gzugs kyi tshe ni / / mig la sogs pa'i skye mched med pa'i phyir lus ma rdzogs pa zhes bya'o /
asti ca tasyām avasthāyāṃ kāyāyatanaṃ manāayatanañca tad apy / aparipūrṇam eva āśritāśrayaparipūryabhāvāt /
# de'i tshe na lus kyi skye mched dang yid kyi skye mched yod mod kyi 'on kyang brten pa dang gnas yongs su rdzogs par med ba'i phyir yongs su ma rdzogs pa nyid do /
ṣaḍāyatanāvasthāyāṃ punaścakṣurādyabhinirvṛtta āśritaḥ paripūrṇo / bhavati /
# skye mched drug gi dus na ni mig la sogs pa mngon par grub pas gnas yongs su rdzogs pa yin no /
kāyāyatanaṃ ca paripūrṇaṃ bhavati taccakṣūr ādyāśritānāṃ / paripūrṇatvāt /
# mig la sogs pa de la brten pa rnams yongs su rdzogs pas lus kyi skye mched kyang yongs su rdzogs pa yin no /
kathaṃ tac cakṣurādi āśritaṃ ? / tat pratibaddhavṛttitvāt /
# ji ltar mig la sogs pa la brten zhe na de la rag las te 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
manāayatanam api ṣaḍvijñānasaṅgṛhītaṃ tadānīṃ
# yid kyi skye mched ni rnam par shes pa drug gis bsdus pa ste /
niravaśeṣāśrayaparipūritāt paripūrṇaṃ bhavati /
# de'i tshe gnas ma lus par yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir yongs su rdzogs pa yin no /
aṅgapratyaṅgaparipūritāś ca ṣaḍāyatanāvasthāyām eva /
# yan lag dang nyid lag yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir skye mched drug gi dus nyid na /
āśrayaparipūraṇāt ṣaḍāyatanena kliśyate jagad iti veditavyaṃ /
# gnas yongs su rdzogs pas skye mched drug gis 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed ces bya'o /
triparicchedāj jagat kliśyata iti sambadhyate / / trayāṇāṃ hīndriyaviṣayavijñānasannipāte indriyasya
# gsum gcod phyir 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro / / gsum ni dbang po dang yul dang rnam par shes pa 'dus so /
sukhādivedanotpattyanukūlo yastriprakāro vikāras tat paricchedaḥ sparśaḥ
# bde ba la sogs pa'i tshor ba 'byung ba dang mthun pa dbang po'i 'gyur ba rnam pa gsum gang yin pa de yongs su gcod pa ni reg pa'o /
ata evāyam indriyavikārasādṛśyaṃ spṛśati tadākāratayeti sparśa ucyate / [p.31]
# de bas na dbang po'i 'gyur ba gang yin pa de'i rnam pa dang 'dra bar reg par byed pas reg pa zhes bya'o /
atha vā ṣaḍāyatanapratyayaḥ sparśa indriyasya sukhādivedanānukūlaṃ / trividhaṃ vikāraṃ prasūte / / upabhogād vedanayeti / / vedanā hi tṛṣṇayopabhujyate āsvādyata ity arthaḥ /
# yang na skye mched drug gi rkyen gyis reg pa ni bde ba la sogs par tshor ba dang mthun pa dbang po'i 'gyur ba rnam pa gsum skyed do; / / nye bar spyod pa ni tshor bas so zhes bya ba la / / tshor ba ni srid pas nye bar spyad pa ste / / ro myong bar byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
puṇyādikarmopabhogād vā vedanopabhogaḥ /
# yang na bsod nams la sogs pa'i las la nye bar spyod pas tshor ba ni nye bar spyod pa zhes bya'o /
atha vopabhogo'tra vedanāyā anubhavaḥ /
# yang na 'dir nye bar spyod pa zhes bya ba ni tshor ba myong ba ste /
sukhādiṣucānubhūyamāneṣu tatra sukhādiparipoṣaṇād
# bde ba la sogs pa myong ba na der bde ba la sogs pa rgyas par gyur pa'i phyir /
anurāgapratighamohaiḥ kliśyate jagat / / karṣaṇād iti / / karṣaṇāt kena kasya veti na vijñāyata ity ata āha tṛṣṇayā / karmākṣiptasya punar bhavasyeti /
# rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba dang gti mug rnams kyis 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do / / sdud pa'i phyir zhes bya ba gang gis gang sdud pa mi shes so / / de'i phyir las kyis btab pa'i yang srid pa sred pas so zhes bya ba smos so /
saṃskārair vijñāne bījaparipoṣaṇenākṣiptasya punar bhavasyodaka / kalpayā tṛṣṇayā sarvagatiṣv aviśeṣeṇātmabhāvābhilāṣayā
# 'du byed rnams kyis yang srid pa'i sa bon rnam par shes pa la gso ba'i phyir btab pa / / yang srid par 'gyur ba'i sa bon chu dang 'dra ba'i sred pa /
yadārdrīkṛtaḥ puar bhava utpattāv upayuṅkte utpattiṃ cāvasthāpayati / tat karṣaṇaṃ / / nibandhanāt /
# 'gro ba thams cad du bye brag med par lus 'dod pa zhes bya bas brlan nas yang srid pa 'byung bar nye bar sbyor zhing 'byung ba nges par 'jog pa gang yin pa de ni sdud pa'o /
kena nibandhanāt kva kasya veti praśnāvakāśe svayam evāha upādānair / vijñānasyopapattyanukūleṣu kāmādiṣv iti /
# sbyor ba'i phyir zhes bya ba la gang gis gang du gang zhig sbyor ba dri bar bya ba'i skabs su bdag nyid kyis len pa rnams kyis rnam par shas pa skye ba dang mthun pa 'dod pa la sogs pa rnams su'o zhes bya ba smos so /
chandarāgalakṣaṇaiścaturbhir upādānair karmākṣiptaṃ vijñānam / utpattyanukūleṣu kāmadṛṣṭiśīlavratātmavādeṣu nibadhnāti avasthāpayati
# mngon par zhan pa dang 'dun pa'i 'dod chags kyi mtshan nyid nye bar len pa bzhi po dag gis las kyis btab pa'i rnam par shes pa skye ba dang mthun pa 'dod pa dang lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs dang bdag tu lta ba dag tu sbyor bar byed 'jog par byed de /
ca vijñānaṃ hi cchandarāgavaśāt tatra vartate /
# 'di ltar 'dun pa'i 'dod chags kyi dbang gis rnam par shes pa der gnas so /
ābhimukhyādity atrāpi parapraśnāvakāśe svayamevaha bhavena kṛtasya / karmaṇaḥ punar bhava vipākadānāyābhimukhīkaraṇād iti /
# mngon du'i phyir zhes bya ba 'dir yang gzhan gyis yongs su dri bar bya ba'i skabs su bdag nyid kyis las byas pa'i rnam par smin pas yang srid par 'byin par mngon par byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
yathānibandhanaṃ vijñānasya pūrvakṛtaṃ karma paunarbhavikaṃ / vāsanāvasthaṃ  vipākaphalaṃ prati vṛttilambhanād bhavaḥ sadbhūta / ākṣiptabhavaś ca nirvṛttaye'bhimukhībhavati evaṃ bhavenābhimukhīkaraṇāj / jagat kliśyate / / duḥkhitāj jātyā jarāmaraṇena ca / / kiṃ ? / kliśyate jagad iti /
# ji ltar sngon byas pa'i las rnam par shes pa'i rgyu yang 'byung bas bag chags kyi dus su gyur pa rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu'i phyir / / 'jug pa rnyed pas srid pa yod par gyur cing srid pa btab pa 'grub par mngon du gyur pa ste / / de ltar na srid pas mngon du'i phyir 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do / / sdug bsngal phyir ni skye ba dang rga shis 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
evaṃ bhavāt punarbhavābhinirvṛttau satyāmādita eva garbhādhāne / śukraśoṇite vijñānasammūrcchanāt kliśyate /
# de ltar srid pa las yang srid pa mngon par 'grub pa yod pa thog ma nyid du mngal du zhugs pa na khu ba dang khrag gi nang na rnam par shes pa myos pas nyon mongs par byed do /
tathā māturāmāśayapakvāśayayor antarāle parivartanāt kliśyate /
# de bzhin du ma'i mngal du zhu ba dang ma zhu ba'i gnas kyi bar na 'gre ldog pas nyon mongs par byed do /
tathā ca mātubhojanacaryayoḥ saṅkaṭaghunoraparityāgād api kliśyate /
# yang de ltar ma'i kha zas dang spyod pa nyam nga ba dang ya nga ba ma spangs pas kyang nyon mongs par byed do /
tathā sambhādhe - nāśucinā mārgeṇa nirgacchati /
# de bzhin du dog pa mi gtsang ba'i lam nas 'byung bas nyon mongs par byed do /
kliśyate jagaj jātaṃ punar jarayā khālityapālityādilakṣaṇayā maraṇena / ca nāmarūpabhedalakṣaṇena priyābhyāṃ yauvanajīvitābhyāṃ bhraśyamānaṃ / kliśyate jagad iti / / gacchatīti jagat / / sabhāgāvakāśāt kṣaṇāvakāśaṃ [p.32] / gacchatīty arthaḥ /
# skyes nas kyang spyi cer dang skra skya ba la sogs pa rga ba'i mtshan nyid dang ming dang gzugs 'jig pa'i 'chi ba'i mtshan nyid dang lang tsho dang srog phangs pa las nyams pas 'gro ba nyon mongs par byed do / / 'gro bar byed pas na 'gro ba ste / / rigs mthun pa'i gnas skabs nas skad cig gi gnas skabs su rab tu 'gro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
kliśYata iti jātijarāvyādhimaraṇādibhis traidhātuke / kṣaṇaparamparayā''javañjavībhāvena ca pīḍyata ityarthaḥ / / kliśyata iti na vyavadāyata ity apare /
# nyon mongs par byed ces bya ba ni / / skye ba dang rga ba dang na ba dang 'chi ba la sogs pas khams gsum du skad cig gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa 'ong zhing 'gro bar gyur pas nyen zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / kha cig na re rnam par byang ba'i ma yin pas nyon mongs pa zhes bya zhe'o /
evam ayaṃ saṅkleśalakṣaṇo dvādaśāṅgaḥ / pratītyasamutpādaśchādanādyekādaśabhir arthair vyavadānavipakṣaḥ /
# de ltar kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yan lag bcu gnyis pa 'di ni sgrib pa'i phyir zhes bya ba la sogs pa don rnam pa bcu gcig gis rnam par byang ba'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs su 'gyur ro /
avidyādy utpattikramaḥ pūrvapūrvasyottarottarāvāhanāt //1-11// / tredhā saṅkleśaḥ - kleśasaṃkleśaḥ karmasaṅkleśaḥ janmasaṅkleśaśca / / tatra kleśasaṅkleśo'vidyātṛṣṇopādānāni / / karmasaṅkleśaḥ saṃskārā bhavaś ca / / janmasaṃkleśaḥ śeṣāṇyaṅgāni / / dvedhā saṃkleśaḥ - hetusaṃkleśaḥ phalasaṃkleśaś ca / / tatra hetusaṃkleśaḥ kleśakarmasvabhāvair aṅgaiḥ / / phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣaiḥ / / saptadhā saṃkleśaḥ saptavidho hetuḥ ...viparyāsahetuḥ ākṣepahetuḥ / upanayahetuḥ parigrahahetuḥ upabhogahetuḥ ākarṣaṇahetuḥ udvegahetuś ca ... / tatra viparyāsahetur avidyā / / ākṣepahetuḥ saṃskārāḥ / / upanayahetur vijñānaṃ / / parigrahahetur nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatane / / upabhogahetuḥ sparśavedane / / ākarṣaṇahetus tṛṣṇopādānabhavāḥ / / udvegahetur jātijarāmaraṇe / / sacaścaiṣa saṃkleśo'bhūtaparikalpāt pravartata iti / / katividhaḥ punar anena dvādaśāṅgena na pratītyasamutpādena samāsataḥ / saṃkleśaḥ pradarśita ityata evedam ucyate so'yaṃ dvādaśāṅgaḥ / pratītyasamutpādaḥ - / tredhā dvedhā ca saṃkleśaḥ saptadhā iti / / ca śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ parivartārthaś ca / / kleśa eva saṃkleśa iti kleśasaṃkleśaḥ / / evaṃ karmajanmasaṃkleśau / / kleśo hi pravartamānaḥ svaparātmanor vyābādhakatvāt saṃkleśaḥ / / yathoktaṃ sūtre'pi - rakto rāgaparīta ātmavyābādhāyāpi cetayate / paravyābādhāyā'pi cetayate / / ubhayavyābādāyāpi cetayate / / evaṃ dveṣo mohaścāpi veditavya iti / / karmajanmasaṃkleśayoścotpādakatvāt saṃkleśaḥ / / tathā hi kleśādhipatyena karma janmākṣipati dṛṣṭasatyasya satyapi karmaṇi / punar bhavākṣepābhāvāt kleśasamudācāreṇa punar bhavabījasya / bhavīkaraṇāt kliṣṭacittasya ca punarbhavapratisandhibandhāj janma / saṅkleśenaiva hetunā / / tato'rhataḥ pratisandhibandhābhāvaḥ kliṣṭacittābhāvāt / / karma ca śubhāśubhaṃ tadātve kāyacittayor āyāsanimittatvād / āyatyāñca vipākadānāt saṅkleśaḥ / / janmā'pi sarvopadravāspadatvāt saṅkleśa iti / / tredhā saṅkleśaḥ / / hetordvidhā bhedāt / / kleśasaṅkleśo vidyātṛṣṇopādānānīti tritayam api kleśātmakatvāt / / karmasaṅkleśaḥ saṃskārā bhavaśceti [p.33] / dvayam api karmātmakatvāt / / ayantu viśeṣaḥ - / svarūpāvasthaṃ karma saṃskārāḥ bījāvasthaṃ bhava iti / / janmasaṃkleśaḥ śeṣāṇyaṅgānīti / vijñānanāmarūpaṣaḍāyatanasparśavedanājātijarāmaraṇāni eṣāṃ / janmasaṅgṛhītatvāt / / dvedhā saṃkleśo hetuphalābhyāṃ prabhidyate / / hetusaṃkleśaḥ kleśakarmasvabhāvair aṅgaiḥ / / phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣair aṅgair iti / / tatra hetusaṃkleśatvaṃ karmakleśānāṃ vijñānādivedanāparyantaṃ / jātyātmakaṃ jarāmaraṇādīnavajanma sampādayitum abhipravṛttatvāt / / phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣair vijñānādibhiḥ karmakleśaphalatvāt / / punaḥ sa eva pratītyasamutpādaḥ saptadhā saṃkleśa iti / viparyāsākṣepopanaya-parigrahopabhogākarṣaṇodvegahetutvāt saptavidho
# ma rig pa la sogs pa'i go rims ni snga ma snga mas phyi ma phyi ma skyed pa'i phyir ro / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yan lag bcu gnyis pa 'dis yang mdor bsdu na nyon mongs pa rnam pa du bstan zhe na / / de'i phyir 'di skad ces rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yan lag bcu gnyis pa / / de yang rnam gsum rnam gnyis kyang / / nyon mongs rnam bdun zhes bya ba smos so / / kyang zhes bya ba'i sgra ni bsdu ba dang go bsnor ba'i tha tshig go / / nyon mongs pa nyid kun nas nyon mongs pa yin pas nyon mongs pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ste / / las kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa yang de bzhin no / / nyon mongs pa 'byung ba na bdag dang gzhan la gnod pa byed pa'i phyir kun nas nyon mongs pa ste / / mdo las kyang ji skad du chags pa'i 'dod chags kyis kun nas dkris pa bdag la yang gnod par sems / / gzhan la yang gnod par sems / / gnyi ga la yang gnod par sems so / / de bzhin du zhe sdang dang rmongs pa yang shes par bya'o zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa 'byung ba'i phyir yang kun nas nyon mongs pa ste / / 'di ltar nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis na las kyis tshe 'phen te / / bden pa mthong ba las yod kyang srid pa 'phen pa med pa dang nyon mongs pa kun tu 'byung bas yang srid pa'i sa bon srid par byed pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa can gyi sems kyang yang srid pa'i nying mtshams sbyor ba'i phyir / / tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa'i rgyu yang yin no / / de bas na dgra bcom pa la nyon mongs pa can gyi sems med pa'i phyir / / nyid mtshams sbyor ba med do / / las kyang dge ba dang mi dge ba ste / / de nyid kyi tshe na lus dang sems sdug bsngal ba'i rgyur gyur pa dang ma 'ongs pa na rnam par smin pa yang 'byin pas kun nas nyon mongs pa'o / / tshe yang gnod pa thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pas nyon mongs pa'o; / / rgyu rnam pa gnyis su bye ba'i phyir kun nas nyon mongs pa gsum mo / / nyon mongs pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ni ma rig pa dang sred pa dang len pa rnams te / / gsum char yang nyon mongs pa'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro / / las kyis kun nas nyon mongs pa ni 'du byed rnams dang srid pa la bya ste / / gnyi ga yang las kyi bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro / / 'di ni bye brag yin te / / rang gi ngo bor gnas pa'i las ni 'du byed rnams so / / sa bon du gnas pa ni srid pa'o / / tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ni / / rnam par shes pa dang ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug dang reg pa dang tshor ba dang skye ba dang rga shi zhes bya ba yan lag lhag ma rnams te / / de dag ni tshe'i nang du 'dus pa'i phyir ro / / kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam gnyis ni rgyu mi dbye bar byas pa ste / / rgyu'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ni nyon mongs pa dang las kyi ngo bo nyid kyi yan lag rnams kyis so / / 'bras bu'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ni yan lag lhag ma rnams kyis so / / de la las dang nyon mongs pa rnams ni rnam par shes pa la sogs pa tshor ba la thug pa skye pa'i bdag nyid can dang rga shi'i nyes dmigs can gyi tshe skyed par rab tu zhugs pa'i phyir ro / / 'bras bu'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ni lhag ma rnam par shes pa la sogs pa rnams kyis te / / las dang nyon mongs pa'i 'bras bu yin pa'i phyir ro / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba de nyid kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa bdun zhes bya ste / / phyin ci log dang 'debs pa dang nye bar khrid pa dang kun 'dzin pa dang nye bar spyod pa dang sdud pa dang skyo ba'i rgyu'i phyir ro /
hetuḥ / / tatra viparyāsahetur avidyeti / / avidyāgato hi tattvasammohād anityādīn nityādirūpeṇa viparyasyatīti /
# rgyu bdun po de lta ma rig pa ni phyin ci log gi rgyu'o zhes bya ba la / / ma rig par gyur pa ni de kho na nyid la rmongs pa'i phyir / / mi rtag pa la sogs pa la rtag pa'i ngo bor mthong bas phyin ci log ces bya'o /
ākṣepahetuḥ saṃskārā iti vijñāne caturaṅgātmajanmabījasya / pratiṣṭhāpanāt /
# 'du byed rnams ni 'debs pa'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba la / / rnam par shes pa la yan lag bzhi'i bdag nyid kyi tshe'i sa bon 'jog pa'i phyir ro /
upanayahetur vijñānam itīha cyutasyopapattiviṣaYa upanayanāt /
# rnam par shes pa ni nye bar khrid pa'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba la 'dir shi 'phos nas skye ba'i yul du nye bar khrid pa'i phyir ro /
parigrahahetur nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatana ity upanītasya / nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatanābhyāṃ nikāyasabhāgaparigrahāt / / pūrvaṃ nāmarūpeṇaiva parigraha ukto jarāyujādikāṃ yonim abhipretya / idānīm upapādukam adhikṛtya ṣaḍāyatanenā'pi parigraha uktaḥ / / atha vā nāmarūpeṇa tat prathamata ātmabhāvamātrasya saṅgraho
# ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug ni kun 'dzin pa'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba ni khrid par gyur pa ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug gi ris mthun pa kun 'dzin pa'i phyir ro / / sngar mngal nas skye ba la sogs pa'i skye gnas la dgongs nas ming dang gzugs kyis kun 'dzin par bshad do / / da ni brdzus te skye ba'i dbang du mdzad de skye mched drug gis kyang 'dzin to zhes bshad do /
vivakṣitaḥ / / iha tv aparipūrṇasya paripūrṇasya ceti nāsti virodhaḥ /
# yang na ming dang gzugs kyis thog ma nyid du lus tsam 'dzin par brjod par bzhed pa'o / / 'dir ni yongs su ma rdzogs pa dang yongs su rdzogs pa 'dzin pas 'gal ba med do /
upabhogahetuḥ sparśavedana iti /
# reg pa dang tshor ba ni nye bar spyod pa'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba la /
sakāraṇenānubhavena kuśalākuśalakarmavipākasyopabhogāt /
# rgyu dang bcas pa'i myong bas dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyi rnam par smin pa la nye bar spyod pa'i phyir ro /
ākarṣaṇahetus tṛṣṇopādānabhavā iti /
# sred pa dang len pa dang srid pa ni sdud pa'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba la /
sa upabhuktakarmavipāko bālas tasyāṃ tasyāṃ vedanāyāṃ tṛṣyati /
# byis pa las kyi rnam par smin pa la spyod pa de tshor ba de dang de la sred par byed de srid pa 'phel nas /
vivṛddhatṛṣṇaś ca tat saṃyogatṛṣṇayā kāmādīn upādatte /
# yang de dang ldan zhing mi 'bral bar sred pas 'dod pa la sogs pa len to /
tad upādānāc cāsya pūrvabhūtaṃ paunarbhavikaṃ karma vāsanāvasthaṃ / pariṇataṃ yathākṣiptavipākadānayā pravṛttiṃ labdhvā bhavo bhavati /
# de blangs pas kyang de'i las sngon byung ba yang srid pa / / bag chags su gnas pa yongs su gyur na ji ltar btab pa bzhin du rnam par smin pa'i 'byin pa'i phyir; 'jug pa rnyed nas srid par 'gyur ro /
sa ca tṛṣṇopādānabhavaḥ saṃskārākṣiptaḥ punar bhavābhinirvṛttaya / ākṛṣyate abhimukhīkriyata iti tṛṣṇopādānabhavā ākarṣaṇahetuḥ /
# de yang 'du byed kyis btab pa'i yang srid pa mngon par grub par bya ba'i phyir / / srid pa dang len pa dang srid pa rnams kyis sdud cing mngon par 'du byed ces bya bas / / sred pa dang len pa dang srid pa rnams ni sdud pa'i rgyu'o /
atha vā tṛṣṇāvaśena cchandarāgānurūpānyatarakarmavāsanābhimukhāt / tṛṣṇopādānabhavā ākarṣaṇahetuḥ / / udvegahetur jātijarāmaraṇe ityevamatra jarmākarṣaṇāt tasmiṃstasmin
# yang na sred pa'i dbang gis 'dun pa'i 'dod chags dang mthun pa gang yang rung ba'i las kyi bag chags mngon du byed pa'i phyir / / sred pa dang len pa dang srid pa ni bsdus pa'i rgyu'o / / skye ba dang rga shi ni skye ba'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba ni /
sattvanikāye jātijarāmaraṇaduḥkham anyacca / śokaparidevaduḥkha-daurmanasyopāyāsaduḥkham anantaprabhedam anubhavatīti
# de ltar 'di ni tshe drangs bas sems can gyi rigs de dang der skye ba dang rga shi'i sdug bsngal dang mya ngan dang smre sngags 'don pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang yid mi bde ba dang 'khrugs pa'i sdug bsngal rab tu dbye ba mtha' yas pa gzhan yang myong bar 'gyur ro /
/ [p.34] / tatra tridhā saṅkleśā'bhidhānena kleśakarmaṇo janmanaḥ
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa gsum du brjod pas nyon mongs pa dang las ni /
sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇahetutvaṃ darśitaṃ /
# tshe'i rgyu thun mong dang thun mongs ma yin pa rab tu bstan to /
kleśo hi janmāṅkurasya sādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ bhūmyādivat /
# nyon mongs pa ni sa la sogs pa ltar tshe'i myu gu'i thun mong gi rgyu'o /
karmatvasādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ aṅkurasyeva bījaṃ tad bhedena janambhedād iti / atha vā nātra pūrvāntāparāntamadhyāntāni trīṇi kāṇḍāni kiṃ tarhi
# las ni thun mong ma yin te / / myu gu'i sa bon ltar de tha dad pas tshe tha dad pa'i phyir ro / / yang na 'dir sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' dang bar gyi mtha' zhes bya ba rabs gsum du ni ma yin gyi /
karmakleśaphalānīti pradarśayati/
# las dang nyon mongs pa dang 'bras bu yid zhes rab tu ston to /
dvividhābhidhānena hetuphalamātram evedaṃ nātrānyaḥ saṅkliśyate
# rnam pa gnyis su brjod pas 'di nyid rgyu dang 'bras bu tsam du zad de / / 'di la byed pa po'am /
kārako vedako veti pradarśayati / / atha vā'tra karmakleśamātram eva hetuḥ / / tayor bhāvābhāvāj janmabhāvābhāvadarśanāt / / atas tat phalam eva janma /
# tshor ba po kun nas nyon mongs pa gzhan med do zhes rab tu ston to / / yang na 'dir las dang nyon mongs pa tsam nyid rgyu ste / / de dag yod pa dang med pas tshe yod pa dang med par snang ba'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir tshe ni de'i 'bras bu nyid do /
tasmānnātra hetuḥ phalaṃ vā sarvatra pañcaskandhikāvastheti / pradarśayati /
# de lta bas na 'di la rgyu 'am 'bras bu ni med kyi dus skabs thams cad du yang phung po lnga nyid do zhes rab tu ston to /
saptadhāhetunirdeśena punar dvividhaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ pradarśitaḥ / ākṣepalakṣaṇo'bhinirvṛttilakṣaṇaśceti / / tatrākṣepalakṣaṇaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ saptyabhir aṅgair nirdiṣṭaḥ / yenākṣīpyate yathākṣipyate yaccākṣipyate tat pradarśanāt /
# rgyu rnam pa bdun bshad pas ni 'phen pa'i mtshan nyid dang mngon par 'grub pa'i mtshan nyid du yang rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba rnam pa gnyis su rab tu bstan to / / de la 'phen pa'i mtshan nyid ni gang gis 'phen pa dang ji ltar 'phen pa dang gang 'phen pa de rab tu bstan pa'i phyir /
abhinirvṛttilakṣaṇaḥ pañcabhir aṅgaiḥ tasyākṣiptasya yenābhinirvṛttir / yathābhinirvṛttir yā cābhinirvṛttiḥ tasyāñca ya ādīnava iti /
# rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i yan lag bdun gyis bstan to / / mngon par 'grub pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'phags pa de gang gis mngon par 'grub pa dang ji ltar mngon par 'grub pa dang gang mngon par 'grub pa dang de'i nyes pa bstan pa'i phyir yan lag lngas so /
kenākṣīpyate ? / avidyāpratyayaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ yathā tattvaṃ mugdhvā viparītaṃ saṃjānāti
# gang gis 'phen zhe na ma rig pa las byung ba'i 'du byed rnams kyis te / / ji ltar de kho na la rmongs nas phyin ci log tu shes te /
kuśalākuśalāniñjyān saṃskārānabhisaṃskāroti /
# dge ba dang mi dge ba dang mi gyo ba'i 'du byed rnams mngon par byed do /
katham ākṣipyate taiḥ saṃskāraiḥ ?
# 'du byed de dag gis ji ltar 'phen zhe na /
vijñāne bījapoṣaṇād utpattibhavyatāyām avasthāpanāt / / kim ākṣipyate ?
# rnam par shes pa las sa bon gsos pas skye bar nus par gnas pa'i phyir ro / / ci gzhig 'phen zhe na /
paunarbhavikaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā ca yathāyogaṃ /
# yang srid pa ba'i ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug dang reg pa dang tshor ba ste ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
tadevam ākṣiptaṃ kenābhinirvartyate ?
# de ltar 'phangs pa de gang gis mngon par 'grub par byed ce na /
yathoktakrameṇa pūrvākṣiptādihotpannāṃ vedanāṃ pratītya yā / tṛṣṇotpannā tat pratyayenopādānena /
# ji skad bshad pa'i rim gyis snga ma 'phangs pas 'dir skyes pa'i tshor ba la brten nas sred pa skyed pa gang yin pa de dag byung ba'i len pas so /
kathaṃ tenābhinirvartyate ?
# ji ltar des mngon par 'grub ce na /
tasya vijñāne vāsanāvasthasya karmaṇas tena bhavīkaraṇāt /
# rnam par shes pa la bag chags su gnas pa'i las de / / des srid par byed pa'i phyir ro /
bahuvidhā hi vijñāne karmavāsanā vartate / vicitrasaṃskāraparibhāvitatvāt /
# 'du byed sna tshogs kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i phyir / / rnam par shes pa la las kyi bag chags rnam pa mang po gnas te /
upādānaviśeṣaparigraheṇa yenātra punar bhavatvaṃ vartate so'tra bhava / ucyate / / kā punaḥ sa'bhinivruttiḥ ?
# len pa'i bye brag gis yongs su gzung ba'i phyir / / gang gis 'di las yang srid pa gnyis par 'gyur ba de ni 'dir srid pa zhes bya'o / / mngon par 'grub pa de gang yin zhe na /
yā tasyākṣiptasya nāmarūpādiksyāyatyāṃ jātiḥ / / tasyaṃ punaḥ satyāṃ ka ādīnavaḥ ?
# ming dang gzugs la sogs pa 'phangs pa des phyis skye ba gang yin pa'o / / de yod pas nyes par 'gyur ba gang yin zhe na /
jarāmaraṇaṃ priyayauvanajīvitabhraṃśādīti / / atra tūpanayahetur nirarthaṃ iti cet na nirarthakaḥ / / vicchinnamaraṇād bhavopapattibhavapravṛttyadhigamanirākaraṇārthaṃ / / sarve caite saṅkleśā abhūtaparikalpāt pravartanta iti / cittacaittāśrayatvāt saṅkleśasya / / uktaṃ hi tat - / abhūtaparikalpaśca cittacaittās tridhātukāḥ / / iti //1-12// [p.35] / {abhūtaparikalpapiṇḍārthaḥ} / piṇḍārthaḥ punar abhūtaparikalpasya navavidhaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ / bhavati / / sallakṣaṇaṃ asallākṣaṇaṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ saṅgrahalakṣaṇaṃ / asallakṣaṇā'nupraveśopāyalakṣaṇaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ / pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ saṃkleśalakṣaṇañca / / piṇḍārthaḥ punar abhūtaparikalpasyeti vistareṇārthanirdeśaḥ / sukhāvabodhārthaṃ piṇḍārthanirdeśo'vismaraṇārthañca / / tato'trārthadvayam uktaṃ / / sallakṣaṇaṃ - / abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti / / asallakṣaṇaṃ - / dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate / iti /
# rga shi de lang tsho dang srog phangs pa 'jig pa'i phyir ro / / 'dir nye bar khrid pa'i rgyu ni don med do zhe na don med pa ma yin te / / 'chi ba'i srid pa chad nas skye ba'i srid pa 'byung bar rtog pa bsal ba'i phyir ro / / kun nas nyon mongs pa 'di dag thams cad ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa las 'byung ngo zhes bya ba ni / / sems dang sems las byung ba rnams ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i gnas yin pa'i phyir te / / de yang / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog ni / / sems dang sems byung khams gsum pa / / zhes bshad pa yin no / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i don bsdus pa ni zhes bya ba ni / / don rgyas par bshad pa bde blag tu khong du chud par bya ba dang mi brjed par bya ba'i phyir don bsdus pa bstan to / / de'i phyir 'dir ni don gnyi ga yang bshad do / / yod pa'i mtshan nyid ni / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya'o / / med pa'i mtshan nyid ni / / de la gnyis po yod ma yin / / zhes bya ba'o / / rang gi mtshan nyid ni /
svalakṣaṇaṃ - / arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ prajāyate / vijñānaṃ // iti / / saṅgrahalakṣaṇaṃ - / kalpitaḥ paratantraś ca pariniṣpanna eva ca / iti /
# don dang sems can bdag rnam rig / / snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni / / rab tu skye'o zhes bya ba'o / / bsdu ba'i mtshan nyid ni / / rtag ba dang ni gzhan dbang dang / / yongs su grub pa nyid kyang ngo /
asallakṣaṇānupraveśopāyalakṣaṇaṃ -
# zhes bya'o / / med pa'i mtshan nyid la 'jug pa'i thabs kyi mtshan nyid ni /
upalabdhiṃ samāśritya nopalabdhiḥ prajāyate / / ityādi / / prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ -
# dmigs pa la ni brten nas su / / mi dmigs pa ni rab tu skye / / zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid ni /
abhūtaparikalpaś ca cittacaittās tridhātukāḥ / iti / / paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ -
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog ni / / sems dang sems byung khams gsum pa / / zhes bya ba'o / / rnam grangs kyi mtshan nyid ni /
tarthārthadṛṣṭir vijñānaṃ tad viśeṣe tu caitasāḥ / iti / / pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ -
# de la don mthong rnam par shes / / de yi bye brag sems las byung / / zhes bya'o / / 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid ni /
ekaṃ pratyayavijñānaṃ dvitīyaṃ aupabhogikaṃ / iti / / saṃkleśalakṣaṇaṃ - / chādanād ropaṇāc caiva nayanāt samparigrahāt / ityādi //
# gcig ni rkyen gyi rnam par shes / / gnyis pa nye bar spyod pa can / / zhes bya'o / / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid ni / / sgrib pa'i phyir dang 'debs pa'i phyir / / khrid pa'i phyir dang kun 'dzin phyir / / zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
evam abhūtaparikalpaṃ navaprakāraṃ khyāpayitvā yathā śūnyatā / vijñeyā tan nirdeśatīti ko'trābhisambandhaḥ ?
# de ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i mtshan nyid rnam pa dgur brjod nas stong pa nyid ji ltar shes par bya ba de ston te zhes bya ba 'dir ji ltar sbyar zhe na /
dvayam anena pratijñātam abhūtaparikalpaḥ śūnyatā ca / [p.36] / saṃkleśapūrvakaṃ ca vyavadānaṃ / / dharmāvabodhāśrayañca dharmatāvadhāraṇam / ityato'bhūtaparikalpanirdeśānantaraṃ yathā śūnyatā vijñeyā tathā / nirdiśati - / lakṣaṇañcā'tha paryāya / iti vistaraḥ /
# 'dis yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa dang stong pa nyid dang sngar kun nas nyon mongs pa la rnam par byang ba dang chos khong du chud pa la brten nas chos nyid nges par 'dzin par 'gyur ba gnyis dam bcas pa yin te / / de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa bshad pa'i 'og tu / / stong pa nyid ji ltar shes par bya ba de ltar 'chad de / / mtshan nyid dang ni rnam grangs dang /
tatra lakṣaṇaṃ hi bhāvābhāvapratiṣedhātmatā sarvatra / śūnyathāprabhedavyāpakatvāt /
# zhes rgya cher ro / / de la mtshan nyid ni dngos po dang dngos po med pa dgag pa'i bdag nyid de / / stong pa nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba thams cad la khyab pa'i phyir ro /
nāmāntaraṃ paryāyaḥ /
# ming gzhan ni rnam grangs so /
paryāyānuguṇaṃ paryāyapravṛttinimittaṃ paryāyārthaḥ / / ākāśavad abhinnalakṣaṇatvān nirvikalpatve'py
# rnam grangs dang mthun pa rnam grangs 'jug pa'i rgyu ni rnam grangs kyi don to / / nam mkha' ltar tha mi dad pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir /
āgantukopakleśasaṃyogaviyogāvasthābhedād bhedaḥ /
# rnam par mi rtog kyang glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang phrad pa dang bral ba'i dus tha dad pas dbye ba'o /
anyaś ca pudgaladharmasamāropabhedād bhedaḥ ṣoḍaśavidhaḥ /
# gzhan yang gang zag dang chos su sgro 'dogs pa tha dad pas dbye ba rnam pa bcu drug go /
sādhanaṃ śūnyatāprabhedapradarśane yuktiḥ /
# sgrub pa ni stong pa nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba ston par byed pa'i rigs pa'o /
kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ yadebhiḥ prakāraiḥ śūnyatā vijñātavyā ?
# ci'i phyir rnam pa de dag gis stong pa nyid shes par bya zhe na /
viśuddhyālambanatvād viśuddhyarthibhir lakṣaṇato vijñeyā /
# rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa yin pas na / / rnam par dag pa 'dod pa rnams kyi mtshan nyid shes par bya'o /
sūtrāntareṣu paryāyanirdeśeṣv asammohārthaṃ paryāyārthaḥ /
# mdo gzhan dag las rnam grangs bshad pa rnams la mi rmongs par bya ba'i phyir rnam grangs so /
paryāyārthā'vabodhārthācchūnyatāyā viśuddhyālambanatvena / niścitatvāt paryāyārthaḥ / / saṃkleśe nirākṛte sā viśuddheti tat saṃkleśaprahāṇāya / yatnotpādanārthaṃ bhedataḥ / / bheda sādhanāvabodhād vikārābhāve saty api bhedaṃ sukhaṃ pratipadyata / iti bhedasādhanato'pi vijñeyeti //1-13// / pṛthaktve sati dharmād anyā dharmateti na yujyate anityatāduḥkhatāvat / / ekatve sati viśuddhyālambanaṃ jñānaṃ na syāt sāmānyalakṣaṇañca / / etena tattvā'nyatvavinirmuktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati / / kathaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vijñeyam iti lakṣaṇaṃ hi prāg uddiṣṭam ityatas tadeva / prathamataḥ pṛṣṭaṃ - / dvayā'bhāvo hy abhāvasya bhāvaḥ śūnyasya lakṣaṇaṃ / [p.37] / iti vijñeyaṃ / / dvayasya grāhyasya grāhakasya cā'bhūtaparikalpe'bhūtaparikalpena vā / parikalpitātmakatvād vasturūpeṇā'bhāvaḥ /
# rnam grangs kyi don khong du chud par gyur na stong pa nyid la rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa nyid du nges pa'i phyir rnam grangs kyi don to / / kun nas nyon mongs pa bsal na / / de rnam par dag go zhes kun nas nyon mongs pa de spangs pa'i phyir 'bad pa skyed pa'i don du dbye ba'o / / dbye ba'i sgrub pa khong du chud na / / 'gyur ba med kyang dbye ba bde blag tu rig pa'i phyir dbye ba'i sgrub pa yang shes par bya'o / / mtshan nyid ji ltar shes par bya zhe na zhes bya ba ni / / mtshan nyid sngar smos pas de'i phyir de nyid dang por 'dri ste / / gnyis dngos med pa'i dngos po yi / / dngos po stong pa'i mtshan nyid do / / zhes bya bar shes par bya'o / / gnyis ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba la / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la'am / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pas kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid yin pas dngos po'i ngo bor med do /
tasya ca dvayābhāvasya yo bhāva etac chūnyatāyā lakṣaṇaṃ /
# gnyis pa dngos po med pa de'i dngos po gang yin pa de ni stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid do /
kārikānuguṇyāc cātra bhāvapratyayaluptanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ /
# tshig le'ur byas pa dang mthun par byas pa'i phyir 'dir yang dngos po'i rkyen ma smos par bstan par lta ba'o /
abhāvasya bhāva iti kim etat ?
# dngos po med pa'i dngos po zhes bya ba de dag gang yin /
abhāvasyātmatvam astitvaṃ / / anyathā dvayabhāvasyāstitvam eva syāt / / tad bhāvasya bhāvato'vidyamānatvāt / / ata evāha - / ity abhāvasvabhāvalakṣaṇatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ paridīpitaṃ bhavati na / bhāvarūpalakṣaṇam iti / / bhāvapratiṣedhavācakatvād abhāvaśabdasya
# dngos po med pa'i bdag nyid ni yod pa nyid do / / gzhan du na de'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po stong pa med pa'i phyir ro / / gnyis kyi dngos po yod pa nyid du 'gyur ro / / de'i phyir de ltar dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid du yongs su bstan pa yin no zhes bya ba smos te / / dngos po'i ngo bo'i mtshan nyid du ni ma yin no / / dngos po med pa'i sgra ni dngos po dgag pa'i tshig yin na /
bhāvaśabdābhāve'pyeṣo'rthovagamyata iti bhāvaśabdo'trādhikaḥ nādhikaḥ
# dngos po'i sgra med kyang don 'di khong du chud par 'gyur bas / / dngos po'i sgra ni 'dir lhag go /
dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatālakṣaṇam itīyati nirdiśyamāne dvayābhāvasya / svātantryam evātra gamyate śaśaviṣāṇābhāvavat na duḥkhatādivad
# lhag ma ma yin te gnyis kyi dngos po med pa stong pa'i mtshan nyid do zhes de tsam zhig bshad na / / gtsor gnyis kyi dngos po med pa nyid du ri bong gi rva dngos po med pa dang 'dra bar khong du chud de / / sdug bsngal nyid la sogs pa ltar chos nyid kyi ngo bor mi rung ngo /
dharmatārūpatā / / tasmādevam ucyate dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatā / / tasya cā'bhāvasyā'bhūtaparikalpe bhāvaḥ śūnyate'ty ucyate /
# de lta bas na 'di skad ces bya ste / / gnyis kyi dngos po med pa ni stong pa nyid do / / dngos po med pa de ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la yod de /
abhāvasya bhāvalakṣaṇaparigṛhītatvād dharmatārūpatā pradarśitā / / atha vā dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatety abhāvaśabdasya sāmānyavācitān na
# stong pa nyid ces bya ba ste dngos po med pa'i dngos po'i mtshan nyid yongs su gzung ba'i phyir chos nyid kyi ngo bor bstan pa yin no / / yang na gnyis kyi dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ces bya ba la /
vijñāyate katamo'trābhāvo'bhipreta ity atyantā'bhāvapradarśanārtham / ucyate - abhūtaparikalpe dvayābhāvasya bhāva iti / / na hi prāg abhāvapradhvaṃsābhāvau svopadānād anyatrākhyātuṃ yujyete / anyonyābhāvasvya caikāśratvaṃ na yujyate ubhayāśritatvāt /
# med pa'i sgra ni thun mong yin pas 'dir med pa zhes bya ba gang las dgongs pa mi shes pas / / gtan med par rab tu bstan pa'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la / / gnyis po'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po zhes bya ba brjod do / / snga na med pa dang zhig nas med pa gnyis ni rang gi nye bar len pa las gzhan du bshad par mi rigs so / / gcig la gcig med pa yang gnyi ga gnas yin pa'i phyir / / gcig tu gnas par mi rigs so /
tasmād bhāvasyābhāvalakṣaṇopādānād grāhyagrāhakayor atyantābhāva / eva śūnyatetyetaj jñāpitaṃ bhavati /
# de'i phyir dngos po'i dngos po med pa'i mtshan nyid nye bar bzung bas / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dag gtan dngos po med pa nyid stong pa nyid ces bya bar de shes par byas pa yin no /
yady abhāvātmikā śūnyatā kathaṃ paramārtha ucyate ?
# gal te med pa'i bdag nyid stong pa nyid yin na / / don dam pa zhes ji skad du bya zhe na /
paramajñānaviṣayatvād anityatāvat na tu vastutvāt / / api cābhāvasvabhāvo naiṣaḥ / / yasmādyaśvā'sau tad abhāvasvabhāvaḥ sa - / na bhāvo nā'pi cā'bhāvaḥ / / kathaṃ na bhāvaḥ ? / yasmād dvayasyā'bhāvaḥ /
# ye shes dam pa'i yul yin pas mi rtag pa nyid bzhin du ste / / dngos po'i phyir ni ma yin no / / de lta mod kyi de ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid kyang ma yin te / / 'di ltar de'i dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid gang yin pa de ni / / yod pa ma yin med pa'ang min / / ji ltar yod pa ma yin zhe na / / 'di ltar gnyis po'i dngos po med pa ste /
bhāvatve hi na dvayabhāvasyātyantābhāvaḥ syāt
# yod pa ni gnyis kyi dngos po gtan med par yang mi 'gyur la /
nā'bhūtaparikalpadharmatā / / kathaṃ nābhāvaḥ ?
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i chos nyid du yang mi 'gyur ro / / ji ltar med pa'ang ma yin zhe na /
yasmād dvayābhāvasya bhāvaḥ /
# 'di ltar gnyis po'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po ste /
nahi dvayābhāvo dvayābhāvasvarūpeṇābhāvaḥ /
# gnyis kyi dngos po med pa ni gnyis kyi dngos po med pa'i ngo bor med pa ma yin te /
so'bhāvaśced dvayasyāstitvaṃ syān na ca syād abhūtaparikalpasya
# de med du zin na gnyis yod pa nyid du 'gyur zhing / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i chos nyid du yang mi 'gyur te /
dharmatā yathā nityaduḥkhatā /
# dper na mi rtag pa nyid dang sdug bsngal ba nyid bzhin no /
sattvasya viparyāsatvena samāropitasya / nityasukhabhāvābhāvasvarūpatvān na bhāvo nāpy abhāva ity ucyate /
# sems can phyin ci log tu gyur pas sgro btags pa'i rtag pa dang bde ba'i dngos po'i dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid yin pas / / yod pa yang ma yin med pa yang ma yin zhes bya'o /
yadi punar abhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatā dharmatāsti kim asau tasmād anyo / vaktavya utānanya ity ato bravīti -
# gal te yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i stong pa nyid chos nyid yin na / / ci ste de las gzhan zhes bya ba'am / / 'on te gzhan ma yin zhe na /
etac ca śūnyatāyā lakṣaṇam iti / / abhāvasya svarūpam eva / [p.38]
# de'i phyir de ni stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid do zhes bya ba smos te / / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid kho na'o /
athavā bhāva evābhāvapratiṣedhātmakaḥ /
# yang na dngos po kho na dngos po med pa dgag pa'i bdag nyid kho na'o /
tasmād abhūtaparikalpāt - / na pṛthaktvaikalakṣaṇaṃ // / pṛthaktve sati dharmād anyā dharmateti na yujyate / / kaḥ punar ayogaḥ ?
# de lta bas na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa dang tha dad gcig pa'i mtshan nyid min / / tha dad pa yin na ni chos nyid las chos nyid gzhan yin pa mi rung ste /
dharmād vibhinnalakṣaṇatvād dharmatā dharmāntaram eva bhavati tad / anyadharmavat / / na ca dharmāntaraṃ dharmāntarasya dharmatā bhavitum arhati tatra punar / dharmāntaram anveṣṭavyam ity anavasthāprasaṅgāt / / anityatāduḥkhatāvad iti / / yathā'nityatā'nityebhyo nānyā duḥkhatā ca duḥkhād eva śūnyatā'pi na
# ji ltar mi rung zhe na chos las mtshan nyid tha dad pas chos nyid chos gzhan nyid du 'gyur te / / de las gzhan pa'i chos bzhin no / / chos gzhan ni chos gzhan gyi chos nyid du mi rung ste / / de la yang chos gzhan btsal dgos pas thug pa med par 'gyur ro / / mi rtag pa nyid dang sdug bsngal ba nyid bzhin no zhes bya ba ni / / ji ltar mi rtag pa nyid mi rtag pa rnams las gzhan ma yin pa dang sdug bsngal ba nyid kyang sdug bsngal ba las gzhan ma yin pa de ltar stong pa nyid kyang stong pa las gzhan ma yin pa zhes bya'o /
śūnyād anyeti / / ekatve sati viśuddhyālambanaṃ na syāt sāmānyalakṣaṇañceti /
# gcig pa yin du zin na ni rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa dang spyi'i mtshan nyid du mi 'gyur ro /
viśuddhyate'neneti viśuddhir mārgaḥ dharmasvalakṣaṇād ananyatvān
# 'dis rnam par dag par byed pas rnam par dag pa ni lam mo / / chos kyi rang gi mtshan nyid las gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
mārgālambanaṃ na syāt dharmasvalakṣaṇavat / / tasmāc ca na sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ yujyate / / svalakṣaṇād ananyatvāt /
# chos kyi rang gi mtshan nyid bzhin du lam gyi dmigs par mi 'gyur ro / / de'i phyir rang gi mtshan nyid las gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir / / spyi'i mtshan nyid du yang mi rung ngo /
tasyāpi dharmasvarūpavat parasparato bheda iti sāmānyatā hīyate / / atha vā svalakṣaṇasya tasmād anyatvād bhāvasvarūpavad bhedābhāvaḥ /
# de yang chos kyi rang gi ngo bo dang 'dra bar phan tshun tha dad pas mnyam pa nyid nyams par 'gyur ro / / yang na rang gi mtshan nyid de las gzhan ma yin pas dngos po'i rang gi ngo bo tha dad pa med do /
tataś ca sāmānyalakṣaṇasyāpy abhāvaḥ bhedāpekṣatvāt
# de'i phyir spyi yang med par 'gyur te / / spyi'i mtshan nyid ni tha dad pa la ltos pa'i phyir ro /
sāmānyalakṣaṇasya / / atha vā viśuddhyartham ālambanaṃ viśuddhyālambanaṃ na bhāvasvalakṣaṇam / ālambyamānaṃ viśuddhim āvahati sarvasattvaviśuddhiprasaṅgāt / / yadyanyānanyatvenāvaktavyā kathaṃ nirgranthavādo nā'lambito bhavati ? / yo hi bhāvasya satastattvānyatvena vyākaroti tena nirgranthavād / ālambyate / / śūnyatā tu na bhāva iti nāstyayaṃ doṣaḥ /
# yang na rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir dmigs pa ni rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa'o / / dngos po ni rang gi mtshan nyid la dmigs pas rnam par dag pa thob pa med de / / sems can thams cad rnam par dag par thal bar 'gyur ro / / gal te gzhan dang gzhan ma yin par mi brjod na / / gcer bu ba smra ba la 'chel bar de ltar mi 'gyur / / dngos po yod pa la de nyid dam gzhan du lung mi ston pa gang yin pa de gcer bu pa'i smra ba la 'chel bar 'gyur ro / / stong pa nyid ni dngos po med pas skyon du 'gyur ba 'di med do /
etena śūnyatā sallakṣanā'bhāvasvarūpalakṣaṇā'dvayalakṣaṇā
# de ltar stong pa nyid 'di ni med pa'i mtshan nyid dang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid dang mi gnyis pa'i mtshan nyid de /
tattvānyatva vinirmuktalakṣaṇā ca paridīpitā /
# de nyid dang gzhan las rnam par grol ba'i mtshan nyid yongs su bstan pa yin no /
uktaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ //1-14// / paryāya idānīm ucyate - / tathatā bhūtakoṭiścā'nimittaṃ paramārthatā / / dharmadhātuś ca paryāyāḥ śūnyatāyāḥ samāsataḥ // iti /
# stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid bshad zin to / / de ni rnam grangs brjod par bya'o / / stong pa nyid ni mdor bsdu na / / de bzhin nyid dang yang dag mtha' / / mtshan ma med dang don dam dang /
paryāyo nāmaikasyārthasya bhinnaśabdaiḥ pratyāyanaṃ / paryāyārthābhidhānam iti paryāya ucyate /
# chos kyi dbyings ni rnam grangs so / / zhes bya ba la / / rnam grangs zhes bya ba ni don gcig la sgra tha dad par grag pa ste rnam grangs kyi don brjod pas rnam grangs zhes bya'o /
tānyabhidhānāni sūtrāntareṣu śūnyataiva nirdiśyante /
# brjod pa de rnams ni mdo gzhan dag las stong pa nyid du ston to /
etac ca paryāyapañcakaṃ yathāpradhānaṃ gāthāyām uktam evam anye'pi / paryāyā ihānuktāḥ pravacanād upadhāryāḥ / [p.39]
