# rnam grangs lnga po de dag gtso bo yin par tshigs su bcad pa las ji skad smos pa de bzhin du rnam grangs gzhan 'dir ma smos te / / gsung rab las khong du chud par bya ba ni 'di lta ste /
tad yathā - advayatā avikalpadhātuḥ dharmatā anabhilapyatā anirodhaḥ / asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇādi //1-15// / kathaṃ paryāyārtho vijñeya ityetad darśayati / / naite śabdā gauṇāḥ kiṃ tarhi anvarthā iti -
# mi gnyis pa nyid dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i dbyings dang chos nyid dang brjod du med pa nyid dang mi 'gag pa nyid dang 'dus ma byas pa dang mya ngan las 'das pa la sogs pa'o / / rnam grangs kyi don ji ltar shes par bya zhe na / / de ston te sgra de dag ni brtags pa ma yin gyi / / don dang ldan pa rnams zhes bya ste /
ananyathā'viparyāsatan nirodhāryagocaraiḥ /
# gzhan min phyin ci log ma yin / / de 'gag 'phags pa'i spyod yul dang /
hetutvāccāryadharmāṇāṃ paryāyārtho yathākramaṃ // iti /
# 'phags pa'i chos kyi rgyu yi phyir / / rnam grangs don de go rims bzhin / / zhes bya'o /
ananyathā'rthena tathateti avikārārthenetyarthaḥ / / tadeva pradarśanārtham āha nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā / / nityaṃ sarvadā'saṃskṛtatvān na vikriyata ityarthaḥ / / aviparyāsārthena bhūtakoṭiḥ / / bhūtaṃ satyam aviparītam ityarthaḥ / / koṭiḥ paryanto yataḥ pareṇānyajjñeyaṃ nāstītyato bhūtakoṭir / bhūtaparyanta ucyate / / kathaṃ tathatā jñeyam ucyate ?
# de la gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir de bzhin nyid de zhes bya ba ni mi 'gyur ba'i don to zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de nyid bstan pa'i phyir rtag tu de bzhin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te / / rtag par dus thams cad 'dus ma byas pa yin pas mi 'gyur zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / phyin ci log ma yin pa'i phyir yang dag pa'i mtha' ste zhes bya ba la yang dag pa ni bden pa dang ma nor ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / mtha' zhes bya ba ni mu med pa ste / / gang phan chad nas shes par bya ba gzhan med pa'i phyir yang dag pa'i mtha' ste / / yang dag pa'i mu zhes bya'o / / ji ltar de bzhin nyid shes par bya ba mu zhes bya zhe na /
jñeyāvaraṇaviśodhanajñānagocaratvāt /
# shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
aviparyāsārthentyanadhyāropānapavādārthena /
# phyin ci log ma yin pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni / / sgro 'dogs pa dang skur ba 'debs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - viparyāsā'vastutvād iti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa phyin ci log gi gzhi ma yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste /
viparyāso hi vikalpaḥ /
# phyin ci log ni rnam par rtog pa'o /
vikalpā'nālambanatvān na viparyāsavastu /
# rnam par rtog pa'i dmigs pa ma yin pas phyin ci ma log pa'o /
nimittanirodhārthenā'nimittam iti /
# mtshan ma 'gog pa'i phyir mtshan ma med pa ste zhes bya ba ni /
atrā'nimittatvaṃ nimittanirodha ucyate /
# 'dir mtshan ma med pa la mtshan ma 'gog pa zhes bya ba'o /
etad eva pradarśanārtham āha - / sarvanimittābhāvād iti /
# 'dir rab tu bstan pa'i phyir mtshan ma thams cad med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
sarvair eva saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtanimittaiḥ śūnyatā śūnyety animittam ucyate / / sarvanimittā'bhāvād animittaḥ / / animittam evā'nimittaḥ /
# 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi mtshan ma thams cad kyi stong pa nyid stong pas mtshan ma med pa zhes bya'o / / mtshan ma thams cad med pa'i phyir mtshan ma med pa ste / / mtshan ma med pa nyid mtshan ma med pa'o /
āryajñānagocaratvāt paramārtha iti paramaṃ hi lokottarajñānaṃ / / tad arthaḥ paramārthaḥ / / etad eva pradarśayann āha - paramajñānagocaratvād iti / / āryadharmahetutvād dharmadhātuḥ /
# 'phags pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul yin pas don dam pa ste zhes bya ba la / / dam pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes te / / de'i don ni don dam pa'o / / 'phags pa'i chos kyi rgyu yin pas chos kyi dbyings te zhes bya ba la / / chos kyi sgra ni 'dir 'phags pa'i chos rnams te /
dharmaśabdenātrāryadharmāḥ samyag dṛṣṭyādayaḥ samyag / vimuktijñānaparyantāśceti /
# yang dag par lta ba la sogs pa dang yang dag par rnam par grol ba dang ye shes la thug pa rnams la bya ste /
taddhetutvād dhātuḥ /
# de dag gi rgyu yin pas dbyings so /
tadeva vibhāvayann āha - āryadharmāṇāṃ tad ālambanaprabhatvād iti /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir 'phags pa'i chos rnams ni de la dmigs pas byung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
svalakṣaṇopādāyarūpadhāraṇe'py ayaṃ dhātuśabdo vartata ity āha / hetvartho hy atra dhātvarthaḥ / / tadyathā [p.40] / suvarṇadhātus tāmradhātū raupyadhātuḥ /
# rang gi mtshan nyid dang rgyur byas pa'i gzugs 'dzin pa la yang khams kyi sgra 'di 'jug pa de'i phyir / / 'dir dbyings kyi don ni rgyu'i don to zhes bya ba smos te / / dper na gser khung dang zangs khung bzhin no /
sūtrāntareṣv anye paryāyā uktā apyanenaiva nyāyena svārthe / nirdeṣṭavyāḥ //1-16//
# mdo gzhan las rnam grangs gsungs pa gzhan dag kyang 'di'i tshul du don bdag gis brtag par bya'o /
śūnyatāyā grāhyagrāhakābhāvarūpatvād bhedam asambhāvayan pṛcchati
# stong pa nyid ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa'i ngo bo yin pas tha dad pa mi srid de /
athavā paryāyārthānantaraṃ bhedo vijñeya ity uktam atas
# 'dri ba'am yang na rnam grangs kyi don gyi 'og tu dbye ba shes par bya bar bstan pas /
tannirdeśānantaraṃ pṛcchati - kathaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ prabhedo vijñeya iti /
# de'i phyir de bshad pa'i 'og tu stong pa nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba ji ltar shes par bya zhe na zhes dris so /
abhūtaparikalpo hi saṃkleśaḥ tasya prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir ucyate /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'o / / de spangs na rnam par dag pa zhes bya ste /
saṅkleśaviśuddhikāle ca śūnyatāvyatiriktam anyan nāsti yat saṅkliśyate / viśuddhyate vā /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa'i dus na yang stong pa nyid ma rtogs par gang kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba'am / / rnam par byang bar 'gyur ba gzhan med do /
tasmāt saṃkleśaviśuddhikālayoḥ śūnyataiva saṅkliśyate viśuddhyate ceti / pradarśanārtham āha - / saṅkliṣṭā ca viśuddhā ca / ity asyāḥ prabhedaḥ / / kadā saṅkliṣṭā kadā nirmaletyanavabodhāt pṛcchati - kasyām / avasthāyāṃ saṃkliṣṭā kasyāṃ ca viśuddheti - / samalā nirmalā ca sā / / iti vistaraḥ /
# de lta bas na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa gnyis kyi dus na yang / / stong pa nyid kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa'o zhes rab tu bstan pa'i phyir ro / / kun nas nyon mongs rnam par dang / / ces bya ba ste / / de'i rab tu dbye'o zhes bya ba smos so / / gang gi tshe nyon mongs la / / gang gi tshe dri ma med pa khong du ma chud nas / / gang gi tshe kun nas nyon mongs la / / gang gi tshe rnam par dag ce na zhes dris pa dang de ni dris bcas dri ma med /
āśrayā'parāvṛttiparāvṛttyapekṣayā samalā ca prahīṇamalā ca / vyavasthāpyate /
# ces rgya cher ro / / gnas gyur pa dang ma gyur pa la ltos pas / / dri ma dang bcas pa dang dri ma spangs par rnam par gzhag go /
yeṣām aviduṣāṃ grāhyagrāhakā'bhiniveśarāgādikleśamalinānāṃ / cittasantānānām apratipatti-vipratipatti-doṣācchūnyatā na prakhyāti / tān prati samalā [p.41] / vyavasthāpyate /
# ma rtogs pa dang log par rtogs pa'i nyes pas mi mkhas pa gang dag gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen cing / / 'dod chags la sogs pa'i nyon mongs pas sems kyi rgyud dri ma can du gyur pa la / / stong pa nyid mi snang ba de dag dri ma dang bcas pa'o zhes rnam par gzhag go /
yeṣām āryāṇāṃ tattvajñānād aviparītacetasāṃ śūnyatā nirantaram / ākāśavad virajaskā prakhyāti tān prati prahīṇamaletyucyate /
# 'phags pa gang dag de kho na mkhyen pas phyin ci log gi sems med pa la stong pa nyid nam mkha' ltar rdul med pa ste rgyun mi 'chad par snang ba de dag ni dri ma spangs pa zhes bya'o /
evaṃ śūnyatāyā āpekṣikā saṃkleśaviśuddhir draṣṭavyā na
# de ltar stong pa nyid ni nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa la ltos pa can yin par blta ste /
malinasvarūpatvena prakṛtyā prabhāsvaratvāt /
# rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i phyir ngo bo nyid dri ma can du ni ma yin no /
yadi samalā bhūtveti vistaraḥ /
# gal te dri ma dang bcas par gyur la zhes bya ba rgya cher 'byung ba ni /
na hy avasthābhedo vikāram antareṇa dṛṣṭaḥ / / vikāraścotpādavināśābhyām anusyūta iti /
# 'gyur ba med par gnas skabs tha dad pa ma mthong la / / 'gyur ba ni skye ba dang 'jig pa dang rjes su 'brel ba ste /
ata āha - kathaṃ vikāradharmiṇītvādanityā na bhavatīti /
# de'i phyir 'gyur ba'i chos can yin pas ji ltar mi rtag par mi 'gyur zhe na zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
na hi saṅkliṣṭāvasthātaḥ śūnyatāviśuddhā'vasthāyām anyo vikāraḥ / / tattvastititā tu svabhāvāntaram anāpadyamānāyā āgantukamalāpagamāt / yasmād - / abdhātukanakākāśaśuddhivac chuddhir iṣyate /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa'i gnas skabs las stong pa nyid rnam par dag pa'i gnas skabs su 'gyur ba gzhan med kyi / / de kho na nyid du gnas par rang bzhin gzhan du 'gyur ba med pa ste / / glo bur gyi dri ma dang bral pa'i phyir 'di ltar / / chu khams gser dang nam mkha' rnams / / dag pa bzhin du dag par 'dod /
tasmād anityā na bhavatīti / / yathaiva hy abdhātukanakākāśānām atatsvabhāvatvān / malasvabhāvatā'bhāve'pyāgantukamalavattvaṃ / / āgantukamalā'pagame ca te viśuddhā eva / svabhāvāntarapratipattimantareṇāpi / / evaṃ śūnyatāpy āgantukamalaiḥ saṅkliśyate, avikṛtasvarūpāpi tad / vigamāc ca viśuddhyatīti /
# de'i phyir mi rtag par mi 'gyur ro / / dper na chu'i khams dang gser dang nam mkha' rnams de'i rang bzhin ma yin pa'i phyir / / dri ma'i ngo bo nyid yin par ma gyur kyang / / glo bur gyi dri mas dri ma can kho na dang glo bur gyi dri ma dang bral na yang rang bzhin gzhan du 'gyur ba med bzhin du rnam par dag pa nyid do / / de bzhin du stong pa'i glo bur gyi dri ma rnams kyis kun nas nyon mongs par gyur yang / / 'gyur pa med pa'i ngo bo yin la / / de dang bral na rnam par dag pa zhes bya'o /
yo hi tameva bhāvaṃ pūrvaṃ saṅkleśalakṣaṇaṃ paścād viśuddhisvabhāvaṃ
# dngos po de nyid sngar kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid dang phyis rnam par dag pa'i rang bzhin du gang rnam par 'jog pa de ni /
vyavasthāpayati tasya vikāradharmanivṛttir na bhavati / vikārasvabhāvatvāt na tu yatrāpy āgantukaṃ tad ubhayaṃ / / tasmān nāsau vikāradharmatāṃ spṛśatīti //1-17// [p.42]
# rang bzhin gzhan du gyur bas 'gyur ba'i chos bzlog par ma gyur gyi / / gang la de gnyi ga yang glo bur yin pa la ni ma yin te / / de lta bas na de 'gyur ba'i chos nyid la reg pa med do /
prabhedanirdeśādhikāre sarve śūnyatāprabhedā vaktavyā ityata āha
# rab tu dbye ba'i skabs yin pas stong pa nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba thams cad brjod dgos te /
-ayam aparaḥ prabheda iti / / ṣoḍaśavidhā śūnyateti vastubhedena ṣoḍaśavidhā bhavati /
# de'i phyir gzhan yang rab tu dbye ba ni stong pa nyid rnam pa bcu drug po 'di lta ste zhes bya ba smos so / / dngos po tha dad pas rnam pa bcu drug tu 'gyur te /
dvayābhāvasvarūpe tu bhedo nāsti /
# gnyis kyi dngos po med pa'i rang gi ngo bo la ni tha dad pa med do /
sā ṣoḍaśavidhā śūnyatā prajñāpāramitāyāṃ paṭhyate - / adhyātmaśūnyatā yāvad abhāvasvabhāvaśūnyateti / / saiṣā samāsato veditavyā -
# nang stong pa nyid ces bya ba nas dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bya ba'i bar du stong pa nyid rnam pa bcu drug po de ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las byung ngo /
bhoktṛbhojanatad dehapratiṣṭhāvastuśūnyatā / / ityevam ādi / / sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sarvadharmasyā'dvayasvarūpatvaṃ /
# de yang mdor bsdu ba zhes bya bar rig par bya'o / / za ba bza' dang de yi lus / / gnas kyi gzhi yi stong pa nyid / / ces bya ba la sogs pa la / / chos thams cad gnyis med pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi phyir stong pa nyid ni spyi'i mtshan nyid do /
nānyathā tan nānātvaṃ śakyate darśayitum ityato vastunānātvena tan / nānātvaṃ darśayati /
# gzhan du na de ni tha dad par bstan par mi nus te / / de'i phyir gzhi tha dad pas de tha dad par ston to /
pūrvaṃ tāvad bhoktā vibhāvayitavyaḥ tat snehābhiniveśatyājanārthaṃ /
# gzhan du na de ni tha dad par bstan par mi nus so / / de la chags pa dang mngon par zhen pa de spangs pa'i phyir /
tat snehābhiniveśo hi buddhatvavimokṣaprāptipratibandhako bhavati /
# thog mar zab gzhig par bya'o / / de la chags pa dang mngon par zhen pa de ni sangs rgyas su 'grub pa dang rnam par thar pa thob pa'i bgegs su gyur pa'o /
tad anantaraṃ tad bhojanaṃ / / tad anantaraṃ tayor adhiṣṭhānaṃ śarīraṃ / / tad anantaraṃ tad adhiṣṭhānasya śarīrasya pratiṣṭhābhājanaloko
# de'i 'og tu de'i bza' ba'o / / de'i 'og tu de gnyis kyi gnas te lus so / / de'i 'og tu za ba la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir /
vibhāvayitavyaḥ bhoktur upakārakatvād / ātmīyasnehagrāhavyāvartanārthaṃ / / etac catur vidhaṃ vastu tac chūnyatā vastuśūnyatety ucyate /
# bdag gir chags pa dang 'dzin pa bzlog pa'i phyir / / de'i gnas te lus kyi rten snod kyi 'jig rten gzhig par bya'o / / gzhi rnam pa bzhi po 'di'i stong pa nyid de ni gzhi stong pa nyid ces bya'o /
tatra bhoktṛśūnyatā ādhyātmikānyāyatanāny ārabhyeti /
# de la za ba stong pa nyid ni nang gi skye mched rnams las brtsams so zhes bya ba ni /
tāni ca cakṣūrādīni yāvan manaḥ paryantāni /
# de dag kyang mig la sogs pa nas yid la thug pa'i bar du'o /
tad anyasya bhoktur abhāvāt / / cakṣūrādīnāñca viṣayopabhogapravṛttidarśanāl lokasya cakṣurādiṣt eva / bhoktṛbhimāna ity ataścakṣūrādyāyatanaśūnyatā bhoktṛśūnyatety ucyate /
# za ba de las gzhan med pas mig la sogs pa yul la nye bar spyod par 'jug par mthong nas mig la sogs pa nyid kyis za bar 'jig rten mngon pa'i nga rgyal byed pas de'i phyir / / mig la sogs pa'i skye mched stong pa nyid la za ba stong pa nyid ces bshad do /
bhojanaśūnyatā bāhyānīti rūpādīni yāvat dharmaparyantāni /
# bza' ba stong pa nyid ni phyi rol gyi rnams so zhes bya ba la / / gzugs la sogs pa nas chos la thug pa'i bar du'o /
tāni viṣayābhāvena bhujyanta iti bhojanam ato bāhyāyatanaśūnyatā / bhojanaśūnyatety ucyate / [p.43] / tayor bhoktṛbhojanayoḥ śarīre parasparā'vinibhāgenā'vasthānāt tad / dehaḥ śarīram ityatas tacchūnyatā'dhyātmabahirdhāśūnyatety ucyate /
# de dag la yul gyi dngos por bza' bar bya bas na bza' ba ste / / de'i phyir phyi rol gyi skye mched stong pa nyid ni bza' ba stong pa nyid ces bshad do / / za ba dang bza' ba de gnyis ni lus dang phan tshun tha dad du mi 'jug par gnas / / de'i lus ni khog pa'o zhes bya ste / / de bas na de'i stong pa nyid ces bya'o /
pratiṣṭhāvastu bhājanalokaḥ sarvatra sattvānāṃ pratiṣṭhāvastutvena / prajānāt /
# gnas kyi gzhi ni snod kyi 'jig rten te / / thams cad du sems can rnams kyi gnas kyi gzhi rab tu 'dogs pas /
ata evāha - tasya vistīrṇatvāt tacchūnyatā mahāśūnyatocyate iti /
# de nyid kyi phyir de rgya che ba'i phyir de stong pa nyid ni chen po stong pa nyid ces bya'o zhes bya ba smos so /
vastuśabdaḥ pratyekam abhisambadhyate /
# gzhi'i sgra ni re re dang yang sbyar bar bya'o /
tasyaivaṃ yogino bodhisattvasya caturvidhajñeyavastuśūnyatāyāṃ
# de ltar shes bya'i dngos po rnams gzhi'i stong pa nyid la rtog pa dang bcas pa'i tshul bzhin yid la byed pas yid la byed pa na /
savitarkeṇa yoniśomanaskāreṇa manaskriyamāṇāyām ayamanyo nimittagrāha
# byang chub sems dpa' rnal 'byor ba de la mtshan mar 'dzin pa gzhan 'di nye bar gnas par 'gyur ro /
upatiṣṭhate yenedaṃ śūnyatājñānenādhyātmikabāhyāyatanādi śūnyaṃ / dṛṣṭaṃ tatra yo grāhyagrāhakābhiniśeśo'yam eva cātra paramārthākāro / yathā tac chrutājñānena dṛṣṭam iti vikalpaḥ / / tasya dviprakārasya yogibhūmibhrāntinimittasya vikalpasya / vibhāvanārthaṃ śūnyta śūnyata paramārtha śūnyatā ca yathākramaṃ / jñanakāralopaṃ kṛutvā nirdiṣṭā / / śūnyathāviṣayatvād vā taj jñānaṃ śūnyatety uktaṃ /
# stong pa nyid shes bya gang gis nang dang phyi'i skye mched la sogs pa 'di stong par mthong ba de la / / gang gzung ba dang 'dzin par mngon par zhen pa dang ji ltar de'i stong pa nyid shes pas mthong ba 'di nyid kyang 'dir don dam pa'i rnam pa'o snyam du rnam par rtog pa la rnal 'byor gyi sa'i 'khrul pa'i mtshan ma'i rnam par rtog pa rnam pa de gnyis gzhig pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dang don dam pa stong pa nyid de go rims bzhin no / / shes pa dang rnam pa ni ma smos par byas te bshad do / / yang na stong pa nyid yul yin pas shes pa dang stong pa zhes bshad pa yin no /
tasya grāhyagrāhakabhāvena śūnyatā śūnyatāśūnyatā / / ādhyātmikāayatanādikaṃ ca tena śūnyatājñānena yathā dṛṣṭaṃ so'tra
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos pos de stong pa nyid ni stong pa nyid do / / nang gi skye mched la sogs pa yang stong pa nyid shes pa des ji ltar mthong ba de /
paramārtha iti paramārthākāreṇa tasya śūnyatā paramārthaśūnyatā / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ? / paramārtho hi śūnyaḥ parikalpitena svabhāveneti /
# 'dir don dam pa'o snyam pa'i rnam pa des stong pa nyid ni don dam pa stong pa nyid do / / ci'i phyir zhe na / / stong pa nyid ni don dam pa ste kun brtags pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong pa zhes bya'o /
ayam anyo'pi nimittagrāhaḥ śūnyatābhāvanopaplavabhūtaḥ yadarthaṃ
# mtshan mar 'dzin pa gzhan 'di ni stong pa nyid bsgom pa'i nyes par gyur pa ste /
bodhisattvaḥ śūnyatāṃ pratipadyate tasya bhāvasvarūpatvaṃ samāropayati
# gang gi phyir byang chub sems dpa' stong pa nyid sgrub pa de yang dngos po'i ngo bor sgro btags pa ste /
tad vibhāvanārthaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatādayaḥ sarvadharmaśūnyatāparyantāḥ / śūnyatā nirdiṣṭāḥ //1-18// [p.44]
# de gzhig pa'i phyir 'dus byas stong pa nyid ces bya ba nas chos thams cad stong pa nyid ces bya ba la thug pa'i bar gyi stong pa nyid bshad do /
kim arthañca pratipadyate -
# ci'i phyir sgrub par byed ce na /
śubhadvayasya prāptyarthaṃ / yāvad buddhadharmāṇāṃ viśūddhyarthaṃ śūnyatāṃ pratipadyate śūnyatāṃ / prabhāvayatītyarthaḥ / / śubhadvayaṃ hi saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtañca mārgo nirvāṇañca / / tābhyāṃ sambadhyate yathākramaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatā'saṃskṛtaśūnyatā ca / / sadāsattvahitāya ca / / iti sarvākāraṃ sarvakālañca mayā sattvahitaṃ kartavyam iti tac / chūnyatā'tyantaśūnyatā / / saṃsārā'tyajanārthañca / iti sattvārthaṃ mayā saṃsāro na parityajyaḥ / / saṃsāre hi parityakte'labdhvā bodhisattvabodhi śrāvakabodhau / vyavatiṣṭhate / / tasya śūnyatā anavarāgraśūnyatā / / kim arthaṃ punas tasya śūnyatā deśyata ity ata āha - anavarāgrasya hi / saṃsārasya śūnyatām apaśYan khinnaḥ saṃsāraṃ parityajeteti / / kuśalasyā'kṣayāya ca // iti / / mayā kuśalamūlāni na kṣīyante nirupādhiśeṣe nirvāṇe'pīti / nāvakiratītyetad evācaṣṭe notsṛjatīti / / yadyevaṃ kathaṃ tarhi nirupadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhātuḥ siddhyati ? / sāsravadharmavipākakāyābhāvāt / / anāsravabhūtadharmakāyasya tu buddhasya bhagavato nirupadhiśeṣe / nirvāṇadhātāv api na vyuparamād iti siddhāntaḥ / / atas tac chūnyatā anavakāraśunyatety ucyate //1-19// [p.45] / gotrasya ca viśuddhyarthaṃ tasya śūnyatā prakṛtiśūnyatā / / atraiva kāraṇamāha - gotraṃ hi prakṛtir iti / / kuta etat / / ata āha - svābhāvikatvād iti / / svabhāvikam anādikālikam anāgantukam ityarthaḥ / / yathā'nādau saṃsāre kiṇcic cetanaṃ kiñcid acetanam evam ihāpi kiñcit / ṣaḍāyatanaṃ buddhagotraṃ kiñcic chrāvakādigotram iti / / na cākasmikatvaṃ gotrasya anādiparamparāgatatvāt cetanācetanaviśeṣavad  iti / / sarvasattvasya tathāgatagotratvād atra gotram iti tathātvaṃ jñeyam ity / anye / / lakṣaṇavyañjanāptaye / / ity ataḥ sānuvyañjanānāṃ mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇānāṃ śūnyatā / lakṣaṇaśūnyatety ucyate / / kiñca - / śuddhaye buddhadharmāṇāṃ bodhisattvaḥ prapadyate // / ante prapadyata ity abhidhānāt sarvatra śubhadvayasya prāptyarthaṃ / bodhisattvaḥ prapadyate / / sadā sattvahitāya ca bodhisattvaḥ prapadyata iti yojyaṃ / / katareṣāṃ buddhadharmāṇām ity ato bravīti balavaiśāradyāveṇikādīnām  iti / / saṃkṣepataḥ sarvabuddhadharmāṇāṃ prāptaye mayā prayatitavyam iti / pratipadyate / / tasmā chūnyatāvibhāvanayā sarvadharmaśūnyatocyate / / kīdṛśī vibhāvaneti ? / jñeye jñānasyāvyāvahitapravṛttiḥ / / evaṃ tāvac caturdaśānānām adhyātmaśūnyatādīnāṃ / sarvadharmaśūnyatāparyantānāṃ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ //1-20// [p.46] / kā punar atra bhoktrādau śūnyatā katamat svarūpam ityata āha - / pudgalasyā'tha dharmāṇām abhāvaḥ śūnyatā'tra hi / / tad abhāvasya sadbhāvastasmin sā śūnyatā'aparā // iti / / tatra yathoktānāṃ bhoktrādīnāṃ pudgaladharmā'bhāvaś ca śūnyatā / / tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvaḥ śūnyatā / / tatra pudgaladharmayor asadbhāvo'bhāvaśūnyatā / / tad abhāvasya sadbhāvo'bhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā / / kim arthaṃ punar eṣā dvividhā śūnyatā'nte vyavasthāpyate ? / ata āha - śūnyatālakṣaṇakhyāpanārtham iti / / kim arthaṃ punaḥ śūnyatākhyāpanamata āha - pudgaladharmasamāropasya tac / chūnyatā'pavādasya ca parihārārthaṃ yathākramaṃ / / pudgaladharmasamāropasya parihārārtham abhāvaśūnyatāṃ vyavasthāpayati / tac chūnyatā'pavādaparihārārthañcā'bhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatāṃ / / yady abhāvaśūnyatā nocyeta parikalpitasvarūpayor dharmapudgalayor / astitvam eva prasajyeta / / yady abhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā nocyeta śūnyatāyā abhāva eva prasajyeta /
# dge ba gnyis thob par bya ba'i phyir zhes bya ba nas / / sangs rgyas chos rnams dag bya'i phyir / / zhes bya ba'i bar dag gis stong pa nyid la sgrub par byed de / / stong pa nyid bsgom mo zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / dge ba ni 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas te lam dang mya ngan las 'das pa'o / / de gnyis ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid dang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid dang go rims bzhin du sbyar ro / / rtag tu sems can phan bya'i phyir / / zhes bya ba la / / rnam pa thams cad du rtag par bdag gis sems can la phan par bya'o snyam pa de'i stong pa nyid ni mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do / / 'khor ba mi gtang bya ba'i phyir / / zhes bya ba ni sems can gyi don du bdag gis 'khor ba yongs su gtang bar mi bya ste / / 'khor ba yongs su btang na byang chub ma rnyed par / / nyan thos kyi sar gnas par 'gyur bas / / de'i stong pa nyid ni thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid do / / ci'i phyir de'i stong pa nyid bshad ce na / / de'i phyir 'khor ba thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid du ma mthong na skyo ste / / 'khor ba yongs su gtong ngo zhes bya ba smos so / / dge ba mi zad bya ba'i phyir / / zhes bya ba ni / / phung po lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa na yang bdag gis dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams mi zad par bya'o snyam pa ste / / mi gtong zhes bya ba ni de mi 'dor bar bshad pa'o / / gal te de lta na ji ltar phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings grub par 'gyur zhe na / / zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos kyi rnam par smin pa'i lus ni med kyi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi zag pa med pa'i dngos po'i chos kyi sku ni phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings na yang rgyun chad par mi 'gyur ro zhes grub pa'i mtha' las 'byung ngo / / de'i phyir de'i stong pa nyid ni dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o / / rigs kyang rnam par dag bya'i phyir / / zhes bya ba la / / de'i stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid de / / de nyid kyi phyir rigs ni rang bzhin zhes bshad do / / 'di ji lta bu zhe na de'i phyir ngo bo nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / ngo bo nyid ni thog ma med pa'i dus can te / / glo bur du byung ba ma yin no zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / ji ltar thog ma med pa can gyi 'khor ba na la la ni sems dang bcas / / la la ni sems med pa de bzhin du 'dir yang skye mched drug po kha cig ni sangs rgyas kyi rigs / / kha cig ni nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs zhes bya'o / / rigs ni grog ma med pa nas gcig nas gcig tu 'ongs pas sems dang sems med pa'i bye brag bzhin te / / glo bur du byung ba ma yin no / / gzhan dag na re sems can thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yin pas / / 'dir rigs zhes bya ba ni de bzhin du shes par bya'o zhe'o / / mtshan dang dpe byad thob bya'i phyir / / zhes bya ba ni / / de'i phyir skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rnams dpe byad bzang po rnams dang bcas pa'i stong pa nyid ni mtshan nyid stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o / / gzhan yang / / sangs rgyas chos rnams dag bya'i phyir / / byang chub sems dpa' sgrub par byed / / sgrub par byed pa tha mar brjod / / dge gnyis thob par bya ba'i phyir / / byang chub sems dpa' sgrub par byed / / rtag tu sems can phan bya'i phyir / / byang chub sems dpa' sgrub par byed / / ces thams cad dang sbyar ro / / sangs rgyas kyi chos de gang dag yin zhe na / / de'i phyir stobs dang mi 'jigs pa dang ma 'dres pa la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba smos so / / mdor na sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad thob par bya ba'i phyir bdag gis 'bad par bya'o zhes sgrub par byed pas de'i phyir rnam par bsgom pa zhes bya ste / / de'i stong pa nyid ni chos thams cad stong pa nyid ces bya'o / / 'dir rnam par bsgom pa zhes bya ba ji lta bu zhen /
tad abhāvāc ca pudgaladharmayoḥ pūrvavad bhāvaḥ syāt / / tatrādhyātmikeṣvāyataneṣu vipākavijñānasvabhāveṣu bālānāṃ / bhoktṛsammateṣu bhoktṛpudgalasya kalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca cakṣurādīnām / abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo'dhyātmaśūnyatā / / bāhyeṣv āyataneṣu rūpādivijñapty ābhāsasvabhāveṣu bālānāṃ / bhogyasammateṣu bhojanasyātmīyasya parikalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca
# shes par bya ba la shes pa bar chad med par 'jug pa ste / / de ltar re zhig nang stong pa nyid la sogs pa nas / / chos thams cad stong pa nyid la thug gi bar du stong pa nyid bcu bzhi rnam par gzhag par shes par bya'o / / za ba po la sogs pa 'di la stong pa nyid gang yin / / ngo bo nyid ni ji lta bu zhe na / / de'i phyir / / gang zag dang ni chos rnams kyi / / dngos po med 'dir stong pa nyid / / de dngos po med pa'i dngos yod pa / / de la de nyid stong nyid gzhan /
rūpādīnām abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo bahirdhāśūnyatā / / tad dehe śarīre bhoktṛpudgalasya bālajanaparikalpitānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ / dehasya cā'bhāvas tad abhāvasya ca bhāvo'dhyātmabahirdhā śūnyatā / / bhājanaloke sattvalokā'bhāvas tat parikalpitasvarūpābhāvas tad / abhāvas tad abhāvasadbhāvaś ca mahāśūnyatā / / śūnyatājñāne paramārthakāre ca jñātur ākāragrahītṛpudgalasya / parikalpitalakṣaṇaśunyatā paramārthākārasya cā'bhāvas tad abhāvas tad / abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo yathākramaṃ śūnyatāśūnyatā paramārthaśūnyatā / ca / / yad arthaṃ bodhisattvaḥ pratipadyate teṣu saṃskṛtādiṣu / sarvabuddhadharmaparyanteṣu [p.47] / bodhisattvapratipattavyeṣu pudgalasya parikalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca dharmāṇām / abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo yathākramaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatā yāvat / sarvadharmaśūnyateti / / tathāhi nāsti saṃskṛtasya svāmī vā prayoktā vā pudgalo nāpi / saṃskṛtaṃ bālajanaparikalpitenātmanā / / saṃkṣepataḥ sarvavikalpagrāhapratipakṣārthaṃ / sarvasūtrāntābhisandhivyākaraṇārthaṃ caitā bodhisattvānāṃ śrāvakair / asādhāraṇāḥ ṣoḍaśaśūnyatā nirdiṣṭāḥ / / atra ca bhagavatā śūnyatāviṣayaḥ śūnyatāsvabhāvaḥ / śūnyatābhāvanāprayojanañca darśitaṃ / / tatra śūnyatāviṣayo bhoktrādyartho yāvat buddhadharmaparyantaḥ / / tat pradarśanaṃ punaḥ śūnyatāyāḥ sarvadharmavyāpakatvajñāpanārthaṃ / / śūnyatāsvabhāvo'bhāvasvabhāvo'bhāvabhāvasvabhāvaś ca / / śūnyatāsvabhāvapradarśanaṃ punar adhyāropāpavādapartipakṣeṇa / sarvadṛṣṭiniḥsaraṇātmakatvajñāpanārthaṃ / / śūnyatābhāvanāprayojanaṃ śubhadvayasya paraptyartham ityārabhya / buddhadharmāṇāṃ prāptaya iti paryantaṃ / / tat pradarśanaṃ punaḥ svaparātmano rūpadharmakāyasampat prakarṣaḥ / śūnyatābhāvanād eva prāpya iti pradarśanārtham iti / / evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ prabhedo vijñeya iti samalāvasthāyāṃ saṃkliṣṭā / nirmalāvasthāyāṃ viśuddhety
# zhes bya ba gsungs so / / de la ji skad de bshad pa'i zab po la sogs pa la gang zag dang chos kyi dngos po med pa ni stong pa nyid do / / dngos po med pa de'i dngos po yod pa yang stong pa nyid do / / da la gang zag dang chos dngos po med pa ni dngos po med pa stong pa nyid do / / dngos po med pa de'i dngos po yod pa ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do / / 'di dag gi nang nas stong pa nyid rnam pa gnyis ci'i phyir tha mar rnam par gzhag ce na / / de'i phyir stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid bstan pa'i phyir zhes bya ba smos so / / stong pa nyid bstan pa yang ci'i phyir zhe na / / de'i phyir gang zag dang chos su sgro 'dogs pa dang de'i stong pa nyid la skur pa 'debs pa bsal ba'i phyir go rims bzhin zhes bya ba smos te / / gang zag dang chos su sgro 'dogs pa bsal ba'i don du dngos po med pa stong pa nyid rnam par gzhag go / / de'i stong pa nyid la skur pa 'debs pa bsal ba'i phyir / / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do / / gal te dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ma brjod na / / kun brtags pa'i ngo bo chos dang gang zag gnyis yod par 'gyur ro / / gal te dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ma bshad na / / stong pa nyid kyi dngos po med par 'gyur ro / / de med na yang gang zag chos gnyis snga ma bzhin du dngos por 'gyur ro / / de la rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin nang gi skye mched byis pa rnams kyis za bar bsams pa rnams la / / za ba'i gang zag dang brtags pa'i mtshan nyid mig la sogs pa rnams med pa dang de'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po yod pa ni nang stong pa nyid do / / phyi'i skye mched gzugs la sogs pa rnam par rig pa snang ba'i ngo bo nyid byis pa rnams kyis spyad par bya bar bsams pa rnams la bdag gis za ba dang yongs su brtags pa'i mtshan nyid gzugs la sogs pa'i dngos po med pa dang de'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po yod pa ni phyir stong pa nyid do / / de'i lus te khog pa la za ba'i gang zag dang byis pa'i skye bos kun brtags pa'i gzugs la sogs pa dang lus kyi dngos po med pa dang de'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po yod pa ni phyi nang stong pa nyid do / / snad kyi 'jig rten la sems can gyi 'jig rten gyi dngos po med pa dang kun brtags pa de rang gi ngo bos dngos po med pa dang de'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po yod pa ni chen po stong pa nyid do / / stong pa nyid shes pa dang don dam pa'i rnam pa la yang / / shes pa po dang rnam pa 'dzin pa po'i gang zag dang kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid stong pa nyid shes pa dang don dam pa'i rnam pa'i dngos po med pa dang de'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po yod pa ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dang don dam pa stong pa nyid de go rims bzhin no / / de ni gang gi phyir byang chub sems dpa' sgrub par byed pa 'dus byas la sogs pa nas / / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la thug gi bar du byang chub sems dpa' bsgrub dgos pa rnams la / / gang zag dang kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid chos rnams kyi dngos po med pa dang de'i dngos po med pa'i dngos po yod pa ni 'dus pas stong pa nyid nas / / chos thams cad stong pa nyid ces bya ba'i bar du go rims bzhin te / / 'di ltar 'dus byas la bdag po'am sbyor ba po'i gang zag kyang med de / / 'dus byas kyang byis pa'i skye bos kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid du med do / / mdor bsdus na rnam par rtog pa'i 'dzin pa thams cad kyi gnyen po dang mdo sde'i dgongs pa thams cad lung bstan pa'i phyir / / nyan thos dang thun mong ma yin pa / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stong pa nyid bcu drug po 'di dag bshad do / / 'dir ni bcom ldan 'das kyis stong pa nyid kyi yul dang stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin dang stong pa nyid bsgom pa'i dgos pa yang rab tu bstan to / / de la stong pa nyid kyi yul ni za ba la sogs pa'i don nas sangs rgyas kyi chos la thug gi bar du'o / / de rab tu bstan pa yang stong pa nyid kyis chos thams cad la khyab par shes par byed pa'i phyir ro / / stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid dang dngos po med pa'i dngos po'i ngo bo nyid do / / stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin rab tu bstan pa yang sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i gnyen por lta ba thams cad las nges par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid du shes par byed pa'i phyir ro / / stong pa nyid bsgom pa'i dgos pa ni dge ba gnyis thob par bya ba nas brtsams te / / sangs rgyas kyi chos thob par bya ba'i bar du'o / / de bstan pa yang bdag dang gzhan gyi gzugs dang chos kyi sku phun sum tshogs pa'i mchog ni stong pa nyid bsgom pa las 'thob po zhes rab tu bstan pa'i tha tshig go /
adhyātmaśūnyatādiṣoḍaśaprakārabhedo'nantarokto veditavyaḥ //1-21// / bhedoddeśānantaraṃ tat sādhanam uddiṣṭam ityatas tannirdeśānantaraṃ / pṛcchati - kathaṃ sādhanaṃ vijñeyam iti /
# de ltar stong pa nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba shes par bya'o zhes bya ba ni dri ma dang bcas pa'i dus na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang dri ma med pa'i dus na rnam par dag go zhes bya ba dang nang stong pa nyid la sogs pa bcu drug tu gyur pa'i dbye ba bshad ma thag pa'i rnam pa yin par shes par bya'o / / dbye ba smos pa'i 'og tu de sgrub pa smos pas dbye ba bshad pa'i 'og tu / / sgrub pa ji ltar shes par bya zhe na zhes dris so /
atra kiṃ sādhyate ?
# 'dir ci zhig pa sgrub par bya zhe na /
āgantukopakleśasaṃkliṣṭatā svabhāvaviśuddhatā ca /
# glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pas kun nas nyon mongs pa nyid dang rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa nyid do /
tatra saṃkliṣṭāsādham adhikṛtyāha - / saṃkliṣṭā ced bhaven nā'sau muktāssyuḥ sarvadehinaḥ / [p.48] / iti /
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa nyid bsgrub pa'i dbang du mdzad de / / gal te nyon mongs de ma gyur / / lus can thams cad grol bar 'gyur / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
muktiḥ saṃkleśaprahāṇaṃ /
# rnam par grol ba ni kun nas nyon mongs pa spangs pa'o /
tat saṃkleśaprahāṇāñca mārgabhāvanātaḥ /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa spangs pa de yang lam bsgoms pas so /
tatra yadi dharmāṇāṃ śūnyatā āgantukair upakleśair anutpanne'pi
# de la gal te gnyen po ma skyes par yang chos rnams kyi stong pa nyid glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyis zhes bya ba la /
pratipakṣe apiśabdād utpanna iva na saṃkliṣṭā bhaved evaṃ sati
# yang gi sgra ni skyes pa dang 'dra bar kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur na /
saṃkleśābhāvād ayatnata eva muktāḥ sarvasattvā bhaveyuḥ /
# de ltar gyur na ni kun nas nyon mongs pa med pas 'bad pa med par sems can thams cad grol bar 'gyur ro /
atyatnata eveti pratipakṣam antareṇaiva /
# 'bad pa med par zhes bya ba ni gnyen po med pa nyid du ste /
na tu pratipakṣam antareṇa prāṇinām asti mokṣa ity avaśyaṃ pṛthag
# gnyen po med par ni srog chags rnams thar pa med do / / de'i phyir so so'i skye bo'i dus na /
janāvasthāyāṃ tathātāyām āgantukair malaiḥ / saṃkliṣṭatā'bhyupagantavyeti /
# de bzhin nyid la glo bur gyi dri ma rnams kyis kun nas nyon mongs pa nyid du gdon mi za bar khas blang dgos te /
evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ saṃkliṣṭaḥ prabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati /
# de ltar stong pa nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba kun nas nyon mongs pa bsgrubs pa yin no /
idānīṃ viśuddhiprabhedaṃ sādhayann āha -
# da ni rab tu dbye ba rnam par dag pa sgrub pa'i phyir /
viśuddhā ced bhavennā'sau vyāyāmo niṣphalo bhavet / iti / / dehinām iti sambadhyate / / athotpanne'pi pratipakṣe apiśabdhād anutpanna iva na viśuddhā bhaved evaṃ / sati mokṣārtha ārambho niṣphalo bhavet pratipakṣabhāvanayāpi / tanmalasyā'vigamāt samalasya vimokṣānupapatteś ca / / na tu mokṣārtha ārambho niṣpahal iṣyate /
# gal te rnam dag de ma gyur / / 'bad pa 'bras bu med par 'gyur / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / lus can rnams dang sbyar bar bya'o / / ci ste gnyen po skyes kyang zhes bya ba la / / kyang gi sgra ni ma skyes pa dang 'dra bar rnam par dag par mi 'gyur na / / de ltar gyur na ni thar par bya ba'i phyir rtsom pa 'bras bu med par 'gyur te / / gnyen po bsgoms kyang dri ma de dang bral bar mi 'gyur ba dang dri ma dang bcas pa ni grol bar mi 'thad pa'i phyir ro / / thar par bya ba'i phyir 'bras bu med par mi 'dod pas /
tasmād avaśyaṃ pratipakṣābhyāsād āgantukopakleśavigamāc chūnyatāyā / viśuddhirabhyupagantavyeti /
# de'i phyir gnyen po goms par byas na / / glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang bral bas / / stong pa nyid kyi rnam par dag pa gdon mi za bar khas blang dgos te /
evaṃ śūnyatāyā viśūddhiprabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati /
# de ltar stong pa nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba rnam par dag pa bsgrubs pa yin no /
atra saṃkleśadharmopādānāt saṃkleśo viśuddhi dharmagrahaṇād viśuddhiḥ /
# 'dir kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos nye bar bzung bas kun nas nyon mongs pa la / / rnam par dag pa'i chos nye bar bzung ba rnam par dag gi /
na tu śūnyatāyā sākṣāt saṃkleśo viśuddhir veṣyate, / dharmaparatantratvādharmatāyāḥ / / ata evāḥ / muktāḥ syuḥ sarvadehinaḥ / iti /
# stong pa nyid la mngon du kun nas nyon mongs pa 'am / / rnam par dag par mi mi 'dod de / / chos nyid ni chos kyi kha na las pas / / de'i phyir / / lus can thams cad grol bar 'gyur /
ata hi dehina iti tadupādānamevoktaṃ /
# zhes gsungs te / / 'dir lus can zhes bya ba ni de'i rgyu nyid du bshad pa yin no /
anyathā vā yadi śūnyatāyāḥ sākṣāt samkleṣo viṣuddadirvā	 bhavet
# gzhan du na gal te stong pa nyid la mngon du kun nas nyon mongs pa'am / / rnam par dag par gyur du zin na ni /
tataḥ kaḥ sambandho dehibhir bhavedyena śūnyatāviśuddhiś ca dehināṃ / viśuddhiḥ śūnyatāsaṃkleśaś ca saṃkleśa ucyate ?  //1-22// [p.49]
# de'i phyir lus can rnams dang 'brel pa ci yod na / / 'di ltar stong pa nyid rnam par dag pas lus can rnams rnam par dag pa dang stong pa nyid kun nas nyon mongs pas kyang / / kun nas nyon mongs pa zhes bya /
yadā ca śūnyatā ca kliṣṭā pṛthagjanāvasthāyāṃ śuddhā / cāryāvasthāyāṃ bhavati ata evedaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati - / na kliṣṭā nāpi cā'kliṣṭā śuddhā'śuddhā na caiva sā / iti / / kathaṃ na kliṣṭā nā'pi cā'śuddhā / / śuddhaiva dvayaśuddhyā prakṛtagamakatvāt / / atraivāgamam āha prakṛtyaiva - / prabhāvasvaratvāc cittasya iti /
# gal te so so'i skye bo'i dus na / / stong pa nyid nyon mongs la / / 'phags pa'i dus na dag pa yin na ni / / de'i phyir / / nyon mongs ma yin mi mongs min; / / de ni dag dang ma dag min / / zhes bya ba 'di grub pa yin no / / ji ltar nyon mongs par gyur pa ma yin la ma dag pa yang ma yin zhe na / / dgag pa gnyis kyis skabs su khong du chud par byed pas dag pa nyid de / / 'dir lus dang sems rang bzhin gyis 'do gsal ba'i phyir ro zhes 'byung ngo /
atra ca cittadharmataiva cittaśabdenoktā cittasyaivaṃ lakṣaṇatvāt /
# 'dir ni sems kyi chos nyid la sems kyi sgar bshad de / / sems nyid ni dri ma'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir ro /
kathaṃ nā'kliṣṭā na viśuddhā kiṃ tarhi kliṣṭaiveti
# ji ltar nyon mongs par ma gyur pa ma yin pa yang ma yin la rnam par dag pa yang ma yin zhe na /
pratiṣedhadvayātpratipādayati / / sā -
# nyon mongs pa nyid yin par dgag pa gnyis kyis khong du chud par byed do /
kleśasyāgantukatvataḥ / / kliṣṭā na tu prakṛtyeti darśayati /
# de yang glo bur gyi nyon mongs pas nyon mongs pa yin gyi rang bzhin gyis ni ma yin zhes ston to /
sā cāgantukair upakleśair upakliśyata ity atrāpy āgamaḥ /
# de yang lung las glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyis nye bar nyon mongs so zhes 'byung ngo /
saṅkliṣṭaviśuddhatayā dvidhā bheda ukte kimarthaṃ punarścaturdhā bheda
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa gnyis su bye ste bshad na / / ci'i phyir dbye ba rnam pa bzhir bshad ce na /
ucyate ? / laukikāl lokottarāc ca mārgād viśeṣārtham ityekaḥ /
# kha cig na re 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam las khyad par du bstan pa'i phyir te /
laukiko hi mārgaḥ svabhūmikair malaiḥ kliṣṭo na tv adharaiḥ tat / pratipakṣatvāt /
# 'jig rten gyi lam ni rang gi sa'i dri ma rnams kyi nyon mongs kyi / / de'i gnyen po'i phyir 'og mas ni ma yin no /
lokottaras tu mārgo mṛdumadhyādibhedād aśuddho 'nāsravatvāt śuddhaḥ /
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam ni chung ngu dang 'bring po la sogs pa'i bye brag gis ni ma dag gi / / zag pa med pas ni dag pa ste /
naivaṃ śūnyateti /
# stong pa nyid ni de lta ma yin no zhe'o /
na kliṣṭety uktvā punaścakṣurādibhyo viśeṣārtham ucyate nāśuddhetyanye
# kun nas nyon mongs pa ma yin no zhes bshad pa la / / gzhan dag na re mig la sogs pa dang bye brag yod pas ma dag pa yin no /
cakṣurādayo hy anivṛttā'vyākṛtatvān na kliṣṭā na ca teṣāṃ sāravatvāt / prakṛtiviśuddhir ity aśuddheti /
# mig la sogs pa ni ma bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan pa yin pas nyon mongs pa ma yin la / / de dag gi zag pa dang bcas pas rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa ma yin pas / / ma dag pa yang ma yin zhes bshad do /
evaṃ na'pi sā kliṣṭeti cheduchyate - na ṣuddheti kuśalasāsravāt / viśeṣaṇārthamāḥ /
# de bzhin du nyon mongs pa med pa yang ma yin zhes bshad pa la / / dag pa ma yin no zhes bya ba ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i dge ba dang bye brag yod pa'i phyir te /
kuśalasāsravaṃ hi saṃsāraparyāpannatvān nā'kliṣṭaṃ /
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i dge ba ni 'khor bar gtogs pas nyon mongs pa med pa ma yin la /
iṣtavipākatvāc ca śuddhaṃ naiva dharmatā / / sā hi kliṣṭā'vasthāyām aśuddhaiveti /
# rnam par smin pa yid du 'ong bas dag pa ste / / chos nyid ni de lta ma yin no / / de ni nyon mongs pa'i dus na nyon mongs pa can yin la ma dag pa nyid ces bshad do /
evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ saṅkleśaviśuddhyoddiṣṭaḥ prabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati / [p.50]
# de ltar stong pa nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa bstan pa 'di bsgrubs pa yin no /
{ śūnyatāpiṇḍdārthaḥ }
# stong pa nyid kyi don bsdus pa ni /
śūnyatāpiṇḍdārtho lakṣaṇatāṃ vyavasthānataśceti veditavyaḥ / / tatra lakṣaṇato 'bhāvalakṣaṇato bhāvalakṣaṇataś ceti dvayābhāvo / hītivacanād abhāvalakṣaṇataḥ abhāvasya ca bhāva iti vacanād / bhāvalakṣaṇataḥ / / bhāvalakṣaṇataś ca na bhāvo nā'pi cā'bhāva iti vacanāt /
# mtshan nyid dang rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / de la mtshan nyid ni dngos po med pa'i mtshan nyid dang dngos po'i mtshan nyid do zhes bya ba la gnyis kyi dngos po med do zhes bshad pas dngos po med pa'i mtshan nyid do / / dngos po med pa'i dngos po zhes bshad pas dngos po'i mtshan nyid do / / dngos po'i mtshan nyid kyang yod pa ma yin med pa'ang ma yin zhes bshad pas /
bhāvābhāvavinirmuktalakṣaṇatas tattvānyatva vinirmuktalakṣaṇaś ceti / / etac ca śūnyatāyā lakṣaṇaṃ /
# dngos po yod pa dang dngos po med pa las rnam par grol ba'i mtshan nyid dang de nyid dang gzhan la rnam par grol ba'i mtshan nyid de 'di ni stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid do /
tasmād abhūtaparikalpān na pṛthaktvaikalakṣaṇam iti vacanāt /
# de bas na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa dang tha dad gcig pa'i mtshan nyid min zhes bshad do /
evaṃ lakṣaṇataḥ piṇḍārthaḥ /
# de ltar na mtshan nyid kyi don bsdus pa'o /
kathaṃ vyavasthānataḥ piṇḍdārtho veditavya ityta āha -
# rnam par gzhag pa'i don bsdus pa ji ltar gzhag par bya zhe na /
vyavasthānaṃ punaḥ paryāyādivyavasthānato veditavyaṃ /
# de'i phyir rnam par gzhag pa ni rnam grangs la sogs pa rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o zhes bya ba smos te /
paryāyatas tadarthas tadabhedas tat sādhanañcetyarthaḥ /
# rnam grangs dang de'i don dang de'i dbye ba dang de sgrub pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
etayā catuḥprakāradeśanayā caturvidhopakleśapratipakṣeṇa svalakṣaṇaṃ
# mtshan nyid la sogs pa rnam pa bzhi po 'di dag bstan pas nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnam pa bzhi'i gnyen por /
karmalakṣaṇaṃ saṅkleśavyavadānalakṣaṇaṃ yuktilakṣaṇañcodbhāvitaṃ bhavati
# rang gi mtshan nyid dang las kyi mtshan nyid dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid dang rigs pa'i mtshan nyid brjod pa yin no /
tatra svalakṣaṇaṃ vikalpasya pratipakṣeṇa tasya hi
# de la rnam par rtog ba'i gnyen por rang gi mtshan nyid de /
bhāvā'bhāvobhayapṛthaktvaikatvagrāhātmakatvatvāt /
# de ni dngos po dang dngos po med pa dang gnyi ga dang tha dad gcig pa nyid du 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid do /
karmalakṣaṇam anadhimuktānāṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇāśratyātrāsasya / pratipakṣeṇa / / abhrāntitathatā karmā'viparyāsakarma sarvanimittaprahāṇakarma / sarvalokottarajñānaviṣayatvā'vasthānakarma / pratilabdhāryadharmahetubhāvakarma ca / / evaṃ śūnyatāsvarūpakarmaśravaṇena prāptagrahāṇāṃ kusīdināṃ / kausīdyāpananārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ /
# stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid thos nas ma mos pa rnams kyis skrag par 'gyur ba de'i gnyen por las kyi mtshan nyid de / / ma nor bde bzhin nyid kyi las dang phyin ci ma log pa'i las dang mtshan ma thams cad spangs pa'i las dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes thams cad kyi yul nyid du gnas pa'i las dang dmigs pa na 'phags pa'i chos kyi rgyu'i dngos po'i las so / / de ltar stong pa nyid kyi rang gi ngo bo dang las thos pa tsam gyis chog par 'dzin pa le lo can rnams kyi le lo bsal ba'i phyir / / rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid do /
kathaṃ sā saṅkleśo bhavati vyavadānaṃ ceti saṃśayināṃ / saṃśayāpanayanārthaṃ yukti lakṣaṇaṃ // / // madhyāntavibhāgaśāstre lakṣaṇaparicchedasya prathamasya ṭīkā // / %	āvaraṇaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ / [p.51] / {tatra vyāpi kleśajñeyā''varaṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ sākalyāt / / prādeśikaṃ kleśā''varaṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāṃ / / udriktaṃ teṣām eva rāgādicaritānāṃ / / samaṃ samabhāgacaritānāṃ / / saṃsārā''dānatyāgā''varaṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāraṇaṃ / apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇā''varaṇāt /
# de ji ltar kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur rnam par dag par 'gyur snyam pa'i som nyi za ba rnams kyi the tshom bsal ba'i phyir rigs pa'i mtshan nyid do / / bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pas mtshan nyid kyi le'ur bcad pa ste dang por 'grel bshad do / / mtshan nyid bshad pa'i 'og tu sgrub pa bshad pa'i skabs yin te / / de'i 'og tu snos pas de'i phyir sgrib pa'i dbang du mdzad de zhes bya ba smos so / / khyab dang nyi tshe lhag pa dang / / mnyam pa dang len pa dang spong ba ni /
ity etad yathāyogam ubhayeṣām āvaraṇam ākhyātaṃ - / bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñca /
# gnyis kyi sgrib par bstan pa yin / / gnyis po dag gi sgrub pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can rnams dang nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can rnams kyi sgrib pa'o /
lakṣaṇanirdeśānantaram nāvaraṇanirdeśā'vasaraḥ, / tadanantaramuddiṣṭatvādityāha - āvaraṇamadhikṛtyāha / / vyāpi prādeśikodriktasamādānavivarjanam / / dvayāvaranamākhyātam / dvayāvaraṇam, bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñcāvaraṇam / / āvaraṇīyārthabhedenāvaraṇasya bhinnatvaṃ pradarśayitum ayaṃ śloka / ārabdhaḥ / / tatra vyāpi kleśajñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāṇām iti / / vyāpnotīti vyāpi, sakalārthāvaraṇāt / / sakalārtho hi svārthaḥ parārthaś ca / / athavā dvividhaṃ kleśaṃ jñeyaṃ cāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvasya / vyāpnotītyupacārād vyāpyucyate / / kleśa evāvaraṇamityāvaraṇasya kleśadharmatvena sārūpyādihopakleśo'pi / kleśaśabdena gṛhyate / / anyathā / navadhā kleśalakṣaṇaṃ / [p.52] / ityatrerṣyāmātsarye na gṛhyetām, tayorupakleśatvāt /
# bsgrib par bya ba'i don tha dad pas sgrib pa tha dad par rab tu bstan pa'i phyir le'u 'di brtsams so / / de la khyab pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa ste zhes bya ba ni khyab par byed pas khyab pa ste / / don mtha' dag la sgrib pa'i phyir ro / / don mtha' dag gi don dang gzhan gyi don to / / yang na nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam gnyis btags pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrib pa la khyab par byed pas khyab pa zhes bya'o / / nyon mongs pa nyid sgrib pas ni sgrib pa'o / / nyon mongs pa nyid kyi chos kho nar 'dra bas / / 'dir ni nye ba'i nyon mongs pa yang nyon mongs pa'i sgrar gzung ngo / / gzhan du na ni nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid rnam pa dgu zhes bya bar phrag dog dang ser sna gnyis gzung bar mi 'gyur te / / de gnyis nye ba'i nyon mongs pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
jñeya evāvaraṇam iti jñeyāvaraṇam / / tena jñeyaprāvṛtatvāj jñānasya viṣaya eva nāsti /
# shes bya ba la sgrib pas shes bya'i sgrib pa ste / / des shes bya rab tu bsgribs pas shes pa'i yul du mi 'gyur ro / / yang na shes bya la ye shes kyi sgrib pa yin te /
jñāne vā jñeyāvaraṇaṃ, jñeyasya jñānotpattipratibandhakatvād iti / jñeyāvaraṇamityatra madhyamapadalopo draṣṭavyaḥ / / tailapātram iva / / tatpunarakliṣṭamajñātam /
# shes spar bya ba la ye shes skye ba'i bgegs byed pa'i phyir ro / / shes bya dang sgrib pa'i bar gyi tshig ma smos par mar gyi bum pa bzhin no / / de yang nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa'o; / / byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can rnams kyis /
bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ asvaparārthasampatprakarṣalābhāya / buddhatvaprāptaye puṇyajñānasambhāraṃ sarvathā sarvatrā'nutiṣṭhatāṃ / tad dvayam api pratibandhakabhūtam / / ityatastadāvaraṇaṃ vyavasthāpyate bodhisattvagotrakāṇām / / tatra vyāpi sarvaviṣayaṃ sakalaṃ sarvathā vyāpnoti /
# bdag dang gzhan gyi don phun du byung ba thob pas sangs rgyas nyid thob par bya ba'i phyir bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs rnams pa thams cad kun la nan tan du bya ba de la gnyi ga yang bgegs su gyur bas de'i phyir de byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can rnams kyi sgrib par rnam par gzhag go / / de la khyab pa ni thams cad yul yin la mtha' dag ces bya ba ni rnam par thams cad la bya na /
kathaṃ sakalaṃ vyāpnotīti jñāyata iti cet - sākalyādāvaraṇaṃ / vyāpītyucyate iti hetunirdeśāt / / atha vā vyāpiśabdo niravaśeṣārtha iti pradarśanāya sākalyādivacanam /
# ji ltar mtha' dag gis khyab par shes par byed par 'gyur zhe na / / mtha' dag gi phyir de khyab pa'i sgrib par brjod de rgyur bstan pas 'gyur ro / / yang na khyab pa'i sgra ni ma lus pa'i don du bstan pa'i phyir mtha' dag gi phyir ro zhes smos so /
prādeśikaṃ kleśāvaraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām iti
# nyi tshe ba ni nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
svārthamātrāvaraṇādupacārādavyāpitvāc ca prādeśikākhyā /
# bdag gi don tsam la sgrib pas sgrib par btags pa dang khyab pa ma yin pa'i phyir nyi tshe ba zhes bya'o /
kiṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānām akliṣṭamajñānaṃ nāsti yasmāt teṣāṃ / kleśāvaraṇam eva vyavasthāpyata iti? / bhavatu, na tu tadāvaraṇaṃ teṣām, tasmin vidyamāne
# nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams la nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa med dam zhe na / / 'di ltar de dag la nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa nyid rnam par gzhag ce na / / yod mod kyi de ni de dag gi sgrib pa ma yin te /
śrāvakapratyekabuddhabodhiprāpteḥ /
# de yod bzhin du nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi byang chub 'thob pa'i phyir ro /
nanvajñānaṃ duḥkhādisatyaviṣaye jñānotpattipratibaṃdhakatvam eva / śrāvakādīnām /
# mi shes pa ni sdug bsngal la sogs pa'i bden pa'i yul la / / nyan thos la sogs pa'i shes pa skye ba'i bgegs su gyur pa yang ma yin nam /
tatas teṣām api dvayāvaraṇaṃ bhavet /
# de bas na de dag la yang sgrib pa gnyi ga yod par 'gyur ro /
tasmān na vaktavyaṃ kleśāvaraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām iti /
# de'i phyir nyan thos la sogs pa la ni nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa kho na'o zhes brjod par mi bya'o zhe na /
naitadevam, ajñānaṃ hi kleṣṭaṃ jñānapratipakṣabhūtaṃ saṃsāramūlaṃ ca
# de ni de lta ma yin te ma rig pa ni nyon mongs spar gyur pa dang rig pa'i mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur pa dang 'khor ba'i rtsa bar 'gyur ba'i phyir /
kleśṣāvaraṇameveti vyavasthāpyate, na tu jñeyāvaraṇaṃ, saṃśaya iva /
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa nyid du rnam par gzhag gi / / shes bya'i sgrib pa ni ma yin te / / so ma nyi bzhin no /
yathā vimatir hi duḥkhādisatyaviṣaye vicikitsā kleśaścocyate na tu / viṣayāntare /
# dper na sdug bsngal gyi tshogs kyi rab tu phye ba'i phyir / / de dag gi sgrib pa ni shes nyon mongs pa zhes bya'i yul gzhan la ni ma yin no /
viṣayāntare hi saṃśaya eva, na kleśo na vicikitsā /
# yul gzhan la ni som nyi nyid de / / nyon mongs pa yang ma yin the tshom yang ma yin no /
evavṃ duḥkhasatyādiviṣaye evā'jñānamavidyā kleśaścocyate, na tu / viṣayāntare /
# de bzhin du sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la sogs pa'i yul nyid la mi shes pa ni ma rig pa dang nyon mongs pa zhes bya ba'i yul gzhan la ma yin no /
viṣayāntare tvajñānam eva, na cā'vidyā naiva kleśaḥ / / tasmāt tasya jñeyajñānamātrapravṛttāvāvaraṇatvāt tajñeyāvaraṇam / ucyate na hi kleśakarmajanmanāmapi, tāni cotpadyanta evāvidyāyā eva /
# yul gzhan la ni mi shes pa nyid yin te / / ma rig pa'am ma yin nyon mongs pa'am ma yin no / / de lta bas na de ni shes par bya ba la ye shes tsam 'jug pa la sgrib pa'i phyir / / shes bya'i sgrib pa zhes bya ste / / ma rig pa ltar nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe rnams kyang 'byung rba ni yin no /
yadyevaṃ bodhisattvānām āvaraṇaṃ na vyavasthāpyate /
# gal te de lta na byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrib par rnam par mi gzhag go zhe na /
naitadevam, bodhisattvānāṃ hi śrutasambhāraprabhāvitatvāt
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni thos pa'i tshogs kyi rab tu phye ba'i phyir /
teṣāmāvaraṇaṃ jñeyāvaraṇam / / taduktam -
# de dag gi sgrib pa ni shes bya'i sgrib pa ste / / de skad du /
āryho'pyagyūḥ pañca vidyāpadāni / nārabhya syāt kadāpi sarvajñaḥ / / tato'nyeṣāṃ nigrahā'nugrahārthaṃ
# rig pa'i gnas lnga dag la brtson par ma byas par / / 'phags mchog cis kyang thams cad mkhyen nyid mi 'gyur te / / de bas gzhan dag tshar gcod rjes su gzung phyir ram /
svajñānārthaṃ vā'rabhet tatra yatnam // iti /
# rang gis shes par bya phyir de la de brtson byed / / ces bshad do /
udṛktaṃ tu mṛdvapi rāgādivastu teṣām eva bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ / rāvakādigotrakāṇañcā'dhimātramabhīkṣṇaṃ ca pravartitaṃ
# lhag pa ni 'dod chags la sogs pa'i dngos po chung yang byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can dang nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can de dag la shas che ba dang rgyun du 'byung ba'o /
rāgādicaritānām āvaranam iti / / yeṣāṃ [p.53]
# 'dod chags la sogs pa spyod pa rnams kyi sgrib pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
mṛdāvapi viṣaye rāgādīnām anyatamat adhimātramabhīkṣṇyaṃ ca / pravartate te rāgādicaritāḥ /
# su dag yul ngan pa la yang 'dod chags la sogs pa gang yang rung ba shas che ba dang rgyun du 'byung ba de dag ni 'dod chags la sogs pa spyod pa'o /
samaṃ punasteṣām eva bodhisattvagotrakāraṇaṃ / śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñcāvaraṇam / / samaṃ hi prakāradvittvābhāvāt /
# mnyam pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can dang nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can de dag nyid kyi sgrib pa ste / / mnyam pa ni de gnyi ga'i rnam pa yang med pa'i phyir ro /
samabhāgacaritānām āvaraṇam iti yeṣāṃ viṣayasādṛśye {sāmīpye?} kleśa
# cha mtshungs par spyod pa rnams kyi sgrib pa'o zhes bya ba ni / / su dag yul dang 'dra bar nyon mongs pa skye'i /
utpadyate na tvabhīkṣṇaṃ te samabhāgacaritāḥ /
# rgyun du ni ma yin pa de dag ni cha mtshungs par spyod pa'o /
saṃsārādānatyāgāvaranamityādi /
# 'khor ba len pa dang gtong ba'i sgrib pa ni zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni /
bhodisattvo hi kāruṇyādhipattyāt saṃsāramupādatte, prajñādhipattyāc / ca saṃsāradoṣaṃ yathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tyajati /
# byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje'i dbang gis 'khor ba nye bar len pa dang shes rab kyi dbang gis 'khor ba'i nyes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mthong ste /
tataḥ kleśābhāve'pi sattvākicanāj janmaparigraho'pratiṣṭhataṃ nirvāṇam,
# stong pas de'i phyir nyon mongs pa med par sems can la lta bas skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa ni / / mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa ste /
saṃsāranirvāṇayor dvayorapratiṣṭhitatvāt /
# 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa gnyis la mi gnas pa'i phyir ro /
tadāvaraṇantu kleśābhibhūtena yathā saṃsāramupādāya / yathābhūtadoṣādarśanāccā'kṛpayā parityajanam /
# de'i sgrib pa ni nyon mongs pas non bzhin du 'khor ba nye bar len pa dang nyes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mthong nas snying rje med par 'khor ba yongs su gtong ba'o /
ajñānamihāvaraṇamucyate kṛpāprajñayoḥ pratibandhakatvādityanye /
# gzhan dag na re snying rje dang shes rab gnyis kyi bgegs su gyur pa'i phyir mi shes pa ni 'dir sgrib pa zhes bya'o zhe'o /
athavā yathoktaṃ mahāratnakūṭe - sa āśayena nirvāṇe tiṣṭhati, saṃsāre / ca prayogeṇa tiṣṭhatīti /
# yang na ji ltar dkon mchog brtsegs pa chen po las / / de'i bsam pa mya ngan las 'das pa la yang gnas la / / 'khor ba na yang sbyor bar gnas pa zhes bstan pa lta bu ste /
etaddhi bodhisattvānām apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam /
# 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'o /
tatra nirvāṇapṛṣṭhībhāvād āśayaprayogābhyāṃ saṃsāramupādatte,
# de la mya ngan las 'das pa la rgyab kyis bltas pa'i phyir / / bsam pa dang sbyor bas 'khor ba la len te /
agotrasthasattva iva / / tathā ca saṃsārapṛṣṭhībhāvānnirvāṇagatābhyāmāśayaprayogābhyāṃ
# rigs med pa'i sems can bzhin no / / de bzhin du 'khor ba la rgyab kyis bltas pa'i phyir / / mya ngan las 'das par song ba'i bsam pa dang sbyor ba gnyis kyis 'khor ba yang yongs su gtong ste /
saṃsāraṃ tyajati, śrāvakādigotrakā iva /
# nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can rnams ji lta ba bzhin no /
evaṃ saṃsārādānaṃ tatparityajanaṃ ca / bodhisattvagotrakāṇāmapratiṣṭhitanirvāṇāvaraṇam,
# de ltar 'khor ba len pa dang de gtong ba yang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa la sgrib pa ste /
saṃsāranirvāṇayorekāntapatitatvāt /
# 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa gnyis las mtha' gcig tu ltung ba'i phyir ro /
bodhisattvās tu tathāgatatvaprāptikāle kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇāt / saṃsāre na tiṣṭhanti nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇe ca, dharmakāyaprabandhān na
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs par gyur pa'i dus na nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa spangs pa'i 'khor ba la mi gnas pa dang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa na yang chos kyi sku rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir /
tiṣṭhanti nirvāṇe śrāvakādivat /
# nyan thos la sogs pa bzhin du mya ngan las 'das pa la mi gnas te /
tataḥ saṃsāranirvāṇayor ubhayhatrāpi na pratiṣṭhantīti /
# de ltar na 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa gnyi ga la yang mi gnas so /
atra bodhisattvasya śrāvakādīnāñca mārge, teṣāṃ prayoge, phale, / apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaṃ ca pratibandhakatvādetāni / pañcavidhānyāvaraṇānyākhyātāni / / ityetad yathāyogamiti yathāsambhavam /
# 'dir byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos la sogs pa'i lam dang de gnyis kyi sbyor ba dang 'bras bu dang mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa la bgegs byed pa'i phyir sgrib pa rnam pa lnga po 'di dag grangs bzhin no / / de ltar 'di dag ni ci rigs par zhes bya ba ni ji ltar mthun mthun du'o /
tatra prathamamantyaṃ ca bodhisattvagotrakāṇām āvaraṇam /
# de la dang po dang tha ma ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can rnams kyi sgrib pa'o /
prathamādavaraṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām āvaraṇam / / itarad dvayaṃ punarubhayeṣām āvaraṇamākhyātam / / tatra ca jñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvānām āvaraṇam uktam / / taccā'kliṣṭamajñānam iti // / nava saṃyojanāni kleśāvaraṇaṃ / / kasyaitāny āvaraṇaṃ / / anunayasaṃyojanaṃ saṃvegasyāvaraṇaṃ / / pratighasaṃyojanam upekṣāyāḥ tena hi [p.54] / pratikūlam api pratighavastu upekṣituṃ na śaknoti / / śeṣāṇi tattvadarśanasyāvaraṇaṃ / / kathaṃ kṛtvā / / tāni hi yathākramaṃ / / saṃkleśasya parijñāne saṃyojanānyāvaraṇaṃ bhavanti / / mānaṃ saṃyojanaṃ hi satkāyadṛṣṭiparijñāne bahvaty āvaraṇaṃ / abhisamayakāle sāntaravyantarā'smimānasamudācāravaśena tad aprahāṇāt / avidyāsaṃyojanaṃ satkāyadṛṣṭivastuparijñāne / tenopādānaskandhā'parijñānāt / / dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhasatyaparijñāne satkāyā'ntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāntad / uttrāsāt mithyādṛṣṭyā cāpavādāt / / parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgasatyaparijñāne anyathā'praśuddhiparāmarśanāt / vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāne tad guṇā'nabhiśraddhānāt / / īrṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ lābhasatkāraparijñāne tad doṣā'darśanāt / / mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ saṃlekhaparijñāne pariṣkārā'dhyavasānāt /} [p.55] / mānādi bhedena /
# dang 'og ni nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can rnams kyi sgrib pa'o / / gzhan gnyis ni gnyi ga'i sgrib pa'o / / de la shes bya'i sgrib pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrib par bshad de / / de yang nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa'o zhes bya bar shes so / / gnyi ga'i sgrib pa'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa la rnam pa du yod pa dang rang bzhin ji lta bu dang gang gi bgegs su gyur pa mi shes te / / de'i phyir / / nyon mongs mtshan nyid rnam dgu'o / / zhes bya ba gsungs te / / sgrib ces bya ba dang sbyar ro / / nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid ni nyon mongs pa'i rang bzhin no / / rnam pa dgu po de ji lta bu zhe na / / de'i phyir kun du sbyor rnams zhes bya ba gsungs so / / sdug bsngal sna tshogs la kun du sbyor bas kun du sbyor ba rnams so / / sdug bsngal sna tshogs kyang 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med par gtogs pa'i lus te / / sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid dang 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid dang 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid de khams gsum dang ci rigs su sbyar ro / / de yang rjes su chags pa'i kun du sbyor ba nas / / ser sna'i kun du sbyor ba'i bar du'o / / de la khong khro ba ni zhe sdang ngo / / phrag dog ni gzhan gyi phun sum tshogs pa la mi bzod pa'o / / ser sna ni yo byad kun 'dzin pa ste / / de gsum ni 'dod par gtogs pa'o / / rjes su chags pa'i kun du sbyor ba ni khams gsum gyi sred pa'o / / de bzhin du nga rgyal dang ma rig pa dang lta ba dang mchog tu 'dzin pa dang the tshom gyi kun du sbyor ba rnams ni khams gsum pa dag nyid do / / 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin pa'i lta ba dang log par lta ba rnams ni lta ba'i kun du sbyor ba'o / / lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa ni / / mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun du sbyor ba'o / / the tshom ni bden pa dang dkon mchog rnams la yid gnyis za ba'o / / gzhan khong khro ba la sogs pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa gang yin pa de dag kyang nyon mongs pa'i rgyu mthun pa dang nyon mongs par gyur pa'i phyir / / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa nyid do / / phrag dog dang ser sna ni gtso bo yin pas kun du sbyor bar bzung ngo / / mdo sde las kyang 'di skad ces / / koo shi ka lha dang mi rnams ni phrag dog dang ser sna'i kun du sbyor ba'o zhes gsungs so / / de dag kyang gang la sgrib pa yin zhe na de'i phyir / / skyo ba dang ni btang snyoms dang de kho na ni mthong ba dang / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / skyo ba ni yid 'byung ba'i rnam grangs su gtogs pa ste / / de bas na rjes su chags pa'i kun du sbyor ba ni kun du skyo ba la sgrib po zhes bya ba smos te / / des lus dang 'tsho ba dang longs spyod dang bu smad la sogs pa dang bsam gtan dang gzug med pa rnams la yang rjes su chags pas / / 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rnams kyis nyen yang khams gsum la mi skyo'o / / khong khro ba'i kun du sbyor ba ni btang snyoms la sgrib ste / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / des ni mi mthun pa zhes rgya cher smos so / / yid mi bde ba'i rgyu yin pas mi mthun pa'o / / khong khro ba'i gzhi ste khong khro ba'i rgyu la btang snyoms su byed cing mngon du mi byed par mi nus so / / rjes su chags pa'i gzhi ni mi mthun pa med pas btang snyoms su mi nus pa ni / / rigs kyi khong khro ba'i gzhi ni mi mthun pa la yang khong khro ba ste; btang snyoms su byed mi nus pas de'i phyir / / rjes su chags pa bas sdig che bar bstan pa'i phyir yang zhes bya ba smos so / / mnyam par 'jog pa na gal te 'du byed kyi btang snyoms thob na / / de ltar de'i sems mnyam par 'gyur ro / / gal te de'i khong khro ba'i kun du sbyor bshas che bar 'gyur na ni / / de'i dbang gis khong khro ba'i rgyu de la btang snyoms mi thob ste / / de byung na bdag gi dmigs pa la gdon mi za bar dmigs par 'gyur ro / / de ltar rjes su chags pa'i kun du sbyor bas ni dben pa nyid mi 'thob po / / khong khro ba'i kun du sbyor bas ni dben par gyur kyang ting nge 'dzin mi 'thob po / / lhag ma bdun po ni de kho na mthong ba la sgrib ces bya ba ni / / ma nor bar mthong ba la sgrib po / / ji lta zhe na zhes bya ba ni mi shes te dri ba'o / / de'i phyir de dag ni go rims bzhin du / / 'jig tshogs lta dang de'i gzhi dang / / zhes bya ba rgya cher gsungs so / / nga rgyal gyi kun du sbyor ba ni 'jig tshogs la lta ba yongs su shes pa la bsgrib pa yin no / / de la 'jig tshogs la lta ba la brten nas sems khengs pa ni nga rgyal te / / de yang nga rgyal las kyang nga rgyal la sogs pa rnam pa bdun no /
ātmātmīyagrāhyagrāhakatvavivekena / bālajanaparikalpitadharmasvabhāvavivekena ca yat satkāyadrṣṭir darśanaṃ
# 'jig tshogs la lta ba la bdag dang bdag gi dang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa las dben pa dang byis pa'i skye bos kun brtags pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin gyis dben par mthong ba gang yin pa de ni /
tat satkāyadṛṣṭiparijñānaṃ /
# 'jig tshogs la lta ba yongs su shes pa'o /
tasya mānasaṃyojanaṃ bhavaty āvaraṇaṃ tad utpattivibandhāt / / kutra katham ityāha - abhisamyakāle / sāntaravyantarā'smimānasamudācāravaśena tad aprahāṇād iti /
# de'i sgrib pa ni nga rgyal gyi kun du sbyor ba yin te / / de skye ba la ba gegs byed pa'i phyir ro / / de yang gang gi tshe ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / mngon par rtogs pa'i dus na nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal bar chad dang bcas pa dang bar chad med par kun du 'byung ba'i dbang gis de ma spangs pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
satyābhisamayakāle nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ /
# bden pa mngon par rtogs pa'i dus ni / / nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dus so /
tatra sāntaraḥ pratipakṣavyavahitaḥ vyantaraḥ pratipakṣā'vyavahitaḥ / / sa cādhimātre mṛdau ca pratipakṣe veditavyaḥ /
# de la bar chad dang bcas pa ni gnyen pos bar du chod pa'o / / bar chad med pa ni gnyen pos bar du ma chod pa ste / / de yang gnyen po che ba dang chung bar rig par bya'o /
yāvat sāntareṇa vyantareṇa cāsmimānena samudācarati na tāvat / satkāyadṛṣṭEḥ prahāṇam asti /
# ji srid du nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal bar chad dang bcas pa dang bar chad med pa kun du 'byung ba de srid du 'jig tshogs la lta ba spong ba med de /
satkāyadṛṣṭibalenaivāsmimānapravṛttitaḥ /
# 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i stobs kyis nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
avidyāsaṃyojanaṃ satkāyadṛṣṭivastuparijñāne āvaraṇam iti sambadhyate / / satkāya dṛṣṭer vastu pañcopādānaskandhāḥ tad ālambanataḥ / / yathoktaṃ sūtre - ye kecicchramaṇā brāhmaṇā vā ātmā ātmeti
# ma rig pa'i kun du sbyor ba ni / / 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i gzhi yongs su shes pa la sgrib po / / 'jig tshogs la lta pa'i gzhi ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga rnams te / / de la dmigs pa las byung ba'i phyir ro / / mdo'i sde las kyang ji skad du /
samanupaśyantaḥ samanupaśYanti abhiniviśamānā abhiniviśante ta imān eva / pañcopādānaskandhānupādāyeti / / kim punas tat parijñānaṃ / [p.56] / ātmanyātma śūnyatāyāḥ skandheṣu
# dge sbyong bram ze gang la la bdag dang bdag gi rjes su lta ba na / / nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po 'di dag nyid la brten nas rjes su blta'o / / mngon par zhen pa na mngon par zhen to zhes gsungs so / / yongs su shes pa de yang ji lta bu zhe na /
bālajanaparikalpitadharmasvabhāvaśūnyatāyāś ca yad darśanam anityato / duḥkhataḥ śūnyato'nātmataḥ samudāyādito vā yad darśanaṃ tat teṣāṃ
# phung po rnams la bdag dang bdag gis stong pa nyid dang byis pa'i skye bos kun brtags pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid du mthong ba gang yin pa dang mi rtag pa nyid dang sdug bsngal ba nyid dang bdag med pa nyid dang kun 'byung ba la sogs par mthong ba gang yin pa de ni de dag yongs su shes pa'o /
parijñānaṃ / / atraiva kāraṇam āha - tenopādānaskandhā'parijñānād iti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa des nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams yongs su mi shes pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
avidyayā hi nityādiprakārāvṛteṣu skandheṣu tat parijñānā'bhāvād
# ma rig pas brtag pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis bsgribs pa'i phung po rnams la de yongs su shes pa med pa'i phyir /
avidyā skandhaparijñānāvaraṇaṃ /
# ma rig pa ni phung po yongs su shes pa la sgrib po /
dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhasatyaparijñāne āvaraṇam iti vartate /
# lta ba'i kun du sbyor ba ni / / 'gog pa'i bden pa yongs su shes pa la sgrib po /
dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ hi tisro dṛṣṭayaḥ satkāyāntagrāhamithyādṛṣṭayaḥ /
# lta ba'i kun du sbyor ba ni lta ba la gsum ste; 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin pa dang log par lta ba rnams so /
tatra satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ pañcasūpādānaskandheṣvātmata ātmīyato veti / darśanaṃ / / antagrāhadṛṣṭir hi tasminnevātmābhikalpitabhāve śāśvatadarśanam / ucchedadarśanaṃ vā /
# de la 'jig tshogs la lta ba ni / / nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga rnams la bdag gam bdag gir lta ba'o / / mthar 'dzin par lta ba ni bdag tu mngon par brtag pa'i dngos po de nyid la rtag par lta ba'am / / chad par lta ba'o /
yena darśanena hetuṃ vā phalaṃ vā kriyā vā sad vā vastu apavadate / mithyā vā parikalpayati tan mithyādṛṣṭiḥ /
# lta ba gang gi rgyu'am 'bras bu'am byed pa'am / / yod pa'i dngos po la skur pa 'debs pa dang log par kun du rtog pa de ni log par lta ba'o /
nirodhasatyaparijñānaṃ śāntādibhir ākaraiḥ /
# 'gog pa'i bden pa yongs su shes pa ni zhi ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams so /
katham punas tat tasyāvaraṇam ityata āha - / satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāntaduttrāsāt mithyādṛṣṭyā cā'pavādād iti
# ji ltar de ni de la sgrib can / / de'i phyir 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba gnyis kyis de la skrag pa dang log par lta bas de la skur pa 'debs pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyām ahaṃ tatra na bhaviṣyāmīti nirodhād / uttrasyati mithyādṛṣṭyā cā'pavadate nāstyeva nirodha iti /
# de la 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dag gis bdag der med par 'gyur ro zhes 'gog pa la skrag par 'gyur ro; / / log par lta bas kyang 'gog pa med do zhes skur pa 'debs so /
tatra satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāṃ śāntataḥ praṇītato nissaraṇataś ca na
# de la 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin par lta bdag gis zhi ba dang gya nom pa dang nges par 'byung bar yongs su mi shes la /
parijānāti mithyādṛṣṭyā nirodhato na parijānāti / / evaṃ dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhaparijñāna āvaraṇaṃ /
# log par lta bas 'gog par yongs su mi shes te de ltar lta ba'i kun du sbyor ba ni 'gog pa yongs su shes pa la sgrib pa'o /
parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgasatyaparijñāne / / tatra parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaśca /
# mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun du sbyor ba ni / / lam gyi bden pa la yongs su shes pa la sgrib ste zhes bya ba de la mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun du sbyor ba ni / / lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin ba'o; / / de la lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa ni /
tatra dṛṣṭiparāmarśo dṛṣṭau dṛṣṭyāśrayeṣu ca pañcasūpādānaskandheṣu / yad utkarṣādito darśanaṃ / / śīlavrataparāmarśaḥ śīlaṃ vrataṃ tad ubhayaṃ tadāśrayān vā
# lta ba dang lta ba'i gnas nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga rnams la mchog la sogs par lta ba gang yin pa'o / / tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa ni / / tshul khrims sam / / brtul zhugs sam / / de gnyi ga'am /
pañcopādānaskandhān śuddhito muktito nairyāṇikato vā samanupaśyato yad / darśanaṃ tacchīlavrataparāmarśaḥ /
# de dag gi gnas nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga rnams la / / dag pa dang grol ba dang nges par 'byin par yang dag par rjes su lta ba'i lta ba gang yin pa de ni tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
mārgasya parijñānam punar nairyāṇikādibhir ākāraiḥ /
# lam yongs su shes pa yang nges par 'byin pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams su shes pa'o /
katham punaḥ parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgaparijñāna āvaraṇam ityata āha - / anyathā 'praśuddhiparāmarśanād iti /
# ji ltar na mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun du sbyor ba lam yongs su shes pa la sgrib ce na / / de'i phyir rnam pa gzhan gyis dag par mchog tu 'dzin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
śīlavratamātrakeṇa vā kāmasukhālayena vā duṣkaracaryayā vā
# tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs tsam gyis sam / / 'dod pa'i bde ba'i gnas kyis sam / / dka' ba spyod pas sam /
sāṃkhyādijñānena vā śuddhiparāmarśanāt /
# grangs can la sogs pa'i shes pas dag par mchog tu 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
dṛṣṭiparāmarśena tu yenaiva śuddhiṃ pratyeti tadevā'grataḥ parāmṛśati /
# lta ba la mchog tu 'dzin pas kyang gang gis dag par yid ches pa de nyid dam par mchog tu 'dzin to /
evaṃparāmarśasaṃyojanena mārgaṃ tyajati anyathā ca śuddhimparāmṛśatīti
# de ltar na mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun du sbyor bas lam bor te rnam pa gzhan gyis dag par mchog tu 'dzin to /
vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāne āvaraṇam iti vartate / / katham ityato bravīti - tad guṇā'nabhiśraddhānād iti / / vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ saty aratneṣu vimatiḥ /
# the tshom gyi kun du sbyor ba ni dkon mchog gsum yongs su shes pa la sgrib ste / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / de'i yon tan la mngon par yid mi ches pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / the tshom gyi kun du sbyor ba ni bden pa de dang dkon mchog rnams la yid gnyis za ba ste /
prakarṣeṇā'panītasarvaguṇadoṣasya paryantāśrayatvena buddharatne / parijñānaṃ / [p.57]
# sangs rgyas dkon mchog la yon tan dang nyes pa thams cad phul du phyin pa dang bsal ba'i mthar thug pa'i gnas su yongs su shes pa'o /
saṃsārasāgarottarakatvena sarvasahetukaduḥkhā'tyantaviyogātmakatvena tat / pratipādakatvena ca dharmaratne parijñānaṃ /
# chos dkon mchog la 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho las sgrol ba dang rgyu dang bcas pa'i sdug bsngal dang gtan du bral ba'i bdag nyid de / / de khong du chud par byed par yongs su shes pa'o /
śrāmaṇyapahalasthatvenānuttaradakṣiṇīyakṣetratvena cāsaṅgharatne / parijñānaṃ /
# dge 'dun dkon mchog la dge sbyong gi 'bras bu la gnas pa dang der zhugs pa dang bla na med pa'i sbyin gnas kyi zhing yin par yongs su shes pa'o /
satyadarśanāt prahīṇavicikitsaścā'vetya prasādalābhena / ratnatrayaguṇe'bhiśraddatte nā'prahīṇavicikitsa iti /
# bden pa dang mthong ba dang the tshom spang ba'i phyir shes nas dad pa rnyed pas dkon mchog gsum gyi yon tan la mngon par yid ches kyi the tshom ma spangs pa ni ma yin no /
ato vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāna āvaraṇam uktaṃ /
# de'i phyir the tshom gyi kun du sbyor ba ni dkon mchog gsum yongs su shes pa la sgrib ces bya'o /
īrṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ lābhasatkāraparijñāna āvaraṇaṃ /
# phrag dog gi kun du sbyor ba ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti yongs su shes pa la sgrib ces bya'o /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - tad doṣā'darśanād iti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / de'i nyes pa mi mthong ba'i phyir ro zhes bya'o /
īrṣyāsaṃYojanaṃ hi lābhasatkārarakto'nyasampatpratighāṃśikaścetaso / vyāroṣaḥ /
# phrag dog gi kun du sbyor ba ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti la chags pa ste / / gzhan gyi phun sum tshogs pa la zhe sdang gi char gtogs pas sems khong nas 'khrug pa'o /
sarvānarthāśrayatvā'vabodho lābhasatkāraparijñānaṃ /
# rnyed pa dang bkur sti la gnod pa thams cad kyi gnas yin par khong du chud pa ni yongs su shes par bya'o /
īrṣyayā tu lābhasatkāraṃ sarvaguṇavipakṣabhūtatvena / vividhā'narthamūlatvena ca na parijānātītyato lābhasatkāra / parijñāna āvaraṇam irṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ /
# phrag dog gis ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti yon tan thams cad kyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur pa dang gnod pa sna tshogs kyi rtsa bar gyur par mi shes pas / / de'i phyir phrag dog gi kun du sbyor ba ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti yongs su shes pa la sgrib po /
mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ saṃlekhaparijñāna āvaraṇam iti / / katham ityata āha - / pariṣkārā'dhyavasānād iti /
# ser sna'i kun du sbyor ba ni yo byad bsnyungs pa yongs su shes pa la sgrib po / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir yo byad la lhag par zhen pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / ser sna ni yo byad rnams la lhag par chags pa ste /
mātsaryaṃ pariṣkāre'ṣv avyavasito rāgāṃśikaścetasa upakaraṇeṣv āgrahaḥ / saṃlekhaḥ pariṣkārair vivekaḥ /
# 'dod chags kyi char gtogs pas 'tshog chas rnams la sems kun du 'dzin pa'o / / yo byad bsnyungs pa ni yo byad rnams las lhag par dben pa'o /
tasya sarvaguṇāśrayavastutvenā'vabodhaḥ parijñānaṃ /
# de la yon tan thams cad kyi gnas kyi dngos por yongs su rtogs pa ni yongs su shes pa'o /
na tu mātsaryeṇa pariṣkārā'dhyavāsānāt sarvaguṇāśrayetvena / parijānātītyataḥ saṃlekhaparijñāne mātsaryāvaraṇatvam uktaṃ /
# ser sna ni yo byad rnams la lhag par chags pas / / yon tan thams cad kyi gnas su yongs su mi shes te / / de'i phyir yo byad bsnyungs pa la sgrib po zhes bshad do /
tatrā'nunayapratighasaṃyojane tattvādhigamaprayogāvaraṇe /
# de la rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba'i kun du sbyor ba ni de kho na rtogs par byed par sbyor ba ni sgrib kyi / / lhag ma rnams ni ma yin no /
śeṣāṇi tu prayuktasya tattvadarśanasyāvaraṇāni tasmād eva teṣām / anukramaḥ / / tadyathā'vaśyaṃ prathamam eva mumukṣūṇāṃ saṃsārāc citttam / udvejayitavyaṃ /
# lhag ma rnams ni de kho na rtogs par byed par zhugs par byed pa la sgrib po / / de nyid kyi phyir de dag gi go rims ni 'di lta ste / / thar pa 'dod pas thog ma nyid du gdon mi za bar 'khor ba la sems skyo bar bya'o; /
tataḥ sarvata upekṣeṇa bhavitavyaṃ /
# de nas thams cad la btang snyoms su bya'o /
tataḥ sarvā'narthamūlatvāt satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ parijñeyā /
# de nas gnod pa thams cad kyi rtsa ba yin pas 'jig tshogs la lta ba yongs su shes par bya'o /
tad anantaraṃ dukḥ samudayātmakatvena tadvastu parijñeaṃ/
# de'i 'og tu de'i gzhi la sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i bdag nyid du yongs su shes par bya'o /
tatastannirodho vijñeyaḥ/
# de nas de 'gog pa shes par bya'o /
tad anantaraṃ lābhamārgo vijñeyaḥ /
# de'i 'og tu thob pa'i lam shes par bya'o /
tataḥ satyadarśanād ratnatraye tad guṇā'vabodhād avetya prasādalābhaḥ /
# de nas bden pa mthong ba dang yon tan de dag rtog pa'i phyir dkon mchog la shes nas dad pa 'thob po /
satyadarśanabalenaiva ca lābhasatkārasaṃlekhayor doṣaguṇadarśī
# bden pa mthong ba'i stobs nyid kyis kyang rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang yo byad bsnyungs pa gnyis kyi nyes pa dang yon tan mthong ba yin no /
bhavatītyevam āvaraṇīyadharmakramahetunā tadāvaraṇakramo veditavyaḥ /
# de ltar bsgrib par bya ba'i chos kyi go rims kyi rgyus de'i sgrib pa'i go rims kyang rig par bya'o /
nanu sarvasyāpi sarvatrāvaraṇatvena saṃbhavād
# thams cad la yang thams cad sgrib pa nyid du srid pa'i phyir /
vastupratiniyamenāvaraṇanirdeśo na yuktaḥ /
# gzhi so sor nges pas sgrib par bshad pa ni mi rigs pa ma yin nam zhe na /
naivā'tra vastupratiniyamaḥ kriyate kintarhi pratyāsattitaḥ prādhānyaiṣa / nirdeśaḥ // / { bodhisattvāvaraṇaṃ } [p.59]
# 'dir gzhi so sor nges par bya ba ni ma yin gyi / / so sor nye bar gnas pa'i phyir gtso bor byas te 'di bstan to / / ci sgrib pa de zad dam zhe na /
kim etad evāvaraṇaṃ / / etat tu sāmānyaṃ bodhisattvaśrāvakādīnāṃ / / bodhisattvānāntvāvaraṇaṃ / / śubhādau daśadhā'paraṃ / / āvaraṇaṃ / / ke ca śubhādaya iti na jñāyate / / ata āha - / aprayogo'nāyatane 'yogavihitaś ca yaḥ / / ityevamādyāvaraṇaṃ / / śubhādayaḥ punaḥ / / śubhaṃ bodhiḥ samādānaṃ
# de ni byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos la sogs pa'i spyi thun no / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrib pa ni / / dge ba la sogs pa bcu la gzhan sgrib pa gang yin pa dang dge ba la sogs pa yang gang yin mi shes te / / de'i phyir / / sbyor ba med dang skye mched min / / rnal 'byor min pas gang bskyed dang / / zhes gsungs pa la sogs pa ni sgrib pa'o / / dge ba la sogs pa ni / / dge dang byang chub yang dag 'dzin /
ityādi daśārthāḥ /
# zhes bya ba la sgos pa don bcu'o /
tatra śubhaṃ hi bodhihetubhūtaṃ sarvakuśalamūlaṃ /
# de la dge ba ni byang chub kyi rgyur gyur pa ste dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad do /
bodhis tu tat phalaṃ /
# byang chub ni de'i 'bras bu'o /
tatra śubhaṃ sāmānyata uddiṣṭaṃ prabhedataḥ svabhāvataś ca na vijñāyata / ity atas tat pratipādanārtham ārabhyate - / samādānaṃ dhīmattā'bhrāntyanāvṛtī / / nānyatrāso'matsaritvaṃ vaśitvaṃ ca / ityetac chubham iti /
# de la dge ba ni spyir bstan pa bas rab tu dbye ba dang rang bzhin mi shes nas de'i phyir de khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir rtsom ste / / yang dag 'dzin / / blo ldan 'khrul med sgrib pa med / / bsngo dang mi skrag ser sna med / / ces bya ba de dag ni dge bzhes bya'o /
bodhir api vacanamātreṇa svabhāvato na vijñāyata ityasyā vibhutvaṃ
# byang chub kyang smos pa tsam gyis rang bzhin mi shes te / / de'i phyir de ni dbang ngo zhes ston to /
darśayati / / śubhasya bodheś ca samādānādīnām iva svātantryeṇāvaraṇanirdeśāt / svātantryam evā'tra vijñāyate na tad deśanirdeśabhāva ityeke / / utpattyāvaraṇaṃ hi śūbhe vyavasthāpyate tac ca bodhicittādīnāṃ
# kha cig na re dge ba dang byang chub dang yang dag par 'dzin pa la sogs pa bzhin du sgrib pa rang gi rgyud yod par bshad pas / / 'dir rang gi rgyud yod pa nyid du shes kyi / / bstan pa dang bshad pa'i dngos por ni ma yin no zhe'o / / skye ba la sgrib pa ni dge ba la rnam par gzhag go / / de yang byang chub kyi sems la sogs pa rnams kyi spyi thun yin gyi /
sāmānyaṃ tasyāḥ śubhotpādyatvāt /
# dge ba ni bskyed par bya ba'i phyir ro /
dhṛtyādyāvaraṇantu samādānādyāvaraṇaṃ samādānādiṣu / vṛttyādyarthabhedāt bodhirapyekopyā prāptavyā cetyatas tasyāḥ
# yang dag par 'dzin pa la sogs pa la sgrib pa dang rten la sogs pa la sgrib pa ni yang dag par 'dzin pa la sogs pa rnams kyi sgrib pa ste tha dad do / / byang chub ni mi 'khrug pa dang thob par bya ba yin pas de'i phyir /
sthityāvaraṇaṃ prāptyāvaraṇaṃ ca vyavasthāpyate / / tasmān nāsty atra svātantryaprasaṅga iti /
# de'i gnas pa la sgrib pa dang thob par bya ba la sgrib pa rnam par gzhag ste / / de bas na de rang gi rgyud du yod par mi 'gyur ro /
kramaś ca teṣāṃ samāsataḥ - kuśalamūlaṃ niravaśeṣaṃ niṣpādya bodhiḥ / prāptavyā /
# de dag gi go rims kyang mdor na dge ba'i rtsa ba ma lus par bsgrubs nas byang chub thob par bya'o /
vyāsataḥ punaḥ prathamata eva bodhicittam utpādayitavyaṃ / svaparārthasampadādhārabhūtatvāt / / tataścittotpādanā'nurūpā dānādiṣu pratipattiḥ yayā bodhisattva / ityākhyāṃ labhate / / tato'saṃkhyeyakalpenābhyasyataḥ puṇyajñānasambhārasañcayād
# rgyas par ni thog ma nyid du byang chub kyi sems bskyed par bya ste / / bdag dang gzhan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa'i gzhir gyur ba'i phyir ro / / de nas sems bskyed pa dang mthun par sbyin pa la sogs pa bsgrub par bya ste / / des byang chub sems dpar mngon no / / de nas bskal pa grangs med par goms par byas te /
āśayaviśodhanārthaṃ pudgaladharmabhrāntipratipakṣeṇā'bhrāntyātmako / darśanamārga utpādayitavyaḥ /
# bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs bsags pas bsam par rnam par sbyang ba'i phyir / / gang zag dang chos la nor ba'i gnyen por ma nor ba'i bdag nyid mthong ba'i lam bskyed par bya'o /
tataścāvaraṇavigamaprabhāvito bhāvanāmārgaḥ prakarṣaṃ netavyo / viśuddhiviśeṣayogārthaṃ / [p.60]
# de nas rnam par dag pa'i khyad par dang ldan par bya ba'i phyir sgrib pa dang bral bas rab tu phye ba bsgom pa'i lam mthar phyin par bya'o /
tataḥ śrāvakādyatikramaṇaprayogeṇa yathopacitāni sarvāṇyetāni / laukikakalokottarāṇi kuśalamūlāni bodhau pariṇāmayitavyāni /
# de nas nyan thos la sogs pa las 'da' bar sbyor bas 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bsags pa de dag thams cad byang chub tu yongs su bsngo bar bya'o /
tataś ca nāmavasthāmāgato mahābodhyāśayatvād buddhabodhisattvānāṃ / gambhīrodāreṣu nirdeśeṣu na trasyati /
# de nas gnas de thob pa dang byang chub chen por bsam par mi byed pas / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bstan pa zab cing rgya che ba rnams la skrag par mi 'gyur ro /
tato bahuśrutapratipattiyukta udāraṃ dharmaṃ nirdiśati / sattvaparipācanārthaṃ /
# de nas mang du thos pa dang rtogs pa dang ldan nas sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir chos rgya cher ston to /
tataḥ paripakvavineyeṣu tadvimocanārthaṃ vaśitvaṃ buddhatvam avāpnotīti /
# de nas 'dul ba yongs su smin nas de dag rnam par dgrol ba'i phyir dbang ste / / sangs rgyas nyid thob po /
atra hi triṃśadāvaraṇāny uktāni āvaraṇīyārthāḥ śubhādayo daśa / cetyataḥ pṛcchati - eṣāṃ tu śubhādīnāṃ kasya katyāvaraṇāni / vijñeyānīti / / ata āha - / trīṇi trīṇi ca eteṣāṃ jñeyānyavaraṇāni hi / iti /
# 'dir sgrib pa sum cu dang bsgrib par bya ba dge ba la sogs pa'i don bcu bshad bas de'i phyir dge ba la sogs pa de rnams la gang la sgrib pa du yod pa mi shes nas dris pa dang de'i phyir / / de dag gi ni sgrib pa rnams / / gsum gsum dag tu shes par bya /
