kuśalasya trīṇyāvaraṇānīti / / aprayogo'nārambhaḥ /
# zhes bya ba gsungs so / / de la sgrib pa gsum zhes bya ba la sbyor ba med pa ni rtsom pa med pa'o /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
yena kleśena na prayujyate pramādena kausīdyena vā yasminn avasthāviśeṣe
# bag med pa'ang le lo'i nyon mongs pa gang gis mi sbyor ba ste /
kleśabījānugate'vyākṛte kliṣṭe vā na prayujyate / / na prayujyate nityaṃ gauravād vā alapatvād vetyapratyoga ucyate na tu / prayogābhāvāt tasminn āvaraṇā'nupapatteḥ /
# nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang ldan pa lung du ma bstan pa'am / / nyon mongs par gyur pa'i gnas skabs kyi bye brag gang du mi sbyor ba'o / / rgyun du ma chud pa'am gus par mi sbyor ba ste / / chung bas na sbyor ba med pa zhes bya'i / / sbyor ba med pa ni ma yin te / / de la sgrib par mi 'thad pa'i phyir ro / / skye mched ma yin pa la sbyor ba ni /
anāyatanaprayogo bodher bodhyāvāhakānāñca kuśalamūlānāṃ yat / pravacanam utpattidvāraṃ tadāyatanaṃ tasmād anyad anāyatanaṃ /
# byang chub dang byang chub thob par byed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams skye ba'i sgo gsung rab gang yin pa de skye mched de / / de las gzhan pa ni skye mched ma yin no /
tasmin prayogo'nāyatane prayoga etasmād bāhyeṣvartheṣu / / tatra kimāvaraṇaṃ ? / yenā'jñānena dṛṣṭikleśena vā'nāyatane prayujyate sa eva ca prayoga / āvaraṇaṃ / / ayoniśaḥ prayoga iti / / yonir upāyaḥ /
# der sbyor ba ni 'di las phyi rol pa rnams skye mched ma yin pa la sbyor ba'o / / de la sgrib pa gang zhe na / / mi shes pa'am lta ba'i nyon mongs pa gang gis skye mched ma yin pa la sbyor ba ste / / sbyor ba de nyid la ni sgrib pa'o / / tshul bzhin ma yin pa la sbyor ba'o zhes bya ba la tshul bzhin ni thabs te /
yasya ya upāyas tasmād anyathā prayogo'yoniśaḥ prayogaḥ /
# gang gi thabs gang yin pa de las gzhan du sbyor ba ni / / tshul bzhin ma yin pa la sbyor ba'o /
ihaiva śāsane paṭhyate yad uta rāgacaraṇabhāvānāṃ hi na / rāgaprahāṇopāyaḥ pratighacaraṇasyā'śubhabhāvaneti /
# bstan pa 'di nyid las 'di lta ste / / 'dod chags spyod pa la byams pa bsgom pa ni 'dod chags spong ba'i thabs ma yin pa dang zhe sdang spyod pa la mi sdug pa bsgom pa zhes 'byung ba'o /
atrā'pyayoniśo manaskāras tannimitto vā prayoga āvaraṇaṃ / / bodhes trīṇi / / yathārtham avabodho bodhiḥ /
# 'dir yang tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa'am / / de'i rgyu ni sbyor ba'i sgrib pa'o / / byang chub kyi sgrib pa gsum ni zhes bya ba / / byang chub ni don ji lta ba bzhin du thugs su chud pa'o /
kuśalasyā'nutpattir iti pūrvoktam eva /
# dge ba mi skye ba zhes bya ba ni gong du bshad pa nyid do /
katham anutpattirāvaraṇaṃ ?
# mi skye ba ji ltar sgrib ce na /
kuśale'sati bodhir na bhavet tataḥ kuśalasyā'nutpattir bodher āvaraṇaṃ /
# dge ba med na byang chub tu mi 'gyur te / / de'i phyir dge ba mi skye ba ni byang chub kyi sgrib pa'o /
yo vā kleśo 'vasthāviśeṣo vā kuśalotpatter āvaraṇaṃ sa eva bodher api /
# yang na gnas skabs kyi bye brag gi tshe dge ba la skye ba la sgrib pa'i nyon mongs pa gang yin pa de nyid byang chub kyi sgrib pa yang yin te /
yo hi yat sambhārasyāvaraṇaṃ niyatam asau tat phalasyāpīti /
# gang tshogs gang gis sgrib par nges pa de ni de'i 'bras bu'i sgrib pa yang yin no /
utpannasyāpy amanasikaraṇaṃ abhāvanā'napekṣetyarthaḥ /
# skyes zin pa yang yid la mi byed pa ni mi bsgom pa ste / / spel bar mi byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
yena kausīdyādikleśena yasminn avasthāviśeṣa utpannam api kuśalaṃ paunaḥ / punyena na manasi karoti tad atrāvaraṇaṃ /
# le lo la sogs pa'i nyon mongs pa gang gis gnas skabs kyi bye brag gang la dge ba skyes kyang yang dang yang yid la mi byed pa de ni 'dir sgrib pa'o /
aparipūrṇasaṃbhāratā ceti /
# tshogs yongs su ma rdzogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
yāvatā sambhāreṇa bodhiḥ prāpyate tāvān [p.61] / puṇyajñānasambhāro'pūrṇaḥ pūrvavad avasthākleśo'lpasambhāro vā /
# tshogs ji snyed kyis byang chub thob par 'gyur ba'i bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs de snyed ma rdzogs pa dang gong ma lta bu'i gnas skabs kyi nyon mongs pa'am tshogs chung ba'o /
anyaḥ punar āha - aviśeṣavacane'pi nirvedhabhāgīnānām / evātrā'nutpattir abhipretā nānyeṣāṃ /
# gzhan dag na re bye brag tu ma bshad kyang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams kyi sgrib pa ni 'dir mi skye ba la bya bar 'dod de /
utpanānām api teṣām evā'manasikaraṇaṃ manasikurvato'py / asaṃbhṛtasambhāra āvaraṇam ucyata iti /
# gzhan dag gi ni ma yin no / / de dag skyes pa yid la mi byed pa dang yid la byed kyang tshogs ma bsags pa ni sgrib pa zhes bya'o zhe'o /
samādānaṃ bodhicittotpāda iti /
# yang dag par 'dzin pa ni byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa ste zhes bya ba ni /
niravaśeṣāḥ puṇyajñānasambhārās tat phalañca buddhatvaṃ sarvasattvāś / ca niruttare nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau pratiṣṭhāpayitavyenā'nena iti
# bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs ma lus pa dang de'i 'bras bu sangs rgyas nyid dang sems can thams cad kyang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings bla na med par gzhag par bya ba nyid du 'dis yang dag par 'dzin cing yongs su len pas na /
samādānaṃ bodhicittotpādaḥ /
# yang dag par 'dzin pa ni byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa'o /
sa punaḥ svaparahitakriyāśayaścetanācchandasahitaḥ /
# de yang bdag dang gzhan la phan par byed pa'i bsam pa ste / / sems pa 'dun pa dang bcas pa'o /
tasyāvaraṇeṣu triṣu gotravaidhuryaṃ / / agotrakaḥ śrāvakādigotrako vā /
# de'i sgrib pa gsum la rigs dang mi ldan pa ni rigs med pa'am / / nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs so /
kalyāṇamitravaidhuryaṃ / / satyapi gotre ye taṃ bodhicittotpāde samādāpayanti tair asamavadhānaṃ
# dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang mi ldan pa zhes bya ba ni rigs yod kyang de gang dag byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa de dag dang mi phrad pa ste /
yān vāgamya bodhir vyāvartate kuśalair vā dharmair na vardhate /
# gang la brten nas byang chub las rnam par ldog pa'am / / dge ba'i chos rnams kyis mi 'phel ba'o /
satyapi kalyāṇamitrasamavadhāne saṃsāraduḥkhena parikhedacittatā
# dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang phrad du zin kyang 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rnams kyis sems yongs su skyo ste /
vipratipannasattvānām udvagacittasyāśu parinirvāṇābhiprāyaḥ /
# sems can log par zhugs pa rnams la sems skyo nas myur du mya ngan las 'da' bar sems so /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
hetuvaikalyaṃ pratyayavaikalyaṃ sattveṣu cā'kāruṇyaṃ kausīdyaṃ vā /
# rgyu dang mi ldan pa dang rkyen dang mi ldan pa dang sems can rnams la snying mi rje ba dang le lo ste /
akāruṇiko hi sattvārthena khidyate kusīdo vā / / dhīmattvaṃ bodhisattvateti /
# snying rje med pa ni sems can gyi don gyis skyo bar 'gyur ba'am sgyid lug par 'gyur ro / / blo dang ldan pa ni byang chub sems dpa' nyid de zhes bya ba ni /
svabhāvena śrāvakādigotrakebhyamtīkṣṇendriyatvāt sarvathā / sarvajñeyopaparīkṣādhikāritvāt gambhīrodāradharmā'dhimukteś ca / bodhisattva eva dhīmān nā'nyaḥ / / bodhisattvatā'viparyastā parārthaparā pratipattiḥ /
# rang bzhin gyis nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can rnam pas dbang po rno ba dang shes par bya ba thams cad kyi rnam pa thams cad la nye bar rtog pa'i skabs yin pa dang chos zab cing rgya che ba la mos pas / / byang chub sems dpa' nyid blo ldan yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin no / / byang chub sems dpa' nyid ni gzhan gyi don phyin ci ma log par sgrub pa'o; /
pratipatter vaidhuryaṃ pāramitādiṣv apravṛttiḥ / / bodhisattvo hi pratipattivṛtto jñeyaḥ /
# sgrub pa dang mi ldan zhes pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa la mi 'jug pa'o / / sgrub pa la gnas pa ni byang chub sems dpa' shes so /
kujano mūrkhajana iti aparīkṣakajana ityarthaḥ /
# skye bo ngan pa ni skye bo blun po'o zhes bya ba ni yongs su mi rtog pa'i skye bo zhes bya ba'i tha tshig ste /
kujano hi pratipattiyuktam api bodhisattvopamitaṃ na jānīte /
# skye bo ngan pa ni sgrub pa dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' la 'de'o zhes mi shes pa'o /
duṣṭajanaḥ pratihata iti bodhisattvadveṣiṇaḥ / / te hi randhrā'nvayitvād bodhisattvasya bhūtān guṇān na paśyanti /
# skye bo sdang ba ni zhe 'gras pa rnams so zhes bya ba ni / / byang chub sems dpa' la zhe sdang ba rnams te / / de dag glags tshol bas byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan yang dag pa rnams ni mi mthong la /
asaddoṣadarśanāt pratigharaudracittād vā bhūtān guṇān / pracchādyā'dhyāropyā'bhūtān doṣān prakāśayanti /
# nyes pa med pa ni mthong ba'am zhe sdang gis gnod par sems pas yon tan yang dag pa rnams bcas te / / sgro btags nas med pa'i nyes pa sgrogs pa'o /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
dānapāramitādivipakṣo 'jñānam pradveṣaśceti / / abhrāntes trīṇi /
# sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang mi shes pa dang zhe sdang ba'o / / 'khrul pa med pa'i sgrib pa gsum ni zhes bya ba ni /
adhyāropāpavādād bhrāntiḥ tat pratipakṣas tu bhrātyabhāvo / darśanamārgaḥ /
# sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i phyir 'khrul pa'o / / gnyen po ni 'khrul pa med pa ste / / mthong ba'i lam mo /
viparyāsadauṣṭhulyaṃ grāhyagrāhakā'bhiniveśavāsanā paripuṣṭir iti
# kha cig na re phyin ci log gi gnas ngan len ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa'i bag chags brtas pa'o zhe'o /
kecit / / sarveṣāṃ darśanaheyānām anuśayānāṃ
# gzhan dag na re mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i bag la nyal thams cad dam /
sarvatragadharmadhātubodhapratibuddhasya [p.62] / vā'kliṣṭasyā'jñānasyālayavijñānasanniviṣṭabījaparipoṣa ity anye /
# chos kyi dbyings thams cad du 'gro bar khong du chud par bya ba'i gegs su gyur pa nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa'i sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa yongs su gsos pa'o zhe'o /
ātmādyabhāva ātmādivikalpo hi viparyāsa ity apare /
# gzhan dag na re bdag la sogs pa med par bdag la sogs par rnam par rtog pa ni phyin ci log go zhe'o /
kleśādyāvaraṇatrayād anyatamā'vaśiṣtateti /
# nyon mongs pa la sogs pa'i sgrib pa gsum las lhag ma gang yang rung ba zhes bya ba de la /
tatra kleśāvaraṇaṃ yastīvrāyatakālasamudācārikleśo rāgādikas tat
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa ni shas che ba dang yun ring po nas 'dod chags la sogs pa kun du 'byung ba ste /
pratipakṣaprayogā'navakāśād abhrānter āvaraṇaṃ /
# de'i gnyen po la sbyor ba'i skabs mi 'byed pas 'khrul pa med pa la sgrib po /
karmāvaraṇamānantaryādikarma yadapāyaniyamanaṃ /
# las kyi sgrib pa ni mtshams med pa la sogs pa'i las ngan song du nges pa gang yin pa'o /
vipākāvaraṇam apāyādayaḥ tatrotpannasyāryadharmotpattibhāgo nāsti /
# rnam par smin pa'i sgrib pa ni ngan song la sogs pa ste / / der skyes pa la 'phags pa'i chos skye ba'i skal ba med do /
teṣāṃ kleśakarmajanmanām anyatamam apy aviśīṣṭam āvaraṇaṃ na punaḥ
# nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe de dag las lhag ma gang yang rung ba zhig sgrib pa yin gyi zad par ni ma yin no /
kṛtsnaṃ / / vimuktiparipācinyāḥ prajñāyā aparipakvatā ceti /
# rnam par grol ba'i yongs su smin par byed pa'i shes rab yongs su ma smin pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
vimuktyāvāhikāyāḥ prajñāyā akarmaṇyatā /
# rnam par grol ba thob par byed pa'i shes rab las su mi rung ba'o /
nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyā aprāptyatvād iti kecit /
# kha cig na re de ni nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i gnas ma thob pa'i phyir zhe'o /
anyetvāhuḥ nirvikalpā'tra prajñā vimuktiparipācinī tat prayogikā ca / dvitīyā / / tayor aparipakvatā tattvādhigamā'yogyatā tad upaniṣadbhāvā'yogyatā / cā'paripūrṇaṃbhāratvād yathākramam iti /
# gzhan dag na re rnam par mi rtog pa dang de la sbyor ba can gnyis ni / / 'dir rnam par grol ba yongs su smin par byed pa'i shes rab po / / de gnyis yongs su ma smin pa ni tshogs yongs su ma rdzogs pa'i phyir de kho na rtogs pa'i 'os ma yin pa dang de'i rgyu'i dngos po'i 'os ma yin pa ste go rims bzhin no zhe'o /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
darśanaheyakleśasya puṣṭavāsanākleśāvaraṇādīnām anyatamā'vaśiṣṭatā / prajñāparipākavibandhabhūtam ajñānaṃ sambhārā'paripūrṇatā ca /
# mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i bag chags brtas pa dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa la sogs pa'i lhag ma gzhan gang yang rung ba dang shes rab yongs su smin pa'i gegs su gyur pa mi shes pa dang tshogs yongs su ma rdzogs pa'o /
āvaraṇaprahāṇam anāvaraṇam iti / / āvaraṇaṃ prahīyate 'nenety āvaraṇāprahāṇam āvaraṇapratipakṣād / anāvaraṇaṃ bhāvanāmārgaḥ / / tasya trīṇi /
# sgrib pa spangs pa ni sgrib pa med pa zhes bya ba ni 'dis sgrib pa spong bar byed pas sgrib pa spong ba ste / / sgrib pa'i gnyen po yin pas sgrib pa med pa ni bsgom pa'i lam mo / / de'i sgrib pa gsum ni lhan cig skyes pa'i gnas ngan len zhes bya ba ni /
sahajaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ bhāvanāheyakleśā'nuśayaḥ / / sahajaṃ vātmadṛṣṭyādīnāṃ / dharmadhātusparśārthādiprativedhavibandhakasyā'kliṣṭasyā'jñānasyālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ
# bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i bag la nyal lo / / yang na bdag tu lta ba la sogs pa lhan cig skyes pa rnams dang chos kyi dbyings mchog gi don la sogs pa rtogs pa'i gegs byed pa nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa'i sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa yongs su gsos pa'o /
paripuṣṭabījaṃ / / kausīdyaṃ mohāṃśikādālasyāc cittā'nabhyutsāhaḥ /
# le lo ni snyom las te gti mug gi char gtogs pas sems mngon par mi spro ba'o /
pramādaś ca viṣayavyāsaṅgaḥ kuśale cā'navadhānaṃ /
# bag med pas ni yul la rnam par chags pa dang dge ba la mi 'jug pa'o /
samādher āsvādinā'tra pramāda ity eke /
# kha cig na re ting nge 'dzin gyi ro myang ba ni bag med pa'o zhe'o /
tatra dauṣṭhulyāc ca mārgaṃ na bhāvayati /
# de la gnas ngan len dang le los ni lam mi bsgom mo /
pramādād akuśalāc cittāṃ na rakṣati /
# bag med pas ni mi dge ba las sems mi srung ba'o /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ? / etad eva trayaṃ /
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na / / gsum po de nyid do /
pariṇātes trīṇi yair anyatra cittaṃ pariṇāmayatīti / / tatra pariṇatirutpannānāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ buddhatvaṃ eva cittena / niyamanaṃ / / tasyāstrīṇyāvaraṇāni /
# yongs su bsngo ba'i sgrib pa gsum ni gang dag gis sems gzhan du sngo bar byed kyi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mi bsngo zhes bya ba de la bsngo ba de ni dge ba'i rtsa ba skyes shing byung ba rnams sangs rgyas nyid du sems kyis nges par byed pa'o / / de la sgrib pa gsum ste /
katamāni trīṇi yair anyatra buddhatvāt saṃsāre śrāvakādibodho vā / cittaṃ pariṇāmayati nā'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksambandhau / / tāni punar bhavasaktir-bhogasakti-līnacittatā ca /
# gsum gang zhe na / / gang dag gis sangs rgyas nyid las gzhan du 'khor ba'am / / nyan thos la sogs pa'i byang chub tu sems yongs su sngo bar byed kyi / / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mi bsngo'o / / de dag kyang srid pa la chags pa dang longs spyod la chags pa dang sems zhum pa dang /
bhavaḥ pañcopādānaskandhāḥ /
# srid pa ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga rnams so /
bhujyanta iti bhogā rūpādayo viṣayāḥ / / tayor abhiṣvaṅgaḥ saktiḥ /
# spyad par bya ba na / / longs spyod de gzugs la sogs pa yul rnams so / / de dag la rnam par chags pa ni chags pa'o /
līnacittatā'nudāracittatā kva buddhatvaṃ kva ca madvidha / ityātmanyasambhāvanā /
# sems zhum pa ni sems rgya chung ba ste / / sangs rgyas nyid du ga la 'grub / / bdag lta bus ga la zhig ces bdag la mi srid par sems so /
tatra ca bhavasaktyā bhogasaktyā ca sugatau cittaṃ pariṇāmayati
# de la srid pa la chags pa dang longs spyod la chags pas ni bde 'gror sems sngo bar byed do /
līnacittatatyā śrāvakādiyāne pariṇāmayati kimatrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# sems zhum pas ni nyan thos kyi theg par sngo bar byed do / / 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
bhavabhogatṛṣṇā kausīdyam akāruṇyañca / [p.63] / atrāsasya trīṇi / / ko'yam atrāsaḥ ?
# srid pa dang longs spyod la sred pa dang le lo dang snying rje med pa'o / / mi skrag pa'i sgrib pa gsum ni zhes bya ba la / / mi skrag pa gang zhe na /
śūnyatāyāṃ gambhīrodāreṣu ca buddhabodhisattvadharmeṣv adhimuktir / abhīrutā /
# stong pa nyid dang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i chos zab cing rgya che ba la mos shing mi 'jigs pa'o /
asambhāvanā pudgale mahāyānanayābhidhyāyinaḥ pudgalasya / bhrāntyā'vagamo vacanañca, śīlasamādhiprajñādiguṇasya / vā'sampratyayaḥ /
# gang zag la mi srid snyam pa ni theg pa chen po'i tshul mngon par brjod pa'i gang zag la ma nor par khong du chud cing 'chad pa dang tshul khrims dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab la sogs pa yon tan la yid mi ches pa'o /
anadhimuktir dharme gambhīrodāranayapratipādake / buddhavacanatvenā'viparītā'rthena cā'sampratyayaḥ / / yathārutavicāraṇā'rthe /
# chos la mi mos pa ni sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab la tshul zab cing rgya che ba khong du chud par byed pa dang don ma log pa'o zhes yid mi ches pa'o /
anutpannā'niruddhādiśāntādyartha yathāśabdam eva pratipadyate na / cābhiprāyikārthatattvam avagacchati /
# don la sgra bzhin du spyod pa ni ma skyes pa dang ma 'gags pa dang gzod ma nas zhi ba la sogs pa'i don la sgra ji bzhin kho nar rtog par byed cing dgongs pa'i don gyi de kho na khong du mi chud pa ste /
tasmād anutpannādyarthā'nadhimuktiḥ /
# de'i phyir ma skyes pa la sogs pa'i don la mi mos so /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
vicikitsā-prajñā-samādhi-vipakṣabhūtajñānam-ābhiprāyikārthamitirūtavicāraṇā / vipakṣabhūtañceti / / amātsaryasya trīṇi /
# the tshom dang shes rab dang ting nge 'dzin gyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur pa mi shes pa dang dgongs pa'i don la spyod pa mi mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur pa'o / / ser sna med pa'i sgrib pa gsum ni zhes bya ba la /
amātsaryaṃ yataḥ saddharmasthitaye'nyānugrahārthaṃ vā dharmadeśanā / / saddharme'gauravaṃ acitrīkāraḥ /
# ser sna med pa ni gang gis dam pa'i chos gnas par bya ba'i phyir ram / / gzhan rjes su gzung ba'i phyir chos ston par byed pa'o / / dam pa'i chos la ched cher mi 'dzin pa ni gces su mi 'dzin pa ste /
tenā'nyasantānā'prāpaṇāc cirasthitikaṃ saddharmaṃ na karoti /
# des gzhan gyi sems kyi rgyud la go bar mi byed pa dang dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas par mi byed pa'o /
lābhasatkārapūjāyāṃ gauravaṃ citrīkāraḥ saddharmagaurave mā'nyo'pi / mattulyo'dhiko vā bhaviṣyatītyāśaṅkā /
# rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang mchod pa la ched cher mi 'dzin pa ni gces su mi 'dzin pa'o / / dam pa'i chos la ched cher 'dzin kyang / / bdag dang gzhan mtshungs sam lhag gi dogs te /
tasmāl lābhādivyavadhānaṃ bhaviṣyatīti bhītyā dharmaṃ na deśayati /
# de'i phyir rnyed pa la sogs pa'i bar chad du 'gyur bas 'jigs nas chos mi 'chad pa'o /
lābhasatkārādhyavasāne'vidyamāne'pi sattveṣvakāruñañceti sattveṣu
# rnyed pa dang bkur sti la lhag par zhen pa med kyang sems can rnams la snying rje med pa zhes bya ba ni /
karuṇābhāvān na deśayati /
# sems can rnams la snying rje med pas chos mi 'chad de /
na hyakāruṇikaḥ sattvaduḥkhenā'pakriyate / / kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# snying rje med pa ni sems can gyi sdug bsngal gyi gnod par mi 'gyur ro / / 'di la sgring [?] pa gang zhe na /
agauravaṃ lābhasakārasaktir akāruñañceti / / vaśitvasya trīṇi āvaraṇānītyarthaḥ /
# ched cher mi 'dzin pa dang rnyed pa dang bkur sti la chags pa dang snying rje med pa'o / / dbang gi sgrib pa gsum ni zhes bya ba la /
vaśitvaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ cittavaśitvānāmprāptir buddhatvaṃ / / tasya trīṇyāvaṇāni punar na jñāyanta ityata āha - yair vibhutvaṃ na / labhate iti /
# dbang ni sems kyi dbang rnam pa thams cad thob pas sangs rgyas nyid dbang ngo / / de'i sgrib pa gsum po dag mi shes pas de'i phyir / / gang dag gis dbang byed pa mi 'thob pa ste zhes bya ba smos so /
cittavaśitvapratibandhād vaśitvasya yair vaśitvaṃ na labhate tānyeva / vaśītvasyāvaraṇānītyāha /
# dbang byed pa ni sems kyi dbang la rag lus pa'i phyir / / gang dag gis dbang byed pa mi 'thob pa de nyid dbang gis sgrib pa'o zhes brjod do /
vibhutvam punar jñānaprahāṇaprabhāvasampannatā / / atha vā vaśitvaparyāye nirdiṣṭatvādyair vaśitvaṃ na labhata iti
# dbang byed pa ni ye shes dang spong ba dang mthu phun sum tshogs pa'o / / yang na gang dag gis dbang byed pa mi 'thob pa zhes bya ba ni dbang gi rnam grangs su bstan pa ste /
vṛddhatvaṃ na labhata ityarthaḥ /
# sangs rgyas nyid mi 'thob ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
śrutavyasanaṃ saddharmaśravaṇenā'tyantaviyogaḥ /
# thos pas phongs pa ni dam pa'i chos nyan pa dang gtan du bral ba ste /
bandhubhir atyantaviyogo bandhuvyasanaṃ / / tat punaḥ śrutavyasanaṃ saddharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarmaprabhavanād
# rtsa lag rnams dang gtan du bral ba la rtsa lag gis phongs pa'o zhes bya ba lta bu'o / / thos pas phongs pa de yang chos kyis phongs par 'gyur pa'i las skyes pas 'gyur te /
bhavati / / svadarśanaparāmarśasthitatvād akalyāṇamitrāśritatvād vā yair
# rang gi lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa la gnas pa'i phyir ram / / mi dge ba'i bshes gnyen la brten pa'i phyir /
avipratisārair mahāyānasūtrāntaḥ pratikṣipto mārabhāṣito'yam
# 'gyod pa med pa gang dag gis theg pa chen po'i mdos de la / / 'di ni bdud kyis smras pa dang ngan song gi rgyu ste /
apāyahetuśca nā'pyambuddhabhāṣita iti anyān api tasmād vicchindayanti [p.64] / likhitaṃ conmṛṣanti dāhayanti pāvayantītyādiprakāraiḥ / saddharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarmotpadyate / saddharmaśravaṇavidhurātmabhāvaparipuṣṭitaḥ / / asati śrutavyasane'lpaśrutatvaṃ jñānasambhārasyā'paripūritā āvaraṇam / iti prakṛtaṃ / / alpaśruto he na śaknoti dharmān pravivektum /
# 'di ni sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa ma yin no zhes spong ba dang gzhan dag kyang de la mos pa bzlog pa dang yi ger bris pa 'phyi ba dang sreg pa dang chur skyur ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis dam pa'i chos nyan pa dang mi ldan pa'i las kyi sa bon yongs su gsos pas / / dam pa'i chos kyis phongs par 'gyur ba'i las rab tu skye'o / / thos pas phongs par ma gyur na yang thos pa nyung ste / / ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su ma rdzogs pas sgrib po zhes sbyar ro / / thos pa nyung ba ni chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa mi nus so /
bahuśrutasyāpi samādher aparikarmtvañcāvaraṇam iti sambandhaḥ /
# mang du thos par gyur kyang ting nge 'dzin yongs su sbyong ba ma byas pa nyid kyang sgrib po zhes sbyar ro /
chandādīnām anyatamā'bhāvāt aparipūrṇatvād bhāvanāyāṃ / vā'ṣṭānāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇām anyatamābhāvāt samādher
# 'dun pa la sogs pa las gang yang rung ba zhig med pa'i phyir ram / / spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad po dag las gang yang rung ba zhig med pas / / bsgom pa yongs su ma rdzogs pa'i phyir ting nge 'dzin yongs su sbyang ba ma byas pa'o /
aparikarmitatvaṃ / / vajropamādīnāṃ vā buddhasamādhīnām apariniṣpannatvam aparikarmitatvaṃ
# yang na sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin rdo rje lta bu la sogs pa yongs su mi sgrub pa ni yongs su sbyang ba ma byas pa'o /
kimatrāvaraṇaṃ ?  dharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarma alpaśrutatvaṃ
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na / / chos kyis phongs par gyur pa'i las dang thos pa nyung ste /
duṣprajñatā samādhipratyanīkaścopakleśo layauddhatyādika iti // / { daśakāraṇāni }
# 'chal pa'i shes rab dang ting nge 'dzin dang mi mthun pa'i bying ba dang rgod pa la sogs pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'o /
[p.65] / tat punaretad āvaraṇam aprayogādikaṃ /
# sgrib pa 'di ni zhes bya ba ni sbyor ba med pa la sogs pa'o /
śubhādau vaśitvaparyantadaśavidhe vastuni /
# dge ba la sogs pa zhes bya ba ni / / dbang la thug gi bar du dngos po rnam pa bcu'o /
yatrā'rthe daśa kāraṇāni bhavantīti - utpattyādau prāptiparyante / yasminn arthe tadāvaraṇaviparyayeṇa prayogādīni
# don gang la byed rgyu rnam pa bcur 'gyur ba zhes bya ba ni skye ba la sogs pa nas / / 'thob pa la thug gi bar gyi don gang la sgrib pa de bzlog na /
samādhiparikarmitatvā'vasānāni daśakāraṇāni bhavanti /
# sbyor ba la sogs pa nas ting nge 'dzin yongs su sbyang ba byas pa la thug pa rnams ni byed rgyu bcur 'gyur ro /
atra cotpattyādikāraṇatvā'viśeṣād bhinnasyā'pi pratyekam apy / abhedanirdeśaḥ /
# 'dir ni so so tha dad kyang skye ba la sogs pa'i rgyu nyid du khyad par med pa'i phyir bye brag med par bstan to /
tad arthādhikāreṇety utpattyyādyarthādhipatyenetyarthaḥ teṣāṃ hi / śubhādīnām utpattyādikāraṇavibandhaṃ vartamānam utpattyādyāvaraṇam
# don de'i skabs kyis zhes bya ba ni skye ba la sogs pa'i don gyi dbang du byas zhes bya ba'i tha tshig ste / / 'di ltar dge ba la sogs pa de dag skye ba la sogs pa'i rgyu la gegs su gyur pa'i tshe na /
ucyate tadyathā kuḍyādikam ālokamāvṛnvat kāryasya cakṣur / vijñānasyāvaraṇam ucyate /
# skye ba la sogs pa la sgrib po zhes bya ste / / dper na rtsig pa la sogs pas snang ba bsgribs na / / de'i 'bras bu mig gi rnam par shes pa la yang sgrib po zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
evaṃ kṛtvaiṣāṃ daśānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ triṃśad āvaraṇaviparyayeṇa triṃśat
# de ltar byas na chos bcu po de dag gi sgrib pa sum cu po bzlog na byed rgyu sum cu bstan pa yin no /
kāraṇaṃ veditavyaṃ / / tatra śubhotpattikāraṇaṃ trīṇi - prayoga āyatanaprayogo yoniśaḥ prayogaś / ca / / tad yathā cakṣur ādaya ityatraiva dṛṣṭāntaḥ /
# de la dge ba skye ba'i byed rgyu gsum ni sbyor ba dang skye mched la sbyor ba dang tshul bzhin la sbyor ba'o / / 'di lta ste / / mig la sogs pa zhes bya ba ni 'dir dpe ste /
cakṣurādayo vijñānasyotpattikāraṇam eva sthityādikāraṇaṃ /
# mig la sogs pa ni rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i byed rgyu nyid yin gyi / / gnas pa la sogs pa'i byed rgyu ni ma yin no /
tatrā'prayogādayaḥ prayogādīnāṃ sākṣād vibandhe vartamānāḥ / paramparayā śubhotpatter api pratibandhakāḥ / / evam utpattyāvaraṇaṃ śubhe draṣṭavyam ityāha tasyotpādanīyatvād iti / śubhe sthityādyasambhavād utpattyāvaraṇam evaitad iti darśayati / / sthitikāraṇaṃ bodhau /
# de la sbyor ba med pa la sogs pa sbyor ba la sogs pa la mngon du gegs su gyur pa na gcig nas gcig tu brgyud de dge ba skye ba la yang gegs byed pas de bzhin du skye ba la sgrib pa ni dge ba la sgrib pa ste / / de'i phyir de bskyed par bya ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / dge ba la gnas pa la sogs pa mi srid pas skye ba'i sgrib pa nyid yin no zhes ston to / / byang chub la ni gnas pa'i byed rgyu yod de /
āśrayaparāvṛttir bodhiḥ āśrayo nirmalatathatā /
# byang chub ni gnas gyur pa'o / / de bzhin nyid dri ma med pa ni gnas pa'o /
atra kāraṇam āha - akopyatvād iti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / mi 'khrugs pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
yāval lokas tāvad avasthānād akopyatvaṃ, nā'nyathā bhavati vinivartate / vā /
# 'jig rten ji srid pa de srid du gnas pas mi 'khrugs pa ste / / gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang rnam par mi ldog pa'o /
śrāvakādīnān tu bodhiḥ svasantāna eva kṛtārthatvād vyāvartate /
# nyan thos la sogs pa'i byang chub ni bdag gi rgyu nyid kyi don byas nas rnam par ldog go /
bodhisattvā hi sarvasattvahitasukhādhyāśayena sambhāreṣu pravartamānā [p.66]
# byang chub sems dpa' ni sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde bar bya ba'i lhag pa'i bsam pas tshogs rnams la 'jug pa na /
āśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇatvād bodher yāvat sattvās tāvad avatiṣṭhantīty
# gnas par gyur pa'i mtshan nyid byang chub sems ji srid pa de srid du gnas par smon te /
ucyate na tv anutpattimātratvāc chrāvakādivat / / utpattiṃ vinā bhāvitatvāt tu sthiter utpattir apyatra bhavati /
# nyan thos la sogs pa ltar mi skye ba tsam gyi phyir ni ma yin no / / gnas pa ni skye ba med par mi 'gyur bas 'dir yang skye ba yod par 'gyur ro /
tasmād bodhisthitikāraṇam evocyate notpattikāraṇaṃ / / na cā'nyat tad vyatirekeṇa sthitikāraṇam astītyata etad evoktaṃ / / viśuddhatathatā vā bodhiḥ /
# de bas na byang chub kyi gnas pa'i byed rgyu nyid brjod kyi skye ba'i byed rgyu ni ma yin no / / de ma gtogs par gzhan gnas pa'i byed rgyu med pas de'i phyir de nyid bshad do / / yang na de bzhin nyid rnam par dag pa ni byang chub ste /
na tathātāyāḥ svabhāvavuśuddhātvād utpattir asti
# de bzhin nyid ngo bo nyid kyis rnam par dag pas skye ba med de /
kintarhyāgantukamlā'pagamād anyantam ebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ sthitirevocyate / notpattiḥ /
# glo bur gyi dri ma med par gyur na byed rgyu de dag gis gtan du gnas pa nyid ces brjod kyi skye ba ni ma yin no /
sthitikāraṇāni punar bodheḥ kuśalotpādo manasikāraḥ paripūrṇasambhāraś / ca / / atra ca śubhānutpattyādayaḥ kuśalotpatyādivibandhe vartamānā bodheḥ / sthitiṃ kurvantīti sthityāvaraṇam uktāḥ /
# byang chub kyi gnas pa'i byed rgyu ni dge ba'i rtsa ba skye ba dang yid la byed pa dang tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa'o / / 'dir yang dge ba la mi skye ba la sogs pa ni / / dge ba skye ba la sogs pa'i gegs su gyur pas byang chub kyi gnas pa la gnod pa byed pa'i phyir gnas pa'i sgrib pa zhes bshad do /
tadyathā catvāra āhārāḥ sattvānām ityatraiva nidarśanaṃ /
# gnas pa'i byed rgyu ni dper na sems can rnams kyi zas gzhi lta bu'o zhes bya ba ni / / 'dir dpe'o /
na hi kavaḍākārādibhir āhārair apūrvāḥ sattvā utpadyante / purvotpannās tu vyavasthāpyanta eva /
# kham gyis za ba'i zas la sogs pa ldan med pa'i sems can skyed par byed pa ni ma yin gyi / / sngar skyes pa rnams gnas par byed pa nyid do /
dhṛtikāraṇam iti / / dhṛtir bodhicittaṃ sarvakuśaladharmādhārabhūtatvāt / / atraiva nidarśanaṃ yadyasyādhārabhūtan tatra tasya dhṛtiḥ / dhāryate'neneti kṛtvā / / tadyathā bhājanalokaḥ sattvalokasyeti /
# rten pa'i byed rgyu zhes bya ba la rten ni byang chub kyi sems te / / dge ba'i chos thams cad kyi gzhir gyur pa'i phyir ro / / gang gi gnas su gang gyur pa de ni de'i rten te / / 'dis 'dzin pas dper na sems can gyi 'jig rten gyi snod kyi 'jig rten lta bu'o zhes bya ba ni 'dir dpe'o /
tat kāraṇaṃ gotraṃ kalyāṇamitrasampannatā cittā'parikhedatā ca /
# de'i byed rgyu ni rigs dang bshes gnyen phun sum tshogs pa dang sems yongs su mi skyo ba'o /
tatra dhṛtikāraṇaviruddhatvād gotravaidhuryādikandhṛter apyāvaraṇam / uktaṃ /
# de la rigs dang mi ldan pa la sogs pa ni rten pa'i byed rgyu dang 'gal bas rten la yang sgrib par bshad do /
etad evāha - dhṛtyāvaraṇaṃ samādāna āvaraṇaṃ
# de'i phyir rten gyi sgrib pa ni yang dag par 'dzin pa la sgrib ste /
bodhicittasyādhārabhūtatvād iti /
# byang chub kyi sems rgyur gyur pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
abhivyaktikāraṇaṃ dhīmattve bodhisattvasya prakāśanīyatvāt /
# gsal ba'i byed rgyu ni blo ldan byang chub sems dpa'i sgrib pa ste / / rab tu bstan par bya ba'i phyir ro /
tacca pratipattisampat sujanavāso duṣṭajanā'vāsaś ca /
# de yang sgrub pa phun sum tshogs pa dang skye bo rung ba dang 'grogs pa dang skye bo gnod par mi sems pa dang 'grogs pa'o /
atra dhīmattve pratipattivaidhuryād ayo'bhivyaktyāvaraṇatvenocyante /
# 'dir sgrub pa dang mi ldan pa la sogs pa ni blo ldan gsal ba'i byed rgyu dang 'gal bas gsal ba'i sgrib pa zhes bya ste /
ata evāha - abhivyaktyāvaraṇaṃ dhīmattve tasya prakāśanīyatvād iti /
# de'i phyir gsal ba la sgrib pa ni blo dang ldan pa la sgrib pa ste / / de bstan par bya ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
tad yathā - āloko rūpasyetyatraiva nidarśanaṃ /
# dper na gzugs kyi snang ba lta bu'o zhes bya ba ni 'dir dpe'o /
āloko hi rūpamātrasyā'bhivyaktikāraṇam eva notpattyādikāraṇaṃ / / vikāraṇam abhrāntau /
# snang ba ni gzugs 'ba' zhig gsal ba'i byed rgyu nyid yin te / / skye ba la sogs pa'i byed rgyu ni ma yin no / / 'gyur ba'i byed rgyu ni 'khrul ba med pa'i rgyu ste /
samāropā'pavādabhrāntiparivṛttyātmakatvād abhrāntir / darśanamārgo'bhrānter vikāra ucyate /
# sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa 'khul pa ldog pa'i bdag nyid yin pas 'khrul pa med pa ni mthong ba'i lam mo / / 'khrul pa med pa'i 'gyur ba zhes bya ba ste /
tadyathā bhasmādayaḥ kāṣṭhādīnāṃ / / tasya trīṇi kāraṇāni - viparyāsadauṣṭhulyopaghātaḥ / kleśādyāvaraṇānāṃ trayāṇām abhāvo [p.67] / vimukti-paripācinyāḥ prajñāyāḥ paripakvabhāvaḥ / / tadyathā agnyādayaḥ pākyādīnām iti /
# dper na shing sha ba la sogs pa'i thal ba la sogs pa lta bu'o / / de'i byed rgyu gsum ni phyin ci log gi gnas ngan len bcom ba dang nyon mongs pa la sogs pa'i sgrib pa gsum med pa dang rnam par grol ba yongs su smin par byed pa'i shes rab yongs su smin pa'o /
pākyo hyodanādikas taṇḍulādivilakṣaṇas tat santānāntarbhūtaḥ / / tat kāraṇaṃ cāgnyādi /
# dper na btso ba la sogs pa'i me la sogs pa lta bu'o zhes bya ba ni 'bras chan la sogs pa dang mi 'dra ba ste / / de'i rgyud du gtogs pa'o / / 'bras la sogs par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba de'i byed rgyu ni me la sogs pa'o /
viśleṣakāraṇam anāvaraṇe /
# 'bral ba'i byed rgyu ni sgrib pa med pa'i rgyu ste /
darśanamārgapraheyādāvaraṇāc cheṣam āvaraṇam anena prahīyata / ityanāvaraṇaṃ bhāvanāmārgaḥ / / tasya trīṇi kāraṇāni - sahajadauṣṭhulyopaghāto vīryam apramādaś ca /
# mthong ba'i lam gyis spangs bar bya ba'i sgrib pa las lhag ma dag 'dis spong bas sgrib pa med pa ni bsgom pa'i lam mo / / de'i byed rgyu gsum ni lhan cig skyes pa'i gnas ngan len bcom pa dang brtson 'grus dang bag yod pa'o /
teṣāñca viśleṣakāraṇapratipakṣatvāt /
# de dag kyang 'bral ba'i byed rgyu ste / / mi 'bral ba'i byed rgyu'i gnyen po yin pa'i phyir ro /
ata evāha - viśleṣāvaraṇam anāvaraṇe /
# de'i phyir 'bral ba la sgrib pa ni sgrib pa med pa la sgrib ste zhes bya ba smos so /
etad api viśleṣakāraṇapratipakṣabhāvenaivāvaraṇaṃ / / atraiva kāraṇam āha - tasyāvaraṇaviṣaṃyogatvād iti /
# de yang 'bral ba'i byed rgyu'i gnyen po'i dngos por sgrib ste / / 'dir rgyu smos pa /
visaṃyujyate'neneti viśleṣaḥ / / pariṇatikāraṇaṃ natau /
# de sgrib pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o / / 'dis 'bral bar byed pas 'bral ba'o / / bsgyur ba'i byed rgyu ni bsngo ba'i rgyu ste /
tasya mahābodhau kuśalamūlaprayojakalakṣaṇatvāt /
# des dge ba'i rtsa ba byang chub chen por sbyor ba'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir ro /
tat punar bhavabhogavaimukhyaṃ līnacittatā'bhāvaś ca /
# de yang srid pa dang longs spyod las phyir phyogs pa dang sems zhum pa med pa'o /
tataś ca pariṇatyāvaraṇaṃ pariṇatikāraṇavibandhena draṣṭavyaṃ /
# de'i phyir bsgyur ba ni byed rgyu'i gegs ni bsngo ba'i sgrib par blta bar bya'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ? / nater mahābodhau cittapariṇatilakṣaṇatvād iti / / sampratyayakāraṇam atrāse /
# ci'i phyir zhe na bsngo ba ni byang chub chen por sems yongs su bsngo ba'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni / / yid ches pa'i byed rgyu ni mi skrag pa'i rgyu ste /
tac ca pudgalasambhāvanā dharmā'dhimuktir ābhiprāyikārthā'dhigamaś ca
# de yang gang zag la srid do snyam pa dang chos la mos pa dang dgongs pa'i don khong du chud pa'o /
ebhir dharmaiḥ sampratyayo bhavatītyataś ca sampratyayakāraṇavibandhena / sampratyayāvaraṇamatrāse / / atraiva kāraṇam āha - asampratyayena trasanād iti /
# chos de rnams kyi yid ches par 'gyur bas de'i phyir yid ches pa'i byed rgyu'i gegs yin pas yid ches pa la sgrib pa ni mi skrag pa la sgrib ste / / 'dir rgyu smos pa / / yid mi ches pas skrag pa'i phyir ro zhes bya'o /
asampratyayena hi dharmasya trasyati / / sampratyāyanakaraṇamamatsaritve /
# yid mi ches pas ni chos la skrag par 'gyur ro / / yid ches par byed pa'i byed rgyu ni /
tat punaḥ saddharme gauravaṃ lābhasatkārapūjādinirapekṣatāa sattveṣu ca / kāruṇyaṃ /
# ser sna med pa'i rgyu ste / / de ni dam pa'i chos cher 'dzin pa dang rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang mchod pa la mi lta ba dang sems can rnams la snying rje ba'o /
sampratyayāyanakāraṇaviruddhatvāc ca sampratyāyanāvaraṇam amatsaritve / 'vasthāpyate /
# yid ches par byed pa'i rgyu dang 'gal bas yid ches par byed pa la sgrib pa ni / / ser sna med pa la sgrib par rnam par gzhag ste /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - dharmā'matsaritvena parasampratyāyanāditi /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa chos la ser sna med pas gzhen yid ches par byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
saddharme'gauravādito dharme mātsarye karoti / / dharmamātsaryeṇa ca pareṣāṃ dharmaṃ na deśayati / / ataḥ sampratyāyanāvaraṇam amatsaritva iti /
# dam pa'i chos ched cher mi 'dzin pa la sogs pas chos la ser sna byed par 'gyur ro / / chos la ser sna byed pas kyang gzhan rnams la chos 'chad par mi byed pas de'i phyir / / yid ches par byed pa la sgrib pas ni ser sna med pa la sgrib pa'o /
vaśitvasya trīṇi kāraṇāni - dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyakarmā'bhāvo / bahuśrutatvaṃ samādhiparikarmitatvañca /
# 'thob pa'i byed rgyu gsum ni chos kyis phongs par 'gyur ba'i las med pa dang mang du thos pa dang ting nge 'dzin yongs su sbyong bar byas pa'o /
tadviruddhatvāc cu tavyasanādikaṃ vaśitva āvaraṇaṃ vyavasthāpyate / / atraiva kāraṇam āha - tasya vaśitvasya vibhutvaprāptilakṣaṇatvād iti /
# de dang 'gal bas thos pas phongs pa la sogs pa ni dbang gi sgrib par rnam par gzhag ste / / 'dir rgyu smos pa / / dbang de la dbang byed pa 'thob pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
kecit tu śubhādīnām evam anukrame kāraṇam āhuḥ /
# kha cig na re dge ba la sogs pa'i go rims kyi rgyu ni 'di lta bu ste /
kuśaladharmopaṣṭabdhasatatir bodhiḥ prāptavyā /
# dge ba'i chos kyi sems kyi rgyud nye bar bstan pas byang chub 'thob pa'i skal ba yod de /
tata āditaḥ śubham uktaṃ /
# de'i phyir thog mar dge ba bshad do /
tad anantaraṃ bodhir uktā /
# de'i 'og tu byang chub bshad do /
bodhicittañcāgamyaitad ubhayasampādane samartho bhavati ā bodher / bodhicittasya sarvakuśaladharmādhārabhūtatvād atas tad anantaraṃ / bodhicittam uktaṃ /
# byang chub kyi sems ni chos dge ba'i chos thams cad kyi gzhir gyur pas byang chub kyi sems la brten nas / / byang chub la thug gi bar du de gnyi ga sgrub nus par 'gyur te / / de'i phyir de'i 'og tu byang chub kyi sems bshad do /
utpāditabodhicittasya ṣaṭpāramitāsu prayogaḥ kujanaduṣṭajanābhyāñca / parihāraḥ /
# byang chub kyi sems bskyed nas pha rol tu phyin pa drug la rab tu sbyor ba dang skye bo ngan pa dang skye bo sdang ba yongs su spong ste /
evam asya bodhisattvabhāvaḥ prakāśībhavati / [p.68]
# de ltar 'di'i byang chub sems dpa'i dngos po bstan pa yin no /
ataḥ samādānānantaraṃ dhīmatvam uktaṃ /
# de'i phyir yang dag par 'dzin pa'i 'og tu blo dang ldan pa bshad do /
evañca prayujyamāno viparyāsaṃ prajahāti aviparyastaṃ ca jñānam / utpādayati / / ato dhīmatvānantaram abhrāntir uktā sa punar darśanamārgaḥ / / tad abhyasanenāvaraṇaṃ vijahātītyatas tad anantaram āvaraṇaprahāṇam / anāvaraṇam uktaṃ /
# de ltar rab tu sbyor ba na phyin ci log spong zhing phyin ci log med pa'i ye shes kyang skyed par byed de / / de'i phyir blo ldan gyi 'og tu 'khrul pa med pa bshad do / / de ni mthong ba'i lam ste / / de la goms pas sgrib pa rnams spong bas de'i phyir / / de'i 'og tu sgrib pa spong ba'i sgrib pa med pa bshad do /
nirāvaraṇasya bhavabhogasaktyabhavād buddhatva eva mānasaṃ pariṇāmayati / nānyatreti / / atas tad anantaraṃ natiruktā /
# sgrib pa med na srid pa dang longs spyod la chags pa med pa'i phyir / / sangs rgyas nyid du yid kyis yongs su sngo bar byed kyi gzhan du ma yin no / / de'i phyir de'i 'og tu bsngo ba bshad do /
evam bhūtasya ca sugambhīreṣv api buddhadharmeṣu prāmodyotpatīratrāsa / ityatas tad anantaramatrāsa uktaḥ / / evaṃ dharmapratyakṣeṇa yena yenopāyena sattvavinayaṃ paśyati / tantamevopāyambhajata iti tasya kuto mātsaryambhaved ityatrāsānantaram / amātsaryam uktaṃ /
# de lta bur ni sangs rgyas kyi chos shin tu zab mo rnams la mchog tu dga' ba skye ste / / mi skrag pas de'i phyir de'i 'og tu mi skrag pa bshad do / / de ltar chos mngon sum du gyur pa thabs gang dang gang gis sems can 'dul bar mthong ba'i thabs de dang de la brten pas / / de la ser sna 'byung bar ga la 'gyur bas / / mi skrag pa'i 'og tu ser sna med pa bshad do /
evam prahīṇāvaraṇaḥ paripūrṇaśukladharmā ca bodhisattvaścittavaśitve / pravartata ityatas tad anantaraṃ vaśitvam uktaṃ / / eṣo'nukrama iti /
# de ltar sgrib pa spangs pa dang dkar po'i chos rnams yongs su rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sems la dbang bar 'gyur bas de'i phyir de'i 'og tu dbang bshad de / / go rims ni 'di'o zhe'o /
asmin paricchede āvaraṇaprasaṅga ityataḥ śubhādīnām utpatīkāraṇāny
# le'ur bcad pa 'dir sgrib pa'i skabs yin pas de'i phyir dge ba la sogs pa'i skye ba'i byed rgyu rnams ni /
āvaraṇavat sūtritāni / / prasaṅgāgatānām antaraślokena saṅgrahaḥ kriyate /
# sgrib pa bzhin du mdor mdzad pas skabs nas 'byung ba rnams par gyi tshigs su bcad pas sdud par mdzad do /
kāraṇaṃ daśadhotpattau sthitau dhṛtyāṃ prakāśane /
# byed rgyu bcu ni skye ba dang / / gnas pa brten dang bstan bya dang /
vikāraviśleṣanatipratyayaprāyaṇāptiṣu //
# 'gyur dang 'bral dang gzhan du dang / / yid ches go byed 'thob rnams la /
eṣa dvitīyo'ntaraśloka udāharaṇasaṅgrahārthaṃ -
# de ni dper brjod bsdu ba'i phyir / / bar gyi tshigs bcad gnyis pa ste /
cakṣurāhārabhūdīpa vahnyādis tad udāhṛtiḥ /
# mig dang zas sam mar me dang / / me la sogs pa de yi dpe /
dātraśilpajñatādhūmahetumārgādayo'pare // / iti // [p.69] / { bodhipakṣyapāramitābhūmiṣv āvaraṇāni }
# zor ba bzo shes du ba dang / / rgyu dang lam la sogs pa gzhan / / zhes bya ba'o / / phyogs dang pha rol phyin sa la / / sgrib pa dag ni gzhan yin no /
pūrvaṃ hyaviśeṣeṇa śubhaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ tadāvaraṇañca /
# sngar ni dge ba dang de'i sgrib pa bye brag tu ma phye bar bshad do /
idānīntu pakṣyetyādibhedena sādhāraṇā'sādhāraṇabhedena ca śubhaṃ / nirdiśati /
# da ni phyogs dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i bye brag dang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i bye brag gis ni dge ba bshad do /
vastvakauśalakausīdyaṃ
# gzhi la mi mkhas le lo dang /
ityādibhedena ca pakṣādīnām āvaraṇaṃ / / tatra sādhāraṇaṃ bodhipakṣāḥ śrāvakabodhisattvayor aviśeṣeṇa / tatrā'vikārāt /
# zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i bye brag gis ni phyogs la sogs pa'i dge ba la sgrib pa bshad do / / der gtogs pas nyan thos dang byang chub sems dpa' gnyi ga'i bya ba bye brag med pa'i phyir / / de la byang chub kyi phyogs ni thun mong ba'o /
asādhāraṇantu pāramitābhūmayo bodhisattvānāṃ karaṇaṃ bodhisattvānām
# pha rol tu phyin pa dang sa rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bya ba thun mong ma yin pa ste /
eva tadādhipatyāt / / pūrvañca śubhādihetvāvaraṇadvāreṇa phalāvaraṇam uktaṃ iha tu sākṣāt
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams nyid de la lhag par byed pa'i phyir ro / / sngar ni dge ba la sogs pa'i rgyu la sgrib pa'i sgo nas 'bras bu la sgrib par bshad do /
phalāvaraṇam eveti pūrvasmād anyad ucyate /
# 'dir ni 'bras bu la dngos su sgrib pa nyid de / / de bas na snga ma las gzhan zhes bya ba'o /
atha vā'prayogādibhyo vastvakauśalādikam anyadeveti tad anyad ucyate /
# yang na sbyor ba med pa la sogs pa las gzhi la mi mkhas pa la sogs pa gzhan nyid de / / de gzhan zhes bya ba'o /
athavā śubhaṃ bodhiścetyatra bodhisattvasyaivopāyasahitayoścaryāphalayor / aprayogādikam āvaraṇam uktaṃ iha tu śubhasyaiva / sādhāraṇasyā'sādhāraṇasya ca bodhipakṣādivibhāgena
# yang na dge ba dang byang chub ces bya ba ni / / 'dir byang chub sems dpa' nyid kyi thabs dang bcas pa'i spyod pa dang 'bras bu la sbyor ba med pa la sogs pa sgrib po zhes bshad do / / 'dir ni byang chub kyi phyogs la sogs pa rnam par 'byed pas /
vastvakauśalādikam aprayogādikād anyad āvaraṇaṃ veditavyaṃ / / tatra śrāvakādibhedena bodhitrayaṃ tadanurūpeṇa smṛtypasthānādayo / mārgaparyantā bodhipakṣā ity ucyate daśa pāramitā daśa ca bhūmayo / yathāsūtraṃ /
# gzhi la mi mkhas pa la sogs pa ni / / sbyor ba med pa la sogs pa las / / dge ba thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i sgrib pa gzhan du rig par bya'o / / de la nyan thos la sogs pa tha dad pas byang chub gsum ste / / de dag dang mthun pas dran pa nye bar gzhag pa la sogs pa nas lam la thug gi bar dag ni byang chub kyi phyogs rnams zhes bya'o / / pha rol tu phyin pa bcu dang sa bcu rnams ni mdo las ji skad 'byung ba bzhin no /
smṛty upasthāneṣu vastvakauśalam āvaraṇam iti / / tāni punaḥ [p.70]
# gzhi la mi mkhas pa ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la sgrib po zhes bya ba la /
kāyavedanācittadharmasmṛtyupasthānāni catvāri /
# de dag ni lus dang tshor ba dang sems dang chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa dang bzhi'o /
teṣām punar vastu kāyavedanācittadharmāḥ tad viṣayatvāt / / tatrāśrayam abhiniveśavastu kāyaḥ /
# de dag gi gzhi ni lus dang tshor ba dang sems dang chos rnams te / / de'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro / / de la gnas su mngon par zhen pa'i gzhi ni lus so /
ātmaparibhogābhiniveśavastu vedanā /
# bdag gi longs spyod du mngon par zhen pa'i gzhi ni tshor ba'o /
ātmābhiniveśavastu cittaṃ /
# bdag tu mngon par zhen pa'i gzhi ni sems so /
ātmasaṅkleśavyavadānābhiniveśavastu dharma iti /
# bdag kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar mngon par zhen pa'i gzhi ni chos rnams so /
kāyādiṣu yaḥ svasāmānyalakṣaṇā'navabodhaḥ sa tatrā'kauśalaṃ /
# lus la sogs pa'i rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid khong du ma chud pa gang yin pa de ni de la mi mkhas pa'o /
tatra svalakṣaṇam anekāśucidravyeṇa saṅgṛhītātmakatvaṃ kāyasya /
# de la lus kyi rang gi mtshan nyid ni mi gtsang ba du ma'i rdzas 'dus pa'i bdag nyid do /
sukhādisvabhāvo vedanāyāḥ / / viṣayaprativijñaptir vijñānasya/
# tshor ba'i ni bde ba la sogs pa'i rang bzhin no / / rnam par shes pa ni yul las so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
dharmāṇāṃ yathāsambhavaṃ /
# chos rnams kyi ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
sāmānyalakṣanampunarnityadukhaśūnya'nātmādyākārāḥ/
# spyi'i mtshan nyid ni mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa'i rnam pa'o /
athavā kāyādiṣv aśuciduḥKhā'nityā'nātmākāreṇā pratipattiḥ
# yang na lus la sogs pa la mi gtsang ba dang sdug bsngal ba dang mi rtag pa dang bdag med pa'i rnam par ma rtog pa'am /
śucisukhanityātmākāreṇa vā vikalpo vastv akauśalam yasmād ajñānaṃ
# gtsang ba dag bde ba dang rtag pa dag / / bdag gi rnam par rtog pa ni gzhi la mi mkhas pa ste / / 'di ltar mi shes pa'am /
darśaṇaṃ vā smṛtyupasthāneṣvāvaraṇaṃ / / prajñāsmṛtisvābhāvye sati smṛtyupasthānānāṃ kasmād vastvakauśalam
# lta ba ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la sgrib pa'o / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams ni shes rab dang dran pa'i rang bzhin yin na /
evāvaraṇam ucyate na tu vastvasmaraṇam apīti ?
# ci'i phyir gzhi la mi mkhas pa ni sgrib pa zhes brjod kyi / / gzhi mi dran pa ni ma yin zhe na /
prajñādhīnapravṛttitvāt / / tathā hi darśanātmakatvāt prajñāyāḥ prajñāpṛṣṭhalabdha ālambane
# shes rab kyi kha na las te 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / 'di ltar shes rab ni mthong ba'i bdag nyid kyi phyir te /
smṛtyādayaḥ pravartante na tu svātantryeṇa prajñāvat / / tasmān nā'smaraṇamatrāvaraṇam uktam iti / / sampyakprahāṇeṣu kauṣīidyaṃ / / kiṃ ? / āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ /
# shes rab kyi rjes las thob pa'i dmigs pa la dran pa la sogs pa rab tu 'jug gi / / shes rab bzhin du rang gi rgyud yod pa ni ma yin te / / de'i phyir mi dran pa ni sgrib pa zhes mi bshad do / / le lo ni yang dag par spong ba rnams la sgrib bo /
vīryaṃ hy atrotpannā'nutpannavipakṣaprahāṇā'nutpātaye / utpannapratipakṣasya bhūyobhāvotpādāya ca pravartamānaṃ / samyakprahāṇākhyāṃ pratilabhate / / tat punar bhedābhāve'pi phalabhedāc caturdhā vyavasthāpyata iti smṛtiḥ / ataḥ samyak prahāṇānāṃ vīryātmakatvād ālasyam āvaraṇam uktaṃ / / ṛddhipādeṣu samādher dvayahīnatāvaraṇam iti / / anenaddharyata ity ṛddhiḥ /
# brtson 'grus kyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs skyes pa dang ma skyes pa spong ba dang mi skyed pa dang gnyen po skyes pa dang ma skyes pa phyir zhing 'byung ba dang skyed pa'i phyir 'jug pa ni yang dag par spong ba zhes bya ba'i ming 'thob bo / / de ni dbyer med kyang 'bras bu tha dad pa'i phyir rnam pa bzhir gzhag go / / de bas na yang dag par spong ba rnams brtson 'grus kyi bdag nyid yin pas le lo ni sgrib par bshad do / / gnyis kyis ting nge 'dzin nyams pa dang zhes bya ba ni / / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la sgrib po / / 'dis rdzu 'phrul byed pas rdzu 'phrul te /
sā ca cchandavīryacittamīmāmsāsamādhiḥ /
# de yang 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin to /
saivardhhipādaḥ ākāśagamananirmāṇādikāyā ṛddheḥ pratiṣṭhābhūtatvāt
# de nyid rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang ba ste / / nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang sprul pa la sogs pa rdzu 'phrul gyi gnas su gyur ba'i phyir ro /
gamanaṃ vā ṛddhiḥ ākāśagamanādikā samṛddhir ityarthaḥ /
# yang na 'gro bas rdzu 'phrul te / / nam mkha' la 'gro ba la sogs pa 'byor pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tasyāḥ pādā ṛddhipādāḥ tadādhāratvāt /
# de'i rkang pa ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa ste / / de'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro /
saiva cchandasamādhyādicaturvidhā samādhiḥ /
# 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa rnam pa bzhi po de nyid ni ting nge 'dzin to /
tatracchandasamādhau chandaprādhānyaṃ tad dvāreṇa samādhilābhāt /
# de la 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin la 'dun pa gtso bo ste / / de'i sgo nas ting nge 'dzin 'thob pa'i phyir ro /
na tu vīryādayas tatra na santi chandasahāyatvād apradhānās tu te
# brtson 'grus la sogs pa yang de na med pa ni ma yin te / / 'dun pa'i grogs byed pa'i phyir /
tatreti na te prakāśitāḥ /
# de dag ni der gtso bo ma yin pas de dag mi bshad do /
evaṃ vīryacittamīmāṃsā samādhiṣu vācyaṃ /
# de bzhin du brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang brjod par bya'o /
samādher dvayahīnatāvaraṇam uktaṃ /
# gnyis kyis ting nge 'dzin nyams pa sgrib par bshad pa de mi shes te /
na taj jñāyate ata āha - aparipūryā ca cchandavīryacittamīmāṃsānām / anyatamavaikalyād bhāvanayā ca prahāṇasaṃskāravaikalyād iti /
# de'i phyir 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa rnams las gang yang rung ba zhig ma tshang ba yongs su ma rdzogs pa dang spong ba'i 'du byed bsgom pa ma tshang bas zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra paripūrihīnatā tāsāṃ chandavīryacittamīmāṃsānām / anyatamavaikalyāt tadādhipatyasya samādher abhāvād bhāvanā hīyata
# de la 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa de dag las gang yang rung ba zhig ma tshang bas yongs su bskal pa nyams te / / de'i dbang gis ting nge 'dzin med pa'i phyir ro /
ity aṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārāṇām anyatama-vaikalyaṃ /
# sgom pa nyams pa ni spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad po dag las ma tshang ba'i phyir ro /
te punaḥ śraddhācchandavīryapraśrabdhismṛtisamprajanyacetanopekṣātmakāḥ
# de dag ni dad pa dang 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang shin tu sbyangs pa dang dran pa dang shes bzhin dang sems pa dang btang snyoms kyi bdag nyid do /
eṣāṃ hi prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ bhāvanayā samādhau vaśitvam avāpyate
# spong ba'i 'du byed 'di dag bsgoms na ting nge 'dzin la dbang thob ste /
nānyathetyata eṣāṃ vaikalyād bhāvanāhīnateti na samādhau vaśitvam / avāpyate /
# gzhan du ma yin no / / de bas na de dag ma tshang na sgom pa nyams pa zhes bya ste / / ting nge 'dzin la dbang mi thob bo /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
chandādipratipakṣāṇāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāñca vipakṣopakleśaḥ yaduta
# 'dun pa la sogs pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang spong ba'i 'du byed kyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'o /
kausīdyatṃ ālambanasampramoṣaḥ layauddatye'saṃskāraḥ saṃskāraśceti /
# 'di lta ste / / le lo dang dmigs pa brjed pa dang bying ba dang rgod pa dang 'du mi byed pa dang 'du byed pa'o /
indriyeṣu mokṣabhāgīyānām aropaṇam iti / / saṃsārād uttrasto mokṣam adhikṛtya [p.71]
# thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams mi skyed pa ni dbang po rnams la sgrib po zhes bya ba ni 'khor bas skrag ste /
kuśalamūlam abhisaṃskaroti tena mokṣalābhaniścayāt mokṣabhāgīyam ucyate / tasmiścāropite śraddhādaya indriyākhyāṃ pratilabhante nānyathetyato
# thar pa'i dbang du byas nas dge ba'i rtsa ba gang mngon par 'du byed pa des thar pa rnyed par nges pas / / thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa zhes bya'o / / de bskyed na dad pa la sogs pa dbang po'i ming 'thob par 'gyur te /
mokṣabhāgīyānām aropaṇam indriyeṣv āvaraṇam uktaṃ /
# gzhan du ma yin pas thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa mi skyed pa ni dbang po rnams la sgrib par bshad do /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# de la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
yenopakleśena mokṣabhāgīyaṃ na rocyate /
# nye ba'i nyon mongs pa gang gis thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa mi skyed pa ste /
sā punar bhavasaktir nirvāṇabhītiś ca / / baleṣu teṣām evendriyāṇāndaurbalayaṃ /
# de ni yang srid pa la chags pa dang mya ngan las 'das pas 'jigs pa'o / / dbang po de dag gi nyam chung ba ni stobs rnams la sgrib po /
āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ / / katham punar indriyāṇān daurbalyam ityata āha - vipakṣavyavakiraṇād iti
# dbang po rnams kyi nyam chung ba ji lta bu zhe na / / de'i phyir mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang 'dre ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
āśraddyakausīdyam uṣitasmṛtivikṣepaduṣprajñātmakena / vipakṣeṇābhibhūtatvād ityarthaḥ / / indriyāṇi hy uṣmagata mūrdhānābhyāṃ prabhāvitāni /
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma dad pa dang le lo dang brjed ngas pa dang gyeng ba dang 'chal ba'i shes rab kyi bdag nyid kyis zil gyis mi gnon zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / do par gyur pa dang rtse mos rab tu phye ba dag ni dbang po rnams so /
etac ca dvividham api nirvedhabhāgīyān durbalam / aśraddhyādivipakṣābhibhavāt / / ata eva tasmāt parihāṇisambhavaḥ /
# nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnam pa gnyis po 'di ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma dad pa la sogs pas zil gyis non pa'i phyir nyam chung ba ste / / de'i phyir 'di las yongs su nyams pa srid do /
nirjitavipakṣatvāt tu śraddhādīni kṣāntyagradharmāvasthāyāṃ / balākhyāmpratilabhante /
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs thul bas bzod pa dang 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog gi dus na dad pa la sogs pa stobs kyis ming 'thob po /
tasmād yat teṣām eva śraddhādīnām uṣmagatamūrdhānāvasthāyāṃ / vipakṣā'bhibhavād daurbalyantad balānām āvaraṇaṃ / / tasmin sati balā'vasthā'sambhavād iti /
# de'i phyir dad pa la sogs pa de dag nyid dro bar gyur pa dang rtse mo'i dus na mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyis zil gyis non nas nyam chung ba gang yin pa de ni stobs rnams la sgrib ste / / de yod na stobs kyi bye brag mi srid do /
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
sa evāśraddhyādiko vipakṣaḥ /
# ma dad pa la sogs pa mi mthun pa'i phyogs de nyid do /
bodhyaṅgeṣu dṛṣṭidoṣaḥ / / āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ / / bodhir hyatra darśanamārgo'bhipretaḥ / / tasyāstāni
# lta ba'i nyes pa ni byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la sgrib po / / byang chub ni 'dir mthong ba'i lam la dgongs pa ste /
smṛti-dharmapravicaya-vīrya-prīty-praśrabdhi-samādhy-upekṣātmakāni / sapta bodhyaṅgāni darśanaheyakleśaprahāṇakāla utpadyanta ityaṅgānīty
# de'i dran pa dang chos rnam par 'byed pa dang brtson 'grus dang dga' ba dang shin du sbyangs pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms kyi bdag nyid byang chub kyi yan lag bdun po de dag ni mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa spong ba'i dus na 'byung bas yan lag rnams zhes bya'o /
ucyate / / yadi tu bodheranukūlatvād aṅgāni syur evaṃ smṛtyupasthānādīnām api / bodhyaṅgatvamprasajyeta / / katham idaṃ bodhyaṅgeṣu dṛṣṭidoṣa āvaraṇam ityata āha - teṣān
# gal te byang chub dang mthun pas yan lag tu 'gyur ro zhe na / / de lta na ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyang byang chub kyi yan lag nyid du thal bar 'gyur ro / / lta ba'i nyes pa ni byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la sgrib po zhes bya ba de ji lta zhe na /
darśanamārgaprabhāvitatvād iti darśanamārgavyavasthāpitatvād ity / arthaḥ /
# de'i phyir de dag mthong ba'i lam gyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te / / mthong ba'i lam du rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
kaḥ punar anyadṛṣṭidoṣaḥ ?
# lta ba'i nyes pa 'di gang zhe na /
parikalpitāḥ pañca dṛṣṭayo vicikitsā'vidayā tadālambanāṣca rāgādayaḥ / sasamprayogāḥ kleṣopakleṣāḥ / / nanu vicikitsā'dayopya attrāvaraṇaṃ / / āvaraṇambhavatu /
# kun brtags pa'i lta ba rnam pa lnga dang the tshom dang ma rig pa dang de la dmigs pa'i 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa rnams so / / the tshom la sogs pa yang 'dir sgrib pa ma yin nam zhe na /
iha tu pradhānavivakṣayā dṛṣṭidoṣopadeśa iti na teṣām anupadeśo / virudhyate /
# sgrib pa yin du zin kyang 'dir gtso bor brjod par bzhed pas lta ba'i skyon smos pa'i phyir de dag ma smos kyang 'gal ba med do /
teṣāñca dṛṣṭyādīnām ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ bījam eva / darśanamārgapraheyatvāt tad āvaraṇam ucyate /
# lta ba la sogs pa de rnams kyi sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa nyid mthong ba'i lam gyis spong ba'i phyir de'i sgrib pa zhes bya'o /
mārgāṅgeṣu samyag / dṛṣṭisaṃkalpakarmāntājīvavyāyāmasmṛtisamādhyākhyeṣū dauṣṭhulyadoṣa / āvaraṇam iti prastutaṃ /
# gnas ngan len gyi nyes pa ni lam gyi yan lag yang dag par lta ba dang rtog pa dang ngag dang las kyi mtha' dang 'tsho ba dang; rtsol ba dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin rnams la sgrib ste /
atraiva kāraṇaṃ āha - teṣām mārgāṅgānāṃ / bhāvanāmārgaprabhāvitatvād iti bhāvanāmārgavyavasthāpitatvād /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / lam gyi yan lag de dag bsgom pa'i lam gyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste / / bsgom pa'i lam la rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir ro /
kaḥ sa dauṣṭhulyadoṣaḥ ?
# gnas ngan len gyi nyes pa de gang zhe na /
vyāsataḥ satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭī sahaje sasamprayoge tadālambanā / viṣayālambanāś ca rāgādayaḥ kleśopakleśāḥ sasamprayogāḥ /
# rgyas par bya ba na ni 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin pa'i lta ba lhan cig skyes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa dang de la yang dmigs pa yul la yang dmigs pa 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa rnams te /
teṣām ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ yad bījantad dauṣṭhulyaṃ /
# de dag gi sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa gang yin pa de ni gnas ngan len to /
saṅkṣepatas tu darśanaprahātavyād anyā sāsravā tacchaktir
# mdor bsdu na mthong bas spang bar bya ba las gzhan pa zag pa dang bcas pa ste /
ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā dauṣṭhulyaṃ /
# de'i nus pa kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa ni gnas ngan len to /
tac ca bhāvanāmārgapraheyatvān mārgāṅgeṣv āvaraṇatvena / vyavasthāpyate / / uktaṃ bodhipakṣeṣvāvaraṇaṃ //2-11// [p.72]
# de ni bsgom pa'i lam gyis spang bar bya ba yin pas lam gyi yan lag gi sgrib par rnam par gzhag go / / byang chub kyi phyogs rnams la sgrib pa ni bshad zin to /
{ pāramitāsvāvaraṇāni } / tad anantaramparāramitāsu vaktavyam ityata āha - pāramitāsvāvaraṇaṃ
# de'i 'og tu pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi bshad dgos pas de'i phyir / / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la sgrib pa ni /
aiśvaryasyā'tha sugateḥ sattvā'tyāgasya cāvṛtiḥ / / iti vistaraḥ /
# phyug po dang ni bde 'gro dang / / sems can mi gtong sgrib pa dang / / zhes rgya cher smos so /
atra daśānāṃ pāramitānāṃ yasyāḥ pāramitāyā yat phalaṃ tadāvaraṇena / tasyā āvaraṇam udbhāvitaṃ /
# 'di la pha rol tu phyin pa bcu po dag gi pha rol tu phyin pa gang gi 'bras bu gang yin pa de la sgrib pas de'i sgrib pa zhes brjod pa yin no /
kimatra kāraṇaṃ yan mātsaryādayo vastuto dānādivibandhe vartamānas tat / phalāvaraṇatvenocyante na punaḥ pāramitāvaraṇatveneti ?
# 'di la ser sna la sogs pa sbyin pa la sogs pa la dngos su gegs byed pa bzhin du ci'i phyir de'i 'bras bu la sgrub par brjod la / / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la sgrib par ni ma bshad ce na /
tat phalārthena dānādau sarvaḥ pravartate / / tasmān mātsaryādiprahāṇa ādarotpādanārthaṃ phalāvaraṇam uktaṃ na / pāramitāvaraṇam iti /
# de'i 'bras bu'i don du sbyin pa la sogs pa la thams cad 'jug ste / / de bas na ser sna la sogs pa spang bar nan tan bskyed pa'i phyir 'bras bu la sgrib par bshad de / / pha rol tu phyin pa rnam la sgrib par ni ma yin no /
athavā mātsaryādikam āvaraṇam aiśvaryādivipakṣabhūtaṃ / dāridryādiphalaṃ janayadaiśvaryādiphalapratibandhāt tadāvaraṇam ucyate / kintāsāmphalaṃ ?
# yang na ser sna la sogs pa sgrib pa phyug po la sogs pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur pa dbul po la sogs pa'i 'bras bu bskyed pa na phyug po la sogs pa'i 'bras bu la gegs byed pas de'i sgrib pa zhes bya'o / / de dag gi 'bras bu gang zhe na /
tatra dānapāramitāyāḥ phalaṃ prādhānyenaiśvaryādhipatyaṃ / / śīlapāramitāyāḥ sugatiḥ /
# de la sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni gtso bor ni phyug po dang bdag po'o / / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni bde 'gro'o /
kṣāntipāramitāyāḥ sattvā'parityāgaḥ / / vīryapāramitāyā doṣaguṇahānivṛddhī /
# bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni sems can yongs su mi gtong ba'o / / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni nyes pa dang yon tan 'bri ba dang 'phel ba'o /
dhyānapāramitāyāḥ śāsane sattvāvatāraṇaṃ / / prajñāpāramitāyā guruvimocanaṃ /
# bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni bstan pa la sems can 'dzud pa'o / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni btsud pa de rnams rnam par grol bar byed pa'o /
upāyakauśalyapāramitāyāṃ bodhipariṇāmanayā kuśalā'kṣayatvaṃ / / prāṇidhānapāramitayāḥ śubhanairantaryaṃ /
# thabs la mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni byang chub tu yongs su bsngo bas dge ba mi zad pa'o / / smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni dge ba rgyun mi 'chad pa'o /
balapāramitāyāḥ kuśaladharmaniyatīkaraṇaṃ /
# stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni dge ba'i chos nges par 'byed pa'o /
jñānapāramitāyā dharmopabhogaḥ sattvaparipācanañca /
# ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni chos la longs spyod pa dang sems can yongs su smin par byed pa'o /
aiśvaryādhipatyāvaraṇam iti / / tatraiśvaryaṃ dhanopakaraṇabahulatā /
# phyug po dang bdag po la sgrib ces bya ba la / / de la phyug po ni nor dang yo byad mang ba'o /
ādhipatyaṃ [p.73] / tad upabhogavaśitvaṃ /
# bdag po ni longs spyod de la dbang ba'o /
asyobhayasyāvaraṇam āvaraṇaṃ dānapāramitāyās tat phalatvāt / / kim punas tat ? / mātsaryaṃ /
# de gnyi ga la sgrib pa ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgrib pa ste / / de'i 'bras bu yin pa'i phyir ro / / de gang zhe na ser sna'o /
sugatyāvaraṇam iti /
# bde 'gro la sgrib ces bya ba la /
śobhanā gatiḥ sugatiḥ manuṣyo devaś ca /
# mdzes par 'gro ba ni bde 'gro ste mi dang lha'o /
tasyāvaraṇam āvaraṇaṃ śīlapāramitāyās tat phalatvāt / / tat punar dauśīlyaṃ kutsitaṃ kāya-vāk-karma / / sattvā'parityāga iti / / upakārivad apakārisattvopādānaṃ /
# de la sgrib pa ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgrib pa ste / / de'i 'bras bu yin pa'i phyir ro / / de ni 'chal ba'i tshul khrims te / / lus dang ngag gi las ngan pa'o / / sems can yongs su mi gtong ba zhes bya ba ni sems can gnod par byed pa la yang phan 'dogs pa bzhin du 'dzin pa ste / / de yang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu'o /
etac ca kṣānti phalaṃ tadāvaraṇaṃ krodhaḥ / / doṣaguṇahānibuddhī iti /
# de'i sgrib pa ni khro ba'o / / nyes pa dang yon tan 'bri zhing 'phel ba zhes bya ba la /
svaparā'pakāraprayuktānām utpannānāṃ prahāṇaṃ / anutpannānāñcā'nutpādo doṣāṇāṃ hāniḥ /
# bdag dang gzhan la gnod pa rab tu zhugs pa skyes pa rnams spong ba dang ma skyes pa rnams mi skyed pa ni nyes pa rnams 'bri ba'o /
svaparā'nugrahapravṛttānām utpannānāṃ / bhūyobhāvo'nutpannānāñcotpādo vṛddhiḥ / / kiṃ punar atrāvaraṇaṃ ? / kausīdyaṃ /
# bdag dang gzhan la phan par zhugs pa skyes pa rnams phyir zhing 'byung ba dang ma skyes pa rnams skyed pa ni yon tan rnams 'phel ba'o / / 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na le lo'o /
vineyāvatāraṇāvaraṇam iti /
# 'dul ba 'dzud pa la sgrib ces bya ba la /
vineyānāṃ śāsane'vatāraṇaṃ / svargā'pavargalābhakāraṇatvenā'bhyupagamāt /
# 'dul ba rnams bstan pa la 'dzud pa ni mtho ris dang byang grol rnyed pa'i rgyur khas len pa'i phyir ro /
upaśāntyā gaurava utpadyamāne sattvāḥ sañjalparddhyāpryatnena / śāsanampratipadyante / / atra ca vikṣepa āvaraṇaṃ / / vimocanāvaraṇam iti / / vimocanaṃ kleśaprahāṇaṃ / / taccā'nuśāsanyā bhavati anuśāsanī ca prajñā nā'nyathetyataḥ / prajñāpāramitāphalaṃ vimocanaṃ / / tadāvaraṇaṃ kliṣṭaprajñā moho duṣprajñā vā / / dānādyakṣayatvāvaraṇam iti /
# nye bar zhi bas gus pa skye ste sems can kun brjod pa dang rdzu 'phrul gyis bsgrib mi dgos par bstan pa rtogs par byed do / / 'di la sgrib pa ni gyeng ba'o / / rnam par grol bar byed pa la sgrib ces bya ba la rnam par grol bar byed pa ni nyon mongs pa spong ba ste / / de yang rjes su bstan pas 'gyur ro / / rjes su bstan pa ni shes rab kyis te / / gzhan gyis ma yin no / / de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni rnam par grol bar byed pa'o / / de'i sgrib pa ni nyon mongs pa can gyi shes rab bam / / gti mug gam / / 'chal pa'i shes rab po / / sbyin pa la sogs pa mi zad pa la sgrib ste zhes bya ba ni sbyin pa dang tshul khrims la sogs pa mi zad pa la sgrib pa gang yin pa de ni /
dānaśīlādīnām akṣayatve yadāvaraṇam tad upāyapāramitāyā āvaraṇaṃ
# thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgrib pa'o / / sbyin pa la sogs pa de yang ji ltar mi zad par 'gyur zhe na /
tat punar dānādyakṣayatvaṃ kathambhavatītyata āha - bodhipariṇāmanayā
# de'i phyir / / byang chub tu yongs su bsngo bas de mi zad pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
tad akṣayatvād iti / / mahābodhipariṇataṃ dānādi kuśalamūlaṃ na kṣīyate buddhatvam iva /
# byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pa'i sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ni sangs rgyas nyid bzhin du zad par mi 'gyur ro /
tadāvaraṇaṃ mahābodhipariṇāmanā lakṣaṇā'nupāyajñatetyeke /
# kha cig na re de'i sgrib pa ni byang chub chen por yongs su bsngo ba'i mtshan nyid kyi thabs mi shes pa'o zhe'o /
anupāyakauśalyaṃ trimaṇḍalagrāhas tadāvaraṇam ity anye /
# gzhan dag na re thabs mi mkhas pa 'khor gsum du 'dzin pa ni de'i sgrib pa'o zhe'o /
sarvajanmasu kuśalanairantarya pravṛttyāvaraṇam iti /
# tshe rabs thams cad du dge ba rgyan mi 'chad par 'byung ba la sgrib ces bya ba la /
kuśalanairantaryaṃ pratidinaṃpratikṣaṇaṃ vā /
# dge ba rgyun mi 'chad pa ni nyin re'am skad cig re re la ste /
tac ca praṇidhānapāramitāyāḥ phalaṃ /
# de yang smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu'o /
katham ityata āha - praṇidhānavaśena tad anukūlopapattiparigrahād iti /
# ji lta zhe na / / de'i phyir smon lam gyi dbang gis de dang mthun pa'i skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
praṇidhāvaśena hi dānādīnāṃ nairantaryapravṛttyā 'nuguṇām upapattiṃ / parigṛhṇāti /
# smon lam gyi dbang gis sbyin pa la sogs pa rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ba dang mthun pa'i skye ba yongs su 'dzin to /
tasyāvaraṇaṃ dānādyanukūlopapattāv apraṇidhānaṃ /
# de la sgrib pa ni sbyin pa la sogs pa dang mthun par smon lam mi 'debs pa'o /
tasyaiva kuśalasya niyatīkaraṇāvaraṇam iti / / pratidinaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ vā niyatīkaraṇaṃ niścayaḥ /
# dge ba de nyid nges par byed pa la sgrib ces bya ba ni nyin re'am skad cig re re la gcig tu byed pa ni nges par byed pa'o /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalābhyāṃ / vipakṣā'nabhibhavād iti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / so sor brtags pa dang bsgoms pa'i stobs kyis mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyis zil gyis mi gnon pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
atra pratisaṃkhyānabalaṃ dhairyasahitā prajñā /
# de la so sor brtags pa'i stobs ni bstan pa dang ldan pa'i shes rab bo /
dhairyaṃ punaḥ prajñaptidharmaḥ / / sahaje vīryasamādhiprajñātraye pratisaṃkhyānatvāt /
# brtan pa ni btags pa'i chos te; brtson 'grus dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab gsum lhan cig skyes pa la btags pa'i phyir ro /
bhāvanābalam abhyāsasahitenā'prayatnena [p.74] / dānādiṣu pravartanaṃ tat pratipakṣeṇa mātsaryādinā'nabhibhavāt /
# bsgom pa'i stobs ni goms pa dang ldan pas bsgrim mi dgos par sbyin pa la sogs pa la 'jug pa'i phyir / / de'i gnyen po ser sna la sogs pas zil gyis mi non pa'i phyir ro /
kimatrāvaraṇaṃ ?
# 'di la sgrib pa gang zhe na /
apratisaṃkhyānabhāvanā daurbalyaṃ /
# so sor ma brtags pa dang bsgom pa nyam chung ba'o /
ātmaparayor dharmasambhogaparipācanāvaraṇam iti / / sambhogikāparṣanmaṇḍale vyavasthānaṃ gambhīrodāramahāyānadharmasya
# bdag dang gzhan chos la longs spyod pa dang yongs su smin par byed pa la sgrib ces bya ba ni longs spyod pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du rnam par gnas te /
sambhogo vicitrākārair nirmāṇakarmābhidharmadeśanayā sattvaparipākaś / ca phalaṃ /
# theg pa chen po'i chos zab cing rgya che ba la longs spyod pa dang sprul pa rnam pa sna tshogs kyi las kyis tshes ston pas sems can yongs su smin par byed pa ni 'bras bu'o /
tadāvaraṇam punar yathābhūtaśrutārthavicāraṇā mandaprajñatā / cāvaraṇam iti /
# de'i sgrib pa ni thos pa'i don la sgra ji bzhin du spyod pa dang shes rab chung ba ni sgrib po zhes bya'o /
atra ca dravyataḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ nāmato daśa / / prajñāpāramitāprabhāvitatvāc catasṛṇām pāramitānāṃ /
# 'di la rdzas su ni pha rol tu phyin pa drug go / / ming du ni bcu ste / / pha rol tu phyin pa bzhi ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
tatra prajñāpāramitā lokottaranirvikalpajñānaṃ / / tena jñānena krameṇa sarvāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ /
# de la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes te / / ye shes des sgrib pa thams cad rim gyis spang ngo /
upāyapraṇidhānabalajñānapāramitāḥ punar / lokottaramārgapṛṣṭhalabdhajñānasaṅgṛhītāḥ /
# thabs dang smon lam dang stobs dang ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi rjes las thob pa'i ye shes kyis bsdus so /
jñānapāramitā prakṛṣṭā satī kathaṃ na nirvikalpa iti ?
# ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mchog yin na ji ltar rnam par mi rtog pa ma yin zhe na /
jñānapāramitā hi nirvikalpajñānapṛṣṭalabdhajñānaṃ /
# ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa na rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi rjes las thob pa'i ye shes te /
taj jñānāvabuddhatvaṃ paricchidya svayaṃ ca dharmasambhogaṃ / pratyanubhavati parāṃś ca pratipācayati /
# ye shes des khong du chud pa yongs su bcad nas bdag nyid kyang chos la longs spyod pa rab tu myong la / / gzhan dag kyang yongs su smin par byad pa yin te /
tac caitan nirvikalpe dvayam api nāstītyato na nirvikalpā / jñānapāramiteti / / uktaṃ pāramitānām āvaraṇaṃ //2-13// / { bhūmiṣvāvaraṇāni } [p.75} / tad anantaraṃ bhūmiṣu vaktavyam ityata āha - bhūmau punar yathākramaṃ
# 'di gnyi ga yang rnam par mi rtog pa la med pas de'i phyir ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rnam par mi rtog pa ma yin no / / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi sgrib pa ni bshad zin to /
sarvatragā'rthe agrārthe niṣyandāgrārtha eva ca /
# de'i 'og tu sa rnams kyi brjod dgos pas de'i phyir / / sa rnams la yang go rims bzhin te / / kun du 'gro don mchog gi don /
iti vistaraḥ / / tatra bhūmayo daśa -
# zhes rgya cher smos so / / de la sa ni bcu ste /
pramuditā-vimalā-prabhākarī-arciṣmatī-sudurjayā-abhimukhī-dūraṅgamā-acalā-sādhumatī-dharmameghā / ca /
# rab tu dga' ba dang dri ma med pa dang 'od byed pa dang 'od 'phro can dang shin tu sbyang dka' dang mngon du gyur ba dang ring du song ba dang mi gyo ba dang legs pa'i blo gros dang chos kyi sprin no /
tatra dharmādhātoḥ sarvatragādyarthe'dhigamād / avakāśaviśeṣottarottarottarapratipattisthānarūpeṇa tad / utpannaguṇavasturūpeṇa ca bhūmaya ucyante / / dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragādyarthe yena yena vihāreṇa bodhisattvo bahulaṃ / viharati tasmin tasmin vihāre'vasthānārthena bhūmyākhyet pare / / vyavasthānampunar bhūmibhiḥ pramuditāyāṃ darṣanamāgotpattitvād
# de la chos kyi dbyings la kun tu 'gro ba la sogs pa'i don du khong du chud pa'i gnas skabs kyi khyad par rnams ni gong nas gong du khong du chud pa'i gnas pa'i tshul dang de las skyes pa'i yon tan gyi gzhi'i tshul gyi sa rnams zhes bya'o / / gzhan dag na re chos kyi dbyings kun du 'gro ba la sogs pa'i don la gnas pa gang dang gang gis byang chub sems dpa' mang du gnas pa'i gnas pa de dang de la gnas pa'i phyir sa zhes bya'o zhe'o / / sa rnams kyi rnam par gzhag pa ni rab tu dga' ba la mthong ba'i lam skye ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' chos mngon par rtogs so /
bodhisattvodharmamabhisameti/ / abhisamita dharmo vimalāyāṃ svarasavāhinam adhiśīlaṃ śikṣāviśeṣaṃ
# chos mngon par rtogs nas dri ma med pa la rang gi ngang gis 'byung ba lhag pa'i tshul khrims bslab pa'i khyad par sgrub ste /
niṣpādayati sarvasūkṣmāpatīdauśśīlyavigamāt /
# ltung ba phra mo'i 'chal ba'i tshul khrims thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
prabhākaryāṃ janmāntare'py acyavanadharmakarmā'dhicittaṃ śikṣāviśeṣaṃ / niṣpādayati /
# 'od byed pa la ni tshe rabs gzhan du yang chos las mi nyams pa lhag pa'i sems bslab pa'i khyad par sgrub po /
arciṣmatīsudurjayā'bhimukhīṣu bodhipakṣasatyapratītyasamutpādālambanam / adhiprajñaṃ śikṣāviśeṣaṃ niṣpādayati /
# 'od 'phro can dang shin tu sbyang dka' dang mngon du gyur la ni byang chub kyi phyogs dang bden pa dang rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba la dmigs pa lhag pa'i shes rab bslab pa'i khyad par sgrub pa'o /
tāsām eva śikṣāṇāṃ śeṣāsu bhūmiṣu caturvidhaṃ phalaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# sa lhag ma rnams la ni bslab pa de dag nyid kyi 'bras bu rnam pa bzhir rig par bya'o /
tatra dūraṅgamāyāmprayatnasahitam animittajñāne'vasthānaṃ / niṣpādayati /
# de la ring du song ba rnams la ni 'bad pa dang bcas par mtshan ma med pa'i ye shes la gnas pa sgrub po /
acalāyām anābhogenānimittajñāne'vasthānaṃ sārdhaṃ kṣetraviśuddhyā / niṣpādayati /
# mi gyo ba la ni lhun gyis grub par mtshan ma med pa'i ye shes la gnas pa zhing rnam par dag pa dang lhan cig sgrub bo; /
sādhumatyāṃ pratisaṃvidguṇaviśeṣaṃ niṣpādayati yena dhārmakathiko / bhavati /
# legs pa'i blo gros la ni so so yang dag par rig pa yon tan gyi khyad par gang gis chos smra bar 'gyur ba sgrub po /
dharmamedhāyāṃ samādhidhāraṇīguṇaviśeṣaṃ niṣpādayati /
# chos kyi sprin la ni ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs kyi yon tan gyi khyad par sgrub po /
dharmadhātau daśavidhe sarvatragādyartha iti / / dharmadhātau daśabhir bodhisattvabhūmibhiḥ sarvatragādyartho'dhigamyate /
# kun du 'gro ba la sogs pa chos kyi dbyings rnam pa bcu la zhes bya ba ni chos kyi dbyings la byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu rnams kyis kun du 'gro ba la sogs pa'i don gang yin pa khong du chud par byed pa'o /
tatra yad akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ tad daśasu bodhisattvabhūmiṣu [p.76]
# de la nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa gang yin pa de ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu la rnam pa bcur go rims bzhin du sgrib ste /
daśavidham āvaraṇaṃ yathākramaṃ tad vipakṣatvād iti bhūmivipakṣatvāt / / bhūmayo hi lokottarasamādhiprajñādyavakāśaviśeṣātmakāḥ /
# de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni sa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs yin pa'i phyir ro / / sa rnams ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab la sogs pa'i gnas skabs kyi khyad par gyi bdag nyid de /
tad utpattivibandhād akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ vipakṣaḥ /
# de dag skye ba'i gegs byed pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs so /
na cā'trakliṣṭamevā'jñānam āvaraṇaṃ kintarhyanye'pi kleśopakleśāḥ /
# de la nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa kho na sgrib par ma zad kyi / / nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dag kyang yin no /
tathā hi pramuditāyāḥ sarva eva darśanamārgapraheyā āvaraṇaṃ /
# 'di ltar rab tu dga' ba la ni mthong ba'i lam gyis spang bar bya ba thams cad sgrib ste /
yasmāt sarvatrārthā'vabodhena darśanamārgeṇa satyeṣu sarve / vipratipattyanuśayāḥ prahīyante bhāvanāpraheyāḥ punaḥ śeṣābhir
# 'di ltar kun du 'gro ba'i don khong du chud par byed pa mthong ba'i lam gyi bden pa rnams la log par rtog pa'i bag la nyal ba thams cad spong ba'i phyir ro / / bsgom pas spang bar bya ba rnams ni sa lhag ma rnams kyis spong ngo /
bhūmibhiḥ / / te tv aprahīṇā api prahīṇavat bodhisattvānāṃ na saṃkleśakarā / bhavantīti / / imam eva cā'rthamadhikṛtyoktā gāthā - / kleśo bodhyṅga āpanno mohopāyaprayogataḥ /
# de dag ni ma spangs kyang spangs pa bzhin te / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams la kun nas nyon mongs par byed pa ma yin no / / don de nyid kyi dbang du mdzad de tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa / / thabs chen rnams dang ldan pa la / / nyon mongs byang chub lan lag 'gyur /
saṃsāro'pyupaśāntātmā tato'cintyas tathāgataḥ //
# 'khor ba'ang zhi ba'i bdag nyid de / / de phyir de bzhin gshegs bsam yas /
daśasu ca bhūmiṣu daśa pāramitā yathākramam atiriktatarā bhavantīti / vacanāt tad vipakṣasyāpi mātsaryādikasya yathākramaṃ prahāṇam iti
# she'o / / sa bcu rnams la pha rol tu phyin pa bcu go rims bzhin du lhag par che ba yin no zhes 'byung ba'i phyir de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs ser sna la sogs pa go rims bzhin du spong bar mngon no /
gamyate / / yadyanyo'pi kleśa āvaraṇaṃ syāt kasmād uktaṃ bhūmiṣv akliṣṭam / evājñānam āvaraṇam iti ?
# gal te nyon mongs pa gzhan yang sgrib na ci'i phyir sa rnams la nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa kho na sgrib par bshad ce na /
asādhāraṇatvāt / / etaddhi bodhisattvānām eva nirvāṇādhigamavibandhair vartate na / śrāvakādīnāṃ /
# thun mong ma yin pa'i phyir te / / de ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kho na la mya ngan las 'das pa thob par bya ba'i gegs su 'gyur gyi / / nyan thos la sogs pa la ni ma yin te /
tathā hi - śrāvakāḥ pratyekabuddhāś ca tasmin satyeva mucyante na tu / bodhisattvā ityato'sādhāraṇaṃ / / etad bhūmiṣv āvaraṇam uktaṃ na tvetad eva bhūmiṣvāvaraṇam iti kṛtvā /
# 'di ltar nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams la de yod kyang grol bar 'gyur la / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni ma yin pas de'i phyir thun mong ma yin no / / de sa rnams la sgrib par bshad kyang / / sa rnams la sgrib pa de kho nar ma zad de /
kleśas tu śrāvakādibhir bodhisattvānāṃ samāna iti tasyāvaraṇatvena / bodhisattvabhūmiṣu na vidhir na pratiṣedha iti tasyā'vacane'pyāvaraṇaṃ na / nivartate /
# nyon mongs pa'i nyan thos la sogs pa dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams la 'dra bas byang chub sems dpa'i sa rnams la de'i sgrib par gzhag pa yang med bkag pa yang med de / / de ma bshad kyang sgrib pa las ldog par mi 'gyur ro /
anya āha - akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ śrāvakādibhir bodhisattvānāṃ samānam iti / bhūmīnāṃ viśeṣeṇāvaraṇam ucyate / / kleśastvānuṣaṅgika iti noktaṃ /
# gzhan na re nyan thos la sogs pa dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams la 'dra bas nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa ni sa rnams la sgrib pa khyad par du bshad kyi /
kleśo'pi śrāvakādibhir bodhisattvānāṃ samāna evetyasāvānuṣaṅgiko na / syād iti /
# nyon mongs pa ni zhar la yod pas ma smos so zhes zer te / / nyon mongs pa yang nyan thos la sogs pa dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams la 'dra ba nyid yin pas de zhar la yod ces bya bar mi rung ngo /
anye tvāhuḥ - yad bhūmīnām ajñānam āvaraṇaṃ tacchrāvakādīnām / akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ sannāpi vimuktivibandhanaṃ /
# gzhan na res rnams kyi mi shes pa'i sgrib pa gang yin pa de nyan thos rnams kyi nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa yin yang thar pa la gegs mi byed de /
yasmācchrāvakā bhūmiṣvajñāne satyeva vimucyante /
# 'di ltar nyan thos dag la sa rnams la mi shes pa yod bzhin du rnam par 'grol lo /
bodhisattvānān tu kliṣṭaṃ nirvāṇādhigame vibandhahetubhāvād iti / / naitadevam ityanye - / akliṣṭaṃ daśadhāvṛtiḥ / iti /
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams la ni mya ngan las 'das pa thob par bya ba la gegs kyi rgyur gyur pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa can no zhe'o / / de ni de lta ma yin te / / nyon mongs can min sgrib pa bcu / / zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
prathamayā hi bhūmyā dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthaṃ pratividhyatīti / / tatra prathamā lokottaraprajñā saparivārā darśanamārgasaṃgṛhītā / / dharmadhātuḥ śūnyatā /
# sa dang po la ni chos kyi dbyings kun du 'gro ba'i don du rtogs te zhes bya ba de la; sa dang po ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab 'khor ba dang bcas pa dang po ba ste / / mthong ba'i lam gyis bsdus pa'o /
sāmānyalakṣaṇenaikatra yathā sarvatrā'pi tatheti sarvatragatvāt / sarvatragaḥ /
# chos kyi dbyings ni stong pa nyid de / / spyi'i mtshan nyid pas gcig la ji lta bar thams cad la yang de bzhin no / / thams cad du song bas kun du 'gro ba ste /
dharmadhātuvinirmukto yasmād dharmo na vidyate // [p.77]
# chos kyi dbyings ni ma rtogs par / / 'di ltar chos ni yod ma yin /
iti vacanaṃ dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvajñāpakaṃ / / pratividhyatīti sākṣātkarotītyarthaḥ / / yena prativedhenātmaparasamatāṃ pratilabhate /
# zhes 'byung ba ni chos kyi dbyings kun du 'gro ba'i khungs yin no / / rtogs zhes bya ba ni mngon du byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig ste / / rtogs pa des bdag gang yin pa de gzhan la /
yo'haṃ sa paro yo vā paraḥ so'ham iti paratrātmani ca śūnyatāyā / abhedadarśanāt svaparātmanor abhedaṃ manyate /
# gzhan gang yin pa de bdag go zhes bdag dang gzhan mnyam pa nyid rab tu thob nas gzhan dang bdag gis stong pa nyid tha dad par ma mthong bas bdag dang gzhan du bye brag gis rlom sems su med do /
ata evāsyāṃ bhūmau dānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati /
# de'i phyir de la sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te /
tato'tra bodhisattvo yathā svārthe tathā parārthe pravartate /
# de'i phyir 'di la byang chub sems dpa' bdag gi don bzhin du gzhan gyi don la rab tu 'jug go /
evaṃ hi prativedhaḥ pratipakṣaḥ pratipakṣaphalañcodbhāvitaṃ / / etac ca tritayam itarāsv api bhūmiṣu vijñeyaṃ /
# 'di ni rtogs pa dang gnyen po dang gnyen po'i 'bras bu bstan pa yin te / / de gsum ni sa gzhan dag tu yang shes par bya'o /
dvitīyayā'grārthaṃ /
# gnyis pa la ni mchog gi don du ste /
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti sambadhyate / / prakṛtiprabhāsvaradarśanāt /
# rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal bar mthong ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs so zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
yenā'syaivaṃ bhavati - tasmāt tarhyasmābhis samāne'bhinirhāre / sarvākārapariśodhanābhinirhāra eva yogaḥ karaṇīya ityāgamaṃ darśayati
# des de 'di snyam du sems te / / de lta bas na sgrub du mtshungs pa la bdag gis rnam pa thams cad du yongs su sbyong ba mngon par bsgrub pa nyid la brtson par bya'o snyam mo zhes lung las bshad do /
sūtre hy uktaṃ - yasmāditi daśakuśalāḥ karmapathāḥ prajñākāreṇa / pratibhāvyamānā yāvac chrāvakayānaṃ saṃvartayanti /
# mdo las kyang 'di skad ces de bas na dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam de dag shes rab kyi rnam par yongs su bsgoms na nyan thos kyi theg pa'i bar du 'gyur ro /
tata uttaraṃ pariśodhitā yāvad pratyeka buddhyānaṃ saṃvartayanti/
# de bas gong du yongs su sbyangs pas rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i bar du 'gyur ro /
tata uttaraṃ pariśodhitā yāvad / bodhisattvabhūmipariśuddhipāramitāpariśuddhicaryāvipulatvāya / saṃvartante / / tata uttaraṃ pariśuddhitaratvād yāvad daśabalabalatvāya saṃvartante / / tasmāt tarhyasmābhis samāne'bhinirhāra iti vistaraḥ /
# de bas gong du yongs su sbyangs pas byang chub sems dpa'i sa yongs su dag pa dang pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag pa dang spyod pa rgyas pa'i bar du 'gyur ro / / de bas gong du yongs su dag pas stobs bcu'i bar du 'gyur ro / / de lta bas na bsgrub tu mtshungs pa la bdag gis zhes rgya cher bshad do /
yasmād etad asyaiva bhavati dvitīyāyāṃ bhūmau tasmāt tarhītyādi / / tasmād dvitīyayā'grārthaṃ pratividhyatīti vijñāyate /
# gang gis 'di ltar de 'di snyam du sems te / / sa gnyis pa la de lta bas na zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste / / de bas na gnyis pa la mchog gi don du rab tu rtogs par mngon no /
abhinirhāraḥ prayatnaḥ kṛtyaṃ vā /
# mngon par bsgrub pa ni 'bad pa'am bya ba'o /
sarvākārapariśodhanaṃ dharmadhātau kliṣṭā'kliṣṭamohanirākaraṇaṃ /
# rnam pa thams cad du yongs su sbyang ba ni chos kyi dbyings la nyon mongs pa can dang nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i rmongs pa sel ba'o /
