tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau śīlapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati
# de bas na sa de la tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te /
viśiṣṭārthaprārthanayā sutarām ātmamātrīkaraṇāt / / tṛtīyayā tan niṣyandāgrārthaṃ / / pratividhyatīti prakṛtaṃ / / dharmadhātuprativedhaprabhāvitatvād buddhavacanasya /
# khyad par du 'phags pa'i don la smon pas bdag shin tu rnam par dag pa'i snod du byed pa'i phyir ro / / gsum pa la ni de'i rgyu mthun pa don gyi mchog tu rtogs te / / sangs rgyas kyi gsung ni chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
yasmāt sarvākārapariśuddhadharmakāyasaṃjñakena dharmadhātuvaśena / prabhāvito dharmadhātuniṣyandaḥ sūtrādiko deśanādharmaḥ /
# 'di ltar rnam pa thams cad du yongs su dag pa chos kyi sku zhes bya ba'i chos kyi dbyings kyi dbang gis chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyu mthun pa mdo la sogs pa bstan pa'i chos rab tu byung ba'i phyir ro /
dharmadhātvagratayā tanniṣYandadeśanādharmāgratayā / dharmadhātupariśuddhinimittatvāc ca /
# chos kyi dbyings mchog yin pas de'i rgyu mthun pas bstan pa'i chos kyang mchog yin pa dang chos kyi dbyings yongs su dag par bya ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
tena dharmadhātuniṣyandasya [p.78] / śrutasyā'gratāṃ viditveti vistaraḥ /
# des chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyu mthun pa thos pa mchog tu rig nas shes pa rgya cher 'byung ba la /
teneti pratividhhadharmadhātunā /
# des zhes bya ba ni chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs pas so /
śrutasyeti śrutasūtrādidharmasya tasyā'gratā viditveti nirvikalpena / jñānena tathā pratyātmaṃ jñātvetyarthaḥ /
# thos pa zhes bya ba ni mdo la sogs pa'i chos thos pa'o / / de la mchog tu rig nas zhes bya ba ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis de bzhin du so sor rang gis shes zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tad artham iti buddhavacanaśravaṇārthaṃ /
# de'i phyir zhes bya ba ni sangs rgyas kyi gsung mnyan pa'i phyir ro /
trisāhasramahāsāhasrapramāṇāyām apy agnikaṇḍāyām ātmānaṃ prakṣiped  iti / / uktaṃ hi sūtre - sa ced idaṃ kaścidevaṃ brūyāt - evam ahaṃ tubhyam idaṃ / dharmapadaṃ samyak sambuddhopanītaṃ bodhisattvacaryāpariśodhanaṃ / saṃśrāvayeyaṃ sa cet tvaṃ mahatyām agnikhaḍāyāṃ samprajvalitāyām / ekajvālībhūtāyām ātmānaṃ prapātayeḥ mahāntaṃ ca / duḥkhavedanopakramaṃ svaśarīreṇopādadyāḥ / / tasyaivaṃ bhavati - utsahe'ham ekasyāpi dharmapadasya / samyaksambuddhopanītasya bodhisattvacaryāpariśodhanasyārthāya / trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātāv agniparipūrṇe brahmalokād ātmānam / utsraṣṭuṃ / / kim punaḥ prākṛtāyām agnikhaḍāyāṃ / / api tu khalu punaḥ sarvair nirayāpāyaduḥkhasaṃvāsair apy asmābhis / sarvabuddhadharmāḥ paryeṣitavyāḥ kiṃ punar manuṣyaduḥkhasaṃvāsair iti / / ata evāsyāmbhūmau kṣāntipāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati śrutārthaṃ / sarvakleśasahanādibhir apy abhedyatvāt /
# me'i 'obs stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i tshad tsam du yang bdag nyid mchong zhes bya ba ni mdo las gsungs pa / / gal te la la zhig de la 'di skad ces zer te / / gal te khyod me'i 'obs chen po 'bar ba / / kun du 'bar ba / / kun du rab tu mched cing 'bar ba / / me lce gcig tu gyur pa'i nang du bdag rab tu mchong zhing sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba chen po myong bar 'gyur ba rang gi lus kyis nyams su len na ngas khyod la chos kyi tshig yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su sbyong ba 'di bshad par bya'o zhe na yang de 'di snyam du sems te / / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa / / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su sbyong ba'i chos kyi tshig gcig gi don du yang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams mas rab tu gang bar tshangs pa'i 'jig rten nas bdag gis bdag dor bar mos na me'i 'obs tha mal bar bdag dor ba lta ci smos / / sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad nyams su bab kyang bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad btsal bar bya na / / mi'i sdug bsngal dang 'grogs pa lta ci smos kyi snyam nas zhes bya ba'o / / de bas na sa de la bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te / / thos pa'i ched du nyon mongs pa thams cad la mi 'byed pa'i phyir ro /
caturthyā niṣparigrahārthaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti prakṛtaṃ / / caturthyam bhūmau samatvād anātmīyatvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyati
# bzhi pa la ni yongs su gzung ba med pa'i don du ste / / chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs so zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / sa bzhi ba la la ni mnyam pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings bdag gi ba med par rab tu rtogs te /
yasmān na dharmadhātoḥ kasyacit samatāstīti / / athavā sarvaviparyāsā'viṣayatvān na kasyacit parigrahaḥ /
# 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings la bdag gang yang med pa'i phyir ro / / yang na phyin ci log thams cad kyi yul ma yin pa'i phyir su'i yongs su bzung ba yang ma yin no /
svayam aviṣayatvān nā'tra kaścit parigrahaḥ / / yasmād dharmatṛṣṇā'pi vyāvartata ityāgamavacanaṃ /
# bdag nyid kyis phyin ci log ma yin pas 'di la yongs su bzung ba gang yang med de / / 'di ltar chos la sred pa yang ldog go zhes lung las 'byung ngo /
evam arciṣmatyāṃ niṣprapañcena jñānena dharmadhātvadhigamād / bodhipakṣadharmaprātpiḥ /
# de ltar 'od 'phro ba can ni spros pa med pa'i ye shes kyi dbyings khong du chud pa'i phyir byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thob ste /
bodhisattvasya yā'pi sūtrādidharmatṛṣṇā pūrvam āsīt sā'pi / vyāvartate / / dhyānasamādhisamāpattir dharmatṛṣṇetyanye / / tasmāt tasyābhūmau vīryapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati / / abhīkṣṇaṃ vāṅmanojalpasamatikrānte bodhipakṣair viharaṇāt / / pañcamyā santānābhedārthaṃ / / dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīty adhikṛtaṃ / / atītā'nāgatavartamānānāṃ sarvabuddhānāṃ paramparato / bodhisattvānāñca santānair ātmanaḥ [p.79] / santānā'bhedaṃ paśyati / / daśabhiścittāśayaviśūddhisamatābhir ityāgamaṃ darśayati / / atītabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca / anāgatabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca
# byang chub sems dpa' mdo sde la sogs pa'i chos la sred pa snga nas yod pa gang yin pa de yang ldog go / / gzhan dag na re bsam gtan dang ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa ni chos la sred pa'o zhe'o / / de bas na sa de la brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te / / lus dang ngag dang yid kyi spyod pa las 'das par rgyun du byang chub kyi phyogs rnams kyis gnas pa'i phyir ro / / lnga pa la ni rgyud tha dad pa med pa'i don du ste / / chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro / / 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar gyi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad nang dang byang chub sems dpa'i rgyud rnams dang bdag tha mi dad cing mtshungs par mthong ngo / / sems dang bsam pa rnam par dag pa mnyam pa nyid bcus zhes bya ba ni lung gis ston te /
pratyutpannabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca / śīlaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca cittaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca / dṛṣṭikāṅkṣāvimativilekhā'panayanaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca / mārgā'mārgajñānaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca / pratipatprahāṇajñānaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca sarvabodhipākṣika / dharmottarottaravibhāvanaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca / sarvasattvaparipācanaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca / / ābhiḥ samatābhiḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ santānā'bhedaṃ pratividhyati / ālayavijñānaparāvṛttilakṣaṇadharmakāyasyā'bhinnatvāt / / tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau dhyānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati / paramārthataḥ satyākārabhāvanābahulatvāt / / ṣaṣṭhyā niṣsaṅkleśaviśuddhyarthaṃ / / dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti sambadhyate / / pratītyasamutpādalakṣaṇaḥ saṅkleśaḥ tasminnāgantukāt prakṛtyā na / saṅkliśyate / / prākṛtikaviśuddherna viśuddhyati / / evaṃ svasaṃvedyākāreṇa nirvikalpena jñānena dharmadhātuṃ / pratividhyatītyatraivāgamaṃ darśayati / / pratītyasamutpāde nāsti sa kaścid dharmo yaḥ saṅkliśyate vā viśuddhyate / veti prativedhāt /
# 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang tshul khrims rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang sems can rnam par dag pas bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang lta ba dang the tshom dang yid gnyis dang 'gyod pa sel bas rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang lam dang lam ma yin pa shes pa rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang lam shes pa rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad gong nas gong du rnam par 'jig pa rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang sems can thams cad yongs su smin par byed pa rnam par dag pa la bsam pa mnyam pa nyid ces bya ba ste / / mnyam pa nyid 'di dag gis sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rgyas thams cad kyi rgyud tha mi dad par rab tu rtogs te / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gnas gyur pa'i mtshan nyid chos kyi sku tha mi dad pa'i phyir ro / / de bas nas de la bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te / / don dam par bden pa'i rnam par bsgoms pa mang ba'i phyir ro / / drug pa la ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba ma yin pa'i don du ste / / chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid kun nas nyon mongs pa ni de la glo bur du 'byung ba'i phyir rang bzhin gyis kun nas nyon mongs pa ma yin no / / rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pas rnam par dag par 'gyur ba ma yin no / / de ltar rang gis rig pa'i tshul gyis rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs so zhes lung de nyid las ston te / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba la gang kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba'am / / rnam par dag par 'gyur ba'i chos de gang yang med par rab tu rtogs pa'i phyir ro /
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ bhūmau bodhisattvaḥ pratītyasamutpādaṃ vidhyati / / tatra na kasyacid dharmasya saṅkleśaṃ vyavadānaṃ vā pratividhyati
# sa drug pa la ni byang chub sems dpa' rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba la rnam par rtogs te / / chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i phyir de la yang chos gang la kun nas nyon mongs pa'am /
dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvāt pratītyasamutpādāṅgañca / saṅkleśamātratvāt na ca tad vyatirikto'nya ātmā'styātmīyo vā yasmin / saṅkleśaḥ saṅkalpyate viśuddhir vā /
# rnam par byang ba med par rtogs so / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i yan lag rnams ni kun nas nyon mongs pa tsam du zad pa'i phyir gang la kun nas nyon mongs pa'am / / rnam par dag par kun du rtogs pa de la gtogs par bdag gam bdag gi med do /
tasmād vā'syāṃ bhūmau prajñāpāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati / nissaṅkleśa viśuddhyarthena pratītyasamutpādagāmbhīryā'vabodhād iti / / saptamyā'nānārthatvaṃ /
# de'i phyir sa de la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te; kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa med pa'i don du rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba za ba mo khong du chud pa'i phyir ro / / bdun pa la ni tha dad pa med pa'i don du ste /
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatītyadhikṛtaṃ /
# chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
tasyāṃ bhūmau bodhisattvo'bhibhavati sarvanimittasamudācārābhāvāt / nimittasamudācāradvārakaṃśca nānātvasamudācāra iti / / ato nimittasamudācārā'bhāvāt saptamyā'nānātvārthaṃ dharmadhātoḥ / pratividhyatīty ucyate /
# sa de la byang chub sems dpa' mtshan ma thams cad mi 'byung bas zil gyis non te / / mtshan ma 'byung ba'i sgo nas tha dad pa 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / de bas na mtshan ma med pa'i phyir bdun pa la tha dad pa med pa'i don du rab tu rtogs so zhes bya'o /
imam evārthaṃ pradarśayann āha - nirnimittatayā / sūtrādidharmanimittanānātvā'samudācārād iti /
# don de nyid rab tu bstan pa'i phyir mtshan ma med pas mdo la sogs pa'i chos kyi mtshan nyid tha dad pa mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
yaiḥ sūtrādidharmanimittair dharmadhātuṃ praviśati [p.80] / tāni balān nānātvena tat praveśatat pṛṣṭalabdhayor abhimukhībhavanti / yāvat ṣaṣṭhī bhūmiḥ /
# sa drug pa'i bar du ni mdo la sogs pa'i chos kyi mtshan ma gang gis chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa de dag shugs kyis de la 'jug pa dang de'i rjes las thob pa'i shes pa gnyis kyis tha dad pa nyid du mngon du 'gyur ro /
saptamyāntu bhūmau sarvanimittaikarasākāreṇa jñanena dharmadhātor / nimitttābhāvatvaṃ pratividhyatīti tāni tāni nimittāni na / samudācaranti / / tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmāv upāyaparamitā'tiriktatarā bhavati yataḥ
# sa bdun pa la ni mtshan thams cad ro gcig pa'i rnam pa'i ye shes kyis chos kyi dbyings mtshan ma med par rab tu rtogs pa mtshan ma de dag mi 'byung ngo / / de'i phyir sa de la thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te /
sarvanimittāny animittatvena pratividhyati nimittakṛtaṃ ca vyavahāraṃ na / virodhayati /
# 'di ltar mtshan ma thams cad ma med pa nyid du yang rab tu rtogs la / / mtshan mar byas pa'i tha snyad kyang mi 'gog ste /
tat prativedhāc ca tasyām eva vaśitvaṃ pratilabhate / / aṣṭamyā'hīnadhikārthaṃ / / dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti sambadhyate /
# de rab rtogs pas kyang de nyid la dbang byed pa rab tu thob pa'i phyir ro / / brgyad pa la ni bri ba med cing 'phel ba med pa'i don du ste / / chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs so zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtipariśuddhatvāt samalā'malā'vasthayor / viśeṣā'bhāvāt / / ata evā'sau nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā tathatetyucyate /
# chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa'i phyir dri ma dang bcas pa dang; dri ma med pa'i dus na yang khyad par med pa'i phyir ro / / de bas na rtag tu de bzhin kho na bas de bzhin nyid ces bya'o /
nimittā'bhāve kvacid api hīnatā nāsti /
# mtshan ma dang bral ba na gang la yang bri ba yang med la /
sanimittatve kvacid apyadhikatvaṃ nāsti / / tathā hi nimittam evā'nimittam iti kiñcid
# mtshan ma yod pa na yang gang la yang 'phel ba yang med do / / la lan re 'di ltar mtshan ma nyid mtshan ma med pa'o zhe'o /
anutpattikadharmakṣāntilābhād ityatraiva kāraṇaṃ /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pas zhes bya ba'o /
aṣṭamyāṃ hi bhūmau bodhisattvo'nutpattikadharmakṣāntipratilambhād / dharmadhātor abhyuccayā'bhāvatvam apacayā'bhāvatvaṃ caivaṃ / pratividhyati / / saṅkleśe vyavadāne vā kasyacid dharmasya / hānivṛddhyadarśanādityapūrvadharmā'nutpādāt /
# sa brgyad pa la byang chub sems dpa' mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pas chos kyi dbyings la bri ba med pa dang lhag ma med pa nyid du de ltar rab tu rtogs so / / kun nas nyon mongs pa ni bri ba med pa'am / / rnam par byang bas na 'phel ba'i chos gang yang med de / / sngon med pa'i chos mi skye ba'i phyir ro /
caturthā vaśitā - nirvikalpavaśitā kṣetrapariśuddhivaśitā jñānavaśitā / karmavaśitā ca / / tatra nirvikalpavaśitāśrayatvaṃ dharmadhātor veditavyaṃ / anābhogenasarvanimittasamudācārā'bhāvāt /
# dbang rnam pa bzhi ste / / rnam par mi rtog pa la dbang ba dang zhing yongs su dag pa la dbang ba dang ye shes la dbang ba dang las la dbang ba'o / / de la lhun gyis grub par mtshan ma thams cad mi 'byung bas chos kyi dbyings ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes la dbang ba'i gnas su rig par bya'o /
saptamyām api nimittasamudācārābhāvaḥ sambhavaty abhisaṃskāreṇa /
# bdun pa yang mtshan ma mi 'byung ba yod mod kyi / / mngon par 'du byed pas yin gyi /
iha tv anabhisaṃskāreṇeti viśeṣaḥ /
# 'dir ni lhun gyi grub pa yin pas bye brag yod do /
kṣetrapariśuddhivaśitāśrayatvaṃ cā'ṣṭamyāpratividhyatīti prakṛtaṃ / / kṣetrapariśuddhivaśitāśrayatvaṃ dharmadhātor yatheṣṭaṃ
# ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing dang 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor kun du bstan pa'i mthu brnyes pas chos kyi dbyings ni zhing yongs su dag la dbang ba'i gnas su rig par bya'o /
buddhakṣetraparṣanmaṇḍalasandarśanaśaktipratilambhāt / / tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau praṇidhānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati / nirvikalpakṣetravaśitālābhena kuśalanirantaraprayogāt /
# de bas na sa de la smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te / / rnam par mi rtog pa dang bzhin la dbang ba thob pas dge ba la bar chad med par sbyor ba'i phyir ro / / dgu pa la ni ye shes la dbang ba'i gnas nyid du ste / / ci zhe na /
jñānavaśitāśrayatvaṃ navamyā / / dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti prakṛutaṃ / / kathame tad vijñayate navamyā jñanavaṣitāśrayatvaṃ pratividhyatīti ? / ata āha - pratisaṃvil lābhāt / / asyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmārthaniruktipratibhānapratisaṃvido'nyair
# chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / dgu pa la ni ye shes la dbang ba'i gnas te / / rab tu rtogs so zhes bya bar ci mngon zhe na / / de'i phyir so so yang dag par rig pa thob pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / sa 'di la chos dang don dang nges pa'i tshig dang spobs pa so so yang dag par rig pa gzhan dag gis mi 'jigs pa rab tu thob po /
aparyāntāḥ pratilabhate / / ato'tra jñānavaśitāśrayatvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividdham iti vijñāyate / / tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau balapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati
# de bas na 'dir ni chos kyi dbyings ye shes la dbang ba'i gnas te / / rab tu rtogs so zhes bya bar mngon no / / de'i phyir sa de la stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te /
prajñābalaviśeṣayogāt / [p.81]
# shes rab kyi stobs kyi khyad par dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
karmavaśitāśrayatvaṃ daśamyā pratividhyatīti sambadhyate /
# sa bcu pa la ni las la dbang ba'i gnas nyid du rtogs so / / de ci mngon zhe na /
kartam etad gamyate ? / ata āha - yathecchaṃ nirmāṇaiḥ sattvārthakaraṇād iti /
# de'i phyir ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du sprul pa rnams kyis sems can gyi don mdzad pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
niścayenā'nena daśamyām bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ karmavaśitāśrayatvaṃ
# 'di ni sa bcu pa la chos kyi dbyings las la dbang ba'i gnas su rab tu rtogs so /
pratividhyati tena tathāgatakarma svādhipatyaṃ pratilabhate /
# des de bzhin gshegs pa'i phrin las rnams la dbang byed pa rab tu brnyes te /
tathā hi sugatatvād daśadiganantalokadhātusthitānāṃ sattvānāṃ / nirmāṇakāyair yatheṣṭaṃ yasya yathā yasmin kāle yat kartavyaṃ tasya / tathā tasmin kāle tat karoti /
# 'di ltar bde bar gshegs pa bzhin du phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas pa na gnas pa'i sems can dag la sprul pa'i sku rnams kyis ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du gang la ji ltar gang gi tshe gang bya ba la / / de ltar de'i tshe de mdzad do /
tasmād asyām bhūmau jñānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati /
# de bas na sa 'di la ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lhag par che ba yin te /
dharmaparibhogasattvaparipākaviśeṣayogād iti /
# chos la longs spyod pa dang sems can yongs su smin par mdzad pa'i khyad par dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
evam āsāṃ yathoktānāṃ bodhisattvabhūmīnāṃ / daśavidhadharmadhātuprativedhasarvākārapariṣodhanavibhandhabūtaṃ yad
# de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu ji skad du bshad pa de dag la chos kyi dbyings rnam pa bcu rab tu rtogs pa rnam pa thams cad du yongs su sbyang ba la gegs su gyur pa /
akliṣṭam ajñānam ekaikāyām api bhūmyām āvaraṇaṃ tat pratipakṣā / bodhisattvānāṃ daśa bhūmayo vyavasthitāḥ navamyā daśamyāśca bhūmeḥ / phalena viśeṣaḥ paridīpito nāvaraṇabheda prativedhaviśeṣeṇa tad vihārasya / kāmapyanirūpyā'vasthāṃ gatatvāt /
# nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pas re re la yang sgrib pa gang yin pa de'i gnyen por byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu rnam par gzhag go / / sa dgu pa dang sa bcu pa dag gi khyad par ni 'bras bus bstan pa yin gyi / / dmigs pa tha dad pa rab tu rtog pa'i khyad par gyis ni ma yin te / / gnas pa cir yang dpyad du med pa'i gnas su phyin pa'i phyir ro /
sarvatragādyarthaprativedhaprayojanaṃ daśabhūmiṣu daśānām pāramitānāṃ / viśeṣagatir yathākramaṃ /
# kun du 'gro ba la sogs pa'i don du rtogs pa'i dgongs pa ni sa cu rnams su pha rol tu phyin pa bcu go rims bzhin du khyad par du 'gro ba'o /
tasmād etad evoktaṃ - bhūmyāvaraṇaṃ pāramitāviśeṣagatyāvaraṇam iti /
# de'i phyir 'di skad ces sa la sgrib pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa rnams khyad par du 'gro ba la sgrib pa'o zhes bshad do /
athavā sūtroktam eva samādhisamāpattyādikam uttarottarabhūmiviśiṣṭam / sarvākāraṃ nānā'vasānaṃ phalaṃ sarvatragādyarthaprativedhaprayojanam / iti //2-16//
# yang na mdo las ting nge 'dzin brgya la snyoms par 'jug pa la sogs pas gong nas gong du khyad par du 'phags pa mchog rnams kyi ye shes kyi mthar thug pa'i 'bras bu gsung pa nyid kun du 'gro ba la sogs pa'i don du rab tu rtogs pa'i dgongs pa zhes bya'o /
{ āvaraṇasamāsaḥ } / prāg uktāni bahuvidhāni sarvāvaraṇāni dvayāvaraṇāntar gatānīti / pradarśanārtham āha - samāsena punaḥ - / kleśāvaraṇam ākhyātaṃ jñeyāvaraṇam eva ca / / katham etad gamyate ? / samāsato dvayam eva na punas tṛtīyam apy astīti /
# sgrib pa rnam pa du ma gong du ma bshad pa thams cad ni sgrib pa gnyis kyi nang du 'dus par rab tu bstan pa'i phyir mdor bsdu na / / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa nyid du bstan zhes bya ba smos so / / mdor bsdu na gnyis kho na ste / / gsum du med do zhes bya ba de ci mngon zhe na /
ata āha - / sarvāñ āvaraṇānīha iti /
# de'i phyir / / der ni sgrib pa thams cad de / / zhes bya ba gsungs te /
atrāntargatānīti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
# nang du 'dus so zhes bya ba ni tshig gi lhag ma'o /
sarvāvaraṇāni dvayāvaraṇāntargatāni nānyat tṛtīyam astīti gamyate /
# sgrib pa thams cad sgrib pa gnyis kyi nang du 'dus pas gsum pa gzhan med par mngon no /
yataś ca sarvāvaraṇānyatraivāntargatānyatasyaiva / sarvāvaraṇasaṅgrāhakasya kleśajñeyāvaraṇadvayasya kṣayāt
# gang gi phyir sgrib pa thams cad 'di nyid kyi nang du 'dus pa de'i phyir sgrib pa thams cad sdud pa nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam pa gnyis po 'di zad na /
sarvāvaraṇebhyo mukhtiriṣyate sarvāvaraṇānā prahāṇa mityarthaḥ / / buddhabūmyā varaṇe'nākhyāte katham atraivāntar bhāvaḥ ?
# sgrib pa thams cad las grol bar 'dod de / / sgrib pa thams cad spong zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / sangs rgyas kyi sa'i sgrib pa ma bshad par de nyid kyi nang du 'dus par ji ltar 'gyur /
na hy abhidhānād antarbhāvaḥ kin tarhi svabhāvāt /
# brjod pas de'i nang du gtogs par 'gyur ba yang ma yin te / / rang bzhin gyis 'dus so /
api ca vyāpyāvaraṇavacanāt tad apy uktam eva /
# de lta mod kyi khyab pa'i sgrib pa bshad pa'i phyir de nyid bshad zin to /
anyathā ca pradeśāvaraṇam eva bhavatīti /
# gzhan du na ni nyi tshe ba'i sgrib pa nyid du 'gyur ro /
athavā buddhabhūmyāvaraṇasaṅgrahārtham āha -
# yang na sangs rgyas kyi sa'i sgrib pa bsdu ba'i don du /
sarvāṇyāvaraṇānīha yat kṣayān muktir iṣyate / [p.82]
# der ni sgrib pa thams cad de / / ce zad nas ni grol bar 'dod /
buddhāvaraṇā'kṣaye na muktir astīti / / ataḥ śeṣāvaraṇavat tad apy āvaraṇam iti pratipāditam bhavati /
# ces bya ba gsungs so / / sangs rgyas kyi sa'i sgrib pa ma zad par grol ba med de / / de'i phyir sgrib pa lhag ma ltar de'i sgrib pa yang bstan pa yin no /
saukṣmyaprakarṣāvasthaṃ tv akliṣṭam ajñānam kleśavāsanāś ca / buddhabhūmer āvaraṇam ucyate /
# nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa rab tu phra ba'i gnas skabs dang nyon mongs pa'i bag chags ni sangs rgyas kyi sa'i sgrib pa zhes bya ste /
tasmāt saukṣmyaprakarṣād anyathā prekṣituṃ na śakyata ityevam ākhyānam / bhavati //2-17//
# de bas na shin tu phra ba'i phyir gzhan du brtag mi nus pas de skad ces bshad par 'gyur ro /
{ āvaraṇapiṇḍārthaḥ } / mahāvaraṇaṃ yad vyāpi kleśajñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrāṇāṃ /
# sgrib pa chen po ni khyab pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni bya ba ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'o /
pratanvāvaraṇaṃ prādeśikaṃ kleśāvaraṇam eva śrāvakādigotrāṇāṃ /
# sgrib pa chung ngu ni nyi tshe ba gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa nyid do /
prayogāvaraṇaṃ yad udriktam iti teṣām eva rāgādicaritānāṃ taiḥ
# sbyor ba'i sgrib pa ni lhag ma gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni 'dod chags la sogs pa spyod pa de dag nyid kyi ste /
prayogā'prāpteḥ /
# des sbyor ba nyid mi 'thob po /
prāptyāvaraṇaṃ yat samam iti samabhāgacaritānāṃ taddhi prāptivibandhe
# 'thob pa la sgrib pa ni mnyam pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni cha mtshungs par spyod pa rnams kyi ste; de 'thob pa'i bgegs su 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
vartate / / prāptiviśeṣāvaraṇaṃ yadādānavivarjane iti bodhisattvagotrāṇām
# thob pa khyad par can la sgrib pa ni len pa dang spong ba gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni / / byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can rnams kyi ste /
adhigamaviśeṣāvaraṇatvāt /
# thob par bya ba khyad par can la sgrib pa'i phyir ro /
apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam adhigamaviśeṣaḥ /
# mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa ni thob par bya ba khyad par can te /
eṣa caiva phalaviśeṣo veditavyāḥ /
# de nyid 'bras bu'i khyad par du yang rig par bya'o /
samyak prayogāvaraṇaṃ yan navadhā kleśalakṣaṇam iti nava / saṃyojanānyāvaraṇam iti vacanāt /
# yang dag par sbyor ba la sgrib pa ni nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid rnam pa dgu gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni kun du sbyor ba dgu ni sgrib po zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro /
tāni samyak prayogasyāvaraṇaṃ bhavanti yathā tathoktaṃ /
# de dag yang dag par sbyor ba la ji ltar sgrib pa de bzhin du bshad zin to /
hetvāvaraṇaṃ yac chubhādau daśavidhetvadhikārād iti /
# rgyu la sgrib pa ni dge ba la sogs pa rnams pa bcu la sgrib pa gang yin pa ste /
taddhi śubhādihetuvibandhadvāreṇāvaraṇaṃ bhavantīti hetvāvaraṇam ucyate
# rgyu'i don gyi skabs kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni dge ba la sogs pa'i rgyu la gegs byed pa'i sgo nas sgrib par 'gyur bas rgyu la sgrib pa zhes bya'o /
tattvapraveṣāvaraṇaṃ yad bodhipakṣyeṣv iti / / tair hi tattvam praviśati /
# de kho na la 'jug pa la sgrib pa ni byang chub kyi phyogs rnams la sgrib pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni de dag gis de kho na la 'jug par byed do /
śubhānuttaryāvaraṇaṃ yat pāramitāsu tata uttari śubhābhāvāt /
# dge ba bla na med pa la sgrib pa ni / / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la sgrib pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni de'i bla na dge ba med pa'i phyir ro /
tad viśeṣagatyāvaraṇaṃ yad bhūmiṣv iti pāramitā eva hi / lokottaraviśeṣāśrayabhūtā bhūmaya ucyante /
# de khyad par du 'gro ba la sgrib pa ni sa rnams la sgrib pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba la / / pha rol tu phyin pa nyid 'jig rten las 'das pa'i khyad par gyi gnas su gyur pa ni sa rnams zhes bya'o /
saṅgrahāvaraṇaṃ yat samāsato dvividham iti kleśāvaraṇaṃ / jñeyāvaraṇañca etena sarvāvaraṇasaṅgrahāt / / piṇḍārthavacanaṃ sukhodgrahaṇadhāraṇārthaṃ / / piṇḍīkṛtaṃ hi sukham udgṛhyate dhāryate ceti // / // āgamānusāriṇyāṃ mādhyantavibhāgaṭīkāyām ācāryabhadantasthi / ramativyākhyātāyām āvaraṇaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ samāptaḥ // / % tattvaparicchedas tṛtīyaḥ / -------------------------------------------------------------------------- [p.83] / āvaraṇa-nirdeśa-anantaraṃ tattva-nirdeśa-avasaraḥ tad- anantaram- uddiṣṭatvād / ity- atas- tattvam- adhikṛtyāhety.āha /
# bsdus pa'i sgrib pa ni mdor bsdus pa rnam pa gnyis po gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa ste / / de dag gis sgrib pa thams cad bsdus pa'i phyir ro / / des bde blag tu len pa dang 'dzin par bya ba'i phyir don bsdus pa bshad do / / bsdu ba byas pas bde blag tu len to / / 'dzin to / / bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa las sgrib pa'i le'ur bcad pa ste gnyis pa'i 'grel bshad do / / sgrib pa bshad pa'i 'og tu de kho na bshad pa'i skabs yin te / / de'i 'og tu smos pa'i phyir ro / / de bas na de kho na'i dbang du mdzad de gsungs pa zhes bya ba smos so /
/tattvasya ca bahu-vidhatvaṃ vidyate/ / / /atas- tadbheda-anavabodhe tattva-sva-rūpaṃ dur-avagamam ity/- atas- tattva-prabhedam / eva-adau pratipādayann- āha - / mūlalakṣaṇatattvaṃ
# de kho na yang rnam pa du ma yod de / / de'i phyir de'i dbye ba khong du ma chud par de kho na'i rang gi ngo bo khong du chud par dka' bas de'i phyir de kho na'i dbye ba nyid dang por bstan pa'i phyir / / rtsa ba mtshan nyid de kho na /
iti vistareṇa daśa-vidhaṃ tattvaṃ / / tatra mūla-tattve 'nya-tattva-antar-bhāva-sandarśana-arthaṃ *mūla-tattva*-vacanaṃ /
# zhes de kho na bcu rgya cher gsungs so / / kha cig na re rtsa ba'i de kho na de la de kho na gzhan 'dus par bstan pa'i phyir rtsa ba'i de kho na bshad do /
/mūla-tattve parijñāna-prahāṇa-sākṣāt-karaṇa-samprayuktasya/ / /doṣa-prahāṇa-arthaṃ/ *lakṣaṇa-tattva-vacanaṃ* /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na la yongs su shes par byed pa dang spong ba dang mngon sum du byed pa la zhugs pa'i nyes pa gzhom pa'i phyir mtshan nyid kyi de kho na bshad do /
saṃsārād- udvega-upāya-pradarśana-artham- *aviparyāsa-tattva-*vacanaṃ /
# 'khor ba la skyo bar bya ba'i thabs rab tu bstan pa'i phyir phyin ci ma log pa'i de kho na bshad do /
udvignasya śrāvaka-yāna-niryāṇa-sandarśana-arthaṃ *phala-hetu-tattva-*vacanaṃ /
# skyo nas nyan thos kyi theg pas nges par 'byung ba bstan pa'i phyir 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na bshad do /
śrāvakas- hi catur.ārya-satya-prati/vedha-bhāvanābhyāṃ niryāti/ / / /sarva-ākāra-jñāna-pratipatty-upāya-sandarśana-artham/ *audārika tattva*vacanaṃ / / sarva-avaraṇa-prahāṇa-upāya-sandarśana-arthaṃ *sūkṣma-tattva*vacanaṃ / / suvyavasthita-dharma-nirdeśa-upāya-sandarśana-arthaṃ sarva-para-pravādini-graha-upāya-sandarśana-arthañ- ca *prasiddha-tattva*-vacanaṃ / / same'pi dharma-dhā/tau/ [p.84}
# nyan thos ni 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi rab tu rtogs pa dang bsgom pa gnyis kyis nges par 'byung ngo / / rnam pa thams cad shes pa bsgrub pa'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir rags pa'i de kho na bshad do / / sgrib pa thams cad spang pa'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir phra ba'i de kho na bshad do / / legs par gnas pa'i chos bstan pa'i thabs bstan pa dang phas kyi rgol ba thams cad tshar gcod pa'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir grags pa'i de kho na bshad do /
/gotra-indriya-āśaya-bhedena viśuddhi-bheda-sandarśana-arthaṃ/ / *viśuddhi-gocara-tattva*-vacanaṃ /
# chos kyi dbyings su mtshungs kyang rigs dang dbang po dang bsam pa'i bye brag gis rnam par dag pa tha dad pa bstan pa'i phyir rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul gyi de kho na bshad do /
sarvākārasaṅkleśavyavadānapraveśopāyasandarśanārthaṃ / saṅgrahatattvavacanaṃ /
# rnam pa thams cad du kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba la 'jug pa'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir bsdu ba'i de kho na bshad do /
tathatām ārabhya sarvasandehavinirvartanasāmarthyasandarśanārthaṃ / prabhedatattvavacanaṃ / / sarvaprakārātmagrāhaṃ nivartya
# de bzhin nyid las brtsams te som nyi thams cad rnam par ldog pa'i mthu bstan pa'i phyir rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na bshad do / / bdag tu 'dzin pa rnam pa thams cad bzlog ste /
nairātmyavyavasthānasāamarthyasandarśanārthaṃ kauśalyatattvavacanam iti
# bdag med pa rab tu gzhag pa'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir mkhas pa'i de kho na bshad do zhe'o /
anye punar āhuḥ mūlatattvaṃ bodhisattvasyāsādhāraṇaṃ /
# gzhan dag na re rtsa ba'i de kho na ni byang chub sems dpa'i ste / / thun mong ma yin pa'o /
tatraiva mithyāprayogapratipakṣatvād dvitīyaṃ /
# de kho na gnyis pa ni de nyid la log par sbyor ba'i gnyen pa'o /
samyagyogānukūlatattvaṃ tṛtīyaṃ /
# de kho na gsum pa ni yang dag pa'i rnal 'byor dang mthun pa'o /
śrāvakapratyekabuddhasādhāraṇatattvaṃ caturthaṃ /
# de kho na bzhi ba ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang mthun pa'o /
partipatyyupāyatattvaṃ pañcamaṃ /
# de kho na lnga pa ni sgrib pa'i thabs so /
lokasādhāraṇatattvaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ /
# de kho na drug pa ni 'jig rten dang thun mong ngo /
tad asādhāraṇatattvaṃ saptamaṃ /
# de kho na bdun pa ni de dang thun mong pa yin pa'o /
jñeyasamāsatattvam aṣṭamaṃ /
# de kho na brgyad pa ni shes bya mdor bsdu ba'o /
prakṛtitattvaṃ navamaṃ /
# de kho na dgu pa ni rang bzhin no /
saṅkleśamūlanirghātanatattvaṃ daśamam iti /
# de kho na bcu pa ni nyon mongs pa'i rtsa ba 'joms pa'o zhe'o /
etāni samāsato daśa tattvāni tathāgatānāṃ / sarvābhisandhivacanāśrayabhūtaṃ / / vistareṇa tattvam aprayeṃ / / atra tattvā nukūlyāt saṃvṛtir api tattvam ityuktam ityeke / / sarvāṇyevaitāni yahoktaiḥ prakārair avisamvādāt tattvānītyanye / / yadyenaprakāreṇa na visamvadati tat tathā tattvam iti kṛtvā //3-2// / {mūlatattvaṃ}
# mdor bsdus pa de kho na bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis ldem por dgongs te gsungs pa'i gnas su gyur ba'o / / rgyas par bya na de kho na dpag tu med do / / kha cig na re 'di la de kho na dang mthun pas kun rdzob kyang de kho na zhes bstan zhe'o / / gzhan dag na re de dag thams cad ni ji skad bshad pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis mi bslu ba'i phyir de kho na rnams zhes bya ba ste / / gang rnam pa gang gis slu bar mi byed pa de ni de bzhin bas de kho na zhes bya'o zhe'o /
tatra mūlatattvaṃ - / svabhāvas trividhaḥ / ityetad aprasiddham ityata āha - parikalpitaḥ paratantraḥ pariniṣpannaś / ceti / / yena [p.85]
# de la rtsa ba'i de kho na ni ngo bo nyid rnam pa gsum ste zhes bya ba de ma grags pas de'i phyir / / kun brtags pa dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs su grub pa ste zhes bya ba smos so /
kāraṇena svabhāvas trividho mūlatattvam ity ucyate tat pradarśayann āha / - tatrā'nyatattvavyavasthāpanād iti /
# ci'i phyir ngo bo nyid gsum la rtsa ba'i de kho na zhes brjod can / / de rab tu bstan pa'i phyir de la de kho na gzhan rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
tatrā'nyasya lakṣaṇāditattvasyā'ntargatatvam ityarthaḥ /
# der mtshan nyid la sogs pa'i de kho na gzhan 'dus so zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
kim arthaṃ svabhāvas trividha upadhāryate ?
# ci'i phyir ngo bo nyid rnam pa gsum nye bar gzung zhe na /
vyavahāraparamārthatad āśrayapradarśanārtham ity eke /
# kha cig na re tha snyad dang don dam pa dang de'i gnas rab tu bstan pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
viparyāsa-tannimitta-tatpratipakṣālambana-pradarśanārtham ityanye /
# gzhan dag na re phyin ci log dang de'i rgyud dang de'i gnyen po'i dmigs pa rab tu bstan pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
bodhisattvānām āvaraṇavisaṃyogārthaṃ prahāṇaparijñāsākṣāt / kriyāvastupradarśanārtham ityanye /
# gzhan dag na re byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrib pa dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir spang ba dang yongs su shes par bya ba dang mngon sum du bya ba'i dngos po rab tu bstan pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
prakṛtyā gambhīrasya prajñāpāramitārūpasya / trisvabhāvadvāreṇā'bhrāntipratipattyartham ityanye / / evaṃ hy uktam abhidharmasutragrāthādvaye -
# gzhan dag na re shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul rang bzhin gyis zab pa ngo bo nyid gsum gyi sgo nas ma nor bar rtogs par bya ba'i phyir ro zhe'o / / de skad du chos mngon pa'i mdo'i nang nas tshigs su bcad pa gnyis las /
māyādideśanāṃ bhūte kalpitān nāsti deśanā /
# byung rten sgyu ma la sogs bstan / / rtags la brten nas med pa bstan /
caturvidhaviśuddhes tu pariniṣpannadeśanā //
# rnam dag rnam pa bzhir brten nas / / yongs su grub pa bstan pa yin /
śuddhiḥprakṛtivaimalyaṃ nārgatālambanan tathā / / viśuddhānāṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ caturdhā grahaṇam mataṃ // iti /
# dag pa de ni rang bzhin dang / / dri ma med dang lam dang dmigs / / rnam par dag pa'i chos kyi rnams / / rnam pa bzhi pos bsdus pa yin / / zhes gsungs so / / byung ba gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid la ltos nas mdo las sgyu ma la sogs pa bstan te / / de ni sgyu ma la sogs pa bzhin du log par snang ba'i phyir ro / / med pa kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la ltos nas med pa bstan to / / rnam par dag pa rnam pa bzhi la ltos nas yongs su grub par bstan to / / rnam par dag pa rnam pa bzhi la rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa ni dri ma dang bcas pa'i dus kyi de bzhin nyid la sogs pa'o / / dri ma med pas rnam par dag pa ni de dag nyid dri ma med pa'i dus na'o / / stong pa nyid la sogs pa 'thob pa'i lam rnam par dag pa ni byang chub kyi phyogs la sogs pa'o / / lam skyed pa'i phyir dmigs pa rnam par dag pa ni chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyu mthun pa bstan pa'i chos mdo'i sde la sogs pa ste / / de la brten nas lam skye ba'i phyir ro / / 'di ltar rnam par dag pa 'di bzhis rnam par byang ba'i chos thams cad bsdus te tshigs su bcad pa gnyis kyi don mdor bsdus pa'o /
laukikalokottaratatpṛṣṭhalabdhajñānaviṣayatvapradarśanārthaṃ / yathāsambhavaṃ trayopādānaṃ svabhāvatam ity anye /
# gzhan dag na re 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa dang de'i rjes las thob pa'i ye shes kyi yul yin par rab tu bstan pa'i phyir ci rigs par ngo bo nyid gsum gzung ngo zhe'o /
kim atra svabhāvatraye tattvam iṣyata iti / / aviparītārtho hi tattvārthaḥ /
# ci'i phyir 'dir ngo bo nyid gsum la de kho na zhas bya bar 'dod ce na zhes bya ba ni de kho na'i don ni ma nor ba'i don yin na /
kimatra svabhāvatraye'viparītatvam iti yasmāt svabhāvatraye tattvam / iṣyata iti pṛcchābhiprāyaḥ /
# ci'i phyir 'dir ngo bo nyid gsum la ma nor ba zhes bya / / 'di ltar ngo bo nyid gsum la de kho na zhes bya snyam du dri bar bsams pa'o /
svabhāvas trividho'sacca nityaṃ / ityādi vistaraḥ /
# ngo bo nyid gsum rtag med ces bya ba la sogs pa rgya cher smos pa la /
parikalpitalakṣaṇaṃ nityam asad iti yatra hi bālānāṃ
# kun du brtags pa'i mtshan nyid ni rtag tu med pa'o zhes bya ba la /
grāhyagrāhakavācyavācakābhiniveśaḥ svapna iva pravartate / / asacca sasvarūpābhāvāt kalpitasvabhāvaḥ /
# gang la byis pa rnams kyis gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang smra ba dang smra bar bya bar mngon par zhen pa'i rmi lam ltar rab tu 'byung ba de ni rang gi ngo bor med pa'i phyir brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid do /
tasmād asadātmakatvād abhrāntitvāc ca parikalpitalakṣaṇam asattvaṃ /
# de'i phyir med pa'i bdag nyid yin pa dang 'khrul pa med pa'i phyir med pa nyid kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid do /
etat parikalpitasvabhāve'sattvam eva tattvam ucyate /
# de'i phyir kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la med pa nyid kyi de kho na zhes brjod do /
aviparītatvād iti aviparītārtho'tra tattvārthaṃ iti darśayati / / paratantralakṣaṇam sacca na ca tattvata iti /
# phyin ci ma log pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la phyin ci ma log pa'i don ni 'dor de kho na'i don du ston to / / gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid ni yod kyang yang dag par na ma yin te zhes bya ba la /
grāhyagrāhakādikalpitavyavahārāśrayatvāt sattvaṃ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la sogs pa brtags pa'i mtshan nyid de tha snyad kyi gnas yin pas yod do /
grāhyagrāhakādyātmakatvenāsattvān na tathā tattvata iti /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i bdag nyid du med pas yang dag par na de bzhin du ma yin no /
etad eva pratipādayann āha bhrāntimātratvād iti /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir 'khrul pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - yat khyāti māyopādānavat tad asti /
# de ni 'di skad du sgyu ma'i rgyu ltar snang ba gang yin pa de ni yod do /
yathā khyāti grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa naitad eva māyāpuruṣādivat / / ato bhrāntir iti /
# ji ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang ba de ni de lta ma yin te / / sgyu ma'i skyes bu la sogs pa bzhin no / / de'i phyir 'khrul pa zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
ityetat paratantrasvabhāve tattvaṃ anyathā vidyamānasya svātmany / avidyamānenākāreṇa prakhyānaṃ / / atrāpyaviparītatvād iti prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate / [p.86] / pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ sadasat tattvataśceti /
# de ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid la de kho na ste / / gzhan du yod pa bdag nyid la med pa'i rnam par snang ngo / / skabs yin pas 'dir yang phyin ci ma log go zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / yongs su grub pa'i mtshan nyid ni / / yod dang med pa kho na ste /
sadasacca tattvaṃ pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ /
# zhes bya ba ni yod pa dang med pa dang de kho na ni yongs su grub pa'i mtshan nyid de /
dvayā'bhāvabhāvātmakatvāt sattvaṃ /
# gnyis pa med pa yod pa'i bdag nyid yin pas yod pas so /
dvayā'bhāvātmakatvād asattvañca /
# gnyis po med pa'i bdag nyid yin pas med pa'o /
viśuddhyālambanatvāt tattvaṃ /
# rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa yin pas de kho na'o /
etat pariniṣpanne svabhāve tattvaṃ / / aviparītatvād iti sambadhyate //3-3// / { lakṣaṇatattvaṃ }
# 'dir ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid la de kho na ste / / phyin ci ma log pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba dang sbyor ro /
svabhāvatrayasya tattvam uktaṃ na tu lakṣaṇam ityataḥ pṛcchati /
# ngo bo nyid gsum gyi de kho na ni bshad na / / mtshan nyid ma bshad de /
athavā mūlatattvā'nantaraṃ lakṣaṇatattvam uktaṃ taccā'prasiddham iti
# de'i phyir dris pa'am yang na rtsa ba'i de kho na'i 'og tu mtshan nyid kyi de kho na bshad la /
pṛcchati lakṣaṇatattvaṃ katamad iti /
# de yang ma grags pas na mtshan nyid kyi de kho na gang zhe na zhes dris te /
ata āha - / samāropā'pavādasya dharmapudgalayor iha / / iti vistaraḥ /
# de'i phyir / / 'di la chos dang gang zag dang / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
pudgaladharmayoḥ samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ yasya jñānān na pravartate / tat parikalpitasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇam iti /
# gang shes nas gang zag dang chos gnyis la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba mi 'byung ba de ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi de kho na'i mtshan nyid do zhes bya ba la /
ātmarūpādayaś ca dharmās tat pratibhāsavijñānavyatiriktasya / tadālambanabhūtāḥ paramārthataḥ santītyabhiniveśaḥ samāropadarśanaṃ /
# bdag dang gzugs la sogs pa'i chos rnams de dag tu snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ma gtogs par de'i dmigs par gyur pa don dam par yod do zhes mngon par zhen pa ni sgro 'dogs par lta ba'o /
vyavahārārtho'pi na santīty apavādadarśanaṃ /
# tha snyad du yang med do zhes bya ba ni skur pa 'debs par lta ba'o /
anya āhuḥ / / pudgaladharmapratibhāsavijñānaparihāro'pavādadarśanam iti / grāhā'pakṣepa iti cintyam etat /
# gzhan dag na re gang zag dang chos su snang ba'i rnam par shes pa spong ba ni skur pa 'debs par lta ba'o zhes zer te / / 'dzin pa spong ba 'di ni bsam dgos pa'o /
pudgaladharmayoḥ samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ yasya lakṣaṇasya paricchedān na / pravartate tat parikalpitasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ samāropāpavādavarjitaṃ / veditavyaṃ / / tac ca vyavahāreṇa tattvaṃ na tu svabhāvena yasmāt
# mtshan nyid gang yongs su gcad pas gang zag dang chos gnyis la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba de ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi de kho na'i mtshan nyid de / / sgro 'dogs pa dang skur ba 'debs pa spangs par rig par bya'o / / de'ang tha snyad du de kho na yin gyi ngo bo nyid kyis ni ma yin no /
parikalpitā'vabodhāddharmapudgalayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanam na / pravartate /
# gang gi phyir kun brtags pa khong du chung na gang zag dang chos gnyis la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba mi 'byung ba zhes bya ba ni mi skye'i zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
na jāyata ity arthaḥ / / grāhyagrāhakayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanam iti vistaraḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba zhes rgya cher 'byung ba la /
grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsabhrāntiryā dharmeṇa pudgalena ca gṛhyate sā / yadi tattvenaivāstītyabhiniviśate evaṃ grāhyagrāhakasamāropaḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba'i 'khrul pa gang la chos dang gang zag tu 'dzin pa de gal te kho na nyid du yod do zhes mngon par zhen na de la bu ni gzung ba dang 'dzin par sgro 'dogs pa'o /
atha grāhyasyeva grāhaksyāpyabhāvam abhiniviśate evaṃ / grāhyagrāhakāpavādaḥ /
# ji ste gzung ba bzhin du 'dzin pa yang med do zhes mngon par zhen na / / de lta bu ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la skur pa 'debs pa'o /
yasya lakṣaṇasya jñānād grāhyagrāhakayoḥ samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ na / pravartate tat paratantrasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ samāropāpavādavarjitaṃ / jñātavyaṃ / / tat punaḥ kalpitayā grāhyagrāhakātmatayā'sattvaṃ tad
# mtshan nyid gang shes nas gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta bar mi 'byung ba de ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid de / / sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa spangs par shes par bya'o / / de yang brtags pa ste gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid du med pa'o /
vyavahārāśrayatvena ca sattvaṃ /
# de'i tha snyad kyi gnas yin pa'i phyir yod pa'o /
evaṃ hi parijñānāt [p.87] / paratantre samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ na pravartate /
# de ltar yongs su shes na gzhan gyi dbang la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba mi 'byung ngo /
bhāvā'bhāva samāropāpavādadarśanam iti vistaraḥ / / kecidāhuḥ yadi śūnyatāṃ bhāva eveti samanupaśYati evaṃ
# dngos po dang dngos po med par sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba zhes rgya cher 'byung ba la kha cig na re / / gal te stong pa nyid dngos po yod pa nyid do zhes yang dag par rjes su lta na /
bhāvasamāropadarśanaṃ bhavati / / athā'bhāva evetyevam abhāvadarśanaṃ / / etad ubhayam api bhāvābhāvadarśanaṃ / / yasya lakṣaṇasya jñānān na te bhāvābhāvadarśane pravartete tat
# de lta ni dngos por sgro 'dogs par lta bar 'gyur ro / / ji ste med pa nyid do zhe na / / de lta bu ni dngos po med par lta ba'o / / mtshan nyid gang shes nas dngos po dang dngos po med par lta ba de gnyis mi 'byung ba ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi de kho na'i mtshan nyid do /
pariniṣpannasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇam iti / / tac ca bhāvā'bhāvāvimuktasvabhāvaṃ /
# kha cig na re de yang dngos po dang dngos po med pa las rnam par grol ba'i ngo bo nyid yin la /
taj jñānāddhi pariniṣpanne svabhāve bhāvā'bhāvapradarśanaṃ na / pravartata ityeke /
# de shes nas yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid la dngos po dang dngos po med par lta ba mi 'byung ngo zhe'o /
anye punar āhuḥ - dvayābhāvasvarūpaiva śūnyatetyabhāvasamāropāntaḥ / bhāvā'bhāvavimuktātmakatve bhāvasvarūpasamāropaṇāt / / bhāvā'bhāvavimuktena dvayā'bhāvasvarūpeṇa / nirvikalpajñānagocareṇā'sau nāstītyabhāvāpavādāntaḥ /
# gzhan na re dngos po dang dngos po med pa las rnam par grol ba'i bdag nyid can la / / dngos po'i ngo bor sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir gnyis po med pa ni rang gi ngo bos stong pa nyid do zhe na / / dngos por sgro 'dogs pa'i mthar 'gyur ro / / de dngos po dang dngos po med pa las rnam par grol ba gnyis su med pa'i rang bzhin rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul du yang med do zhe na / / dngos po med par skur ba 'debs pa'i mthar 'gyur ro zhes zer ro /
bhāvā'bhāvayoḥ pratyekaṃ samāropā'pavādadarśanasyābhisambandhāc / cintyam etad vyākhyānādvayam ityaparaḥ /
# gzhan na re dngos po dang dngos po med pa gnyis la so sor sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba dang sbyar bas bshad pa 'di gnyis kyang bsam dogs pa'o zhe'o /
bhāvo'tra dvayā'bhāvasya bhāvaḥ /
# 'dir dngos po ni gnyis po med pa'i dngos po ste /
taṃ yadi bhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevaṃ bhāvaḥ samāropito bhavati /
# gal te de la dngos po nyid du 'dzin na de lta na ni dngos por sgro 'dogs par 'gyur ro /
yady abhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevam apodito bhavati /
# ji ste dngos po med pa nyid du 'dzin na de lta na ni skur pa 'debs par 'gyur ro /
bhāvo'pidvayābhāvasthaṃ yadi ucchedato gṛhṇātyevaṃ / bhāvo'tyantābhāvatvena samāropito bhavati/
# 'dir ni dngos po med pa na ni gnyis po'i dngos po med pa ste / / gal gte de la chad pa nyid du na de lta na ni dngos po med pa'ang shin tu med pa nyid pas sgro 'dogs par 'gyur ro /
atha dvayata eva gṛhṇātyevam apodito bhavati yasmādetad dvayābhāvena / prabhāvitaṃ /
# ji ste gnyis po nyid du 'dzin na de lta na ni skur par 'gyur te / / 'di ltar de ni gnyis kyi dngos po med pas rab tu phye ba yin no /
athavā taṃ bhāvā'bhāvasvarūpeṇa gṛhṇātyevaṃ samāropito bhavati / / athā'bhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevaṃ saṃkleśo vyavadānañcā'poditam bhavatīti / / etad antadvayavidhātanaṃ pariniṣpannatve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ / / nanu pūrvam api trisvabhāvalakṣaṇam uktaṃ - / arthād abhūtakalpāc ca dvayābhāvāc ca deśitaḥ // iti / / tatra svabhāvo lakṣaṇam iha tu cihnam iti nāsti punaruktatā / / yajjñānān na pravarteta taddhi tattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ /
# yang na gal te dngos po'i ngo bor 'dzin na de lta na ni sgro btags par 'gyur ro / / ji ste dngos po med pa nyid du 'dzin na de lta na ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba la yang skur pa 'gyur te / / mtha' gnyis spangs pa 'di ni yongs su grub pa nyid kyi de kho na'i mtshan nyid do / / don phyir yang dag min rtogs phyir / / gnyis po med pa'i phyir bshad do / / zhes ngo bo nyid gsum gyi mtshan nyid sngar yang bshad ma zin na ma zhe na / / der ni ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid do / / 'dir ni gang shes nas mi 'byung ba de ni de kho na'i mtshan nyid do /
iti pudgalādisamāropāpavādadarśanaṃ yaj jñānān na pravartate tan / mūlatattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ //3-4//
# zhes bya ba'i mtshan ma yin pas zlog pa med do / / gang shes nas gang zag la sogs par sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba mi 'byung ba de ni rtsa ba'i de kho na'i mtshan nyid do /
{ aviparyāsatattvaṃ } [p.88] / lakṣaṇatattvānantaram aviparyāsatattvaṃ vaktavyaṃ tad anantaram / uddiṣṭatvād ityata āha - aviparyāsatattvam iti vistaraḥ /
# de'i 'og tu bshad pa'i phyir mtshan nyid kyi de kho na'i 'og tu phyin ci ma log pa'i de kho na brjod par bya ste / / de'i phyir phyin ci ma log pa'i de kho na ni zhes bya cher smos so /
anityaduḥkhaśūnyā'nātmato hi / nityasukhaśuddhātmaviparyāsapratipakṣatvād aviparyāsatattvam ity ucyate
# mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa ni rtag pa dang bde ba dang gtsang ba dang bdag tu phyin ci log pa'i gnyen po yin pas phyin ci ma log pa'i de kho na zhes bya'o /
mūlatattve tad anyatattvāntarbhāvaḥ pūrvaṃ pratijñāta ityataḥ pṛcchati
# rtsa ba'i de kho na'i nang du de kho na gzhan 'dus so zhes sngar dam bcas pas de'i phyir /
- mūlatattve katham iti vistaraḥ /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na der ji ltar zhen zhes rgya cher dris so /
anityāditeti / / anityādayo ye'nityaduḥkhaśūnyā'nātmaprakārās te'nityādayaḥ /
# mi rtag pa la sogs pa nyid ces bya ba ni mi rtag pa la sogs pa gang dag yin pa mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa'i rnam pa de dag mi rtag pa la sgos pa'o /
tad bhāvo'nityāditā /
# de'i dngos po ni mi rtag pa la sogs pa nyid do /
mūlatattve'viparyāsatattvasyāntarbhāvapradarśanārtham āha -
# rtsa ba'i de kho na'i nang du phyin ci ma log pa'i de kho na 'dus par bstan pa'i phyir /
asadartho hy anityārtha / iti vistaraḥ /
# mi rtag don ni med don dang / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
trividho hy anityārthaḥ - asadarthaḥ utpādavyārthaḥ samalāmalatārthaś / ca /
# mi rtag pa'i don ni rnam pa gsum ste / / med pa'i don dang skye zhing 'jig pa'i don dang dri ma dang bcas shing dri ma med pa'i don do /
yaḥ sarvadā tathāsti sa nityaḥ /
# gang dus thams cad du de bzhin du yod pa de ni rtag pa ste /
tad viparīto'nityaḥ /
# de las bzlog pa ni mi rtag pa ste /
teṣu yathākramam iti / / tatra sarvadā'sadarthā'nityārthena parikalpitasvabhāvo'nityaḥ /
# de dag tu go rims bzhin no zhes bya ba ni de la dus thams cad du med pa'i don mi rtag pa'i don gyis kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ni mi rtag pa'o /
asannityam anityam iti niruttinyāyena veditavyamityanye /
# gzhan dag na re nges pa'i tshig gi tshul du na rtag pa med pa ni mi rtag par rig par bya'o zhe'o /
pratikṣaṇamutpādavyahalakṣaṇenā'nityārthenā'nityaḥ paratantrasvabhāvaḥ
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid ni skad cig re re la skye zhing 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid yin te / / mi rtag pa'i phyir mi rtag pa'o /
tasya pratyayotpādyatvād vināśe cā'hetukatvāt / / samalāmalatā'rthalakṣaṇenāgantukenā'nityārthenā'nityo'vikāradharmo'pi / pariniṣpannasvabhāva iti /
# de ni rkyen las byung ba dang 'jig pa la rgyu med pa'i phyir ro / / yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid mi 'gyur pa'i chos yin du zin kyang dri ma dang bcas pa dang dri ma med pa nyid kyi don gyi mtshan nyid glo bur gyi don mi rtag pa'o /
duḥkhamādānalakṣmākhyaṃ
# sdug bsngal len dang mtshan nyid dang /
iti vistaraḥ / / duḥkham api trividhaṃ - upādānaduḥkhaṃ lakṣaṇaduḥkhaṃ sambandhaduḥkhañca
# zhes rgya cher 'byung ba la sdug bsngal ba la yang rnam pa gsum ste / / nye bar len pas sdug bsngal ba dang mtshan nyid kyis sdug bsngal ba dang 'brel bas sdug bsngal ba'o /
tatra kalpitasvabhāva upādānato duḥkhaṃ /
# de la brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ni nye bar len pas sdug bsngal te /
aparijñātenehā'mutra vā duḥkham upādīyata iti duḥkhaṃ /
# yongs su ma shes pas 'di'am gzhan na sdug bsngal nye bar len pas sdug bsngal lo /
yathā ca tenā'parijñātena duḥkham upādīyate tat pradarśayann āha - [p.89
# ji ltar na de yongs su ma shes pas sdug bsngal nye bar len pa de bstan pa'i phyir /
pudgaladharmābhiniveśopādānād iti /
# gang zag dang chos la mngon par zhen pa nye bar len pa'i phyir zhes bya ba smos te /
tad bhāvagrāhadvāreṇa pudgaladharmam abhiniviśata iti / pudgaladharmābhiniveśaḥ /
# des dngos por 'dzin pa'i sgo nas gang zag dang chos su mngon par zhen pas na gang zag dang chos la mngon par zhen pa'o /
sa ca dvayapatitatvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ /
# de yang gnyis su lhung ba'i phyir kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid de /
parikalpitasvabhāvā'bhiniveśād duḥkhaprabandha ityevam uktaṃ na punaḥ
# kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la mngon par zhen pa ni sdug bsngal gyi rgyun gyi rgyu yin pas de skad bshad kyi /
parikalpita eva duḥkhaṃ / / tad abhāvāt /
# kun brtags pa nyid ni sdug bsngal ma yin te / / de med pa'i phyir ro /
athavā parikalpitasvabhāvaḥ pudgaladharmābhiniveśena
# yang na kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid gang zag dang chos la mngon par zhen nas dngos po'i ngo bor nye bar len pa ste /
vasturūpeṇopādīyata ityevam upādānataḥ kalpitaḥ svabhāvo duḥkhaṃ /
# de ltar nye bar len pas brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la mngon par zhen pa ni sdug bsngal lo /
paratantraḥ svabhāvo lakṣaṇato duḥkham iti sambadhyate / / tisro hi duḥkhatā - duḥkhaduḥkhatā vipariṇāmadaḥkhatā saṃskāraduḥkhatā / ca /
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid ni mtshan nyid kyi sdug bsngal zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro / / mtshan nyid kyi sdug bsngal ba ni sdug bsngal nyid rnam pa gsum ste; sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid dang 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid dang 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid do /
tāś ca tisro'pi duḥkhatāḥ paratantraduḥkhatā iti lakṣaṇato duḥkhaṃ /
# sdug bsngal rnam pa gsum po de dag ni gzhan gyi dbang gi sdug bsngal te / / mtshan nyid kyi sdug bsngal ba'o /
pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ sambandhato duḥkhaṃ /
# yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid ni 'brel pas sdug bsngal ba'o /
ca śabdaḥ samuccaryārthaḥ / / kathaṃ sambandhataḥ ?
# yang zhes bya ba'i sgra ni bsdu ba'i don to / / ji lta zhe na / / 'brel pa'i phyir te /
ity ata āha - duḥkhasambandhād iti /
# de'i phyir sdug bsngal dang 'brel pa'i phyir bya ba smos so /
paratantrasvabhāvo duḥkhaṃ /
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid ni sdug bsngal te /
tad dharmasya pariniṣpannasyā'pi duḥkhasambandhād duḥkham ucyate /
# de'i chos nyid yongs su grub pa yang sdug bsngal dang 'brel pa'i phyir sdug bsngal zhes bya'o /
atraiva mūlatattve yathākramam iti tatropādānato duḥkhaṃ parikalpitaḥ / / lakṣaṇataḥ paratantraḥ /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na nyid kyi nang du go rims bzhin no zhes bya ba de la / / nye bar len pas sdug bsngal ni kun brtags pa'o / / mtshan nyid kyis ni gzhan gyi dbang ngo /
sambandhataḥ pariniṣpannaḥ //3-6//
# 'brel pas ni yongs su grub pa'o /
abhāvaścāpyatadbhāvaḥ prakṛtiḥ śūnyatā matā / iti /
# dngos med de yi dngos ma yin / / rang bzhin gyis ni stong par 'dod / / ces bya ba la stong pa nyid ni rnam pa gsum ste /
trividhā śūnyatā - amāvaśūnyatā atadbhāvaśūnyatā prakṛtiśūnyatā / ca /
# dngos po med pas stong pa nyid dang de ma yin pas stong pa nyid dang rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid do /
tatrā'bhāvaśūnyatā parikalpatasya svabhāvasya /
# da la dngos po med pas stong pa nyid ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid de /
etat pratipādayann āha - parikalpitalakṣaṇaṃ [p.90 / ] śaśaviṣāṇādisvarūpavad bhrāntyā na kenacit prakāreṇa yenāpi sattvaṃ / grāhyaṃ nāsti ityabhāva evā'sya śūnyateti / / atadbhāvaśūnyatā paratantrasya /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir / / kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid ni ri bong gi rva la sogs pa'i rang bzhin ltar mngon sum dang rjes su dpag pa rnam pa gang gis kyang yod par gzung du med de / / dngos po med pa nyid pas de'i stong pa nyid do zhes bya ba smos so / / de ma yin pas stong pa nyid ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid de /
etad eva pratipādayann āha - paratantralakṣaṇaṃ tathā nāsti yathā / bālair dvayātmanā parikalpyate /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir / / gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid ni ji ltar byis pa rnams kyis gnyis kyi bdag nyid du kun brtags pa de ltar med kyi /
na tu sarvathā nāsti yathā cā'sti tathā / śuddhalaukikajñānenādhigamyate /
# ji ltar dag pa 'jig rten pa'i ye shes kyis rtog par 'gyur pa lta bu yang ye med pa ni ma yin te /
tasyā'tadbhāvaḥ śūnyateti /
# de bas na de ma yin pas de'i stong pa nyid do zhes bya ba smos so /
prakṛtiśūnyatā pariniṣpannasya /
# rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid de /
ata evāha - pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ dvayābhāvasvabhāvatvāc
# de'i phyir yongs su grub pa'i mtshan nyid ni gnyis po med pa'i dngos po'i ri bo 'di yin pa'i phyir stong pa nyid kyi ngo bo nyid do /
chūnyatāsvabhāvam eveti / / tasmāt prakṛtir eva svabhāva evā'sya śūnyatā / / alakṣaṇañca nairātmyaṃ / iti vistaraḥ / / trividhaṃ nairātmyaṃ - alkṣaṇanairātmyaṃ vilakṣaṇanairātmyaṃ / svalakṣaṇanairātmyañca / / tatra parikalpitasya svabhāvasya lakṣaṇā'bhāvād alakṣaṇam eva / nairātmyaṃ / / ata evāha - parikalpitasya svabhāvasya lakṣaṇam eva nāstītyalakṣaṇam
# de bas na rang bzhin kho na ste ngo bo nyid kho nas de'i stong pa nyid do zhes bya ba smos so / / mtshan nyid med pas bdag med dang / / zhes rgya cher 'byung ba la bdag med pa yang rnam pa gsum ste / / mtshan nyid med pas bdag med pa dang mi mthun pa'i mtshan nyid kyis bdag med pa dang rang gi mtshan nyid kyis bdag med pa'o / / de la kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ni mtshan nyid kyis dngos po med pas mtshan nyid med pa nyid bdag med pa ste /
evāsya nairātmyaṃ nānyena prakāreṇeti darśayati / / paratantrasya vilakṣaṇanairātmyaṃ yasmāt paratantrasyāsti lakṣaṇaṃ
# de'i phyir kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ni mtshan nyid kyis med pa'i phyir mtshan nyid med pa nyid de'i bdag med pa zhes bya ba smos te / / rnam pa gzhan gyis ni ma yin par ston to / / gzhan gyi dbang ni mi mthun pa'i mtshan nyid kyis bdag med pa ste /
vasturūpaṃ / / na tu tad yathā bālaiḥ parikalpyate dvayatvena / / tad vilakṣaṇam iti parikalpitalakṣaṇenā'sadṛśaṃ / / paratantralakṣaṇaṃ tan nairāmyaṃ /
# 'di ltar gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid ni dngos po'i ngo bor yod kyang des byis pa rnams kyis gnyis su ji ltar kun brtags pa de ltar ni yod pa ma yin no / / de dang mi mthun pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya ba ni kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid dang mi 'dra ba ste / / gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid de'i bdag med pa'o /
evaṃ parikalpitenātmanā nairātmyam asya darśītaṃ bhavati /
# de ltar na kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid kyis de'i bdag med par bstan pa yin no /
svalakṣaṇaṃ nairātmyaṃ pariniṣpannasya /
# rang gi mtshan nyid kyis bdag med pa ni yongs su grub pa ste /
yataḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvo grāhyagrāhakābhāvarūpatvān nairātmyam / eveti svalakṣaṇam asya nairātmyam iti pariniṣpannasya dharmasya / nairātmyasvabhāvatāṃ darśayati / / kaḥ punar anayoḥ śūnyatā'nātmatayor viśeṣaḥ ?
# 'di ltar yongs su grub pa ni ngo bo nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir bdag nyid med pas de bas na rang gi mtshan nyid de'i bdag med pa'o zhes bya ba ni yongs su grub pa'i chos la bdag med pa'i ngo bo nyid du ston to / / stong pa nyid dang bdag med pa 'di gnyis la khyad par ci yod ce na /
yadyatra nāsti tat tena śūnyaṃ /
# kha cig na re gang na gang med pa de ni des stong la /
yat tu yasyātmā svabhāvo na bhavati tat tenā'nātmetyayam anayor viśeṣa / ity eke /
# gang zhig gang gis bdag ste ngo bo nyid ma yin pa de ni bdag med pa ste / / 'di gnyis kyi khyad par ni 'di yin no zhe'o /
arthataḥ ko'pi viśeṣo nāsti vyavasthānabhedena tu bhedaḥ / / yasmādyadyatra nāsti tena tasya niḥsvabhāvatām upādāya nairātmyam / itarasya tu tatrā'niṣpannasvabhāvatām upādāya śūnyatvam iti / [p.91] / trividhe mūlatattve samāropāpavādāntayoḥ / pratipakṣeṇāgantukamalapradarśanena ca yathākramaṃ trividhā'nityatā
# kha cig na re don du khyad par gang yang med mod kyi rnam par gzhag pa'i bye brag gis tha dad de; 'di ltar gang na gang med pa des de'i ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir bdag med pa dang cig shos ni de la yongs su ma grub pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi phyir stong pa nyid do zhe'o / / sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' gnyis kyi gnyen po dang glo bur gyi dri ma bstan pa'i phyir ro / / rtsa ba'i de kho na rnam pa gsum la go rims bzhin du mi rtag pa nyid rnam pa gsum yongs su bstan te /
paridīpitā / / sā'sadartha'nityatā utpādabhaṅgā'nityatā samalanirmalā'nityatā ca /
# med pa'i don mi rtag pa nyid dang skye zhing 'jig pa mi rtag pa nyid dang dri ma dang bcas shing dri ma med pa'i mi rtag pa nyid do /
evaṃ yāvat trividhaṃ nairātmyam ityuktam aviparyāsatattvaṃ //3-7//
# de bzhin du bdag med pa rnam pa gsum gyi bar du bstan pa ni phyin ci ma log pa'i de kho na'o /
{ phalahetutattvaṃ  } / tad anantaraṃ phalahetutattvaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha - phalahetumayantattvaṃ
# de'i 'og tu 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na brjod dgos te / / de'i phyir 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na nyid la zhes rgya cher smos so /
mūlatattvaṃ iti vistaraḥ / / tatra saṅkleśapakṣam adhikṛtya duḥkhasatyaṃ phalatattvaṃ /
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs kyi dbang du mdzad de / / sdug bsngal gyi bden pa ni 'bras bu'i de kho na'o /
samudayasatyaṃ hetutattvaṃ vyavadānapakṣe'pi nirodhasatyaṃ phalatattvaṃ
# kun 'byung gi bden pa ni rgyu'i de kho na'o / / rnam par byang ba'i phyogs la yang 'gog pa'i bden pa ni 'bras bu'i de kho na'o /
mārgasatyaṃ hetutattvaṃ /
# lam gyi bden pa ni rgyu'i de kho na'o /
evaṃ duḥkhādīni catvāri satyāni phalahetutattvaṃ /
# de ltar sdug bsngal la sogs pa bden pa rnam pa bzhi ni 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na'o /
mūlatattve duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgasatyam ityuktaṃ /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na nyid la sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam gyi bden pa rnams so zhes bshad na /
tac ca na vijñāyate kathaṃ mūlatattvaṃ duḥkhādisatyasvabhāvam ityataḥ
# de yang ji ltar na rtsa ba'i de kho na sdug bsngal la sogs pa bden pa'i ngo bo nyid yin pa mi shes na / / de'i phyir /
pṛcchati - kathaṃ trividhaṃ mūlatattvaṃ duḥkhādisatyam iti ? / ata āha - yatas tad anityādilakṣaṇaṃ -
# ji ltar rtsa ba'i de kho na rnam pa gsum la sdug bsngal la sogs pa'i bden pa zhes bya zhe na zhes bya ba dris pa dang; de'i phyir 'di ltar de mi rtag pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid kyis te /
duḥkhasatyaṃ tato mataṃ / iti /
# de'i phyir sdug bsngal bden par 'dod ces bya ba smos te /
anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmatāyā duḥkhasatyalakṣaṇatvāt tac ca samastaṃ / pratyekaṃ kalpitādiṣv astīti vistareṇoktaṃ /
# mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa nyid ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i mtshan nyid pas de dag thams cad kun brtags pa la sogs pa re re la yod par rgyas par bstan te /
ataḥ kalpitādayaḥ pratyekaṃ duḥkhasatyatvenābhipretā iti /
# de'i phyir kun brtags pa la sogs pa re re la sdug bsngal gyi bden pa nyid du 'dod do /
trividhena samudayā'rthena mūlatattvaṃ samudayasatyaṃ yathākramaṃ /
# kun 'byung ba'i don rnam pa gsum gyis rtsa ba'i de kho nar kun 'byung ba'i bden pa'i go rims bzhin no /
sa eva samudayo na jñāyata ityata āha - trividhaḥ samudayārthaḥ /
# kun 'byung ba'i de nyid mi shes pas de'i phyir / / kun 'byung ba'i don rnam pa gsum ni /
vāsanā'tha samutthānam avisaṃyoga eva ca // iti /
# bag chags dang ni kun nas 'byung / / ma bral ba yang de bzhin no / / zhes bya ba smos te /
trividhaḥ samudayo vāsanāsamudayaḥ samutthānasamudayaḥ / avisaṃyogasamudayaś ca /
# rnam pa gsum ni bag chags kyi kun 'byung ba dang kun nas byung ba'i kun 'byung ba dang ma bral ba'i kun 'byung ba'o /
tatra vāsanāsamudayaḥ parikalpitasvabhāvo veditavyaḥ /
# de la bag chags kyi kun 'byung ba ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid du shes par bya ste /
ata āha - parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśavāsaneti /
# de'i phyir kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la mngon par zhen pa'i bag chags so zhes bya ba smos te /
asti hi parikalpite svabhāve'stītyabhiniveśam upādāya laukikā dharmā / vikalpakleśavāsanāṃ vyavasthāpayanti na tu vigatābhiniveśā lokottarā /
# kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid med par yod do zhes mngon par zhen pa nye bar bzung nas 'jig rten gyi chos rnam par rtog pa'i bag chags 'jog par byed kyi / / mngon par zhen pa med pa 'jig rten las 'das pa dag ni ma yin te /
tataḥ parikalpitasvabhāvo vāsanāsamudaya ucyate / / samutthānasamudayaḥ paratantraḥ / / samutthāna ātmalābhaḥ / / sa yato bhavati sa samutthānasamudayaḥ [p.92] / samudetyasmād iti kṛtvā /
# de bas na kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la bag chags kyis kun 'byung ba zhes bya'o / / kun nas byung ba'i kun 'byung ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid do / / kun nas byung ba zhes bya ba ni bdag thob pa ste / / de gang las byung ba de ni de las 'byung ngo zhes bya ba'i phyir kun nas 'byung ba'o /
sa punaḥ kiṃsvarūpa ityata āha - karmakleśā iti /
# de yang rang bzhin ji lta bu zhe na de'i phyir las dang nyon mongs pa rnams so zhes bya ba smos te /
te ca vastusvarūpatvāt paratantrasvabhāvaḥ / / avisaṃyogasamudayasthatāyā iti / / katham ityata āha - āvaraṇā'visaṃyoga iti /
# de dag kyang dngos po'i rang bzhin yin pas gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid do / / ma bral ba'i kun 'byung ba ni de bzhin nyid la bya ste / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / sgrib pa dang ma bral zhes bya ba smos te / / de ni 'di skad du /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - yāvadāvaraṇair na visaṃyuktā tathatā tāvat / samudeti duḥkham iti /
# de bzhin nyid ji srid du sgrib pa rnams dang ma bral ba de srid du sdug bsngal kun 'byung zhes bya ba'am /
āvaraṇair avisaṃyuktā vā tathatā samudayadharmateti samudayanāmmlābha
# sgrib pa rnams dang ma bral ba'i de bzhin nyid ni kun 'byung ba'i chos nyid yin pas kun 'byung ba'i ming 'thob po zhes bya bar bstan par 'gyur ro /
iti //3-8// / trividhena nirodhena mūlatattvaṃ nirodhasatyaṃ / / tac ca na vijñāyata ityata āha - trividho nirodhaḥ -
# 'gog pa rnam pa gsum gyis rtsa ba'i de kho nar 'gog pa'i bden pa yin na de yang mi shes nas de'i phyir /
svabhāvadvayanotpattir malaśāntidvayaṃ mataṃ / iti /
# 'gog pa rnam pa gsum ni; ngo bo nyid dang gnyis mi skye / / dri ma zhi ba gnyis su 'dod / / ces bya ba smos so /
tatra svabhāvā'nutpattiḥ parikalpitasya yasya hi niḥsvabhāvatvād / ātyantikyanutpattir vandhyāputravat /
# de la ngo bo nyid kyis mi skye ba ni kun brtags pa ste / / de ni mo gsham gyi bu bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pas gtan du mi skye ste /
grāhyagrāhakayor anutpattiḥ paratantrasya /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis mi skye ba ni gzhan gyi dbang ste /
tasyāpi grāhyagrāhakasvarūpābhyām atyantarahitatvād / dvayabhrāntyātmanā'nutpattiḥ /
# de yang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis kyi rang bzhin dang gtan bral ba'i phyir 'khrul pa gnyis kyi bdag nyid du mi skye ba'o /
malaśāntidvayaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ / / ca śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ /
# dri ma zhim pa gnyis ni yongs su grub pa'o / / kyang zhes bya ni bsdu ba'i don to /
tat punar na vijñāyata ityata āha - pratisaṃkhyānirodhatathatākhyam iti
# de yang mi shes nas de'i phyir so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa dang de bzhin nyid ces bya ba'o zhes bya ba smos so /
malaṃ dvividhaṃ rāgādyāvaraṇaṃ parikalpitaś ca /
# dri ma ni rnam pa gnyis te / / 'dod tshags la sogs pa'i sgrib pa dang kun brtags pa'o /
tatrā'nāsveṇa jñānenāśrayād bīja uddhṛte rāgādimalānām atyantam / anutpādātmikā śāntiḥ pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ /
# de la zag pa med pa'i ye shes kyi sa bon gnas nas bton te / / 'dod chags la sog pa'i dri ma rnams gtan mi skye ba'i bdag nyid kyis zhi ba ni so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa'o /
tathatāgocareṇā'dvayajñānena parikalpitamalasyā'nutpādātmikā śāntis / tathatā /
# de bzhin nyid du spyod yul pa gnyis su med pa'i ye shes kyis kun brtags pa'i dri ma mi skye ba'i bdag nyid kyis zhi ba ni de bzhin nyid do /
etaddhi dvayaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ /
# 'di gnyis ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid do /
eṣa trividho nirodhaḥ kalpitādau mūlatattve yathāsaṃkhyaṃ vijñeyaḥ / [p.93]
# 'gog pa rnam pa 'di gsum ni brtags pa la sogs pa rtsa ba'i de kho nar go rims bzhin du shes par bya'o /
anye tu tathatāprativedhena kleśaparikalpitamaladvayaśāntir iti / malaśāntistathatety ucyate dvayanirodhaḥ prakṛtinirodhaśceti vacanāt /
# gzhan dag na re de bzhin nyid rab tu rtogs pas nyon mongs pa dang kun brtags pa'i dri ma gnyis zhi ba ni de bzhin nyid ces brjod do / / gnyis 'gog pa dang rang bzhin 'gog pa zhes 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
prakṛtir iti tathatā prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvāc cittasyeti /
# rang bzhin zhes bya ba ni sems rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i phyir de bzhin nyid la bya'o /
atas tathatālambanādyo nirodhaḥ sa prakṛtinirodha ity ucyate /
# de'i phyir de bzhin nyid la dmigs pas 'gog pa gang yin pa de ni rang bzhin gyis 'gog pa zhes bya ste /
niruddhamātraṃ pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ / / nirodhyate'syām iti nirodhastathatetyapare /
# 'gag pa tsam la so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa zhes bya'o zhe'o / / kha cig na re 'dir 'gags pas 'gog pa ni de bzhin nyid do /
nirodhasya punar anutpādātmakatvāt sarve svabhāvānutpattyādikaṃ / saṃkṣipya nirodhasatyam ity ucyate /
# 'gog pa ni mi skye ba'i bdag nyid pas ngo bo nyid kyis mi skye ba la sogs pa thams cad bsdus te 'gog pa'i bden pa zhes bya'o /
ukto nirodhasatyasya mūlatattve'ntarbhāvaḥ /
# 'gog pa'i bden pa rtsa ba'i de kho nar bsdus pa bshad zin to /
tad anantaraṃ tu mārgasatyam antarbhāvayitavyam ityataḥ pṛcchati - / mārgasatyaṃ trividhamūlatattve kathaṃ vyavasthāpyata ityata - / parijñāyāṃ prahāṇe ca / ityādi / / parikalpitasya parijñāna iti /
# de'i 'og tu lam gyi bden pa bsdu bar bya ste; de'i phyir lam gyi bden pa rtsa ba'i de kho nar rnam pa gsum du ji ltar rab tu gzhag ce na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir / / yongs su shes par bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so / / kun brtags pa ni yongs su shes par bya ba'o zhes bya ba la /
parikalpitato'tyantam asanneveti tasya parijñānam eva na prahāṇaṃ / / na hyasataḥ prahāṇaṃ yujyate / / paratantrasya parijñāne prahāṇe ca /
# kun brtags pa ni gtan med pa nyid pas de ni yongs su shes par bya bar zad kyi spang du med de med pa ni spang bar mi rung ngo / / gzhan gyi dbang ni yongs su shes par bya ba dang spang ba'o zhes bya ba la /
paratantro hi yathā khyāti tathā'sattvaṃ vijñeyaṃ na tu
# gzhan gyi dbang ni ji ltar snang ba de ltar med par shes par bya'i /
sarvātmatvenāsattvaṃ kalpitavat /
# brtags pa bzhin du thams cad kyi bdag nyid kyis med par ni ma yin no /
karmakleśayor bhāvātmatvāt prahātavyaś ca /
# las dang nyon mongs pa ni dngos po'i bdag nyid yin pas spang bar bya ba yang yin no /
pariniṣpannasya praijñāne prāptisākṣātkaraṇe ceti /
# yongs su grub pa ni yongs su shes par bya ba dang thob par mngon sum du bya ba'o zhes bya ba la /
pariniṣpanno hi bhāvābhāvavinirmuktalakṣaṇam ataḥ parijñeyaḥ / āśrayaparāvṛttitāyāś ca /
# yongs su grub pa ni dngos po dang dngos po med pa las rnam par grol ba'i mtshan nyid dang gnas gyur pa nyid du yongs su shes par bya zhing /
āśayaparāvṛttitā vinirmuktadharmakāyatvena sākṣātkartavyeti śūnyatā / parijñeyā / / nirodhaḥ sākṣātkartavyaḥ prāptisākṣātkriyayā /
# gnas par gyur pa nyid rnam par grol ba chos kyi skur mngon sum du bya ba yin pas stong pa nyid ni yongs su shes par bya ba'o / / 'gog pa ni thob par mngon sum du byas pas mngon sum du bya ba'o /
ubhayaṃ cobhathetyanye / / dvividhā hi parijñā - jñānaparijñā prahāṇaparijñā ca /
# kha cig na re gnyis la rnam pa gnyis gnyis te yongs su shes pa rnam gnyis ni shes pa'i yongs su shes pa'i dang spong ba'i yongs su shes pa'o /
tatra jñānaparijñāyaparijñeyaṃ prathamaṃ tṛtīyañca /
# de la dngos po dang gsum pa ni shes pa'i yongs su shes pas yongs su shes par bya ba'o /
dvitīyaṃ tūbhayaparijñeyaṃ /
# gnyis pa ni gnyis kas yongs su shes par bya'o /
sākṣātkriyāpi dvidhā - jñānasākṣātkriyā prāptisākṣātkriyā ceti
# mngon sum du bya ba rnam pa gnyis ni / / shes par mngon sum du bya ba dang thob par mngon sum du bya'o /
tatra jñānasākṣātkriyayā trayam api sākṣātkartavyaṃ /
# de la shes par mngon sum du bya bas ni gsum char yang mngon sum du bya'o /
prāptisākṣātkriyayā tu tṛtīyam eva /
# thob par mngon sum du bya bas ni gsum pa nyid do zhe'o /
evam atra mūlatattve parijñā prahāṇasākṣātkriyāyāṃ mārgasatya / vyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ na tu tatrāntarbhāvāt /
# de ltar rtsa ba'i de kho na 'dir yongs su shes par bya ba dang spang bar bya ba dang mngon sum du bya ba rnams kyis lam gyi bden pa rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'i /
atra ca satyacatuṣṭayena yaḥ saṅkleśo yataś ca tayoś ca viśuddhir yā / yataśca tat paridīpitaṃ /
# de'i khongs su gtogs par bsdu ba ni ma yin no / / de la bden pa bzhis ni kun nas nyon mongs pa gang yin pa dang; gang las byung ba dang de gnyis rnam par dag pa gang yin pa dang gang las 'gyur pa de rnams yongs su brjod do /
anukramas tveṣāṃ yathā'bhisamayam iti / / { audārikasūkṣmatattvaṃ } [p.94] / audārikasūkṣmatattvañceti / / audārikatattvaṃ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ sūkṣmatattvaṃ tu paramārthasatyaṃ / / yata ādāvaudārikeṇa sattvān paripācayati paripakvāṃs tu sūkṣmeṇa
# de dag gi go rims ni ji ltar mngon par rtogs pa bzhin du'o / / rags pa dang phra ba'i de kho na ni zhes bya ba la / / rags pa'i de kho na ni kun rdzob kyi bden pa'o; / / phra ba'i de kho na ni don dam pa'i bden pa ste / / 'di ltar dang por rags pas sems can rnams yongs su smin par byed do / / yongs su smin par gyur nas phra bas rnam par grol bar byed de /
vimocayati ataḥ pūrvam audārikaṃ paścāt sūkṣmaṃ / / kārikā'nuguṇyād viparyayoktiḥ /
# de'i phyir dang por ni rags pa'o / / phyis ni phra ba'o / / tshig le'ur byas pa dang mthun par bya ba'i phyir bzlog se gsungs so /
tatrā'samāhitajñānaviṣayatvāt saṃvṛti satyam audārikatattvaṃ /
# de la mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i shes pa'i yul yin pas kun rdzob kyi bden pa ni rags pa'i da kho na'o /
samāhitajñānaviṣayatvāt paramārthasatyaṃ sūkṣmatattvaṃ /
# mnyam par bzhag pa'i shes pa'i yul yin pas don dam pa'i bden pa ni phra ba'i de kho na'o /
athavā vijñānaviṣayatvād audārikaṃ /
# yang na rnam par shes pa'i yul yin pas na rags pa'o /
jñānaviṣayatvāt sūkṣmaṃ / / sarvatattvānāṃ mūlatattve'ntarbhāvaḥ pratijñāta ityataḥ pṛcchati - tan / mūlatattve kathaṃ veditavyaṃ ? / ityata āha - / prajñaptipratipattitaḥ / / tathodbhāvanayaudāraṃ iti /
# ye shes kyi yul yin pas na phra ba'o / / de kho na thams cad rtsa ba'i de kho nar bsdu bar dam bcas bas na / / de'i phyir de rtsa ba'i de kho nar ji ltar rig par bya zhe na zhes dris te de'i phyir / / brtags pa dang ni shes pa dang /
prajñaptiḥ pratipatīr udbhāvanā caudārikatattvaṃ mūlatattve veditavyaṃ
# de bzhin brjod pa rags pa yin / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / brtags pa dang shes pa dang brjod pa rnams ni rags pa'i de kho nar rig par bya'o /
etad eva pratipādayann āha - trividhā hi saṃvṛtir iti vistaraḥ /
# de nyid bstan par bya ba'i phyir kun rdzob ni rnam pa gsum ste zhes rgya cher smos so /
asato'rthasya rūpaṃ ghaṭaḥ paṭaśceti vyavasthānaṃ prajñaptisaṃvṛtiḥ /
# don med pa la gzugs dang bum pa dang snam bu zhes bya bar rnam par gzhag pa ni brtags pa'i kun rdzob po /
rūpavedanāsaṃjñādisvabhāvaviśeṣeṇa nāmābhilāpaḥ prajñaptisaṃvṛtir / ityanye /
# kha cig na re gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes la sogs pa'i rang bzhin dang bye brag gi ming gis brjod pa ni brtags pa'i kun rdzob bo zhe'o /
abhilāpāpekṣayā yad vyavahriyate rūpaṃ vedaneti vā tat / prajñaptisaṃvṛtir iti kecit /
# kha cig na re brjod pa la ltos nas gzugs dang tshor ba zhes bya bar tha snyad 'dogs pa gang yin pa de ni brtags pa'i kun rdzob bo zhe'o /
taccaitad asattvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ /
# sems dang sems las byung ba bzhin du med pas na kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid do /
pratipattisaṃvṛtir vikalpena yena rūpādayo ghaṭādayaś ca [p.95] / vijñānanirbhāsād abahirbhūtam api bahirbhūtam iva vasturūpeṇa yathā / vyavasthānam abhiniviśate sa vikalpaḥ pratipattisaṃvṛtiḥ / / udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiśceti / / caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ /
# shes pa'i kun rdzob ni rnam par rtog pa gang gis gzugs la sogs pa dang bum pa la sogs pa rnam par shes pa snang ba las; pha rol na med kyang phyi rol na yod pa bzhin du ji ltar rnam par gnas pa ltar dngos po'i ngo bor mngon par zhen pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni shes pa'i kun rdzob po / / brjod pa yang kun rdzob po zhes bya ba la / / yang zhes bya ba'i sgra ni bsdu bar bya ba'i don te /
vikalpā'bhilāpātikrāntasyāpi pariniṣpannasya śūnyatā tathatā samalā / nirmaletyevam ādibhiḥ paryāyaiḥ sandarśanam udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiḥ /
# yongs su grub pa ni rnam par rtog pa dang brjod pa las 'das kyang stong pa nyid dang de bzhin nyid dang dri ma dang bcas pa dang dri ma med pa la sogs pa'i rnam grangs kyis bstan pa ni brjod pa'i kun rdzob bo /
tayā trividhayā saṃvṛttyā saṃvṛtisatyatvaṃ mūlatattve yathākramaṃ / veditavyaṃ / / saṃvṛtir vyavahāraḥ /
# kun rdzob rnam pa gsum po des kun rdzob kyi bden pa nyid de / / rtsa ba'i de kho nar go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o / / kun rdzob ni tha snyad do /
prajñaptir ityabhidhānaṃ /
# btags pa zhes bya ba ni brjod pa ste /
arthābhāve'bhidhānamātreṇa vyavahāraḥ prajñaptisaṃvṛtiḥ /
# don med par brjod pa tsam gyis tha snyad du bya ba ni btags pa'i kun rdzob bo /
ata evārthābhāvāt prajñaptisaṃvṛtyā parikalpitaḥ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ /
# de bas na don med pa'i phyir btags pa'i kun rdzob kyis kun brtags pa kun rdzob kyi bden pa'o /
avidyamāne'rthe'rthābhiniveśaḥ pratipattis tayā vyavahāraḥ / pratipattisaṃvṛtiḥ /
# don med bzhin du don du mngon par zhen nas shes pa des tha snyad 'dogs pa de ni shes pa'i kun rdzob ste /
sā punar abhiniveśavikalpaḥ /
# de ni mngon par zhen pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o /
tasmāt pratipattisaṃvṛtyā saṃvṛttisatyaṃ paratantraḥ /
# de bas na shes pa'i kun rdzob kyi gzhan gyi dbang kun rdzob kyi bden pa'o /
tathatādiśabdair nirabhilāpyasya dharmadhātor yā saṃsūcanā / sodbhāvanā /
# chos kyi dbyings brjod du med pa la de bzhin nyid la sogs pa'i sgras brjod pa gang yin pa de ni brjod pa ste /
tayā dharmadhātor vyavahāra udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiḥ /
# des chos kyi dbyings la tha snyad 'dogs pa ni brjod pa'i kun rdzob bo /
ataścodbhāvanāsaṃvṛtyā pariniṣpannaḥ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ / / tatra prajñaptyudbhāvanāsaṃvṛtyor avasarasaṅgrahavyavasthānaṃ / veditavyaṃ na tu svabhāvata iti / / uktaṃ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ // / idānīṃ paramārthasatyaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha - / paramārthantu ekataḥ / iti / / kalpitaparatantrayoḥ paramārthato'sambhavatvaṃ / / satyaṃ punar ekasmāt [p.96] / pariniṣpannād eva svabhāvād veditavyaṃ /
# de bas na brjod pa'i kun rdzob kyis yongs su grub pa kun rdzob kyi bden pa'o / / de la brtags pa dang brjod pa'i kun rdzob gnyis ni skabs su bsdus nas rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'i / / rang bzhin gyis ni ma yin no / / kun rdzob kyi bden pa bshad zin to / / de ni don dam pa'i bden pa brjod par bya ste / / de'i phyir / / dam pa'i don ni gcig pu'o / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / brtags pa dang ni gzhan dbang gnyis ni don dam par mi srid pa'i phyir don dam pa'i bden pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid gcig pur rig par bya'o /
sa punaḥ pariniṣpannaḥ kena kāraṇena paramārtha ucyate ? / ityata āha - / arthaprāptipratyayā hi paramārthas tridhā mataḥ / iti / / trividho hi paramārthaḥ - arthaparamārthaḥ prāptiparamārthaḥ / prayatiparamārthaś ca / / tatrārthaparamārthas tathatā / / paramo hi lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ tasyārtho viṣaya iti kṛtvā tathatā
# yongs su grub pa de yang ci'i phyir don dam pa zhes bya zhe na / / de'i phyir / / don dang thob dang sgrub pa ni / / don dam rnam pa gsum du 'dod / / ces bya ba gsungs so / / don dam pa ni rnam pa gsum ste / / don dam pa dang thob par bya ba don dam pa dang sgrub pa don dam pa'o / / de la don dam pa de bzhin nyid de / / dam pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes so / / de'i yul yin pas don te /
paramārtha ity ucyate indriyārthavat / / tadeva pradarśayann āha - paramasya jñānasyārtha iti kṛtveti /
# dbang po rnams kyi don bzhin du / / de bzhin nyid ni dam pa'i don / / zhes bya'o / / de nyid bstan pa'i phyir ye shes dam pa'i don yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
ālambanabhāvena vyavasthānād ityarthaḥ /
# dmigs pa'i dngos por rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
jñānā'pṛthaktvāt tasmin kāla ālambanaṃ na vartate
# ye shes dang tha mi dad pa'i phyir de'i tshe dmigs par 'gyur ba ni ma yin gyi /
vijñaptimātrapratibhāsavat /
# rnam par rig pa tsam snang ba bzhin te /
tadyathā yeṣāṃ vijñaptimātraṃ kṣamate na teṣāṃ rūpādivijñaptimātraṃ / muktvā rūpādipratibhāsā vidyante /
# dper na gang dag rnam par rig pa tsam du bzod pa de dag gzugs la sogs pa rnam par rig pa tsam ma gtogs par gzugs la sogs par snang ba ni med pa lta bu'o /
prāptiparamārtho nirvāṇaṃ ekāntanirmatathatāśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇam / / kathaṃ paramārtha ityata āha - paramo'rtha iti kṛtvā / / paramaścāsāvarthaśceti kṛtvā paramārthaḥ /
# thob par bya ba don dam pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa ste / / shin tu dri ma med pa'i de bzhin nyid gnas gyur pa'i mtshan nyid do / / ji ltar na don dam pa zhes bya zhe na / / de'i phyir don gyi dam pa yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / de ni dam pa yang yin la don yang yin pas na don dam pa ste /
tatra saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtadharmāgratvāt paramaḥ mārgaprayojanatvād arthaḥ /
# de 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams kyi mchog yin pas dam pa'o / / lam gyi dgos pa yin pas na don to /
tathā hi mārgo nirvāṇaprāptiprayojanaḥ /
# 'di ltar mya ngan las 'das pa thob par bya ba ni lam gyi dgos pa ste /
nirvāṇantvarthaḥ sarvāpakāradoṣarahitatvāt / / yasmād doṣasahito'nartha ity ucyate /
# gnod pa'i nyes pa thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir mya ngan las 'das pa ni don to / / 'di ltar nyes pa dang bcas pa la ni don med pa zhes bya'o /
pratipattiparamārtho mārgaḥ / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ? / paramo'syārtha iti kṛtvā / / viṣayaḥ prayojanaṃ vārthaḥ /
# sgrub pa don dam pa ni lam ste / / ci'i phyir zhe na / / de'i don ni dam pa yin pa'i phyir ro / / don ni yul lam dgos pa ste /
viṣayas tathatā prayojanaṃ nirvāṇaṃ /
# yul ni de bzhin nyid do / / dgos pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa'o /
viṣayadvāreṇa parama ucyamāne katham anyo'nyasamarthanaṃ na syāt ? / anyo'nyasamarthanaṃ cet ko doṣa iti ? / niścayābhāvaḥ / / naivaṃ bhaviṣyaty anyonyasamarthanāt siṃhavanavat / / katham asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇākhyaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ ca mārgākhyaṃ / pariniṣpannasvabhāva ucyate ? / paramārthasatyaṃ hi pariniṣpannasvabhāvo nirdiṣṭaṃ / / mārgas tu pariniṣpannon na yujyate / / na pūrvāparabhāgābhāva iti kṛtvā / / tasmān na mārgaḥ paramārthasatyaṃ na cā'pariniṣpanne / paramārthasatyasaṃgraha iti / / ata āha - / nirvikārā'viparyāsapariniṣpattito dvayaṃ // iti / / athavā katham asaṃkṛtaṃ nirvāṇākhyaṃ saṃskṛtañca mārgākhyaṃ / pariniṣpannasvabhāva [p.97] / ucyate / / pariniṣpanno hi tathatā / / eṣā ca dvayalakṣaṇarahitatvaṃ paratantrasyeti na nirvāṇamārgayoḥ / pariniṣpannatā yujyate / / tadidam avācyaṃ yatas tatra dvayābhāvaḥ pariniṣpanna eva /
