# yul gyi sgo nas dam pa zhes bya na / / ji ltar na gcig la gcig brten par mi 'gyur / / gcig la gcig brten par gyur na ci nyes she na / / gtan la bab pa med par 'gyur ro / / gcig la gcig brten du zin kyang de ltar mi 'gyur te / / seng ge dang nags bzhin no / / don dam pa'i bden pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid du bstan la / / lam la ni snga ma dang phyi ma'i cha med pa ma yin pas yongs su grub par mi rung ste / / de bas na lam ni don dam pa'i bden pa ma yin la / / yongs su ma grub pas kyang don dam pa'i bden par bsdur mi rung na 'dus ma byas dang 'dus byas yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid du ji skad brjod ce na / / de'i phyir / / 'gyur med phyin ci ma log pa / / yongs su grub pa rnam pa gnyis / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / yang na yongs su grub pa ni de bzhin nyid de / / de yang gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid gnyis dang bral ba nyid pas mya ngan las 'das pa dang lam gnyis yongs su grub pa nyid du mi rung na mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya ba 'dus ma byas dang lam zhes bya ba 'dus byas gnyis yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid do zhes ji skad du bya zhe na / / 'di ni klan kar mi rung ste / / 'di ltar de la gnyis po med pa ni yongs su grub pa nyid de /
na tu dvayābhāva eva pariniṣpanna iti tad anyapratiṣedhaḥ / / atas tad anyac ca /
# gnyis po med pa nyid yongs su grub pa zhes de las gzhan dgag par mi byed de / / de bas na de las gzhan yang ste /
nirvikārā'viparyāsapariniṣpattito dvayam api pariniṣpanna iti
# 'gyur ba med pa dang phyin ci ma log par yongs su grub pa gnyis kyang yongs su grub pa zhes sbyar ro /
sambaddhyate asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇaṃ tathatā ca /
# 'dus ma byas ni mya ngan las 'das pa dang de bzhin nyid de /
asaṃskṛtam ananyathābhāvād avikārapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannaṃ /
# 'dus ma byas ni gzhan du 'gyur ba med pa'i phyir 'gyur ba med par yongs su 'grub pas yongs su grub pa'o /
saṃskṛtaṃ mārgasaṃgṛhītaṃ nānyatra /
# 'dus byas ni lam gyis bsdus pa la bya'i gzhan la ma yin te /
aviparyāsapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannam iti sambadhyate / / katham ityato 'bravīt - punar jñeyavastuviparyāsād iti /
# phyin ci ma log par yongs su grub pas yongs su grub pa zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / ji lta zhe na / / de'i phyir / / shes bya'i dngos po la phyin ci log med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
yasmān na punar jñeye viparyāsam āpadyate tasmān na mārgo'pi / pariniṣpanna ityataśca dvayor api saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtayoḥ pariniṣpannatvaṃ / pṛthag abhiprāyād ityavirodhaḥ //3-11// / { prasiddhatattvaṃ } / tatra - / lokaprasiddham ekasmāt iti / / yathābhidhānam asambhavāt parikalpitād eva tat nānyasmāt tasya tu
# gang gi phyir shes par bya ba la phyin ci log tu mi 'gyur ba de'i phyir lam yongs su grub pa yin te / / de bas na bsam pa tha dad pa'i phyir 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas gnyi ga yang yongs su grub pa yin pas 'gal ba med do / / de la / / gcig gis 'jig rten grags pa ste / / zhes bya ba ni ji ltar brjod pa bzhin du med pa kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis te /
svarūpaṃ na jñāyata ityata āha - yasmin vastunīti vistaraḥ /
# de gzhan gyis ni ma yin no / / de'i rang gi ngo bo mi shes pas de'i phyir / / dngos po gang la zhes bya ba rgya cher smos so; /
saṃketaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitasambandhajñānaṃ /
# brda ni ming dang ming can 'brel par shes pa'o /
saṃstavas tasya vāramvāramprayogadarśanaṃ /
# 'dris pa ni de la yang dang yang du sbyor zhing lta ba'o /
tatrā'nupraviṣṭayā buddhyeti /
# de la rjes su zhugs pa'i blo zhes bya ba la /
kaḥ punar buddheḥ saṃketasaṃstavānupraveśaḥ ?
# brda la 'dris pa'i rjes la zhugs pa'i blo gang zhe na /
tat smaraṇāt /
# de dag dran pa ste /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - saṃketasaṃstavānusmaraṇānugatatyā buddhyā sarveṣāṃ / laukikānāṃ śāstravidāṃ tad avidāṃ ca vyāhṛtibhāve kvacit [p.98] / pṛthyvyeveyam ityādivaṃśādidarśanatulyateti / / etal lokaprasiddhaṃ tattvaṃ / / lokaprasiddhyā tat tathaiveti kṛtvā /
# de ni 'di skad du brda la 'dris pa'i dran pa'i rjes su song ba'i blos 'jig rten pa bstan bcos shes pa dang de mi shes pa thams cad kyis tha snyad du btags pa'i dngos po gang la la 'di ni sa yin no zhes bya ba la sogs par lta ba mthun pa yin no zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / de ni de kho na bzhin du 'jig rten du grags pa'i phyir de ni 'jig rten gyi grags pa'i de kho na zhes bya'o / / gsum gyis rigs pa'i grags pa'o /
trayādyuktiprasiddhakaṃ / iti / / trividham api hi svabhāvam adhikṛtya yuktiḥ kriyata iti / / ataḥ svabhāvatrayeṇa yuktiprasiddhatvaṃ vyavasthāpyate / / tac ca na vijñāyata ityataḥ pradarśayann āha - yat satāṃ / yuktārthapaṇḍitānām ityādi / / tatra santo ye yuktārthapaṇḍitāḥ /
# zhes bya ba ni ngo bo nyid rnam pa gsum gyi dbang du mdzad de rigs pa zhes bya bas na de'i phyir ngo bo nyid gsum gyis rigs pa'i grags pa'i de kho nar rnam par gzhag go / / de yang mi shes te / / de bas na de bstan pa'i phyir / / gang zag dam pa rigs pa'i don la mkhas pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so / / de la dam pa dag ni gang dag rigs pa'i don la mkhas pa dag go /
tārkikā ye mīmāṃsakāḥ /
# rtog ge pa dag ni gang dag dpyod pa can dag ste /
pūrvasya vyākhyānāśayasya paścān nirdeśoktiḥ / / athavā santo'nveṣakāḥ kiṃ kuśalam iti /
# snga ma bshad par bsams nas tshig phyi ma brjod do / / yang na dam pa dag ni dge ba ci zhes tshol ba can dag go /
yuktā'rthapaṇḍitā / apekṣākāryakāraṇopapattidharmatāyukticatuṣṭayā'viruddhārthakṛtakauśalāḥ
# rigs pa'i don la mkhas pa dag ni ltos pa dang bya ba byed pa dang 'thad pa dang chos nyid kyi rigs pa bzhi dang mi 'gal ba'i don la mkhas pa dag go /
tārkikās tuhapohasamarthās tathāgatapravacanasamāśrayeṇā / viparītaśāstrapraṇetāraḥ /
# rtog ge ba dag ni rtog pa dang sel nus pa dag dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rab la brten nas bstan bcos phyin ci ma log par byed pa'o /
mīmāṃsakāḥ svaparaśāstrapaṇḍitāḥ śreyodoṣaparīkṣakāḥ / / kecit mīmāṃsakā iti na paṭhanti / / ta evam āhuḥ - satām ityukte ke punaḥ santaḥ ityata āha - / yuktārthapaṇḍitā iti /
# dpyod pa can dag ni bdag dang gzhan gyi bstan bcos la mkhas par gyur pa dang legs pa dang nyes pa dpyod pa dag go / / kha cig las ni dpyod pa can / / zhes mi 'byung ste / / de dag 'di skad du / / dam pa zhes brjod pa'i dam pa de gang zhe na / / de'i phyir / / rigs pa'i don la mkhas pa dag / / ces bya ba smos so /
te ca tarkabhūmau bhāvābhūmau ca vyavasthitatvād dvividhāḥ / / tasmāt tārkikā ity ucyanta iti /
# de dag kyang rtog ge pa'i sa dang bsgom pa'i sa la gnas pa'i phyir rnam pa gnyis te / / de'i phyir rtog ge pa dag ces bya ba smos so zhes zer ro /
teṣāṃ ca kaścil lokaprasiddhānusārītyata āha pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityeti / pramāṇatrayāvirodhena /
# de dag las kyang kha cig ni 'jig rten gyi grags pa'i rjes su 'brang bas na / / de'i phyir tshad ma gsum la brten nas zhes bya ba smos te / / tshad ma gsum dang mi 'gal bar zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
pramāṇatrayaṃ punaḥ pratyakṣam anumānam āgamaś ca /
# tshad ma gsum ni mngon sum dang rjes su dpag pa dang lung ngo [?] /
tatra pratyakṣaṃ pañcendriyajaṃ mānasaṃ ca sukhaduḥkhādisamvedanaṃ /
# de la mngon sum ni dbang po lnga las skyes pa dang bde ba dang sdug bsngal la sogs pa myong ba'i yid do /
trirūpaliṅgenānumeuyārthajñānam anumānaṃ / / āptavāgāgamaḥ /
# tshul gsum pa'i rtags kyi rjes su dpag par bya ba'i don la shes pa ni rjes su dpag pa'o / / yid ches bas bstan pa ni lung ste /
āptāḥ punar anṛtahetuvimuktāḥ /
# yid ches pas ni brdzun du smra ba'i rgyu dang mi ldan pa dag go /
athavā pratyakṣānumānāgamaprasiddhena hetunā dṛṣṭāntena ca tat / prasiddhasyaiva sādhyasya paramprati sādhyatvāt pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityeti
# yang na mngon sum dang rjes su dpag pa dang lung gis rab tu grub pa'i gtan tshigs dang dpes bsgrub par bya ba sgrub pa de nyid gzhan la sgrub par byed pas tshad ma gsum la brten nas zhes bya ba smos te /
upapattisādhanayuktyā prasiddhaṃ vastu iti /
# 'thad pa sgrub pa'i rigs pas grags pa'i dngos po'o zhes bya ba la /
upapattis trirūpaṃ liṅgaṃ sādhyapratipādanopāyatvāt /
# 'thad pa ni bsgrub par bya ba rtogs par byed pa'i thabs yin pas tshul gsum pa'i rtags so /
upapatteḥ sādhanam upapattisādhanaṃ trirūpaliṅgākhyānaṃ tena tat / pratipādanāt /
# 'thad pa'i sgrub pa ni 'thad pa sgrub pa ste / / des rtogs par bya ba'i phyir tshul gsum pa'i rtags brjod pa'o /
yuktir upāyo yena prayoganiyamena liṅgasya trirūpyam ākhyāyate / / athavopapātir ananyathāsambhavaḥ / / sādhanyuktir avayavasambandhaḥ / / upapatteḥ sādhanayuktir iti vigrahaḥ / / athavopapattir eva sādhanayuktir iti vigrahaḥ / / anyasādhanayuktibhyo vyavacchedārtham upapattigrahaṇaṃ /
# rigs pa ni thabs te / / sbyor ba nges pa gang gi rtags kyi tshul gsum brjod pa'o / / yang na 'thad pa ni gzhan du mi srid pa'o / / sgrub pa'i rigs pa ni cha'i sbyor ba ste / / 'thad pa sgrub pa'i rigs pa'o zhes tshig rnam par sbyar ba'o / / yang na 'thad pa nyid sgrub pa'i rigs pa yin par tshig rnam par sbyar bar bya'o / / sgrub pa'i rigs pa gzhan dag las dbye ba'i phyir 'thad pa smos te /
evaṃ pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityopapattisādhana yuktyā yat prasiddhaṃ vastu / trayāṇāṃ bhāvanām anyatamat tad yuktiprasiddham ucyate /
# de ltar na tshad ma gsum la brten nas 'thad pa sgrub pa'i rigs pas gang grags pa'i dngos po ngo bo nyid gsum gyi nang nas gang yang rung ba ste rigs pas grags pa zhes bya'o /
uktaṃ prasiddhatattvaṃ //
# grags pa'i de kho na bshad zin to /
{ viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ } / [p.99]
# de'i 'og tu rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul brjod dgos te /
tad anantaraṃ tu viśuddhiviṣayaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha - / viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ dvividham iti /
# de'i phyir / / rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul gyi de kho na rnam pa gnyis te zhes bya ba smos so /
tattu yathā dvividhaṃ tat pradarśayann āha - / kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocaraṃ jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarañceti / kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhiḥ kleśāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ /
# de yang ji ltar rnam pa gnyis su 'gyur ba de bstan pa'i phyir / / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul dang shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul lo zhes bya ba smos so / / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa ni nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa spangs pa ste /
kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhaye kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhau vā jñānaṃ / kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānaṃ /
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir ram / / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag par byed pa'i ye shes ni nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes te /
kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhiprayojanaṃ tan nimittaṃ vetyarthaḥ /
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag par bya bar dgos pa'am / / de'i rgyu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tasya kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaram iti viṣaya ityarthaḥ /
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes de'i spyod yul zhes bya ba ni yul zhes pa'i tha tshig go /
evaṃ jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaram api vaktavyaṃ /
# de bzhin du shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul la yang brjod par bya'o /
tatra kleśāvaraṇaṃ sarve darśanabhāvanāmārgaprahātavyāḥ kleśopakleśā
# de la nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa ni mthong ba dang bsgom pa'i lam gyis spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad do /
ityato darśanabhāvanātad upacārajñanaviṣayaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānāṃ / yat tattvaṃ duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgasatyam ucyate tat
# de bas na mthong ba dang bsgom pa dang de dang nye bar spyod pa'i ye shes kyi yul ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi de kho na gang yin pa sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam rnams kyi bden pa zhes bya ba ste /
kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaraṃ /
# de ni nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul lo /
jñātavyaṃ jñeyaṃ / / tac ca sarvātmanā pañca vidyāsthānāni /
# shes par bya ba ni shes bya ste / / de ni mdor na rig pa'i gnas lnga dag go /
tāni punar adhyātmavyākaraṇahetucikitsāsarvaśilpakarmasthānākhyāni /
# de dag ni nang dang brda sprod pa dang gtan tshigs dang gso ba dang bzo dang las kyi gnas zhes bya ba thams cad do /
tatra jñānavibandhabhūtam akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ jñeyāvaraṇaṃ /
# de la ye shes kyi gegs su gyur pa nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa ni shes bya'i sgrib pa'o /
tad viśodhanaṃ lokottarajñānānulomādhimukticaryābhūmisaṅgṛhītaṃ tat / pṛṣṭhalabdhañca jñānaṃ /
# de rnam par sbyong ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes kyi rjes su mthun pa'i mos pas spyod pa'i sar bsdus pa dang rab tu dga' ba la sogs pa sa bcu gcig tu bsdus pa dang de'i rjes las thob pa'i ye shes so /
tat punar bodhisattvatathāgatasantānavartiṃ /
# de yang byang chub sems dpa' dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs kyi rgyud la mnga' ba ste /
tasya ca tathatā sarvatragādyarthamukhenālambanam ityato
# de ni kun du 'gro ba'i don la sogs pa'i sgo nas de bzhin nyid la dmigs pas de'i phyir /
jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarasya tattvaṃ tathatā /
# shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi de kho na ni de bzhin nyid do /
phalahetutattvoktyā sūkṣmatattvoktyā ca viśūddhigocaraṃ dvividham api / nirdiṣṭam eveti punar asya vidhānaṃ vyarthaṃ / / na vyarthaṃ /
# 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na bshad pa dang phra ba'i de kho na bshad pas rnam bar dag pa'i spyod yul rnam pa gnyis kyang bshad zin na / / 'di brjod pa don med par mi 'gyur ram zhe na /
yatas tat phalahetutattvaṃ sūkṣmaṃ ca vastu vyavasthānata uktaṃ /
# don med par mi 'gyur te / / 'di ltar 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na dang phra ba'i de kho na ni dngos po rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir bshad do /
atra tvāvaraṇaṃ yathā viśuddhyate tathaitan nirdiṣṭaṃ /
# 'dir ni sgrib pa ji ltar rnam par dag par 'gyur ba ste /
idaṃ dvividhaṃ viśuddhigocaram ekasmāt pariniṣpannād eva svabhāvāt / kīrtitaṃ /
# de'i phyir de skad bstan to / / rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul 'di rnam pa gnyis ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid gcig pus brjod de /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - na hyanyaḥ svabhāvo viśuddhijñānagocaro / bhavatīti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / ngo bo nyid gzhan ni rnam par dag pa'i ye shes rnam pa gnyis kyi spyod yul ma yin no zhes bya ba'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ? / abhūtaparikalpasya dauṣṭhulyamaladvayena samalabhūtatvāt parikalpitasya / cāsattvāt /
# ci'i phyir zhe na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni gnas ngan len gyi dri ma gnyis kyis dri ma can du gyur pa'i phyir ro / / kun brtags pa ni med pa'i phyir ro /
dvividhajñānaviṣayasya tu dharmatāyā viśuddhiviṣayatattvaṃ / pariniṣpannād eva vyavasthāpyata iti / / uktaṃ viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ //3-12// / { saṅgrahatattvaṃ } / [p.100] / tad anantaraṃ tu saṅgrahatattvaṃ vaktavyam ityataḥ pṛcchati - kathaṃ
# ye shes rnam pa gnyis kyi yul ni chos nyid yin pas rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul gyi de kho na ni yongs su grub pa nyid kyis rnam par gzhag go / / rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul gyi de kho na bshad zin to / / de'i 'og tu bsdu ba'i de kho na brjod dgos te /
trividhe mūlatattve saṅgrahatattvaṃ veditavyam iti / / saṅgrahatattvaṃ trividhe mūlatattve saṃgṛhītaṃ pradarśayann āha -
# de'i phyir rtsa ba'i de kho na rnam pa gsum du bsdu ba'i de kho na ji ltar rig par bya zhe na zhes dris pa dang rtsa ba'i de kho na rnam pa gsum du bsdu ba'i de kho na 'dus par bstan pa'i phyir /
nimittasya vikalpasya nāmnaśca dvayasaṃgrahaḥ / / iti vistaraḥ /
# rgyu dang rnam par rtog pa dang / / ming ni rnam pa gnyis su bsdu / / zhes rgya cher gsungs te /
dvaye paratantre parikalpite ca saṅgrahaḥ /
# gzhan gyi dbang dang kun brtags pa gnyis su bsdu'o /
tatra saṅgrahatattvaṃ pañca vastūnītyata āha - yathāyogaṃ pañca / vastūny ārabhyeti /
# de la bsdu ba'i de kho na ci rigs su sbyar ro zhes bya ba ni gar 'os par rtsa ba'i de kho nar dngos po lnga dag 'dus par rig par bya ba'i go rims bzhin du ni ma yin no /
yathāyogaṃ mūlatattve pañca vastūni saṅgṛhītāni veditavyāni na tu / yathākramaṃ / / pañca punar vastūni nimittaṃ nāma vikalpas tathatā samyag jñānaṃ ceti / sarvasya jñeyasyāsmin  pañcavidhe vastuni saṅgrahād etat pañcavidhaṃ
# dngos po lnga ni rgyu mtshan dang ming dang rnam par rtog pa dang de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i ye shes te / / shes par bya ba thams cad dngos po rnam pa lnga po 'dir bsdu ba'i phyir dngos po rnam pa 'di lnga la bsdu ba'i de kho na zhes bya'o /
vastu saṃgrahatattvam ity ucyate / / tatra nimittam ālayavijñānaṃ kliṣṭamanaḥpravṛttivijñānāni ca / / anyo'nyanimittabhāvān nimittaṃ /
# kha cig na re de la rgyu mtshan ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dang nyon mongs pa can gyi yid dang 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams te / / phan tshun rgyu'i dngos po yin pas rgyu mtshan no /
nāma yat tasyaiva nimittasyā'nabhilāpyasyāpi sato'kṣinikocavad sūcakam
# ming ni rgyu mtshan gang yin pa de nyid brjod du med du zin kyang mig brda bzhin du go bar brjod pa'o /
abhidhānaṃ / / yathoktanimittasvabhāvaviśeṣavikalpakāstraidhātukapratisaṃyuktāścittacaittā / vikalpaḥ / / śūnyatā tathatā /
# ji skad du smras pa'i rgyu mtshan gyi rang bzhin dang bye brag tu rnam par rtog pa khams gsum pa dang ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba ni rnam par rtog pa'o / / stong pa nyid ni de bzhin nyid do /
samyag jñānaṃ lokottaraṃ tathatālambanaṃ /
# yang dag pa'i ye shes ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ste / / de bzhin nyid la dmigs pa'o /
kramaḥ punar eṣāṃ tatra saṅkleśaprajñaptivastutvān nimittam ādau /
# de dag gi go rims ni de la kun nas nyon mongs par gdags pa'i dngos po yin pas na dang por rgyu mtshan no /
saṅkleśaprajñaptitvād anantaraṃ nāma /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa zhes btags pa'i phyir de'i 'og tu ming ngo /
yathā nāma tathā saṅkleśaprajñaptivastuvikalpatvāt tad anantaraṃ / vikalpaḥ /
# ming ji lta ba de bzhin du kun nas nyon mongs par gdags pa'i dngos po la rnam par rtog pa'i phyir de'i 'og tu rnam par rtog pa'o /
sa ca saṅkleśas tathatāsamyag jñānena nirudhyata iti tad anantaraṃ / tathatā samyag jñānañceti kecit /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa de yang de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i ye shes kyis 'gag par 'gyur bas na de'i 'og tu de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i ye shes so zhe'o /
bhrāntinimittaṃ bhrāntidauṣṭhulyaṃ tan nimittam iti / / tasmād bhrāntis tasya nimittaṃ prakṛtiśamas tatra jñānaṃ // / ity anayā gāthayā'sya pañcavidhasya vastuno'rtha ity anye /
# gzhan dag na re / / 'khrul pa'i rgyu ni 'khrul pa ste / / de yi rgyu ni gnas ngan len / / de bas 'khrul pa de yi rgyu / / rang bzhin zhi bde shes pa / / zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'dis dngos po lnga'i don to zhe'o /
tatrā'dhyātmikacakṣurādivijñānsaṃgṛhītāyā bhrānter nimittaṃ / bāhyādhyātmikā rūpādicakṣurādisaṃgṛhītā bhrāntiḥ / / tasyā bāhyādhyātimikāyā bhrānter nimittaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ /
# de la nang gi mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes par bsdus pa rnams kyi 'khrul pa'i rgyu ni phyi nang gi gzugs la sogs pa dang mig la sogs par bsdus pa'i 'khrul pa'o / / phyi nang gi 'khrul pa de dag gi rgyu ni gnas ngan len te /
tat punar ālayavijñānavāsanā / / tasyā vāsanāyā nimittaṃ saiva bāhyādhyātmikabhrāntiḥ / / tasmāt tatrābhilāpapravṛttiḥ /
# de yang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i bag chags so / / bag chags de'i rgyu ni phyi nang gi 'khrul pa de nyid do / / de lta bas na de la brjod pa 'jug go /
abhilāpavaśāc ca vāsanāyā avasthānam ālayavijñāne /
# brjod pa'i dbang gis kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la bag chags gnas so /
prakṛtiśama iti tathatā /
# rang bzhin gyis zhi ba zhes bya ba ni de bzhin nyid de /
prakṛtyā kliṣṭatvād dharmadhātoḥ /
# rang bzhin gyis kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings so /
tatra ca jñānam iti tathatālambanaṃ mārgasaṃgṛhītaṃ yaj jñānaṃ /
# de shes pa zhes bya ba ni de bzhin nyid la dmigs pa lam du gtogs pa'i ye shes gang yin pa'o /
tatra nimittavikalpayoḥ paratantreṇa saṅgrahaḥ hetupratyayotpāditatvāt / [p.101]
# de la rgyu dang rnam par rtog pa gnyis ni rgyu dang rkyen gyis bskyed pa'i phyir gzhan gyi dbang du bsdu'o /
nāmnaḥ parikalpiteneti / / yathānāmārthābhāvān nāmnaḥ parikalpitena saṅgrahaḥ /
# ming ni kun brtags par zhes bya ba la ming ji lta ba bzhin du don med pas ming ni kun brtags par bsdu'o /
evam adhikārasaṅgrahaḥ parikalpitena nāmno na svabhāvasaṅgrahaḥ iti yad
# de ltar na skabs yin pa'i phyir kun brtags par ming bsdus kyi / / ngo bo nyid kyis bsdus pa ni ma yin no /
uktaṃ niṣsvabhāvasiddhatvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvo / nimittādipañcavastubhir na saṅgṛhīta iti tan na virudhyate tatra
# ngo bo nyid med par grub pa las kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ni rgyu la sogs pa dngos po lngas ma bsdus so zhes gang bshad pa dang 'gal ba med do /
svabhāvasaṅgrahasya vivakṣitatvāt / / samyag jñānasatattvasya iti /
# der ni ngo bo nyid bsdu bar 'dod pa'i phyir ro / / yang dag ye shes rab kho na / / zhes bya ba ni /
sadā śobhanaṃ vā tattvaṃ satattvaṃ tathatā śūnyatālambanādvayajñānaṃ / tat pṛṣṭhalabdhaśuddhalaukikaṃ ca samyag jñānaṃ /
# rtag tu'am mdzes pa'i de kho na ste de bzhin nyid do / / stong pa nyid la dmigs pa gnyis su med pa'i ye shes dang de'i rjes las thob pa dag pa 'jig rten pa ni yang dag pa'i ye shes so /
tathatāsamyag jñānayor avikārā'viparyāsapariniṣpattyā yathākramaṃ / pariniṣpannatvād ekenaiva pariniṣpannena svabhāvena saṅgraha iti / / tad uktaṃ saṅgrahatattvaṃ //3-13//
# de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i ye shes de gnyis ni 'gyur ba med pa dang phyin ci log med pa'i yongs su grub pas go rims bzhin du yongs su grub pa'i phyir yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid gcig pus bsdus so / / bsdu ba'i de kho na bshad zin to /
{ prabhedatattvaṃ } / idānīṃ prabhedatattvaṃ katividhaṃ kathañca tanmūlatattve saṅgṛhītam
# rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na la rnam pa du ma yod pa dang de rtsa ba'i de kho nar ji ltar bsdu ba mi shes nas de'i phyir /
iti na vijñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati - prabhedatattvaṃ mūlatattve katham / veditavyam iti / / ata āha - saptavidhaṃ prabhedatattvaṃ /
# rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na rtsa ba'i de kho nar ji ltar rig par bya zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir / / rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na rnam pa bdun te zhes bya ba smos so /
katham ityata āha - pravṛttitattvaṃ lakṣaṇatattvam iti vistaraḥ /
# gang zhe na de'i phyir / / 'jug pa'i de kho na dang mtshan nyid kyi de kho na zhes bya ba rgya cher smos te /
yaiva ca sandhinirmocaranasūtre saptavidhā tathatā nirdiṣṭā / pravṛttitathatāyāvat samyag pratipattitathateti saivā'tra saptavidhaṃ / prabhedatattvam ityuktā pravṛttitattvaṃ yāvat samyakpratipattitattvam iti
# dgongs pa nges par 'grel pa las 'jug pa'i de bzhin nyid nas yang dag par sgrub pa'i de bzhin nyid kyi bar du de bzhin nyid rnam pa bdun bka' stsal pa gang yin pa de nyid 'dir 'jug pa'i de kho na nas / / yang dag par sgrub pa'i de kho na'i bar du rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na rnam pa bdun du bshad do /
tatra pravṛttitattvaṃ yā saṃsārā'navarāgratā saiva ca pravṛtti tathatā / yasmān na jātu tasyāgratāyogo bhavati /
# de la 'jug pa'i de kho na ni gang 'khor ba la thog ma dang tha ma med pa'o / / de nyid 'jug pa'i de bzhin nyid de / / 'di ltar de ni nam yang thog ma dang ldan par mi 'gyur ro /
lakṣaṇatattvaṃ pudgaladharmanairātmyaṃ / [p.102]
# mtshan nyid kyi de kho na ni gang zag dang chos la bdag med pa ste /
ananyatvāc caturvidhalakṣaṇatathatā /
# gzhan du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir de nyid mtshan nyid kyi de bzhin nyid do /
vijñaptitattvaṃ vijñaptimātratā dharmāṇāṃ /
# rnam par rig pa'i de kho na ni chos rnams kyi rnam par rig pa tsam nyid do /
nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ vijñaptyāśrayabhāvād vijñptitattvam ity apare /
# kha cig na re rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes sam / / rnam par rig pa'i gnas 'di ni rnam par rig pa'i de kho na'o zhe'o /
ananyathābhāvatvād vijñaptitattvasya vijñaptitathatocyate /
# rnam par rig pa'i de kho na ni gzhan du 'gyur ba med pa'i phyir rnam par rig pa'i de bzhin nyid ces bya'o /
sanniveśatattvaṃ duḥkhasatyaṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ duḥkhasanniviṣṭatvāt / / saiva ca tathatā nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā /
# gnas pa'i de kho na ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa ste / / 'du byed rnam sdug bsngal bar gnas pa'i phyir ro / / de nyid rtag par de bzhin pas na de bzhin nyid do /
mithyāpratipattitattvaṃ samudayasatyaṃ /
# log par sgrub pa'i de kho na ni kun 'byung ba'i bden pa ste /
sā punar yā teṣu saṃskāreṣu guṇadarśanena pravṛttiḥ /
# de yang gang 'du byed de dag la yon tan du lta bas 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
viśuddhitattvaṃ kleśajñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhiḥ /
# rnam par dag pa'i kho na ni nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa ste /
sā punas tathā nirodhasatyañca / / āśrayaparāvṛttyātmatā nirodhātmatā nirodhasatyam evetyapare /
# de ni de bzhin nyid dang 'gog pa'i bden pa'o / / kha cig na re gnas gyur pa'i bdag nyid 'gog pa'i bden pa nyid do zhe'o /
samyakpratipattitattvaṃ mārgasatyaṃ /
# yang dag par sgrub pa'i de kho na ni lam gyi bden pa'o /
vijñaptitattvaṃ yoniśaḥ prayogaḥ /
# gzhan dag na re rnam par rig pa'i de kho na ni tshul bzhin du sbyor ba ste /
samyakpratipattitattvaṃ vijñaptitattvaṃ ca mārgasatyam evetyanye / / etāny api trīṇi tattvāni nityaṃ tathaiveti tathatāvacanam bhavati /
# yang dag par sgrub pa'i de kho na dang rnam par rig pa'i de kho na yang lam gyi bden pa nyid do zhe'o / / de kho na gsum po 'di dag kyang rtag tu de bzhin bas de bzhin nyid ces bya bar 'gyur ro /
tatra - / pravṛttitattvaṃ dvividhaṃ
# de la 'jug pa de kho na rnam pa gnyis /
mūlatattvaṃ veditavyaṃ parikalpitaparatantralakṣaṇaṃ / / tatra pravṛttir janmanāmanādimān prabandhaḥ / / sā cā'vidyamānatvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ / / yeṣāṃ tu sa prabandhaṣthe hetuprabhāvitatvāt paratantraḥ svabhāvaḥ /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na kun brtags pa dang gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o zhes bya ba de la 'jug pa ni tshe'i rgyun thog ma med pa can te / / de ni med pas kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid do / / rgyun de su dag gi yin pa de dag ni rgyus rab tu phye ba'i phyir gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid de /
evaṃ yeṣāṃ yā ca pravṛttis tat pravṛttitattvam iti nirdiṣṭaṃ bhavati /
# de ltar gang dag gis yin pa dang 'jug pa gang yin pa de ni 'jug pa'i de kho na zhes bstan pa yin no /
athavā kleśakarmajanmanām anādimān utpādaḥ saṃsārapravṛttir ityucyate
# yang na nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe rnams kyi 'byung ba thog ma med pa can ni 'khor bar 'jug pa zhes bya'o /
sā ca parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśaprabhāvetetyāha - / pravṛttitattvaṃ dvividhaṃ
# de yang kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la mngon par zhen pas rab tu phye ba ste / / de'i phyir / / 'jug ste kho na rnam pa gnyis /
mūlatattvam ity uktaṃ / / tathā - / sanniveśakupannatā / iti / / mithyāpratipattiḥ kupannatā /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na zhes bya ba smos so / / de bzhin du / / gnas pa dang ni ngan par zhugs / / zhes bya ba la log par sgrub pa ni ngan par zhugs pa'o /
tathaiva dvividhaṃ mūlatattvam iti duḥkhasamudayayor / hetupratyayaprabhāvitatvāt parikalpitaviṣayatvāc ca / sanniveśamithyāpratipattitattvaṃ dvividhe saṃgṛhītaṃ /
# de bzhin du rtsa ba'i de kho na rnam pa gnyis su'o zhes bya ba ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba gnyis rgyu dang rkyen gyis rab tu phye ba dang kun rtog pa'i yul yin pa'i phyir gnas pa dang log par sgrub pa'i de kho na rnam pa gnyis su bsdu ba'o / / mtshan nyid rnam par rig dang dag /
ekaṃ lakṣaṇavijñaptiśuddhisamyak prapannatā / / lakṣaṇatattvaṃ vijñaptitattvaṃ viśuddhitattvaṃ samyak pratipattitattvaṃ
# yang dag sgrub pa gcig pu'o / / zhes bya ba ni mtshan nyid kyi de kho na dang rnam par rig pa'i de kho na dang rnam par dag pa'i de kho na dang yang dag par sgrub pa'i de kho na ste /
etāni catvāri tatvāny ekam eva mūlatattvaṃ yad uta pariniṣpannaḥ / svabhāvaḥ /
# de kho na 'di bzhi ni rtsa ba'i de kho na gcig kho na ste / / 'di ltar yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid do /
tatra lakṣaṇatattvaviśuddhitattvayor ananyathāpariniṣpannatvāt / pariniṣpannaḥ /
# de la mtshan nyid kyi de kho na dang rnam par dag pa'i de kho na gnyis ni gzhan du 'gyur ba med par yongs su grub pas yongs su grub pa'o /
vijñaptitattvaṃ samyak pratipattitattvaṃ cā'viparyāsapariniṣpattyā / pariniṣpannaḥ / [p.103]
# rnam par rig pa'i de kho na dang yang dag par sgrub pa'i de kho na gnyis ni phyin ci ma log par yongs su grub pas yongs su grub pa'o /
atra pravṛttisanniveśamithyāpratipattitattvais tribhiḥ sattvasāmyaṃ
# 'di la 'jug pa dang gnas pa dang log par sgrub pa'i de kho na gsum gyis ni sems can rnams mnyam par bstan to /
darśitaṃ / / lakṣaṇavijñaptitattvābhyāṃ dharmasāmyaṃ /
# mtshan nyid dang rnam par rig pa'i de kho na gnyis kyis ni chos mnyam pa'o /
viśuddhitattvena bodhisāmyaṃ /
# rnam par dag pa'i de kho nas ni byang chub mnyam pa'o /
samyakpratipattitattvena prajñāsāmyaṃ pradarśitam iti / / āha ca - / sattvasāmyaṃ tribhiḥ proktaṃ dharmasāmyaṃ dvayena tu / / bodhiprajñāsāmyam evam ekaikena pradarśitaṃ // / iti //3-14// / { kauśalyatattvaṃ }
# yang dag par sgrub pa'i de kho nas ni shes rab mnyam par bstan to / / smras pa / / sems can mnyam par gsum gyis brjod / / chos rnams mnyam pa gnyis kyis te / / de ltar byang chub blo mnyam par / / re re rab tu bstan pa yin /
prabhedatattvānantaraṃ kauśalyatattvam uddiṣṭaṃ / / kuśalyatattvaṃ darśanapratipakṣeṇaety uktaṃ /
# rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na'i 'og tu mkhas pa'i de kho na bshad de / / de bas na de bstan pa'i phyir / / mkhas de kho na rnam bcu ni / / bdag tu lta ba'i gnyen po'o /
tatpunaḥ skandhādiṣu kathaṃ daśavidham ātmadarśanam iti na jñāyata
# zhes gsungs zhes bya ba smos so / / phung po la sogs pa la bdag tu lta ba rnam ba bcu po de yang ji lta bu yin pa de mi shes nas /
ityataḥ pṛcchati - katham eṣu skandhādiṣu daśavidham ātmadarśanam iti ? / ata āha -
# de'i phyir phung po la sogs pa la bdag tu lta ba rnam pa bcu po de dag ji lta zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir /
ekahetutvabhoktṛtve kartṛtvavaśavartate /
# gcig dang rgyu dang za ba dang / / byed pa dang ni dbang sgyur dang /
ādhipatyārthanityatve kleśaśuddhyāśraye'pi ca // / yigotvā'muktamuktatve ātmadarśnam eṣu hi / iti / / skandhādiṣv iti sambadhyate /
# bdag po'i don dang rtag pa dang / / nyon mongs pa dang dag pa'i gnas / / rnal 'byor can dang ma grol grol / / de dag la ni bdag tu lta / / zhes bya ba gsungs te / / phung po la sogs pa la zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
eṣa tu daśavidha ātmā'sadgrāha [p.104] / ityātmano'sattvād asadgrāha ityāha /
# bdag med pa la 'dzin pa rnam pa 'di bcu ni zhes bya ba ni bdag med pa'i phyir med pa la 'dzin pa zhes bya ba smos so /
yadyātmā nāsti kathaṃ grāhaparatantraḥ sannirviṣayo grāhaḥ pravartata
# gal te bdag med na gzung ba'i gzhan gyi dbang du gyur pa'i 'dzin pa ji ltar yul med pa la 'jug ce na /
iti ?natveṣa nirviṣayaḥ skandhādiṣu pravartate /
# 'di ni yul med pa ma yin te / / phung po la sogs pa la 'jug go; /
tasmāt teṣāṃ pratipakṣeṇa daśavidhaṃ skandhādikauśalyam uktaṃ /
# de'i phyir de dag gi gnyen por phung po la sogs pa la mkhas pa rnam pa bcu bshad do /
kathaṃ punaḥ skandhādiṣv evāyam ātmagrāho natvāmā sanniścīyate ?
# ji ltar na 'di phung po la sogs pa la bdag tu 'dzin gyi bdag ni yod pa ma yin par nges she na /
yataḥ skandhādivyatirikta ātmā yuktyā parīkṣyamāṇo nopalabhyate /
# 'di ltar phung po la sogs pa ma gtogs bar bdag ces bya ba rigs pas yongs su brtags na dmigs su med do /
yadātmatvādīnām ātmakriyāsvarūpaṃ tat sarvam api pravartate / skandhādiṣvevetyataḥ skandhādaya evātmagrāhanibandhanam iti pratīyate /
# bdag tu smra ba dag bdag gi bya ba dang rang bzhin gang yin pa de dag thams cad kyang phung po la sogs pa la 'jug ste / / de'i phyir phung po la sogs pa nyid bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gzhi yin par mngon no /
ebhir daśavidhair ātmābhiniveśo nāmātmagrāhaḥ pravartate nānyair
# bdag tu mngon par zhen pa rnams ni rnam pa 'di bcus bdag tu 'dzin pa 'byung gi gzhan dag gis ni ma yin te /
ityataḥ skandhādikauśalyaṃ sarvātmagrāhasya pratipakṣatvena veditavyaṃ /
# de'i phyir phung po la sogs pa la mkhas pa ni bdag tu 'dzin pa thams cad kyi gnyen por rig par bya'o / / 'di lta ste /
yad uta ekatvagrāha iti pañcopādānaskandheṣu piṇḍātmagrāhataḥ tat
# gcig pur 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po dag la ril po'i bdag tu 'dzin pa ste /
pratipakṣeṇa skandhakauśalyaṃ /
# de'i gnyen por phung po la mkhas pa'o /
hetutvagrāha iti cakṣurādīnāṃ prayojakatvād ātmani hetutvagrāhaḥ tat
# rgyur 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pas bsgo ba'i phyir bdag la rgyur 'dzin pa ste /
pratipakṣeṇa dhātukauśalyaṃ /
# de'i gnyen por khams la mkhas pa'o /
evam anyeṣv api vipakṣapratipakṣaṃ vaktavyaṃ /
# de bzhin du gzhan dag la yang mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po brjod par bya'o /
athavātmatvāt sarvaṃ pravartata ityayaṃ hetutvagrāhaḥ /
# yang na bdag nyid las thams cad 'byung ngo snyam pa 'di ni rgyud 'dzin pa ste /
yasya veṣṭam aniṣṭañceha janmani phalaṃ tasya śubhāśubhasya karmaṇa ātmā / hetur iti cetanā hetutvagrāhaḥ /
# las dge ba dang mi dge ba gang yin pa de'i 'bras bu tshe 'di la 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa'i rgyu bdag yin par sems pa ni rgyur 'dzin pa'o /
bhoktṛtvagrāha iti ātmā bhoktā cetanatvāt /
# za bar 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni sems yin pa'i phyir bdag ni za ba'o /
vyaktāvyaktaṃ tu bhojanam acetanatvāt /
# gsal ba dang mi gsal ba ni sems med pa'i phyir bza' ba'o /
athavā yasya śubham aśubhaṃ karmabhir utpadyate sa eva tat phalānāṃ / bhokteti bhoktṛtvagrāhaḥ /
# yang na dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las rnams kyi bar du skye ba gang yin pa de nyid de'i 'bras bu la za bar byed do snyam pa ni za bar 'dzin pa'o /
kartṛtvagrāha iti ātmaiva sukṛta-duṣkṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ karteti yo grāhaḥ
# byed par 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni legs par byas pa dang nyes par byas pa'i las rnams bdag nyid kyis byed par 'dzin pa gang yin pa'o /
yo vā karaṇādyupetas tās tāḥ kriyāḥ karoti sa ātmeti kartṛtvagrāhaḥ /
# yang na byed pa dang ldan pa gang zhig bya ba de dang de dag byed pa ni bdag go zhes byed par 'dzin pa'o /
svatantragrāha iti yat svairaṃ vaśitvaṃ sa ātmā yo'dhikāraḥ sa ātmeti / yo grāhaḥ /
# rang dbang du 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni rang dgar dbang byed pa gang yin pa de ni bdag go / / dbang de bya ba gang yin pa de ni bdag go zhes bya bar 'dzin pa gang yin pa'o /
hetvanurūpasyaiva vā phalasyotpattau vaśitvam asyeti svatantragrāhaḥ /
# yang na rgyu dang 'bras bu 'byung ba la dbang byed do snyam pa ni rang dbang du 'dzin pa'o /
adhipatitvagrāha iti yo'dhipatiḥ prabhurīśvaraḥ sa ātmeti /
# bdag por 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni bdag po dang rje bo dang dbang phyug gang yin pa de ni bdag go snyam du sems pa'o /
phalasyaiva vā'nurūpeṇācaraṇaṃ tad adhipatitvād / ātmetyadhipatitvagrāhaḥ /
# yang na 'bras bu dang mthun par de la spyod pa'i bdag po ni bdag go snyam du sems pa ni bdag por 'dzin pa'o /
nityatvagrāha iti hetvādivastunā pañcavidhenā'viśuddho'pyātmā nitya / eva / anyathā [p.105]
# rtag par 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni rgyu la sogs pa dngos po rnam pa lngas rnam par ma dag kyang bdag rtag pa kho na'o /
tv akṛtābhyāgamaḥ kṛtasya nāśaśca / / tathā smṛteḥ pratyabhijñānasya cābhāvaḥ prasajyate /
# gzhan du nam byas pa dang phrad pa dang byas pa chud zos pa dang de bzhin du dran pa dang so sor ngo shes pa yang med par 'gyur ro /
saṅkliṣṭvyavadānatvagrāha iti saṅkleśavyavadānāśrayatvāt / / yogitvagrāha iti ātmani manaso dhāraṇaṃ yogaḥ prāṇamanasor vā nigrahaḥ
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i rten yin pa'i phyir ro / / rnal 'byor can du 'dzin pa zhes bya ba la / / bdag la yid 'dzin pa ni rnal 'byor ro /
ātmano manasāṃ saṃyogaviśeṣo yogaḥ so'syāstīti yogī /
# yang na dbugs dang yid 'gog pa'o / / bdag dang yid sbyor ba'i khyad par ni rnal 'byor te / / de la 'di yod pa ni rnal 'byor can no /
amuktamuktatvagrāhaśceti ātamno bandhād vimuktir iti yo vikalpaḥ //
# ma grol ba dang grol ba 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni bdag sngar bcings pa las grol lo snyam du rnam par rtog pa gang yin pa'o /
katham idaṃ daśavidhaṃ kauśalyatattvaṃ mūlatattve'ntarbhavatīti /
# mkhas pa rnam pa bcu po 'di dag rtsa ba'i de kho nar ji ltar 'du shes na zhes bya ba la /
kauśalyaṃ hi skandhādiṣu vaicakṣaṇyaṃ / / tat kathaṃ triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhavati ? / asambhāvayataḥ praśnaḥ /
# mkhas pa zhes bya ba ni phung po la sogs pa la mkhas pa yin na / / de ngo bo nyid gsum po dag tu ji ltar 'dus te / / mi srid do snyam nas dris pa'o /
yatas triṣu svabhāveṣu te skandhādayo'ntarbhūtā iti kauśalyaviṣayā ete / kauśalyaśabdenodbhāvitāḥ / / na tu tasminn eva kauśalya iti / / ataḥ akuśalyatattvasyāpy adhikāratas tatrāntarbhāvo na tu svarūpata iti
# 'di ltar ngo bo nyid gsum du phung po lnga la sogs pa de dag 'dus so zhes bya ba ni mkhas pa'i yul la 'dir mkhas pa zhes bya ba'i sgrar brjod kyi mkhas pa de nyid ma yin te / / de lta bas na mkhas pa'i de kho na skabs kyis der bsdu ba'i dngos po ni ma yin par rig par bya ste /
veditavyaṃ tadyathā phalahetutattvamārgasatyaṃ triṣvantarbhūtam uktam iti / nanvevam api naiva vijñāyante yathā'ntarbhūtā iti pṛcchati katham / antarbhūtā iti ataścāha - / parikalpavikalpārthadharmatā'rthena teṣu te / iti /
# 'di lta ste dper na 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na lam gyi bden pa gsum du 'dus par bshad pa lta bu'o / / de nyid ji lta 'dus pa'ang ma shes nas / / ji ltar 'dus shes na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir / / kun du rtog dang rnam rtog don / / chos nyid don gyi de dag der /
teṣu triṣu svabhāveṣu te skandhādayo'ntarbhūtā ityadhikṛtaṃ /
# zhes bya ba gsungs te / / ngo bo nyid gsum du phung po la sogs pa de dag 'dus so zhes bya ba'i skabs yin no /
tatra dhātvādibhyaḥ pūrvaṃ skandhānām antarbhūtatvaṃ prakāśayitavyaṃ / prathamaṃ nirdiṣṭatvāt tatrāpi rūpasyeti / [p.106]
# de la khams la sogs pa pas sngar bstan pa'i phyir phung po rnams thog mar bsdus la bshad par bya'o / / de dag las kyang gzugs su bsdu bar bya ste /
ata āha - trividhaṃ rūpaṃ / / kathaṃ ? / parikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ vikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ dharmatārūpañca / / tatra kiṃ parikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ ? / yo rūpasya parikalpitaḥ svabhāva iti /
# de'i phyir gzugs la rnam pa gsum ste / / gang zhe na kun brtags pa'i gzugs dang; rnam par brtags pa'i gzugs dang chos nyid kyi gzugs so / / de la kun brtags pa'i gzugs gang zhe na /
tac ca yā'nyatra nāmnopalabdhis tatra viṣayasvabhāvaḥ parikalpyate / / so'tyantam asattvāt parikalpita ity ucyate /
# gang gzugs kyi kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid do zhes bya ba ni da'ang gang ming du dmigs pa ma gtogs par de la yul gyi ngo bo dngos por yongs su rtog pa ste; de gtan med pa'i phyir kun brtags zhes bya'o /
vikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ yo rūpasya paratantraḥ svabhāva iti / hetupratyayapratibaddha ityarthaḥ /
# rnam par brtags pa'i gzugs ni gang gzugs ni gang gzugs gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid do zhes bya ba ni rgyu dang rkyen la rag las zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
kim arthaṃ punar idaṃ vikalpitaṃ rūpam ucyata ityata āha - tatra hi
# ci'i phyir 'di rnam par brtags pa'i gzugs zhes bya zhe na / / de'i phyir de la gzugs su rnam par rtog par byed do zhes bya ba smos te /
rūpavikalpaḥ kriyata iti / / yasmād rūpakhyātavijñāne'dṛṣṭatattvair aparijñātarūpasaṃjñatvād / rūpābhiniveśaḥ kriyate yathā skandheṣv ātmagrāhaḥ / / tasmāt paratantre vikalpitaṃ rūpam ityucyate / / dharmatārūpaṃ yo rūpasya pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva iti / / tad vikalparūpaparikalpitarūpavigatātmikā śūnyatā / / yathā rūpam iti / / yathā rūpam tridhā bhittvā triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhāvitam evaṃ / vedanādayaḥ skandhadhātvādayaś ca yojyā iti / vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānaskandhā dhātvāyatanāni / pratītyasamutpādāṅgāny-āyatanānāyatanāni-indriyāṇi adhvatrayaṃ / satyacatuṣṭayaṃ yānatrayaṃ saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtañcetyetad api vedanādikaṃ / dhātvādikañca pratyekaṃ parikalpitavikalpitadharmatāsvabhāvabhedatas / tridhā bhittvā triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhāvayitavyaṃ / / tatra pratibhāseṣu vedanādiṣu yo'tyantam asadbhūto grāhyagrāhakabhāvo / rūpapratibhāseṣu yathā grāhyabhāvaḥ parikalpyate sā parikalpitā
# 'di ltar de kho na ma mthong ba rnams kyis yongs su ma shes te / / gzugs su snang ba'i rnam par shes pa la gzugs su 'du shes nas gzugs la mngon par zhen par byed de / / dper na phung po la bdag tu 'dzin pa bzhin no / / de bas na gzhan gyi dbang la rnam par brtags pa'i gzugs zhes bya'o / / chos nyid kyi gzugs ni gang gzugs kyis yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid do zhes bya ba de ni rnam par brtags pa'i gzugs dang kun brtags pa'i gzugs de dag dang bral ba'i bdag nyid stong pa nyid do / / gzugs ji lta ba zhes bya ba ni gzugs la gsum du phye ste ngo bo nyid gsum du bsdus pa de bzhin du tshor ba la sogs pa'i phung po rnams dang khams dang skye mched la sogs pa la yang sbyar bar bya'o zhes bya ba ni tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa'i phung po dang khams dang; skye mched rnams dang rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i yan lag rnams dang gnas dang gnas ma yin pa dang dbang po rnams dang dus gsum dang bden pa bzhi dang theg pa gsum dang 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas te tshor ba la sogs pa dang khams la sogs pa de dag kyang kun brtags pa dang rnam par brtags pa dang chos nyid kyi ngo bo nyid kyi bye brag gis rnam pa gsum gsum du phye ste / / ngo bo nyid gsum du bsdu bar bya'o / / de la gzugs su snang ba rnams la gzung ba'i dngos por rtog pa bzhin du tshor ba la sogs par snang ba de la / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po gtan med pa bzhin du yang kun rtog pa gang yin pa de kun brtags pa'i tshor ba nas kun brtags pa'i rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o /
vedanā yāvat parikalpitaṃ vijñānaṃ / / yasmin grāhyagrāheka vikalpaḥ kriyate sā vikalpitā vedanā yāvad / vikalpitaṃ vijñānaṃ / / dharmatāvedanā yo vedanāyāḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ /
# gang la gzung ba dang 'dzin par rtog par byed pa de ni rnam par brtags pa'i tshor ba nas rnam par brtags pa'i rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o / / chos nyid kyi tshor ba ni gang tshor ba'i yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid de /
evaṃ yāvad dharmatāvijñānaṃ veditavyaṃ / / evaṃ dhātvāyatanādiṣv api yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vistareṇa vaktavyaṃ /
# chos nyid kyi rnam par shes pa'i bar du de bzhin du brjod par bya'o / / de bzhin du khams dang skye mched rnams la yang ci rigs par rgyas par brjod par bya'o /
rūpavedane yāvat saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtam iti yo nāmābhidheyo bhāvaḥ so'pi / porikalpitaparatantrapariniṣpannasvabhāvo veditavyaḥ / / kathaṃ ?
# gzugs dang tshor ba nas 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas zhes bya ba'i bar du ming gis brjod par bya ba'i dngos po gang yin pa de yang kun brtags pa dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid du rig par bya'o /
tatra rūpādisvabhāvaprajñaptatvāt parikalpitaḥ / prajñaptyadhiṣṭhānabhāvāt paratantraḥ pratyayaparatantratvāt tasyaiva / rūpādibhāvātyantavigatatvaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ /
# ji lta zhe na / / de la gzugs la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid du brtags pa'i phyir kun brtags pa'o / / gdags pa'i gnas kyi dngos po yin pas gzhan gyi dbang ste / / de nyid rkyen gzhan la rag las pa'i phyir ro / / gzugs la sogs pa'i dngos po dang gtan dang bral ba nyid yongs su grub pa'o; /
nanu paratantra eva manuṣyādibhāvena nāmnocyate na parikalpita ity / anarthaka / [p.107] / eva parikalpitavikalpaḥ / / nānarthakaḥ /
# gzhan gyi dbang nyid gzugs la sogs pa'i dngos por ming du brjod kyi kun brtags pa'i ni ma yin no / / kun brtags par rnam par rtog pa don med pa nyid du mi 'gyur ram zhe na /
tatra manuṣyādisvabhāvasyādhyāropitatvāt /
# don med pa ma yin te / / de la gzugs la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid du sgro btags pa'i phyir ro /
yathā hi nāmārthe pravartate tathā tathaiva nāsti / / bālas tu tat svabhāvam abhiniviśanti tac ca mithyā'dhyavasitaṃ na tu / bhūtārtheneti / / kuta etat ? / nāmārthayoḥ sārūpye vairūpye ca vācyavācakabhāvavyāvṛttitaḥ /
# ji lta ji lta bur don la ming 'jug pa de lta de lta bur med mod kyi byis pa rnams de'i ngo bo nyid du mngon par zhen to / / de'ang log par mngon par zhen pa yin gyi yang dag pa'i don du ma yin par ci mngon zhe na / / mthun nam mi mthun yang rung ste / / ming dang don gnyis kyis brjod par bya ba dang rjod pa'i dngos po ldog pa'i phyir ro /
yadi vṛkṣādiśabdānāṃ tad arthānāṃ cābhinnarūpatā evaṃ nāmnas / tadarthaṃ rūpā'vyatirekād vācakatvaṃ vyāvartyate'rthavat /
# gal te shing la sogs pa'i sgra dang de dag gi don rnams tha dad pa'i ngo bo ma yin du zin na / / de lta na ni ming dang de dag gi don gyi ngo bo tha mi dad pa'i phyir don bzhin du brjod pa ldog par 'gyur ro /
arthasyāpi nāmasvarūpā'vyatirekād vācyatvaṃ vihīyate / niyamahetvabhāvāt /
# don kyang ming gi ngo bo dang tha mi dad na brjod par bya ba las nyams par 'gyur te nges pa'i rgyu med pa'i phyir ro /
namno'pi vānyat vācakārthasya ca vācyaṃ prasajyata / ityanavasthāprasaṅgāth/ / ekasya cārthasya nāmabahutve nāmnaścārthabahutve'nekarūpatā prasajyate / ekasya tu bahusvarūpatvaṃ na yujyate /
# yang na ming gis brjod pa yang gzhan la don gyi brjod par bya ba yang gzhan du 'gyur bas thug pa med par 'gyur ro / / don gcig la ming mang po'am / / ming gcig la yang don mang por gyur na du ma'i ngo bor 'gyur te / / gcig ni du ma'i ngo bor mi rung ngo /
abhāvavācakānām arthavatām asattvaṃ tad arthasyābhāvarūpatvāt tad
# dngos po med pa'i brjod pa dag kyang don bzhin du med par 'gyur te / / de'i don dngos po med pa'i phyir ro /
arthasyāpi vā sattvaṃ nāmno'stitvād iti / / vairūpye'pi śabdānurūpyeṇārthapratyayābhāvaḥ / / śabda eva hi tatra vṛkṣo nārthaḥ /
# yang na ming yod pa'i phyir de'i don kyang yod par 'gyur ro / / mi mthun pa yang sgra dang mthun par don shes pa med de / / de la shing ni sgra nyid de don ni ma yin no /
arthastu na vṛkṣo nāpyavṛkṣaḥ / / tasmād vṛkṣaśabdārthasya na vṛkṣajñānaviṣayatvaṃ tad
# don ni shing yang ma yin shing ma yin pa'ang ma yin no / / de'i phyir shing gi sgra'i don ni shing zhes pa'i yul du mi 'gyur te /
arthasyā'vṛkṣātmakatvāt /
# de'i don ni shing gi bdag nyid ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
tad vidhañca śabdārthayor vācyavācakabhāvavyāvṛttiḥ / / vailakṣaṇye ca vācyavācakaniyamo na syāt niyamakāraṇābhāvāt /
# de ltar sgra dang don gnyis rjod pa dang brjod par bya ba'i dngos po las ldog go / / mi mthun na yang nges pa'i rgyu med pa'i phyir rjod pa dang brjod par bya ba nges pa med par 'gyur ro /
nāma cārtham utpādayed abhivyañjayed vā /
# ming gis don bskyed dam gsal bar byed grang na /
tatra notpādayati utpanne'rthe nāmakaraṇāt /
# de la skyed par byed pa ni ma yin te / / skyes zin pa'i don la ming 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
utpanno'pi punaḥ punar utpādayitavya iti prasaṅga punaḥ panar / nāmakaraṇāt / / nāpyabhivyañjayati yasmād arthaṃ gṛhītvā nāma kriyate na ca / gṛhītasyābhivyañjakaṃ yuktaṃ / / tenaiva nāmnā tamevārtham anyo na gṛhṇāti yas tan na jānāti / / tadeva tasyaivārthasyābhivyañjakaṃ cānabhivyañjakañceti na yuktaṃ /
# yang dang yang ming 'dogs pas skyes zin pa yang yang dang yang bskyed dgos par thal bar yang 'gyur ro / / gsal bar byed pa yang ma yin te / / 'di ltar don rtogs nas ming 'dogs na rtogs zin pa la ni gsal bar bya ba mi rigs so / / ming de nyid kyis don de nyid yin par su de mi shes pa gzhan dag gis ni mi rtogs so / / de nyid don de nyid gsal bar byed pa yang yin /
nābhivyañjakapradīpādayo vyaṅgyam arthaṃ vyutpattyapekṣā vyañjayanti
# gsal bar mi byed pa yang yin zhes bya bar ni mi rung ste / / gsal bar byed pa sgron ma la sogs pa dag ni gsal bar bya ba'i don shes pa la ltos nas gsal bar byed pa ma yin no /
na ca vyaṅgyeṣu ghaṭapaṭādiṣu vyañjakaniyamo dṛṣṭa iti sarvo'rthaḥ / sarveṇa nāmnā'bhivyajyeta /
# gsal bar bya ba bum pa dang snam bu la sogs pa la gsal bar byed pa nges pa yang ma mthong bas don thams cad la ming thams cad kyis gsal bar byed par 'gyur du 'ong ngo /
na ca gandhādiṣu niyamābhāvaḥ /
# dri la sogs pas nges pa yang ma yin te /
yatmāt kuthārajalādīnāṃ gandhādyutpādayitṛtvam iṣṭaṃ na tu / vyañjakatvaṃ / [p.108]
# 'di ltar ste'u dang chu la sogs pa ni dri la sogs pa'i skyed pa por 'dod kyi gsal bar byed pa ni ma yin no /
tasmād vācyavācakābhiniveśo grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśavad asadarthaṃ / eveti pratīyate /
# de bas na rjod pa dang brjod par bya ba la mngon par zhen pa ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa bzhin du don med pa nyid du mngon no /
evaṃ triṣu svabhāveṣu skandhādīnām anantarbhāvād daśavidhaṃ / kauśalyatattvaṃ mūlatattva eva draṣṭavyaṃ /
# de ltar na ngo bo nyid gsum du phung po la sogs pa 'dus pa'i phyir mkhas pa'i de kho na rnam pa bcu ni rtsa ba'i de kho na nyid du blta'o /
skandhādikauśalyam idam idamātmadarśanapratipakṣatvenoktaṃ /
# bdag tu lta ba'i gnyen por phung po la sogs pa'i don ni bshad de /
yasmistvarthe skandhādikauśalyaṃ vipakṣātmadṛṣṭapratipakṣaḥ / skandhādyartho nokta ityataḥ sa idānīm ucyate //3-16// / { skandhārthaḥ } / amekartvābhisaṅkṣepaparicchedārtha āditaḥ / / ādita ityādāv ucyata iti sambadhyate / / āditas tāvat skandhā ucyante / / te ca trividhenārthena veditavyāḥ / / anekatvārthena yat kiñcid rūpam atītānāgatapratyutpannamādhyātmikaṃ
# don gang la phung po la sogs pa la mkhas pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs bdag tu lta ba phung po la sogs pa'i don ni ma bshad pas de brjod par bya ste / / thog mar du ma nyid dang ni / / bsdus dang yongs su phye ba'i don / / zhes bya ba smos so / / thog mar zhes bya ba ni dang por brjod do zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / de la thog ma kho nar phung po bshad de / / de dag kyang don rnam pa gsum du rig par bya ste / / du ma'i don ni gzugs gang ci'ang rung ste /
vā bāhyaṃ vā audārikaṃ vā sūkṣmaṃ vā hīnaṃ vā praṇītaṃ vā yadvā / dūre yadvā'ntike ityevam anekārthena bahūnām atītānāgatādīnāṃ
# 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba'am nang gi'am phyi'i'am rags pa'am phra ba 'am ngan pa'am gya nom pa'am rgyang ring po'am thag nye ba de lta bu dag ni du ma'i don te /
dravyāṇāṃ skandhaśabdenoktatvāt / / abhisaṅkṣipyetivacanād abhisaṃkṣepārthena skandha iti / / abhisaṃkṣiptetyekīkṛtya /
# 'das pa la sogs pa'i rdzas mang po dag la phung po zhes brjod pa'i phyir ro / / bsdus pa'i don ni phung po ste / / bsdus nas gcig tu byas pa'o /
paricchedārthena ca skandha iti sambadhyate / / caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ anekārthābhisaṃkṣepārthadvayasyāpi /
# yongs su phye ba'i don yang phung po zhes bya ba dang sbyar te / / kyang zhes bya ba'i sgra ni du ma'i don dang bsdus pa'i don gnyis kyang bsdu ba'i don to /
atra kāraṇam āha - skandhānāṃ rūpādilakṣaṇasya vedanādilakṣaṇebhyaḥ / pṛthag vyavasthāpanād iti / / pṛthakparicchinna iti paryāyaḥ /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / gzugs kyi mtshan nyid kyi phung po ni tshor ba la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid las tha dad du rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
kim atra kāraṇam ebhis tribhiraṅgaiḥ skandhārtho vyavasthāpyate ?
# tha dad pa yang yongs su phye ba ni rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o / / 'dir ci'i phyir na yan lag 'di gsum gyi phung po'i don rnam par gzhag ce na /
rāśyartho hi skandhārtha ityata evaṃ vyavasthāpyate / / evañca loke rāśyartho dṛṣṭaḥ / / yo'neko'bhisaṃkṣītaḥ paricchinnaḥ sa rāśir ityucyate / / yathā rūpaskandha evaṃ vedanādayo'pi skandhā veditavyāḥ / / tatra yo'yam ekātmagrāho yathā puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca / bhāvyam ityādi tasya [p.109] / pratipakṣeṇa yathā skandhārthe kauśalyaṃ kāryaṃ tathoktaṃ / / katham iti ?
# phung po'i don ni spungs pa'i don te zhes bya bas na de'i phyir de ltar rnam par gzhag ste / / 'jig rten na yang mthong ba'i phyir ro / / de ltar 'jig rten na yang du ma dang bsdus pa dang yongs su phye ba gang yin pa de dag ni spungs pa zhes brjod par mthong ngo / / gzugs kyi phung po ji lta ba de bzhin du tshor ba'i phung po la sogs pa yang rig par bya'o / / de la ji ltar byung ba gang yin pa dang 'byung bar 'gyur ba gang yin pa la sogs pa 'di dag thams cad ni skyes bu yin no zhes bdag gcig pur 'dzin pa gang yin pa de'i gnyen por ji nas phung po'i don la mkhas par bya ba bshad de / / ji lta zhe na /
atītādibhinnarūpādiṣvaikadhyam abhisaṃkṣipteṣu / rūpādiskandhaprajñāpanāt / / etac ca trividhasammohapratipakṣeṇa trividhaskandhavyavasthāpanaṃ /
# 'das pa la sogs pa tha dad pa'i gzugs la sogs par gcig tu bsdus pa rnams la gzugs la sogs pa'i phung por gdags pa'i phyir ro / / de yang rmongs pa rnam pa gsum gyi gnyen po phung po rnam gsum gzhag ste /
trividhaḥ sammoha ekatvasammohaḥ saṃvṛti sammoho lakṣaṇasaṅkīrṇasammohaś / ca // / { dhātvarthaḥ } / skandhārthānantaraṃ dhātava uddiṣṭāḥ /
# rmongs pa rnam pa gsum ni gcig tu rmongs pa dang bzlum pa la rmongs pa dang mtshan nyid 'dres pa la rmongs pa'o / / phung po'i 'og tu khams rnams bstan te /
tasmāt skandhārthānanataraṃ dhātvartham āha -
# de bas na phung po'i don gyi 'og tu khams kyi don gsungs pa /
grāhakagrāhyatad grāhavījārthaścāparo mataḥ / iti /
# 'dzin dang gzung dang de 'dzin pa / / sa bon don de gzhan du 'dod / / ces bya ba'o /
aparaśabdo'tra dhātāveva sambadhyate skandhānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt / / ata eva bhāṣyakāro'pyāha katamo'paraḥ / / dhātur iti /
# gzhan zhes bya ba'i sgra ni khams nyid dang sbyar te phung po'i 'og tu bstan pa'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir bshad pa byed pas kyang / / gzhan gang zhe na /
bījārtho dhātvarthaḥ tadyathā svarṇo sati svarṇadhātur ucyate
# khams so zhes bya ba smos so / / sa bon gyi don ni khams kyi don te / / dper na gser yod pa'i rdo rje la gser gyi khams zhes bya ba ste /
svarṇabījam iti gamyate /
# gser gyi sa bon zhes bya bar mngon pa lta bu'o /
sa ca phalabhedāt tridhā bhidyate - grāhakadhātuḥ grāhyadhātuḥ tad / grāhadhātuṣca /
# de yang 'bras bu tha dad pas rnam pa gsum du dbye ste / / 'dzin pa'i khams dang gzung ba'i khams dang de 'dzin pa'i khams so /
tatra grāhakabījārthaścakṣurdhātvādayaḥ / / cakṣurdhāturādir yeṣāṃ manaḥparyantās te cakṣur dhātvādayaḥ /
# de la 'dzin pa'i sa bon gyi don ni mig gi khams la sogs pa ste; gang dag mig gi khams nas yid kyi khams la thug gi bar gyi khams de dag mig gi khams la sogs pa'o /
te ca rūpādiviṣayagrāhāśrayabhūtatvād grāhakāḥ /
# de dag kyang gzugs la sogs pa yul 'dzin pa'i gnas su gyur pa'i phyir 'dzin pa dag go /
sajātīyānāṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ hetutvād dhātava ucyante /
# rigs mthun pa'i mig la sogs pa dag gi rgyu yin pa'i phyir khams rnams zhes bya'o /
grāhyabījārtho rūpadhātvādayo dharmadhātuparyantāḥ /
# gzung ba'i sa bon gyi don gzugs kyi khams la sogs pa nas chos kyi khams la thug gi bar dag go /
cakṣurādivijñānaviṣayatvād grāhyāḥ /
# mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i yul yin pa'i phyir gzung ba dag go /
te'pyevaṃ sabhāgānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ hetubhāvād dhātava ucyante /
# de dag kyang de bzhin du gzugs la sogs pa mtshungs pa rnams kyi rgyu'i dngos po yin pas khams rnams zhes bya'o /
tad grāhabījārthaścakṣurvijñānadhātvādayaḥ /
# de 'dzin pa'i sa bon gyi don ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams la sogs pa ste /
rūpādipratipattisvabhāvatvād rūpādigrāhāścakṣurivjñānādayo / manovijñānaparyantāḥ /
# gzugs la sogs pa la shes pa'i ngo bo nyid yin pas gzugs la sogs pa la 'dzin pa mig gi rnam par shes pa nas yid kyi rnam par shes pa la thug gi bar dag go /
te'pi sabhāgānām eva cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ hetubhūtatvād dhātava / ucyante cakṣurvijñānadhātvādayo manovijñānadhātuparyantāḥ /
# de dag kyang mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa mtshungs pa rnams kyi rgyur gyur pa'i phyir khams rnams zhes bya ste / / mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams nas yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi bar dag go /
anye tvāhuḥ - cakṣurādyabhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānaṃ / yathākramaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ bījaṃ /
# kha cig na re mig la sogs pa la mngon par zhen pa'i las kyi bag chags bsgos pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni mig la sogs pa'i sa bon te go rims bzhin no /
tathā rūpādyabhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānaṃ yathākramaṃ / rūpādīnāṃ bījaṃ /
# de bzhin du gzugs la sogs pa la mngon par zhen pa'i las kyi bag chags bsgos pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni gzugs la sogs pa'i sa bon te go rims bzhin no /
tathā cakṣurādivijñānābhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānam eva / cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ yathākramaṃ bījam iti /
# de bzhin du mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa la mngon par zhen pa'i las kyi bag chags bsgos pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i sa bon te go rims bzhin no /
evaṃ tvālayavijñānam eva dhātuśabdavācyaṃ na cakṣurādaya iti cintyam / etat /
# de ltar na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid la khams zhes bya ba'i sgrar brjod kyi / / mig la sogs pa la ni mi bya'o zhes te / / 'di ni bsam dgos pa'o /
kartṛkriyākarmasammohavyāvartanārthaṃ trividhe bījārthe dhātur / vyavasthāpitaḥ /
# byed pa dang bya ba dang las rnams la rmongs pa ldog par bya ba'i phyir sa bon gyi don rnam pa gsum la khams rnam par gzhag go /
atra pūrvacakṣurādaya uttaracakṣurādīnām eva hetavo bhavanti na
# 'di la mig la sogs pa snga ma ni mig la sogs pa phyi ma dag gi rgyur gyur pa yin gyi /
tatrānyaḥ kaścid ātmā'nyo vā hetuvidyata ityevaṃ dhātukauśalyād / ātmani hetugrāhavyāvṛttiḥ //3-17// [p.110]
# 'di la rgyu bdag ces bya ba gzhan gang yang med do / / de ltar na khams la mkhas na bdag la rgyur 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur ro /
{ āyatanārthaḥ } / dhātvarthānantaram āyatanānām artho vaktavyaḥ / / ata āha -
# khams kyi don gyi 'og tu skye mched rnams kyi don brjod par bya ste / / de'i phyir /
veditārthaparicchedabhogāyadvārato'paraṃ / iti /
# tshor dang don rnams yongs gcod kyi / / nyer spyod 'byung sgo gzhan yin no / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
dhātor aparāṇāṃ hyāyatanapratītyasamutpādādīnāṃ bahutvād / aparaśabdasya ca sāmānyatvāt praśnaḥ kim aparam iti /
# khams rnams las gzhan pa ni skye mched dang rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba la sogs pa mang zhig kyang yod la / / gzhan zhes bya ba'i sgra ni spyir brjod pa'i phyir /
dhātubhyo'nantaram uddiṣṭatvād arthata āyataneṣvevāyam / aparaśabdo'vatiṣṭhata iti jñāpanārtham āha - āyatanam iti /
# gzhan gang yin zhes dris pa dang khams rnams kyi 'og tu bshad pa'i phyir don gyis na skye mched rnams las gzhan zhes bya ba'i sgra 'di gnas par bstan pa'i phyir / / skye mched do zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra veditopabhogāyadvārārthena ṣaḍādhyātmikānyāyatanāni /
# de la nang gi skye mched drug po dag ni tshor ba'i nye bar spyod pa skye ba'i sgo'i phyir ro /
arthaparicchedopabhogāyadvārārthena ṣaḍ bāhyānīti /
# phyi'i drug po dag ni don yongs su gcod pa'i nye bar spyod pa skye ba'i sgo'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la sogs pa la /
āyadvārārthaṃ āyatanārthaḥ /
# skye ba'i sgo'i don ni skye mched kyi don to /
āya āgamaḥ / / taṃ veditārthaparicchedopabhogayos tanvantītyāyatanāni /
# skye ba ni 'byung ba ste tshor ba dang don yongs su gcod pa'i nye bar spyod pa gnyis kyi skye ba de mched par byed pas skye mched do /
veditasaṃjñopabhogāyadvārebhedanādhyātmikabāhyaprabhedaḥ /
# tshor ba dang 'du shes kyi nye bar spyod pa skye ba'i sgo'i bye brag gis phyi dang nang du dbye ste /
veditaṃ hi sukhaduḥkhā'duḥkhā'sukhaṃ / / tadevopabhujyata ity upabhogaḥ /
# tshor ba ni bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa'o / / de nyid nye bar spyod pas na nye bar spyod pa ste /
anubhūyata ityarthaḥ /
# myong ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tasya vedanopabhogasyāyadvāram ādhyātimkānyevāyatanāny uktāni /
# nang gi skye mched rnams ni tshor ba'i nye bar spyod pa de skye ba'i sgor bshad do /
satyapi viṣayāṇāṃ tadāyadvārabhāve cakṣurādīnām āśrayāṇām / anugrahopaghātatvena tat pravīṇatvena cāsādhāraṇatvenāśrayatvāt sati
# yul rnams kyang de skye ba'i sgo yin mod kyi gnas mig la sogs pa ni phan 'dogs pa dang gnod pa byed pa dang de la yang rab tu shes pa dang thun mong ma yin pas gnas su gyur pa'i phyir mig la sogs pa yod na de'i sgo nas tshor ba las spyod par 'gyur gyi /
cakṣurādau taddvāreṇa vedanopabhogān nāstīti / / arthaparicchedaḥ saṃjñā arthanimittodgrahaṇātmakatvāt /
# med na ni ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / don yongs su gcod pa ni 'du shes te / / don la mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyi phyir ro /
saivārthapratipattyatmakatvād viṣayam upabhuṅkte / / tadāyadvārabhāvena bāhyānyāyatanānyuktāni na tvādhyātmikāni / satyapi tadāyadvārabhāve yasmād
# de nyid don rtogs pa'i bdag nyid yin pas yul rnams la nyer bar spyod do / / de skye ba'i sngos po'i sgo yin pas ni phyi rol gyi skye mched rnams bshad kyi / / nang gi rnams ni ma yin te /
viṣayābhāve'rthaparicchedopabhogābhāvaḥ satyapy ādhyātmike / cakṣurādyāyatane /
# sgye ba'i sgo yin du zin kyang 'di ltar yul gyi dngos po med na nang gi mig la sogs pa'i skye mched yod kyang don yongs su gcod pa la nye bar spyod pa med par 'gyur ro /
veditārthaparicchedayoḥ sasamprayogayor ayadvārabhāvatvād / etānyāyatanāni veditavyāni / / pradhānaṃ hi dvayagrahaṇaṃ /
# tshor ba dang don yongs su gcod pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa dag skye ba'i sgo'i dngos po yin pa'i phyir skye mched 'di dag rig par bya ste / / gtso bor ni gnyis gzung ngo /
grahaṇaprādhānyaṃ punaḥ karmaphalopabhogād arthaparicchedātmakatvāc ca
# gtso bor gzung ba ni las kyi 'bras bu la spyod pa dang don yongs su gcod pa'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
veditārthaparicchedopabhogamukhena bhoktṛvikalpaḥ pravartata ityato
# tshor ba dang don yongs su gcod pa la nye bar spyod pa'i sgo nas za ba por rnam par rtog pa 'byung ste /
dvividhenārthenāyatane vyavasthānaṃ kṛtaṃ /
# de'i phyir don gnyis kyis skye mched rnam par gzhag pa byas so /
evam āyatanakauśalyaṃ bhoktā''dhyātmikānyāyatanāni bhojanam / āyatanāni bāhyāni /
# de ltar skye mched la mkhas pa za ba po ni nang gi skye mched rnams yin la / / bza' bar bya ba ni phyi'i rnams yin te /
nānyo bhoktetyātmani bhoktṛtvagrāho vyāvartate /
# za ba po'i bdag med do snyam nas bdag za pa por 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur ro /
yad uktaṃ cakṣuāradyāyatanānām anugrahopaghātāt tad adhiṣṭhāna eva / bhoktṛtvavyavahāra iti tad ayuktaṃ /
# mig la sogs pa'i skye mched la phan pa dang gnod pa'i phyir de'i gnas nyid za ba por tha snyad btags so zhes gang bshad pa de mi rigs te /
rūpapratiṣedhena cakṣurādīnām āyatanānām apy asattvādātmavad iti / naiṣa / [p.111] / upālambhaḥ /
# gzugs bkag pa'i phyir bdag bzhin du mig la sogs pa'i skye mched rnams kyang med pa'i phyir ro zhe na / / 'di ni klan kar mi rung ste /
yasmāt parikalpitarūpasyaivātra pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na vikalpatārūpasya
# 'di ltar kun brtags pa'i gzugs kho na 'dir dgag par bya'i / / rnam par brtags pa'i gzugs ni ma yin no /
tatra cakṣurādiprapañcaparibhāvitakarmākṣiptatvenālayavijñānaṃ / pariṇāmaviśeṣaprāptamādhyātmikam āyatanaṃ / / tan nimittasya pravṛttivijñānasya rūpādipratibhāsaṃ bāhyāyatanaṃ / / ya ālayavijñānasya sādhāraṇārthapratibhāso yaś ca sattvapratibhāsaḥ
# de la mig la sogs par spros pas bsgos pa'i las kyis 'phags pas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa 'gyur ba'i khyad par rnyed pa ni nang gi skye mched do / / rgyu de las byung ba 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa la gzugs la sog par snang ba ni phyi'i skye mched do /
so'pi grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsasya / pravṛttivijñānasyotpattāvadhipatipratyayatvād bāhyam āyatanam ucyate / na tu tad viṣayatvād iti /
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa thun mong gi don du snang ba gang yin pa dang sems can du snang ba gang yin pa de yang gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa skye ba'i bdag po'i rkyen yin pa'i phyir phyi'i skye mched ces bya'i / / de yul du gyur pa'i phyir ni ma yin no /
nanvevaṃ dvayam āśritya cakṣur vijñānādaya utpadyanta iti sūtravacanena / virudhyate /
# de ltar na go mdo sde las gnyis la brten nas mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa skye'o zhes 'byung ba dang mi 'gal lam /
rūpādipratibhāso vijñānād bhinnaḥ . / na ca tadeva tasyaivotpattipratyayo yuktaḥ /
# gzugs la sogs par snang ba ni rnam par shes pa las tha dad na de nyid skye ba'i rkyen du de nyid 'gyur bar ni mi rigs te /
utpannānutpannāvasthayor bhāvād abhāvāc ca svātmani vṛttivirodhāt /
# skyes pa dang ma skyes pa'i dus na yod pa dang med pa'i phyir ro / / bdag nyid la 'jug pa 'gal ba'i yang phyir ro /
tasmād avaśyaṃ vijñānanirbhāsād bhinnā rūpādayo'bhyupagantavyā iti / naiṣo'pyupālambhaḥ /
# de lta bas na gdon mi za bar rnam par shes pa snang ba las tha dad par gyur pa gzugs la sogs par khas blang bar bya'o zhe na / / 'di yang klan kar mi rung ste /
yasmād pādinirbhāsavijñānṃ sabhāgavijñānotpattaye pratyayavijñāne / vāsanām ādhatte /
# 'di ltar gzugs la sogs pa'i snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni 'dra ba'i rnam par shes pa skye bar bya ba'i phyir rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa la bag chags 'jog go /
vasanāpariṇāmāc ca rūpādyābhāsaṃ punar vijñānaṃ jāyate /
# bag chags yongs su gyur nas yang gzugs la sogs par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa skye ste /
evaṃ vijñānanirbhāsātmakatvena vāsanāhito vijñānapratyaya ukta iti / na sūtravirodhaḥ /
# de ltar rnam par shes pa gzugs la sogs par snang ba'i bdag nyid kyi bag chags bskyed pa rnam par shes pa'i rkyen yin par bshad pas na mdo sde dang 'gal bar 'gyur ba med do /
evaṃ rūpādinirbhāsasyālambanārtho'py upapannaḥ svanirbhāsākārasya / vijñānasya pratyayatvāt /
# de ltar na rang snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'i rkyen yin pa'i phyir gzugs la sgos par snang ba ni dmigs pa'i don du 'thad do /
athavā yathā bāhyārthavādibhir vijñānena sahaja ālambanapratyayo / vyavasthāpyate janyajanakavad abhāve'pi tad bhāvābhāvābhyāṃ
# yang na ji ltar phyi'i don du smra ba dag gis bskyed par bya ba dang skyed pa po lta bur med kyang de yod pa dang med pa las rnam par shes pa yod pa dang med par 'gyur ba'i dbang du byas nas /
vijñānabhāvābhāvāvadhikṛtya evam ihāpi rūpādinirbhāsasya / vijñānasya vā'satyapi janyajanakabhāve tad bhāvābhāvayor / vijñānabhāvābhāvavyabhicārāt pratyayapratyayitvaṃ vyavasthāpyate / / rūpanirbhāsavijñānayor abhinnatvād dṛṣṭāntena mukhyato'sādṛśyam iti / na bhedopacārāt /
# rnam par shes pa dang lhan cig skyes pa ni dmigs pa'i rkyen du 'jog pa de bzhin du 'dir yang gzugs la sogs pa snang ba'i rnam par shes pa bskyed par bya ba dang skyed pa po'i dngos por med kyang de yod pa dang med pa las rnam par shes pa yod pa dang med par 'gyur ba 'khrul pa med pa'i phyir rkyen dang rkyen can du rnam par gzhag go / / gzugs su snang ba dang rnam par shes pa gnyis tha mi dad pa'i phyir / / dpe dang dngos su mi 'dre'o zhe na / / ma yin te /
tadyathā grāhyagrāhakavikalpādhiṣṭḥānatvāt / svapnamāyāgandharvanagarādivijñānaṃ paramārthato'abhinnam api
# tha dad par gdags pa'i phyir ro / / dper na rmi lam dang sgyu ma dang dri za'i grong khyer la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa don dam par tha mi dad mod kyi /
grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa bhinnam iva vyavasthāpyata / ālambyālambakabhāvatvena tathā'nyatrāpi nāsti virodhaḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i gnas yin pa'i phyir gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par tha snyad kyi tha dad pa lta bur dmigs par bya ba dang dmigs par byed pa'i dngos por rnam par gzhag pa de bzhin du gzhan la 'gal ba med do /
api cālambyālambakabhāvaḥ sarvatropacaryata eva na mukhyo'sti /
# gzhan yang dmigs par bya ba dang dmigs par byed pa'i dngos po ni thams cad du yang gdags pa nyid du zad kyi dngos su med de /
nahi vijñānam utpannam anutpannaṃ vā viṣayam ālambate /
# rnam par shes pa ni skyes pa'am ma skyes pas kyang yul la dmigs par mi 'gyur te /
utpattyanantaravināśitvāt kriyākāle'navasthānād asattvāc ca /
# skyes ma thag tu zhig pa'i phyir dmigs par byed pa'i tshe mi sdod pa dang med pa'i phyir ro /
viṣayaścotpanno'nutpanno vobhayathā'pyālambanatvenāyogyaḥ / / utpannasyā'navasthānād anutpannasya cāsattvāt /
# yul yang skyes pa dang ma skyes pa gnyis ka la yang dmigs su mi rung ste / / skyes pa ni gnas pa med pa dang ma skyes pa ni med pa'i phyir te /
nahi nirādhārālambanakriyā yujyate /
# gzhi med pa la ni dmigs par byar mi rung ngo /
yasyāpi sattāmātreṇa kāryakāraṇabhāva evālambyālambakabhāvas / tasyāpi vartamānasya vijñānasyālambanaṃ nirarthakaṃ [p.112]
# gang gi ltar yod pa tsam gyis rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos po de nyid dmigs par bya ba dang dmigs par byed par 'jog pa de'i ltar na yang da ltar gyi rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa ni don med par 'gyur te /
bhavati tadātmatvena siddheḥ /
# de'i bdag nyid du grub zin pa'i phyir ro /
utpadyamānasyāpi nirarthakam asattvāt /
# skye ba'i tshe'ang don med par 'gyur te / / med pa'i phyir ro /
notpadyamānasya nirarthakaṃ yasmād viṣayasadbhāve vijñānaṃ tan / nirbhāsam ātmānaṃ pratilabhate / / yadi viṣayanirbhāso vijñānasya bāhyārthanimittaḥ evam
# skye ba'i tshe don med par mi 'gyur te / / 'di ltar yul gyi dngos po yod na rnam par shes pa der snang ba'i bdag nyid 'thob pa'i phyir ro zhe na / / gal te yul du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'i rgyu phyi rol gyi don yin te /
atītānāgatasvapnādivijñānasya nirākāratvaṃ vartate / / tad arthābhāvād vā sattvaṃ / / na vikalaiḥ pratyayaiḥ kāryam utpadyate atiprasaṅgāt / / na cāsataḥ pratyayatvaṃ yujyate /
# de lta na 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang rmi lam la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnam pa med par 'gyur ro / / yang na de'i don med pas med pa nyid du 'gyur ro / / rkyen ma tshang ba ni 'bras bu 'byung bar mi rung ste / / ha cang thal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / med pa ni rkyen du mi rung ngo /
na ca bāhyārtha ālambanapratyayo vijñānasya tena vināpi bhāvāt /
# phyi'i don yang rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa'i rkyen du mi 'gyur te / / de med kyang 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
tasmāt sarvam eva vijñānaṃ taimirikādīnām iva / bāhyārthālambananirapekṣam evābhyupagantavyaṃ //
# de bas na rab rib can la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa thams cad phyi'i don dmigs pa la mi ltos pa nyid khas blang bar bya'o /
{ pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ } / āyatanā'rthānantaraṃ pratītyasamutpādārtho vaktavya ityata āha - / pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ / / punar hetuphalāyāsā'nāropā'napavādataḥ //
# skye mched kyi don gyi 'og tu rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i don brjod dgos te / / de'i phyir rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i don te / / rgyu dang 'bras bu rtsol ba la / / sgro 'dogs med cing skur 'debs med /
nirīhānityasamarthapratyayotpādanārthaḥ / / yathoktaṃ sūtre'pi - etad asmin satīdambhavati /
# ces bya ba smos so / / g yo ba med pa dang mi rtag pa dang nus pa'i rkyen las byung ba'i don to / / mdo sde las kyang 'di skad du / / 'di yod pas 'di 'byung /
asyotpādādidam utpadyate yad utāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā iti vistaraḥ
# 'di skyes pa'i phyir 'di skye ba ste / / 'di ltar ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ba rgya cher gsungs pa lta bu'o /
ayaṃ ca pratītyasamutpādo hetupahalakriyāṇāṃ / samāropāpavādapratiṣedheneṣyata iti pratipādayann āha -
# 'di yang rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i rgyu dang 'bras bu dang byed pa rnams la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa dgag par 'dod pa bstan pa'i phyir /
hetuphalakriyāṇām asamāropavādārthaḥ pratītyasamutpādārtha iti /
# rgyu dang 'bras bu dang byed pa rnams la sgro 'dogs pa med pa dang skur ba 'debs pa med pa'i don ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i don to zhes bya ba smos so /
āyāsaśabdena tu kriyoktā /
# rtsol ba zhes bya ba'i sgra ni byed par bshad do /
tatra hetusamāropaḥ avidyādīn hitvā puruṣeśvarāṇupradhāṇādīnāṃ / hetutvakalpanāt /
# de la rgyu la sgro 'dogs pa ni ma rig pa la sogs pa bor nas skyes bu dang dbang phyug dang bdag dang gtso bo la sogs pa la rgyu nyid du rtog pa'i phyir ro /
etad eva pratipādayann āha - saṃskārādīnāṃ jarāmaraṇaparyantānāṃ
# de bstan par bya ba'i phyir / / 'du byed la sogs pa tha ma rga shi la thug pa dag gi mi mthun pa'i rgyu la rtog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
viṣamahetukalpnād iti / / saṃskārādīnāṃ hy anityānāṃ nityaḥ puruṣādiko hetur viṣamo visadṛśa
# 'du byed la sogs pa mi rtag pa rnams kyi rgyu skyes bu la sogs pa rtag pa ni mi mthun pa ste / / mi 'dra ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ityarthaḥ / / athavā hetuḥ svarūpavikriyā'pekṣo bījādiko'ṅkurādīnāṃ dṛṣṭaḥ /
# yang na rgyu'i rang bzhin 'gyur ba la ltos nas sa bon la sogs pa la myu gu la sogs pa mthong ste /
na ca nityasya svarūpavikriyā'stīti viṣamahetau hetutvakalpanād / hetusamāropaḥ / [p.113]
# rang bzhin rtag pa la ni 'gyur ba med do / / mi mthun pa'i rgyu nyid la rgyur rtog pa'i phyir rgyu la sgro 'dogs pa'o /
hetvapavādo nirhetukatvakalpanād iti saṃskārādīnāṃ / nirhetukotpādābhyupagamād avidyādīnāṃ saṃskārādihetutvam apoḍhaṃ / bhavati /
# rgyu la skur pa 'debs pa ni rgyu med pa can du rtog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni 'du byed la sogs pa rgyu med par skye bar khas blangs pas 'du byed la sogs pa'i rgyu ma rig pa la sogs pa gsal ba yin no /
phalasamāropaḥ sātmakānāṃ saṃskārādīnām / avidyādipratyayapravṛttikalpanād iti /
# 'bras bu la sgro 'dogs pa ni bdag dang bcas pa'i 'du byed la sogs pa ma rig pa la sogs pa'i rkyen las 'byung bar rtog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la /
satyātmani saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttitvaṃ na tv astīti / saṃskārādiphaleṣv ātmasamāropa ityeke /
# kha cig na re bdag yod na ni 'du byed la sogs pa ma rig pa la sogs pa'i rkyen rnams las 'byung gi / / med na ni ma yin no zhes 'bras bu 'du byed la sogs par bdag sgro 'dogs na 'bras bu la sgro 'dogs pa zhes bya'o zhe'o /
ātmadravyasamavāyitvena tad anugrahopaghātakartṛtvena vā sātmakānāṃ / saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttikalpanāt phalasamāropa ityapare
# gzhan dag na re bdag gi rdzas dang ldan pas sam / / de phan pa dang gnod pa byed pas bdag dang bcas pa'i 'du byed la sogs pa ni ma rig pa la sogs pa'i rkyen las 'byung bar rtog pa'i phyir 'bras bu la sgro 'dogs pa zhes bya'o /
phalāpavādo na santy avidyādipratyayāḥ saṃskāradaya iti kalpanād iti / / tad yathā - sucaritaduścaritaparalokāpavādināṃ nāsti sucaritaṃ nāsti / duścaritaṃ nāsti paraloka iti /
# 'bras bu la skur pa 'debs pa ni 'du byed la sogs pa ma rig pa la sogs pa'i rkyen gyis 'byung ba med par rtog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste / / legs par spyad pa yang med / / nyes par spyad pa yang med / / 'jig rten pha rol yang med do zhes med pa rnams legs par spyad pa dang nyes par spyad pa dang 'jig rten pha rol la skur pa 'debs par smra ba'o /
kriyāsamāropo'vidyādīnāṃ saṃskārādyutpattau vyāpārakalpanād iti / / yadi vasturūpam arthāntarabhūtaṃ saṃskārādyutpattāv avidyādayaḥ / kurvantīti kalpyeta evaṃ kriyāsamāropaḥ / / kriyāpavādo nissāmarthyakalapanād iti /
# byed pa la sgro 'dogs pa ni 'du byed la sogs skye ba la ma rig pa la sogs pa byed par rtog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni gal te 'du byed la sogs pa skye ba la ma rig pa la sogs pa dngos po'i rang bzhin don gzhan du gyur pa zhig byed par rtog pa de lta bu ni byed pa la sgro 'dogs pa'o / / byed pa la skur pa 'debs pa ni nus pa med par rtog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la /
avidyādīnāṃ sattāmātreṇa saṃskārāṇāṃ hy utpādanasamarthānām api / niḥsāmarthyakalpanāt kriyāpavādaḥ /
# ma rig pa la sogs pa yod pa tsam gyis 'du byed la sogs pa skye bar nus pa yin yang nus pa med par rtog pa'i phyir byed pa la skur pa 'debs pa'o /
tad abhāvād asamāropānapavādo veditavya iti / / tasya hetuphalakriyāṇāṃ samāropāpavādasyābhāvād asamāropānapavādo
# de med pa'i phyir sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa med par rig par bya'o zhes bya ba ni rgyu dang 'bras bu dang byed pa rnams la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa de med pa'i phyir sgro 'dogs pa med pa dang skur pa 'debs pa med par rig par bya'o /
veditavyaḥ / / evam idaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam avidyādivyatirekeṇātmanyanyasmin
# de ltar rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa 'di ni ma rig pa las gzhan pa bdag gam gzhan yang rung ste /
vā yaḥ kartṛtvagrāhas tasyaṃ pratipakṣeṇa veditavyaṃ /
# byed par 'dzin pa gang yin pa de'i gnyen po yin par rig par bya'o /
na hy atrātmānyo vā'vidyāvyatirekeṇa śubhāśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kartā /
# 'di la ma rig pa ma gtogs par dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las rnams byed pa ni bdag gam gzhan yang rung ste med do /
anyaḥ saṃskāravyatirekeṇa vijñānasya kartā nāsti /
# 'du byed rnams ma gtogs par rnam par shes pa'i byed pa gzhan med do /
evaṃ sarvatrāpi yathāyogaṃ vaktavyaṃ nirīhebhyo'nityebhyaḥ / samarthebhyaścāvidyādibhyaḥ saṃskārādyutpattitaḥ //3-18// / { sthānā'sthānārthaḥ } [p.114] / pratītyasamutpādānantaraṃ sthānā'sthānārtho vaktavya ityata āha - / aniṣṭeṣṭaviśuddhīnāṃ / iti vistaraḥ /
# thams cad du yang ci rigs par brjod par bya ste / / ma rig pa la sogs pa gyo ba med pa mi rtag pa la sogs pa nus pa yod pa dag las 'du byed la sogs pa 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i don gyi 'og tu gnas dang gnas ma yin pa'i don brjod dgos te / / de'i phyir / / mi 'dod 'dod dang rnam dag dang / / mnyam du 'byung dang dbang byed dang / / 'thob dang kun du spyod pa dag / / gzhan dbang nyid kyi don de gzhan / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
sthānāsthānaṃ saptavidhapāratantryārthena veditam iti / / tatra sthānaṃ hetuḥ asthānamahetuḥ / / yathoktaṃ gāthāyāṃ -
# gnas dang gnas ma yin pa ni gzhan gyi dbang nyid rnam pa bdun gyi don gyis rig par bya ste zhes bya ba de la gnas ni rgyu yin no / / gnas ma yin pa ni rgyu ma yin te / / ji skad du /
satyaṃ vaden na ca kruddhed dadyād alpoo'pi yācitaḥ /
# bden par smra zhing khro ba med / / slong la chung yang sbyin par bya /
ebhis tribhir iha shtānair devānāṃ samitiṃ vrajet // / hetubhir iti gamyate / / athavā sthānaṃ sambhavaḥ asthānaṃ punar asambhavaḥ /
# rnam pa 'di gsum gnas kyis ni / / lha yi nang du skye bar 'gyur / / zhes tshigs su bcad pa las 'byung ba lta bu ste rgyu yin par mngon no / / yang na gnas ni srid pa'o / / gnas ma yin pa ni mi srid do /
tat kauśalyaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyaṃ / / paratantrasya bhāvaḥ pāratantryaṃ /
# de la mkhas pa ni gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa'o / / gzhan gyi dbang gi dngos po ni gzhan gyi dbang nyid de /
parāyattatetyarthaḥ / / tac ca saptavidham api triṣvantarbhavati karmakleśajanmapāratantryeṣu /
# gzhan la rag las zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / rnam pa de bdun yang las dang nyon mongs pa dang tshe'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid gsum du 'dus so /
tatrāniṣṭe pāratantryam iti / / aniṣṭā duargatayaḥ / / tatra gamanaṃ duścaritāyatattvaṃ pāratantryañceti pradarśayann āha -
# de la mi 'dod pa'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni zhes bya ba la / / mi 'dod pa ni ngan 'gro rnams te / / der 'gro ba gzhan gyi dbang nyid du bstan pa'i phyir /
duśaritena prāṇātipātādinā kāyavāṅmanaḥkarmasaṇggṛhītena / saprayogapṛṣṭhenā'nicchato'pi durgatigamād iti / / durgatayo narakāḥ pretāstiryañcaś ca /
# nyes par spyod pa srog gcod pa la sogs pa lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las su bsdus pa sbyor ba dang bcas pa dang mjug gis mi 'dod bzhin du yang ngan 'gror 'gro ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
teṣām ekāntena duḥkhatvān na kasyacit tatra gamanecchā bhavati /
# ngan 'gro dag ni sems can dmyal ba dang yi dags dang dud 'gro'o / / de dag ni shin tu sdug bsngal ba'i phyir der 'gro 'dod pa ni su yang med mod kyi /
karmaṇāṃ balavattvād durgatigetutvāc ca duścaritasyānicchato'pi tatra / karmavaśād eva gamanaṃ bhavati /
# las rnams stobs dang ldan la ngan 'gro'i rgyu yang yin pas nye bar spyod pa ni mi 'dod bzhin du las kyi dbang gis der 'gro bar 'gyur ro /
iṣṭe pāratantryaṃ sucaritena sugatigamanād iti / / iṣṭaṃ sugatigamanaṃ / / sugatir devā manuśyāś ca /
# 'dod pa'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni legs par spyad pas bde 'gror 'gro ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la / / 'dod pa ni bde 'gror 'gro ba'o / / bde 'gro ni lha dang mi'o /
sucaritaṃ saprayogapṛṣṭhebhyaḥ prāṇātipātādibhyo viratiḥ / dānamānasatkārādikriyā śāstṛguruṇānvitādiṣu maitrīkaruṇādayaś ca
# legs par spyod pa ni srog gcod pa la sogs pa sbyor ba dang bcas pa dang 'jug pa rnams las log pa dang; ston pa dang bla ma dang yon tan dang ldan pa la sogs pa la sbyin pa dang rim gro dang bkur sti la sogs pa byed pa dang byams pa dang snying rje la sogs pa yon tan gyi khyad par rnams so /
guṇaviśeṣāḥ / / pāratantryaṃ sucaritamantareṇānyathā prārthayatām api / sugatigamanābhāvāt / / sucaritapratibaddhataiva sugatyutpatteḥ /
# gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni legs par spyad pa med par gzhan gyis ni 'dod du zin kyang bde 'gror 'gro ba med pa'i phyir te / / bde 'gror skye ba ni legs par spyad pa la rag lus pa nyid do /
viśūddhau pāratantryam iti vistaraḥ / / viśuddhiḥ kleśaprahāṇaṃ /
# rnam par dag pa'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni ches rgya cher 'byung ba la rnam par dag pa ni nyon mongs pa spangs pa'o /
pañca nivaraṇāni kāmacchando vyāpādaḥ styānamiddhamauddhatyakaukṛtyaṃ / vicikitsā ca / / styānamiddhamekīkṛtya auddhatyakaukṛtyañca pañca bhavati / / abhedena kuśalapakṣaṃ nivṛṇvantīti nivaraṇāni bhedena punar yathākramaṃ / pravrajatyābhiratiṃ tad anurūpe kāyavākkarmāṇi sabrahmacāribhiḥ samyak / coditasya samyak pratipattiṃ śamathakāle'līnatāṃ pragrahakāle'vikṣepaṃ / śamathavipaśyanākāle svarasavāditāṃ chādayantīti nivaraṇāni / / tānyaprahāyātyaktvā yāvat sapta bodhyaṅgānyabhāvayitveti /
# sgrib pa lnga ni 'dod pa la 'dun pa dang gnod sems dang rmugs pa dang; gnyid dang rgod pa dang 'gyod pa dang the tshom mo / / rmugs pa dang gnyid gcig tu bsdus / / rgod pa dang 'gyod pa gcig tu bsdus te lngar 'gyur ro / / dge ba'i phyogs la sgrib par bye brag med pas sgrib pa rnams so / / bye brag tu ni sgrib pa rnams zhes mngon par dga' ba dang lus dang ngag gi las mi cha ba la tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa rnams kyis legs par blangs pa la legs par sgrub pa dang zhi gnas kyi dus na ma bying ba dang rab tu 'dzin pa'i dus na mi gyeng ba dang zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gi dus na rang gi ngang gis 'jug pa la rim pa bzhin du bsgribs pas na sgrib pa rnams zhes bya'o / / de dag ma spangs lags zhes bya ba ni ma btang ba'o / / byang chub kyi yan lag bdun gyi bar du ma bsgoms na zhes bya ba la /
yāvad iti paryantopadeśāt smṛtyupasthānasamyak / prahāṇarddhipādendriyabalānām api grahaṇaṃ /
# bar du zhes bya ba ni mtha' brjod pa ste / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams dang yang dag par spong ba rnams dang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams dang dbang po rnams dang stobs rnams kyang bsdu'o /
duḥkhasyāntā'karaṇād iti / / duḥkhasyānto [p.115]
# sdug bsngal gyi mtha' mi byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la /
yatra duḥkhaṃ nāsti tac ca nirvāṇaṃ tasyākaraṇam aprāptir nirvāṇaṃ na / prāpnotītyarthaḥ /
# sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ni gang na sdug bsngal med pa ste / / de ni mya ngan las 'das pa'o / / de mi byed pa ni mi 'thob pa ste / / mya ngan las 'das pa mi 'thob po zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
athavā duḥkhasyānto yasmād duḥkhādanyaduḥkhaṃ na sandhīyate tat
# yang na sdug bsngal gyi mtha' zhes bya ba ni sdug bsngal gzhan dang mtshams mi sbyor ba'o /
tādṛśaṃ duḥkhaṃ na karotītyapratisandhikaṃ duḥkham na karotītyarthaḥ /
# de ni sdug bsngal de lta bu dang mtshams sbyor bar mi byed pa ste / / sdug bsngal du mi byed pa'i phyir ro /
pañca nivaraṇaprahāṇapratibaddhatā viśuddhau pāratantryaṃ /
# sgrib pa lnga spangs pa la rag lus pa'i phyir rnam par dag pa gzhan gyi dbang nyid do /
samotpattau pāratantryaṃ dvayor apūrvācaramayor iti sahitayor ityarthaḥ / / tathāgatayoścakravartinoścaikasmil lokadhātāvanutpādād iti /
