# mnyam du 'byung ba'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni de bzhin gshegs pa dang 'khor los sgyur ba gnyis gnyis snga phyi med par zhes bya ba ni lhan cig ces pa'i tha tshig go /
tathāgatayos trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhātur abhipretaḥ /
# de bzhin gshegs pa gnyis dang 'khor los sgyur ba gnyis 'jig rten gyi khams gcig tu mi 'byung zhes bya ba ni /
cakravartinos tu cātur dvīpaka iti kecit / / tathāgatayor api cātur dvīpaka evetyapare / / buddhā hi bhagavanto dharmakāyādhipatyāt trisāhasramahāsāhasre
# kha cig na re de bzhin gshegs pa gnyis stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su mi 'byung bar 'dod kyi / / 'khor los sgyur ba ni gling bzhi par 'byung bar mi 'dod do zhe'o /
lokadhātau pratyekaṃ cātur dvīpakeṣu nirmāṇakāyenābhisambodhiṃ / parinirvāṇaṃ ca darśayanti / / tathā hi yadekasmiñcāturmahādvīpake tuṣiteṣu manuṣyeṣu ca / cyutijanmaparigraho bodhisattvānām prayojanaṃ / / taditareṣv api cātur dvīpakeṣu samānaṃ / / tasmād akaniṣṭhabhavana evābhisambuddho bhagavān nirmāṇakāyena
# gzhan dag na re de bzhin gshegs pa gnyis kyang gling bzhi pa nyid du mi 'byung ngo zhes zer te / / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi sku'i dbang gis stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su gling bzhi pa re rer yang sprul pa'i skus mngon par byang chub pa dang yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa yang ston to / / 'di ltar gling bzhi pa gcig tu dga' ldan dang mi rnams kyi nang du yang tshe yongs su 'dzin pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis dgongs pa ste / / de ni gling bzhi pa gzhan du'ang 'dra'o /
trisāhasramahāsāhasre vantargateṣu sarvacāturdvīpakeṣu / tuṣiteṣūpapattiṃ manuṣyeṣu ca janmaparigrahādikaṃ sarvaṃ darśayatīti / manyante /
# de lta bas na 'og min gyi gnas nyid du bcom ldan 'das mngon par sangs rgyas nas sprul pa'i skus stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi khongs su gtogs pa'i gling bzhi pa re rer yang dga' ldan du skye ba dang 'chi 'pho dang mi'i nang du tshe yongs su 'dzin pa la sogs pa thams cad ston to snyam du sems so /
tatra ca samasaṃvartanīyakarmāyattatā buddhacarkravartyutpatteḥ / sahabhāve pāratantryaṃ /
# 'di la sangs rgyas dang 'khor los sgyur ba 'byung ba ni mnyam par 'gyur ba ma yin pa'i las la rag lus pas lhan cig tu skye bar 'gyur ba gzhan gyi dbang nyid do /
ādhipatye pāratantryaṃ striyā cakravartitvādyakaraṇād iti / cakravartisaṃvartanīyasya karmaṇaḥ pumātmabhāva eva / vipākadānasāmarthyāt / / na hi strīḥ stryādiratnopabhogasamarthā / / ādiśabdena śakratvādr gṛhyate /
# dbang byed pa'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni bud med 'khor los sgyur ba la sogs pa mi byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'khor los sgyur bar 'gyur ba'i las kyi rnam par smin pa ni skyes pa'i lus kyis smin par nus te / / bud med la ni bud med rin po che la spyod pa'i mthu med pa'i phyir ro / / sogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgras ni brgya byin la sogs pa bsdu'o /
samprāptau pāratantryaṃ stryāpratyekānuttarabodhyanabhisambodhāt /
# 'thob pa'i gzhan gyi dbang ni bud med kyis rang byang chub dang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs par byang chub par mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la /
prāptir buddha-pratyekabuddhatvādhigamaḥ /
# 'thob pa ni sangs rgyas dang rang byang chub nyid 'thob pa'o /
tatra pāratantryaṃ puruṣasya prāptir na tu striyaḥ /
# de la gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni skyes pas 'thob par 'gyur gyi bud med kyis 'thob par mi 'gyur te /
tasyā hi saṃsargābhāvāt khaḍgavat / tribhūmiśāstrītvāsambhavādyathākramaṃ /
# de ni go rims bzhin du bse ru lta bur 'dre ba med pa dang sa gsum gyi ston par mi srid pa'i phyir te /
sā punaḥ sarvadhūrtajanagamyā alpaprajñatvād / anācāryakābhisambodhāyogyā ceti /
# de'ang skye bo gyon can thams cad kyi spyod yul yin pa dang shes rab chung bas slob dpon med par mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i 'os ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
samudācāre pāratantryaṃ dṛṣṭisampannasya vadhādyasamudācārāt
# kun du spyod pa'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni lta ba phun sum tshogs pa gsod pa la sogs pa kun du mi spyod la /
pṛthagjanasya ca samudācārād iti / / dṛṣṭisampanno dṛṣṭasatyaḥ /
# so so'i skye bo ni kun du spyod pa'i phyir te zhes bya ba lta ba phun sum tshogs pa ni bden pa mthong ba'o /
vadhaḥ prāṇātipātaḥ / [p.116] / ādiśabdenādattādānādayaḥ saṃgṛhyante / / te vadhādayaḥ kāyavāk-kriyāsvabhāvā dṛṣṭisampannasya na samudācaranti
# gsod pa ni srog gcod pa yin; sogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgras ni ma byin par len pa la sogs pa bsdus te / / gsod pa la sogs pa de dag ni lus dang ngag gi bya ba'i rang bzhin no /
darśanamārgeṇa vadhādi-duścaritasamutthāpakakleśaprahāṇāt pṛthagjanasya
# mthong ba'i lam nyid kyi gsod pa la sogs pa nyes par spyod pa kun nas slong ba'i nyon mongs pa spongs pa'i phyir lta ba phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa ni kun du mi spyod do /
samudācaranti tad aprahāṇāt / / tad aprahāṇaṃ punas tat pratipakṣeṇa mārgānutpannatvāt /
# so so'i skye bo ni de ma spangs pa'i phyir kun du spyod do / / de ma spangs pa yang de'i gnyen por lam ma skyes pa'i phyir ro /
evam aniṣṭādipāratantryānugatam asthānakauśalyaṃ puruṣeśvarādau / svātantryāgrāhapratipakṣaḥ /
# de ltar mi 'dod pa la sogs pa gzhan gyi dbang nyid kyi rjes su song ba / / gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa ni skyes bu dang dbang phyug la sogs pa rang dbang can du 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o /
yadi hi svatantraḥ kaścit syān na duścaritena durgatiṃ gacchet /
# gal te rang dbang can 'ga' zhig yod na ni nyes par spyad pa las ngan 'gror 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro /
evam anyatrāpi vācyaṃ //3-19//
# de bzhin du gzhan dag la yang brjod par bya'o /
{ indriyārthaḥ } / sthānāsthānārthanirdeśānantaram indriyārtho vaktavya ityata āha -
# gnas dang gnas ma yin pa'i don bstan pa'i 'og tu dbang po rnams kyi don brjod dgos pas de'i phyir dbang po ni rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis te zhes bya ba smos te /
indriyaṃ dvāviṃśatividham iti cakṣurindriyaṃ yāvad / ājñātāvindriyāvasānaṃ / / atra punar ādhipātyarthaṃ indriyārthaḥ / / kasya punaḥ kvādhipatyam ityata āha -
# mig gi dbang po nas kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po la thug gi bar du'o / / de la dbang po'i don ni dbang byed pa'i don to / / gang zhig gang la dbang byed pa de mi shes nas / / de'i phyir /
grahaṇasthānasandhānabhogaśuddhidvayārthataḥ / iti /
# 'dzin dang gnas dang rgyun mi 'chad / / spyod dang dag pa gnyis kyi phyir / / zhes bya ba gsungs te /
atra ca dvayādhipattyārthata iti yuktau kārikānukūlārtham / ādhipatyaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ /
# 'di la gnyis pa dbang byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba rigs pa las tshig le'ur byas pa dang mthun par bya ba'i phyir dbang byed pa zhes bya ba'i sgra ni mi smos par blta'o /
tasmād bhāṣyakāra āha - teṣu tadādhipatyād iti /
# de bas na bshad pa byed pas / / de dag la de dbang byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
grahaṇārtheneti / / arthaśabdo'tra prayojanavācī / / grahaṇaprayojanaṃ nimittaṃ tatrendriyam iti darśayati /
# 'dzin pa'i phyir zhes bya ba la / / phyir zhes bya ba'i sgra ni 'dir dgos pa yin par brjod de / / 'dzin pa'i dgos pa ste ched yin la /
evam anyatrāpi yathāyogaṃ vaktavyaṃ /
# de bzhin du gzhan dag la yang ci rigs par brjod par bya'o /
teṣvityarthagrahaṇādiṣu ādhipatyam ityadhikaprabhutvam ityādhipatyaṃ / hetutvam ityarthaḥ /
# de dag la zhes bya ba ni don 'dzin pa la sogs pa la'o / / dbang byed ces bya ba ni lhag par dbang bas na dbang byed pa ste rgyu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
rūpādayo dharmaparyantā rūpādiviṣayāḥ /
# gzugs la sogs pa chos la thug pa dag ni gzugs la sogs pa yul rnams te /
teṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ cakṣurādivijñānaṃ /
# de dag la 'dzin pa ni mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'o /
tatra cakṣurādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām ādhipatyaṃ / / cakṣuṣo niravaśeṣarūpaprabhedavijñānāśrayatvād rūpādīnām / adhikaprabhutvam itīndriyam ucyate / / na tu nīlarūpaṃ pītarūpādivijñānasyālambanaṃ bhavati / / evaṃ śrotrādiṣv api yathāsambhavaṃ vistareṇa vācyaṃ / / sthāne jīvitendriyasyeti /
# de la mig la sogs pa dbang po drug dbang byed pa ni mig ni gzugs kyi bye brag ma lus pa'i rnam par shes pa'i rten yin pas gzugs la sogs pa la lhag par dbang byed pas na dbang po zhes bya ste / / gzugs sngon po ni gzugs ser po la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i dmigs par mi 'gyur ro / / de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa la yang ci rigs su rgyas par brjod par bya'o /
jīvitendriyaṃ punaḥ karmavāsanāvidhaṃ vipākasantāne'sati / vicchittipratyaye pūrvpūrvakṣāṇasarūpeṣūttarottarakṣaṇeṣu / pratisandhisāmarthyaṃ / / sthāne jīvitendriyasyādhipatyam ityatraiva kāraṇam āha - tad
# gnas par bya ba la ni srog gi dbang po dbang byed de zhes bya ba la; srog gi dbang po ni sngon gyi las kyi bag chags kyis 'phangs pa'i rnam par smin pa'i rgyud la bar du gcod pa'i rkyen med na skad cig snga mas 'dra ba'i skad cig phyi ma phyi ma rnams su mtshams sbyor ba'i mthu yod pa'o / / gnas par bya ba la ni srog gi dbang po dbang byed ces bya ba la rgyu smos pa /
ādhipatyenā'maraṇād iti /
# 'di'i dbang gis mi 'chi ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ste /
amaraṇaṃ pūrvakarmākṣiptanikāyasabhāgānuvṛttiḥ / / satyapi sattvasthitikāraṇatve nāhārādīnām indriyatvaṃ /
# mi 'chi ba ni sngon gyi las kyis 'phangs rigs mthun pa'i rjes su 'jug go / / kha zas la sogs pa ni sems can gnas pa'i rgyu yin du zin kyang dbang po ma yin te /
tat sadbhāve'pyāyuṣaḥ kṣaye'vasthānā'sadbhāvāt / [p.117]
# de dag yod bzhin du tshe zad pa gnas pa med pa'i phyir ro /
rūpārūpyadhātāv asatyapi kavaḍīkārāhāre / jīvitendriyādevā'vasthānasadbhāvāt /
# gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams na kham gyis za ba'i zas rnams med kyang srog gi dbang po nyid kyis gnas pa yod pa'i phyir ro /
na ca tatra sparśādīnām avasthāna ādhipatyaṃ yujyate /
# de na reg pa la sogs pa ni gnas par dbang byed par mi rung ste /
nirodhā'saṃjñisamāpattyavasthāyām āsaṃjñike ca sparśādyabhāve'pi / sattvānāṃ sthitisambhavād iti /
# 'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i gnas dang 'du shes med pa dag la reg pa la sogs pa med kyang sems can rnams gnas par srid pa'i phyir ro /
kulasandhāne strīpuruṣendriyayor ādhipatyam iti /
# rigs 'tshob pa la pho dang mo'i dbang po gnyis dbang byed de zhes bya ba la /
putrotpattau kulāvyuparatatā vartata iti putrotpattiḥ kulasandhānaṃ / / etad eva darśayann āha - prasavādhipatyād iti /
# bu byung na rigs rgyun mi 'chad par 'gyur bas bu 'byung ba ni rigs 'tshob pa'o / / de nyid bstan pa'i phyir 'byung bar dbang byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
kāyendriyapradeśa eva kaścid ādhipatyaviśeṣāt strīpuruṣendriyākhyaṃ / pratilabhate /
# lus kyi dbang po'i phyogs 'ga' nyid de / / dbang byed pa'i bye brag gis pho dang mo'i dbang po zhes bya ba 'thob po /
yatra stīndriyaṃ puruṣendriyañcas tastatra kulavyavasthānam asti / / tad vaśena kulo na vyuparamate /
# gang na pho'i dbang po dang mo'i dbang po yod pa de na rigs rnam par gzhag pa yod de / / de'i dbang gis rigs rgyun mi 'chad do /
kāmāvacareṣv api ca deveṣu strīndriye puruṣendriye ca sati / kulavyavasthānaṃ nā'satīti /
# 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha rnams la ni pho'i dbang po dang mo'i dbang po yod pa la rigs rnam par gzhag gi med pa la ni ma yin no /
nahi gandharvādīnāṃ tatrādhipatyaṃ satyapi gandharvādau paṇḍakādiṣu / strīpuruṣendriyayor asadbhāve putraprasavasāmārthyābhāvāt /
# dri za la sogs pa la dbang byed pa med de dri za la sogs pa yod du zin kyang / / pho dang mo'i dbang po med pa ma ning la sogs pa la bu 'byung ba'i mthu med pa'i phyir ro /
āhārādīnāṃ punaḥ sattve'saṃkhyātatvāt satyapyādhipatye nendriyatvaṃ
# zas la sogs pa ni dbang byed pa yin yang sems can gyi grangs su ma gtogs pas dbang po zhes mi bya'o /
upabhoge vedanendriyāṇāṃ / / ādhipatyam ityadhikṛtaṃ /
# nye bar spyod pa la ni tshor ba'i dbang po rnams te zhes bya ba ni dbang byed ces bya ba dang sbyar te /
katham ityata āha - kuśalākuśalakarmaphalopabhogād iti /
# ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyi 'bras bu la nye bar spyod pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
vedanendriyāṇi pañca - sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ saumanasyaṃ daurmanasyam upekṣā ca
# tshor ba'i dbang po ni lnga ste / / bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms so /
tarhi kuśalākuśalakarmaphala upabhujyate anubhavātmakatvāt /
# de dag ni myong ba'i bdag nyid yin pas dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyi 'bras bu spyod kyi /
na nāmarūpasya tadādhipatyaṃ vedanāsambhārabhāvāt /
# ming dang gzugs ni de la dbang byed pa ma yin te / / tshor ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
tat sambhārabhāvaś ca vedanāpradhānatvād vipākasyeti /
# de'i rgyu'i dngos po ni tshor ba rnam par smin pa'i gtso bo yin pa'i phyir ro /
laukikaviśuddhiḥ prahāṇaṃ laukikakleśānāṃ /
# 'jig rten pa'i rnam par dag pa ni 'jig rten pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams spang pa'o /
tatra śraddhādīnām iti / śraddhā-vīrya-smṛti-samādhi-prajñā-pañcendriyāṇāṃ / / ādhipatyam iti vartate /
# de la dad pa la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni dad pa dang brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi dbang po dang lnga ste / / dbang byed ces bya bar snyegs so /
teṣām aśraddhādipratipakṣetvena laukikamārgaprabhāvitatvāt /
# de dag ni ma dad pa la sogs pa'i gnyen po yin pa dang 'jig rten pa'i lam gyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
mokṣabhāgīyaprabhāvitatvād ity apare /
# gzhan na re thar pa'i cha dang mthun pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro zhe'o /
lokottaraviśuddhāvanājñānamājñāsyāmīndriyādīnām ityādhipatyam / iti vartate /
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam par dag pa ni kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni dbang byed do zhes bya bar snyegs te /
lokottaramārgeṇa kleśānāṃ prahāṇaṃ lokottaraviśuddhiḥ /
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyis nyon mongs pa rnams spangs pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam par dag pa'o /
tatrānājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriyājñātāvīndriyāṇāṃ / trayāṇām ādhipatyaṃ /
# de la kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po gsum ni dbang byed pa ste /
teṣāṃ darśanabhāvanā'śaikṣamārgeṣu yathākramaṃ saṃgṛhītatvāt /
# de dag mthong ba dang bsgom pa dang mi slob pa'i lam du rim pa bzhin du bsdus pa'i phyir ro /
tatra śraddhādīnāṃ pañca manaḥsukhasaumanasyopekṣāṇi / cānāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa sambhavam adhikṛtyaitāni navendriyāṇi / darśanamārge'nājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyaṃ / / bhāvanāmārga ājñendriyaṃ / / aśaikṣaṃārga ajñātāvīndriyam ity ucyate / / yogācārāṇāṃ tv anyathā vyavasthānaṃ / [p.118] / anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriye dvaye daśendriyāṇi / / pūrvokteṣu navasu daurmanasyam adhikaṃ prakṣipya daśa bhavanti / / ājñātāvendriyan tu navaiva / / tatra prayogamārge nirvedhabhāgīyātmake pañcadaśasu ca / darśanamārgakṣaṇeṣu manaindriyaṃ pañca / śraddhādīnyanāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa yathāsaṃbhavaṃ / sukha-saumanasya-daurmanasyopekṣendriyāṇāṃ cānyatamād daurmanasyendriyaṃ
# de la dad pa la sogs pa lnga dang yid dang bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms rnams ni mi lcogs pa med pa la sogs pa la brten pa'i bye brag gis ci rigs pa'i dbang du byas te / / dbang po dgu ni mthong ba'i lam la ni kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po'o / / bsgom pa'i lam la ni kun shes pa'i dbang po'o / / mi slob pa'i lam la ni kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o / / rnal 'byor pa rnams ni gzhan du rnam par 'jog ste / / kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa'i dbang po gnyis la ni dbang po bcu ste / / sngar smos pa dgu'i nang du yid mi bde ba bsnan na bcur 'gyur ro / / kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po la ni dgu nyid do / / de la nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i bdag nyid sbyor ba'i lam dang mthong ba'i lam skad cig bco lnga dag la ni yid kyi dbang po dang dad pa la sogs pa lnga dang mi lcogs pa med pa la sogs pa la brten pa'i bye brag gis ci rigs par bde ba dang yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms kyi dbang po rnams las gang yang rung ba'o /
punaḥ prayogakāle nirvedhabhāgīyapṛṣṭhenottaravimokṣaspṛhāsaṅgṛhītaṃ / veditavyaṃ / / tadetat saṃbhavato daśavidham indriyaṃ /
# yid mi bde ba'i dbang po ni sbyor ba'i dus na nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i 'og tu thar pa mchog 'dod pas bsdus par rig par bya'o / / dbang po 'di bcu ni ci rigs par sbyar bar bya ste /
anājñātam evājñātuṃ pravṛttatvād anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyam / ucyate /
# sngon kun mi shes pa'i de kho na kun shes par bya ba'i phyir zhugs pas mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o /
tadeva daśavidham indriyaṃ ṣoḍaśadarśanamārgakṣaṇādyāvad vajropamaḥ / samādhir ityetasmin śaikṣamārgam ājñendriyam ity ucyate
# mthong ba'i lam skad cig ma bcu drug nas rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi bar du slob pa'i lam de la dbang po rnam pa bcu po de nyid kun shes pa'i dbang po zhes bya ba ste /
apūrvājñātājñeyābhāvāt /
# sngon mi shes pa shes par byar med pa'i phyir ro /
aśaikṣamārge daurmanasyendriyavyatiriktāni / śiṣṭānyājñātāvīndriyākhyāṃ pratilabhante /
# mi slob pa'i lam la yid mi bde ba'i dbang po ma gtogs par lhag ma rnams kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po'i ming 'thob po /
ājñātāvīndriyam iti ājñātāvīndriyam ucyate /
# kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po yin pas kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o /
evam indriyakauśalasya yaḥ puruṣanārāyaṇeśvarādiṣv adhipatigrāhaḥ sa / vyāvartate // / { adhyārthaḥ } / indriyārthānantaram adhvatrayo vaktavya ityata āha -
# de ltar na dbang po la mkhas pa ni skyes bu dang mthu bo che dang sred med kyi bu la sogs pa la dbang por 'dzin pa gang yin pa de ldog par 'gyur ro / / dbang po'i don gyi 'og tu dus gsum gyi don brjod dgos pas / / de'i phyir /
phalahetūpayogārthanopayogāt tathā'paraṃ // iti /
# 'bras bu rgyu rnams spyad zin dang / / de bzhin ma spyad gzhan yin no / / zhes bya ba smos te /
tatra janmakāraṇaṃ hetuḥ / / phalaṃ janamasaṃgṛhītaṃ / / phaladānaṃ hetor upayogaḥ /
# de la rgyu ni skye bar byed pa'i rgyu'o / / 'bras bu ni tshes pa sdus pa'o / / rgyu spyad zin pa ni 'bras bu phyung zin pa'o /
phalasyopāyogo'nubhūtasya parikṣayaḥ / / evam prakāraścātīto hetus tatphalaṃ cetyataḥ phalasya
# 'bras bu spyad zin pa ni myong nas yongs su zad pa ste / / rnam pa de lta bu'i rgyu dang de'i 'bras bu ni 'das pa'o /
taddhetoścopayogārthenānīto'dhvā /
# de'i phyir 'bras bu dang de'i rgyu spyad zin pa'i phyir 'das pa'i dus so /
tenaiva prakāreṇa phalasya hetoścā'nupayogārthenā'nāgato'dhvā /
# rnam pa 'di nyid kyi 'bras bu dang rgyu ma spyad pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i dus so /
vartamānaḥ punar adhvā vartamānaṃ janma / / hetordattaphalatvād hetūpayogārthena tatphalañca vartamānaṃ
# da ltar byung ba'i dus ni da ltar gyi tshe'i rgyus 'bras bu byin pa'i phyir rgyu spyad pa'i don dang de'i 'bras bu ni da ltar gyi tshe rjes su 'brang ba nyid de /
janmā'nuvartata eveti phalā'nuyogārthena ca veditavyaḥ /
# 'bras bu ma spyad pa'i phyir da ltar byung ba'i dus su rig par bya'o /
bhāvānāñca pratikṣaṇaṃ hetuphalabhāvatvena kṣaṇatvam / adhikṛtyā'dhvavyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# dngos po rnams kyi skad cig so so ni rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos po yin pas skad cig nyid kyi dbang du byas te dus rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
tatra hetūpayogaḥ svaphalasyotpādānāt /
# de la rgyu spyad zin pa ni rang gi 'bras bu bskyed pa'i phyir ro /
phalopayogaḥ phalasya janmānantaravināśāt / / evaṃ phalahetūpayogārthenātīto'dhvā phalahetvor / anupayogārthenānāgato'rdhveti prakṛtaṃ / / kāryānutpādād anutpannasya ca vināśābhāvāt phalahetvor anupayogo
# 'bras bu spyad zin pa ni 'bras bu skyes ma thag tu 'jig pa'i phyir ro / / de ltar 'bras bu dang rgyu ma spyad pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i dus te / / dgos pa ma bskyed pa dang ma skyes pa la zhig pa med pa'i phyir 'bras bu dang rgyu ma spyad par rig par bya'o /
veditavyaḥ / [p.119] / hetūpayogaphalānupayogārtheneti kāryotpādanād hetūpayogaḥ / / kāryā'vināśātphalā'nupayogaḥ / / evam adhvakuśalasya nityātmeti grāho vyāvartate / / adhavyatiriktasyānyasyā'nupalabdhatvāt //3-20// / { catussatyārthaḥ } / adhvatrayārthānantaraṃ catuḥsatyārtho vaktavya ityata āha - / vedanāsanimittārthatan nimittaprapattitaḥ / / iti vistaraḥ / / vedanā duḥkhārtha iti loke rūḍhaṃ /
# rgyu spyad la 'bras bu ma spyad pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni dgos pa bskyed pa'i phyir rgyu spyad pa zhes bya'o / / dgos pa ma zhig pa'i phyir 'bras bu ma spyad pa zhes bya'o / / de ltar dus la mkhas pa ni dus ma gtogs par gzhan mi dmigs pa'i phyir bdag rtag par 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur ro / / dus gsum gyi don gyi 'og tu bden pa bzhi'i don brjod dgos pas / / de'i phyir / / tshor ba rgyu dang bcas pa'i don / / de yi rgyu ni sgrub pa yin / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / tshor ba ni sdug bsngal gyi don to zhes 'jig rten na grags so / / bstan bcos las kyang gang ci tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'dir sdug bsngal lo zhe'o /
śāstre ca yat kiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti vacanāt / / satyavyavasthāyāṃ sarvā sāsravā sanimittā sukhā duḥkhā sukhāduḥkhā
# bden pa rnam par gzhag pa ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba rgyu dang bcas pa thams cad sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i don yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir bshad pa byed pas kyang /
ca vedanā duḥkhasatyārtha iti pradarśayan bhāṣyakāra āha - tatra / duḥkhasatyaṃ vedanāsanimittārtheneti / / sarvā vedanā duḥkham iti kuta etat ?
# de la sdug bsngal gyi bden pa ni tshor ba rgyu dang bcas pa'i don zhes bya ba smos so / / tshor ba thams cad sdug bsngal yin par ci mngon zhe na /
ata āha - yatkiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti kṛtveti / / sā ca vedanā duḥkha duḥkhatāvipariṇāmaduḥkhatā-saṃskāraduḥkhatābhir / yathāsambhavaṃ duḥkhā / / saṃskāraduḥkhatayaiva vā duḥkhā / / vedanānimittaṃ panar vedanāsthānīyā dharmā veditavyā iti / / sukhaduḥkhā'duḥkhāsukhavedanīyā dharmā vedanāsthānāni /
# de'i phyir gang ci tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'dir sdug bsngal lo zhes bya ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / tshor ba de dag kyang sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid dang 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid dang 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid rnams su ji ltar mthun du sbyar te / / sdug bsngal ba'o / / yang na 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyi sdug bsngal ba'o / / tshor ba'i rgyu ni tshor ba'i gnas kyi chos rnams su rig par bya'o zhes bya ba la / / bde ba dang sdug bsngal ba dang sdug bsngal ba yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin myong bar 'gyur ba'i chos rnams ni tshor ba'i gnas rnams so /
evaṃ pañcaskandhā duḥkhasatyaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ /
# de ltar phung po lnga po dag ni sdug bsngal gyi bden par bstan pa yin no /
tan nimitta pratipattitaḥ samudayasatyam iti /
# de'i rgyu ni sgrub pa yin / / kun 'byung ba'i bden pa ste zhes bya ba la /
tac chabdena duḥkhasatyam abhisambadhyate /
# de'i zhes bya ba'i sgra ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa dang sbyar ro /
duḥkhaṃ yayā pratipattyā janyate sā pratipattiḥ samudayasatyaṃ /
# sgrub pa gang gis sdug bsngal skyed pa ni bsgrub pa ste kun 'byung ba'o /
sā punar vedanāyāṃ vedanāsthāniyeṣu ca dharmeṣu tṛṣṇāhetupūrvikā / kāyavāṅmanaḥ pracalasvarūpā / / saṃkṣepataś ca bhavasamudbhavikaṃ karmasamudaya satyam ity uktam bhavati /
# de yang tshor ba dang tshor ba'i gnas kyi chos rnams la sred pa'i rgyu sngon du song ba'i lus dang ngag dang yid rab tu gyo ba'i ngo bo nyid do / / mdor na yang srid pa kun nas slong ba'i las ni kun 'byung bar bstan pa yin no /
tayoḥ śamārthena nirodhasatyam iti /
# de gnyis zhi ba'i phyir 'gog pa'i bden pa'o zhes bya ba la /
tayor iti duḥkhasamudayasatyayoḥ /
# de gnyis zhes bya ba ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i bden pa gnyis so /
śamārthenety utpādanārthena /
# zhi ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni mi skye ba'i phyir ro /
evañca sahetukaduḥKhānutpādalakṣaṇatvān nirodho dvividha uktaḥ
# de ltar rgyu dang bcas pa'i sdug bsngal mi skye ba'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir 'gog pa la rnam pa gnyis su bstan pa yin te /
samudayaśamārthena sopadhiśeṣaḥ duḥkhopaśamārthena nirupādhiśeṣa iti
# kun 'byung ba zhi ba'i phyir phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa'o / / sdug bsngal zhi ba'i phyir phung po'i lhag ma med pa'o /
tayor evādhikṛtayor duḥkhasamudayayoḥ pratipakṣārthena / duḥkhasamudayanirodhagāminī pratipan mārgasatyaṃ /
# de nyid kyi dbang du byas nas sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba gnyis kyi gnyen po'i phyir sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba 'gog par 'gyur ba'i lam ni lam gyi bden pa'o /
tadevaṃ satyakuśalasya saṅkleśavyavadānamātrāvagatatvāt tadanyaḥ / saṅkleśavyavadānagraho vyāvartate tasyābhāvād iti //3-21// / { yānatrayā'rthaḥ } [p.120]
# de ltar bden pa la mkhas pa ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba tsam rtogs nas de dag las gzhan pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur te / / de med pa'i phyir ro /
satyārthānantaraṃ yānatrayārthaṃ pratipādyata ityata āha - / guṇadoṣā'vikalpena jñānena / iti vistaraḥ /
# bden pa rnams kyi don gyi 'og tu theg pa gsum gyi don bstan par bya ste / / de'i phyir / / yon tan skyon dang rnam mi rtog / / shes pas gzhan las bdag gis ni / / nges par 'byung phyir gzhan zhes bya / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
jñānaśabda ubhayatra sambadhyate / / guṇadoṣajñānenā'vikalpajñānena ceti /
# shes pa zhes bya ba'i sgra ni yon tan dang skyon shes pa dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes zhes bya ba gnyis ka dang sbyar bar bya'o /
athavā'ntare vikalpaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ / / tatra guṇadoṣajñānena parataḥ svayañceti ata evāha - vṛttau yathāyogam  iti /
# yang na bar du rnam par rtog / / ces bya ba'i sgra zhig ma smos par blta bar bya'o / / de la yon tan dang skyon shes pa ni gzhan las dang bdag gis zhes phye ste brjod par bya'o / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi ni bdag nyid kyis te / / de bas na 'grel pa las ci rigs su sbyar bar bya'o zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñāneneti /
# de la mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba la yon tan dang skyon du shes zhes bya ba la /
nirvāṇaśabdenātra mārganirodhau saṅgṛhītau yathā praśāntaśabdaḥ /
# mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya ba'i sgra ni 'dir lam dang 'gog par gzung ste / / dper na rab tu zhi ba zhes bya ba'i sgra bzhin no /
tatra nirodhe śāntādyākāraiḥ mārge nairyāṇikādyākārair jñānaṃ / nirvāṇe guṇajñānaṃ /
# de la 'gog pa la ni zhi ba'i rnam pa la sogs pa dang lam la nges par 'byin pa'i rnam pa la sogs par shes pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa la yon tan du shes pa'o /
saṃsāro'pi duḥkhasamudayātmakaḥ /
# 'khor ba ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i bdag nyid de /
tatrā'py anityaduḥkhādyākāraiḥ samudayapratyayādyākāraiś ca jñānaṃ / saṃsāre doṣajñānaṃ /
# de yang mi rtag pa dag sdug bsngal ba'i rnam pa la sogs pa dang kun 'byung ba dang rkyen gyi rnam pa la sogs par shes pa ni 'khor ba la skyon du shes pa'o /
parataḥ śrutveti buddhabodhisattvādibhyo nirvāṇasaṃsārayor / guṇānyathokān doṣāṃś ca śrutveti /
# gzhan las thos zhes bya ba ni sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' la sogs pa las mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba gnyis kyi yon tan dang skyon ji skad du smos pa thos pa'o /
niryāṇārtheneti saṃsāranirgamārthena /
# nges par 'byung ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'khor ba las byung ba'i phyir ro /
śrāvakayānam iti paradghoṣasaṃniśrayeṇa niryāṇāt śrāvakāyanm iti
# nyan thos kyi theg pa zhes bya ba ni gzhan gyi sgra la brten nas nges par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaṃ darśayati /
# nyan thos kyi theg pa zhes bya bas ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa las bye brag tu ston to /
tenaiveti nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñānena svayam aśrutvā parato / buddhabodhasattvebhyo niryāṇārthena pratyekabuddhayānaṃ /
# de nyid kyis zhes bya ba ni mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba gnyis la yon tan dang skyon du shes nas sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' gzhan las ma thos par bdag gis nges par 'byung ba'i phyir rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'o /
svayam aśrutveti śrāvakayānād viśeṣaṇaṃ /
# gzhan las ma thos par bdag gis shes par bya ba ni nyan thos kyi theg pa las bye brag tu bstan to /
avikalpena jñāneneti saṃsāranirvāṇayor anabhilāpyadharmatāprativedhād / avikalpaṃ jñānaṃ /
# rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis zhes bya ba ni 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i chos gnyis brjod du med par rtogs pa'i phyir rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes te /
svayam eva parato'śrutvā niryāṇārthena mahāyānaṃ /
# gzhan las ma thos par bdag nyid kyis nges par 'byung ba'i phyir theg pa chen po'i /
atra hi jñāneneti pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaḥ /
# 'dir ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa las ye shes kyis bye brag tu byas so /
anye tvāhuḥ - pudgalanairātmyaviṣayeṇa guṇadoṣā'vikalpena jñānena / parataḥ śrutvā niryāṇaṃ śrāvakayānaṃ /
# gzhan dag na re gzhan las thos nas gang zag la bdag med pa'i yul can yon tan dang skyon du rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis nges par 'byung ba ni nyan thos kyi theg pa'o /
śravaṇanirapekṣasya svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ pratyekabuddhayānaṃ /
# mnyam pa la mi ltos par bdag nyid kyis nges par 'byung ba ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'o /
dharmanairātmyaviṣayeṇā'pratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaprāpakenā'vikalpena jñānena / svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ mahāyānam ucyate / / etad vyākhyānaṃ bhāṣyeṇa virudhyate /
# mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa thob par byed pa chos la bdag med pa'i yul can rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi bdag nyid kyis nges par 'byung ba ni theg pa chen po zhes bya'o / / rnam par bshad pa 'di ni 'grel pa dang 'gal lo /
evaṃ yānatrayakuśalasya yogamātradarśanād ātmā yogīti grāho / vyāvartate // [p.121] / [ saṃskṛtā'saṃskṛtārthaḥ } / idānīṃ saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtārthaṃ pratipādayann āha - / saprajñaptisahetukāt / / nimittātpraśamāt sārthāt paścimaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ // iti / / kim idaṃ paścimaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ ? / ityata āha - saṃskṛtā'saṃskṛtam iti sarvapaścād udiṣṭatvāt /
# de ltar theg pa gsum la mkhas pa ni rnal 'byor tsam du zad par mthong bas bdag rnal 'byor can du 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur ro / / nga ni 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi don bstan pa'i phyir / / btags bcas rgyur bcas rgyu mtshan dang / / rab tu zhi ba don bcas ni / / tha ma nyid du bshad pa yin / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / tha mar bshad pa de gang zhe na / / de'i phyir / / 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas so zhes bya ba smos te /
tatra saṃskṛtaṃ saprajñaptikāt sahetukāc ca nimittāt asaṃskṛtaṃ punaḥ
# thams cad kyi tha mar bshad pa'i phyir ro / / de la 'dus byas ni btags pa dang bcas shing rgyu dang bcas pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis rnam par gzhag go /
sārthāt praśamād vyavasthāpitaṃ /
# 'dus ma byas ni don dang bcas pa'i rab tu zhi bas rnam par gzhag go /
prajñaptihetunimittaṃ punar ajñānāt / / tat pradarśayann āha - tatra saprajñaptir nāmakāyādaya iti /
# btags pa dang rgyu dang rgyu mtshan yang mi shes nas de bstan par bya ba'i phyir / / de la btags pa ni ming gi tshogs la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba smos so /
prajñapyete svabhāvaviśeṣau bhāvānāṃ nāmapadakāyābhyām iti / nāmapadakayau prajñaptiḥ /
# ming dang tshig gi tshogs kyi dngos po dag gi ngo bo nyid dang khyad par gnyis btags pas na ming dang tshig gi tshogs gnyis ni btags pa'o /
vyañjanakāyas tu tad ubhayābhivyañjakatvāt prajñaptiḥ /
# yi ge'i tshogs ni de gnyi ga gsal bar byed pa'i phyir btags pa'o /
hetuḥ punar bījasaṅgṛhītam ālayavijñānam iti / / tac ca sarvasāsravadharmavāsanānvitam adattaphalaṃ / samudayasatyasaṅgṛhītaṃ / / ata eva dattaphalād vyavacchedārthaṃ bījasaṅgṛhītam ityāha /
# rgyu ni sa bon du bsdus pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o zhes bya ba de yang zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad kyi bag chags kyi rjes su song ba 'bras bu ma byin pa kun 'byung ba'i bden par bsdus pa nyid de / / 'bras bu byin pa las rnam par dbye ba'i phyir / / sa bon du bsdus pa zhes bya ba smos so /
nimittaṃ pratiṣṭhādehabhogasaṅgṛhītam ityālayavijñānam iti prakṛtaṃ /
# rgyu mtshan ni gnas dang lus dang longs spyod du bsdus pa zhes bya ba ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
pravṛttivijñānasaṅgṛhītaśca manadugrahavikalpa iti / / tatra pratiṣṭhā bhājanalokaḥ / / tadābhāsam ālayavijñānaṃ /
# 'jug pa ni rnam par shes par bsdus pa yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog par bsdus pa'o zhes bya ba de la gnas ni snod kyi 'jig rten te / / der snang ba'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o /
pratiṣṭhātmanā saṅgṛhītam iti pratiṣṭhāsaṅgṛhītaṃ /
# gnas kyi bdag nyid du bsdus pas na gnas su bsdus pa'o /
dehaḥ sendriyaṃ śarīraṃ tadābhāsam ālayavijñānaṃ dehasaṅgṛhītaṃ
# lus su snang ba'i rang bzhin la lus su bsdus pa zhes bya'o / / lus ni dbang po dang bcas pa'i khog pa lus der snang ba'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o /
dehātmanopagatam ityarthaḥ / [p.122]
# lus su bsdus pa ni lus kyi bdag nyid dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
bhogasaṅgṛhītatamedevottaram uktaṃ /
# longs spyod du bsdus pa ni gong du bshad pa de nyid de /
tad dvayaṃ śeṣāṇi vijñānānyadhipativastutvena bhuñjata iti bhogaḥ /
# de gnyis la yang rnam par shes pa gzhan dag dbang byed pa'i dngos por longs spyod pas na longs spyod do /
athavā annapānādiko'rtho bhujyata iti bhogaḥ /
# yang na bza' ba dang btung ba la sogs pa'i don la longs spyod pas na longs spyod de /
tan nirbhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ bhogasaṅgṛhītaṃ /
# der snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni longs spyod du bsdus pa'o /
etat saprajñapti sahetukaṃ nimittaṃ sasamprayogaṃ / paratantrasvabhāvasaṅgṛhītatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# btags pa dang bcas shing rgyu dang bcas pa'i rgyu mtshan de ni mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo bsdus pa'i phyir 'dus byas su rig par bya'o /
samprayogaścaittāḥ / / tat saṃskṛtaṃ na kevalaṃ tadeveti darśayati / / kasya punas tannimittaṃ ?
# mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa ni sems las byung ba ste / / 'dus byas de ni de nyid 'ba' zhig ma yin par bstan to / / de yang gang gi rgyu mtshan zhe na /
nāmakāyādīnāṃ / / teṣāṃ tat svabhāvaviśeṣasaṃsūcakatvāt tadanusāreṇa ca
# ming gi tshogs la sogs pa'i rgyu mtshan te / / de ni de dag gi ngo bo nyid dang khyad par rjod par byed pa'i phyir ro /
svabhāvaviśeṣābhiniveśināṃ cittacaittānāṃ manaudgrahavikalpākhyānāṃ / nimittaṃ /
# de dag gi rjes su 'brang bas rang bzhen dang bye brag la mngon par zhen pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog pa zhes bya ba rnams kyi rgyu mtshan yang yin no /
manaudgrahavikalpaścālayavijñānasya nimittaṃ /
# kha cig na re yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog pa yang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i rgyu mtshan te /
tasmin vāsanapoṣaṇatvād ityeke /
# de la bag chags brtas par byed pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
anye tu manyante - svabhāvaviśeṣaprajñāpanāt prajñapter nimittaṃ / saṃjñāṃ nimittodgrahaṇātmiketi vacanāt /
# gzhan dag ni rang bzhin bye brag tu 'dogs pas na 'dogs pa'i mtshan ma ni 'du shes te / / mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyi phyir ro /
pratiṣṭhādehabhogasaṃgṛhītam ālayavijñānaṃ nidānanimittaṃ / vāsanāpoṣaṇatvāt /
# gnas dang lus dang longs spyod du bsdus pa kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni bag chags brtas par byed pa'i phyir gzhi'i rgyu mtshan no /
ālambananimittañca mana udgrahavikalpā ālambananimittīkaraṇārthena / / ālambanālambana nimittaṃ cobhayathā nimittīkaraṇād iti /
# yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog pa rnams ni dmigs pa mtshan mar byed pa'i phyir dmigs pa'i rgyu mtshan yang yin la / / gnyi ga mtshan mar byed pa'i phyir dmigs pa dang dmigs par byed pa'i rgyu mtshan yang yin no snyam du sems so /
tatra mano yan nityaṃ manyanākāram iti /
# de la yid la gang rtag ru rlom sems pa'i rnam pa'o zhes bya ba la /
ahaṃ mameti yan nityaṃ manyate tanmata ucyate /
# bdag gam bdag gi zhes bya ba gang rtag par rlom sems pa de ni yid ces bya ste /
tac ca samprayuktam ātmamohātmadṛṣṭyātmasnehātmamānaiḥ pañcabhiś ca / sarvatragair vedanāsaṃjñācetanāsparśamanaskārair iti /
# de ni bdag tu rmongs pa dang bdag tu lta ba dang bdag la chags pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang kun du 'gro ba lnga po tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa dang reg pa dang yid la byed pa dag dang mtshungs par ldan no /
udgrahaḥ pañca vijñānakāyā iti viṣayasvarūpagrahaṇalakṣaṇatvāt
# 'dzin pa ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga po zhes bya ba ni yul gyi rang bzhin gyi ngo bo 'dzin pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir ro /
svasaṃvedyā ityākhyātum aśakyatvād udgraha ucyate /
# rang rig pa yin pas brjod mi nus pa'i phyir 'dzin pa zhes bya'o /
vikalpo manovijñānaṃ / / tasya dharmasvasāmānyalakṣaṇavikalpakatvād iti /
# rnam par rtog pa ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa ste / / de ni chos rnams kyi rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid la rnam par rtog pa can gyi phyir ro /
etatsarvaṃ saprajñaptisahetukaṃ nimittaṃ karmakleśābhyām / abhisaṃskṛtatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ /
# btags pa dang bcas shing rgyu dang bcas pa'i rgyu mtshan 'di las nyon mongs pa gnyis kyis mngon par 'dus byas pa'i phyir 'dus byas so /
asaṃskṛtaṃ punaḥ praśamaś ca nirodhaḥ praśamārthaś ca tathateti yuktaṃ
# 'dus ma byas ni rab tu zhi ba'i 'gog pa dang rab tu zhi ba'i don de bzhin nyid de bzhin nyid de zhes bya ba la /
nirodhasya praśamasvarūpatvaṃ sannimittaduḥkhapraśamalakṣaṇāt /
# rgyu dang bcas pa'i sdug bsngal rab tu zhi ba'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir 'gog pa ni rab tu zhi ba'i bar rung na /
kathaṃ tathatā praśamārtham ucyata iti ? / praśamasyārtha iti kṛtvā /
# de bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu zhi ba'i don ces bya zhe na / / rab tu zhi ba'i don yin pa'i phyir ro /
nanu ca nirodhena tathatayā na kaścit sambandho'sti kathaṃ praśamārthatvaṃ
# 'gog pa dang de bzhin nyid gnyis 'brel pa ci yang med pa snyam na / / ji ltar rab tu zhi ba'i don zhes bya zhe na /
tathatāyā mārgālambanatvāt /
# de bzhin nyid ni lam gyi dmigs pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
mārgasya punaḥ kathaṃ praśamatvaṃ ? / tena praśamanāt /
# ji ltar na lam yang rab tu zhi ba nyid ces bya zhe na / / des rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
nirvāṇaṃ praśamaḥ praśamanāt /
# rab tu zhi ba'i phyir mya ngan las 'das pa ni rab tu zhi ba'o /
anena ca praśamanāt praśamo mārgaḥ /
# 'dis rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i phyir lam yang rab tu zhi ba'o /
evaṃ vigrahabhedād ekābhidhānena nirvāṇamārgayor grahaṇaṃ praśama iti /
# de ltar na tshig rnam par sbyar ba tha dad pa'i phyir brjod pa gcig gis mya ngan las 'das pa dang lam gnyi ga rab tu zhi ba zhes bya bar bzung ngo /
mārgasatyaṃ punaḥ kiṃ saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtaṃ ? / saṃskṛtaṃ utpādyatvāt /
# ci lam gyi bden pa 'dus byas sam 'on te 'dus ma byas she na / / bskyed par bya ba yin pas 'dus byas so /
yadi karmakleśābhyām anabhisaṃskṛtād asaṃskṛtena ca prabhāvitād / asaṃskṛtam iti brūyān na doṣaḥ syād iti /
# gal te las dang nyon mongs pas mngon par 'dus ma byas pa dang 'dus ma byas kyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir 'dus ma byas zhes brjod na nyes pa med do /
ityetenārthena skandhādiṣu jñānaṃ skandhādikauśalyaṃ veditavyam iti / [p.123]
# de ltar don 'dis phung po la sogs pa shes pa ni phung po la sogs pa la mkhas par rig par bya'o zhes bya ba ni /
anekatvābhisaṃkṣepaparicchedārtha āditaḥ /
# thog ma du ma nyid dang ni / / bsdus dang yongs su phye ba'i don /
iti vistareṇa sarvatra vācyaṃ //3-22// / { tattvapiṇḍārthaḥ } / tattvasya piṇḍārthaḥ / / samāsato dvividhaṃ tattvaṃ / / vistareṇa daśavidham uktaṃ / / ataḥ samāsato dvividham ityāha - ādarśatattvaṃ dṛśyatattvañca /
# zhes bya ba ste / / rgyas par thams cad la brjod par bya'o / / de kho na'i don bsdus pa ni mdor bsdu na de kho na rnam pa gnyis so / / rgyas par ni rnam pa bcur bshad do / / de bas na mdor bsdu na rnam pa gnyis te zhes bya ba smos so / / rnam pa gnyis po ji lta bu zhe na / / me long lta bu'i de kho na dang snang ba'i de kho na'o zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra mūlatattvam ādarśatattvaṃ /
# de la rtsa ba'i de kho na de ni me long lta bu'i de kho na ste /
tat punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ / / kim arthaṃ punas tad ādarśatattvam ityucyate ? / śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇatattvādīnāṃ tatra darśanāt /
# de yang ngo bo nyid gsum mo / / ci'i phyir de la me long lta bu'i de kho na zhes bya zhe na / / mtshan nyid kyi de kho na la sogs pa lhag ma rnams der snang ba'i phyir ro /
dṛśyatattvaṃ yat lakṣaṇatattvādikaṃ pūrvanirdiṣṭaṃ navavidhaṃ / / kimarthaṃ tad dṛṣyatattvam ity ucyate ?
# snang ba'i de kho na ni mtshan nyid kyi de kho na la sogs pa sngar bstan pa rnam pa dgu gang yin pa'o / / ci'i phyir de dag snang ba'i de kho na zhes bya zhe na /
tasya mūlatattve darśanāt nirabhimānadṛśyatattvaṃ lakṣaṇatattvaṃ /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na la snang ba'i phyir ro / / nga rgyal med pa snang ba'i de kho na ni mtshan nyid kyi de kho na ste /
tena hi nirabhimāno bhavati / / pudgaladharmayor grāhyagrāhakayor bhāvābhāvayoś / cā'samāropānapavādaviparyāsa dṛśyatattvam aviparyāsalakṣaṇaṃ /
# gang zag dang chos dang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang dngos po dang dngos po med pa la sgro mi 'dogs pa dang skur pa mi 'debs pa'i phyir des nga rgyal med par 'gyur ro / / phyin ci log gi gnyen po snang ba'i de kho na ni phyin ci ma log pa'i mtshan nyid de /
taddhi nityādiviparyāsapratipakṣabhūtaṃ /
# de ni rtag pa la sogs par phyin ci log gi gnyen por gyur pa'o /
śrāvakayānaniryāṇadṛśyatattvaṃ phalahetumayaṃ tattvaṃ /
# nyan thos kyi theg pas nges par 'byung ba snang ba'i de kho na ni 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na ste /
caturāryasatya prativedhabhāvanayā śrāvakaniryāṇaṃ /
# 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi rab tu rtogs shing bsgoms pas nyan thos nges par 'byung ngo /
mahāyānaniryāṇadrśyatattvaṃ sūkṣmaudārikatattvaṃ /
# theg pa chen pos nges par 'byung ba snang ba'i de kho na ni phra ba dang rags pa'i de kho na ste /
audārikena saṃvṛtisatyena sattvaparipācanāt sūkṣmeṇa paramārthasatyena / vimocanāt mahāyānena niryāti /
# rags pa kun rdzob kyi bden pas sems can rnams yongs su smin par byed pa dang phra ba don dam pa'i bden pas rnam par grol bar byed pa'i phyir theg pa chen pos nges par 'byung ba'o /
paravādinigrahadṛśyatattvaṃ prasiddhatattvaṃ /
# phas kyi rgol ba tshar gcod pa snang ba'i de kho na ni grags pa'i de kho na'o /
katham ityata āha - dṛṣṭānasanniśrayeṇa yuktyā nigrahād iti /
# ji lta zhe na / / de'i phyir / / dpe la brten te rigs pas tshar gcod pa'i phyir zhes bya ba smos te /
nigrahe lokaprasiddho dṛṣṭāntaḥ / / yuktiprasiddhaśabdāśrayād yuktiḥ /
# tshar gcod pa la dpe ni 'jig rten du grags pa'o / / rigs pa ni rigs pas rab tu grub pa la brten pa'o /
mahāyānābhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ viśuddhijñānagocaratattvaṃ /
# theg pa chen po mngon par brjod pa snang ba'i de kho na ni rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi de kho na ste /
[p.124] / taddhi kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarād anyasyābhidyotaka āgamaḥ / / tat punar mahāyānaṃ /
# des ni nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi lung gzhan mngon par brjod pa ste / / de ni theg pa chen po'o /
sarvākārajñeyapraveśadṛśyatattvaṃ saṃgrahatattvaṃ / / tac ca pañca vastūni tatra sarvajñeyānupraveśāt / / avitathatā'bhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ prabhedatattvaṃ / / tena hi bhāvānāmavitathatathatā'nanyatathatayor abhidyotanāt / / ātmagrāhavastusarvābhisandhipraveśadṛśyatattvañceti kauśalayatattvaṃ / / tena hy ātmagrāhavastu sarvābhiprāyamukhena praviśatīti yathā pūrvam / uktaṃ daśabhir abhiprāyaiḥ skandhādiṣv ātmagrāhapravṛttitvaṃ / / tattvapiṇḍārthavacanaṃ sukhadhāraṇārtham arthād grantham ākarṣatīti / / asammohāparikhedārthañca paridṛṣṭādhikāraparyantasya hi na parikheda / upajñāyate nāpi sammoho yathoddeśanirdeśādhigamād utapdyate / / uktaṃ tattvaṃ // / // āgamānusāriṇyāṃ madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkāyām ācāryabhadantasthi / ramatyuparacitāyāṃ tattvaparicchedastṛtīyaḥ samāptaḥ // / %	pratipakṣabhāvanā'vasthāphalaparicchedaścaturthaḥ / { pratipakṣabhāvanā } [p.125] / tattvapratipādanānantaraṃ pratipakṣabhāvanā vaktavyā tatrā'vasthā / phalaprāptiś ca /
# shes bya'i rnam pa thams cad la 'jug pa snang ba'i de kho na la bsdu ba'i de kho na dngos po lnga ste / / de ni shes par bya ba thams cad la 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / ma nor ba de bzhin nyid mngon par brjod pa snang ba'i de kho na ni rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na ste / / des dngos po rnams kyi ma nor ba de bzhin nyid dang gzhan ma yin pa de bzhin nyid mngon par brjod pa'i phyir ro / / bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gzhi la dgongs pa thams cad rtogs par snang ba'i de kho na zhes bya ba ni mkhas pa'i de kho na ste / / des bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gzhi la dgongs pa thams cad kyi sgo nas rtogs te / / bsam pa bcu po dag gis phung po la sogs pa la bdag tu 'dzin pa 'jug par sngar ji skad du bstan pa'o / / de kho na'i don bsdus pa smos pa ni bde blag tu 'dzin pa'i phyir te / / don gyis tshig 'dren pa'i phyir ro / / rmongs pa med pa dang yongs su skyo ba yang med par bya ba'i phyir te / / skabs kyi mgo mjug yongs su mthong na yongs su skyo ba mi skye'o / / ji ltar bstan pa bzhin du bshad pa rtogs pas rmongs pa yang mi 'byung ngo / / de kho na bshad zin to / / bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa las de kho na'i le'ur bcad pa ste gsum pa'i 'grel bshad do / / de kho na bshad pa'i 'og tu gnyen po bsgom pa dang de'i gnas dang 'bras bu thob pa bshad dgos te /
atas tatpratipādanārthaṃ caturthaparicchedārambhaḥ /
# de bas na de bstan pa'i phyir le'ur bcad pa bzhi pa brtsams so /
tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt pratipakṣabhāvanāpratibaddhatvāc ca tad / avasthāphalaprāptyor uddeśaḥ /
# de kho na'i 'og tu bstan pa dang gnyen po bsgom pa la rag lus pa'i phyir de'i gnas dang 'bras bu thob pa gnyis kyang smos so /
sūtre pratipakaṣatvena bodhipakṣo'numata iti pradarśanārtham āha - / pratipakṣabhāvanā bodhipakṣyabhāveneti / / te hi yathoktāvaraṇavipakṣaprahāṇāya bhāvyamānaḥ prabhavantīti / pratipakṣā ucyante /
# bstan pa'i mdor byas pa las gnyen po ni byang chub kyi phyogs su bzhed par bstan pa'i phyir / / gnyen po bsgom pa ni byang chub kyi phyogs bsgom pa ste zhes bya ba smos so / / de dag bsgoms na mi mthun pa'i phyogs sgrib pa ji skad bstan pa rnams spang bar bya ba la mthu yod par 'gyur bas gnyen po rnams zhes bya'o / / de rnams kyang sum cu rtsa bdun te /
te punaḥ saptatriṃśat - catvāri smṛtypasthānāni yāvadāryāṣṭāṅga
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi nas 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i bar du'o /
mārgāḥ / / tad bhāvanā bṛṃhaṇāropaṇā abhyāso bahulā kriyeti paryāyāḥ /
# de rnams bsgom pa ni spel ba dang bskyed pa dang goms par bya ba dang lan mang du bya ba zhes bya ba'i rnam grangs so /
sedānīṃ vaktavyā tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt /
# de yang de kho na'o 'og tu bstan pa'i phyir de yang brjod par bya'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaiva pūrvam ucyate nānyā / bodhipakṣabhāvanā ? / āha - tatra tāvadādau - / dauṣṭhulyāt tarṣahetutvāt / iti vistaraḥ / / tatreti bodhipakṣabhāvanāyāṃ /
# byang chub kyi phyogs bsgoms pa la ci'i phyir dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa nyid thog mar bshad kyi gzhan ni ma yin zhe na / / de la re zhig dang por / / gnas ngan len phyir sred rgyu'i phyir / / zhes rgya cher smos so / / de la zhes bya ba ni byang chub kyi phyogs bsgoms pa la'o /
tāvacchabdārthaḥ kramārthaḥ / / ādau tāvat smṛtyupasthānabhāvanocyate / / paścād anyeṣām apīti /
# re zhig ces bya ba ni rim gyi don te / / thog mar dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa ji bshad la / / gzhan yang phyis bshad do zhes bya bar 'gyur ro /
nirvāṇasaṃsāryor guṇadoṣā'navabodhāt / / saṃskāreṣu sukhaśucinityātmābhiniveśena bālānāṃ bhavabhoge'bhivacanaṃ [p.126]
# mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba gnyis kyi yon tan dang nyes pa mo rtogs pa'i phyir 'du byed rnams la bde ba dang gtsang ba dang rtag pa dang bdag tu mngon par zhen pas byis pa rnams srid pa dang longs spyod la mngon par dga' zhing mya ngan las 'das pas skrag go /
nirvāṇārthaṃ trāsaḥ / / sa ca guṇadoṣānavabodhaḥ sukhādyabhiniveśaś ca satyadarśanād vinivartata
# yon tan dang nyes pa ma rtogs pa dang bde ba la sogs pa la mngon par zhen pa de yang bden pa mthong nas ldog par 'gyur te /
ityataḥ saṃsārād udvajanārthaṃ nirvāṇe cābhimukhīkaraṇārthaṃ / catuḥsatyāvatārāya smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaivādāv uktā /
# de'i phyir 'khor ba la skyo bar bya ba'i don dang mya ngan las 'das pa mngon sum du bya ba'i don du bden pa bzhi la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa nyid thog mar bshad do /
kāyena hi dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyata iti / / dauṣṭhulyaṃ duḥsthitatā /
# lus kyis ni gnas ngan len rab tu ston zhes bya ba la / / gnas ngan len ni ngan par gnas pa ste /
tathā hi pratidinam abhisaṃskriyamāṇo vikriyata eva kāya iti kāyena
# 'di ltar nyin gcig bzhin mngon par 'dus byas kyang lus 'gyur ba nyid pas lus kyis ni gnas ngan len rab tu ston to /
dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate / / tataś ca kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati /
# de'i phyir lus la yongs su brtags pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go / / de ci'i phyir zhe na /
kim artham etad ityāha - tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti /
# de'i mtshan nyid ni gnas ngan len dang bcas pa'i 'du byed yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste /
yasmād duḥkhasatyasya sadauṣṭhulyāḥ saṃskārāḥ lakṣaṇaṃ svabhāvaḥ
# 'di ltar sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i mtshan nyid ngo bo nyid ni gnas ngan len dang bcas pa'i 'du byed rnams yin la /
kāyena ca dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam / avatarati / / dauṣṭhulyaṃ na vijñāyata ityata āha - dauṣṭhulyaṃ hi saṃskāraduḥkhateti
# lus kyis kyang gnas ngan len du rab tu ston pas / / de'i phyir lus la yongs su brtags pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go / / gnas ngan len mi shes pas de'i phyir / / gnas ngan len ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid de zhes bya ba smos so /
saṃskāro bhāvanām utpattiḥ /
# 'du byed ni dngos po rnams kyi skye ba'o /
sa ca sarvaviplavastv iti dauṣṭhulyamāryāṇāṃ pratikūlatvāc ca duḥkhatā / yathoktaṃ -
# de yang gnod pa thams cad kyi gzhi yin pas gnas ngan len yin la / / 'phags pa rnams dang mi mthun pa'i phyir sdug bsngal nyid de / / ji skad du /
anartho janmedaṃ sati hi janane santi ripavo
# skye 'di gnod yin pa skye ba yod na rga dang 'chi ba dang /
jarā-mṛtyu-vyādhi-vyasana-bandha-prabhṛtayaḥ / / anarthās te na syur yadi na bhavato nāśavibhavā-
# nad dang phongs pa gsod dang 'ching ba la sogs pa dgra rnams yod / / gal te 'jigs mad skye ba med gyur gnod pa de dag med /
vajāte vṛkṣe syān na hi dahanadavavāyucyutir api //
# shing skyes med na me dang rlung dang nags mes 'gyel mi 'gyur / / zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
tayeti saṃskāraduḥkhatayā na vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatābhyāṃ / tayor āvyāpitvāt saṃskāraduḥKhatānimittatvāc ca /
# des zhes bya ba 'di 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyis so / / 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid gnyis kyis ni ma yin te; de gnyis khyab pa ma yin pa dang 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
sarvaṃ sāsravaṃ vastvāryā duḥkhatā paśyanti nā'nāsavaṃ mārgasatyasya
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i dngos po thams cad 'phags pas sdug bsngal du gzigs kyi zag pa med pa ni ma yin te /
janmotpattipratipakṣatvāt na tu pṛthagjanā viparyāsasthānāśrayatvāt /
# lam gyi bden pa na che'i gnyen po yin pa'i phyir ro / / phyin ci log gi bsam pa nyams pa'i phyir so so'i skye bo rnams kyis ni ma yin no /
sūtre'py uktaṃ - samāsataḥ pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkham iti / / saṃskāraduḥkhatā'karmaṇyatetyanye / / na dauṣṭhulyam akarmaṇyātetyapare / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# mdo'i sde las kyang mdor na nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga ni sdug bsngal lo zhes gsungs so / / gzhan dag na re 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid ni las su mi rung ba'o zhes zer ro / / gzhan na re las su mi rung ba ni gnas ngan len ma yin no /
akarmaṇyātāyāḥ sāsravatvād avaśyaṃ sāsravatāṃ / bījakāraṇotpannā'bhyupagantavyā /
# ci'i phyir zhe na / / las su mi rung ba'i zag pa dang bcas pa'i phyir nges par zag pa dang bcas pa ni sa bon gyi rgyu las byung bar khas blang dgos na /
sā tv abījāpyarthasantāne kadācid āhārādyapacārād bhavati / / na cāsau dauṣṭhulyaṃ bhavitum arhatya nāsravatvād iti /
# de ni dgra bcom pa'i rgyud la sa bon med kyang res 'ga' kha zas dang gnas pa la sogs pa drags pa las 'byung ngo / / de ni zag pa med pa yin pa'i phyir gnas ngan len zhes byar mi rung ngo zhes zer ro /
ataś ca sāsravadharmabījam ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ / dauṣṭhulyenātreṣyate /
# de bas na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos kyis sa bon gnas pa ni 'dir gnas ngan len du 'dod do /
ayaṃ sukhaduḥkhā'sukhā'duḥkhasahitaḥ kāyastat phalaṃ /
# bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal ba yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang lhan cig pa'i lus 'di ni de'i 'bras bu'o /
tasmāt sukhādyavakāśasahitena kāyena pratikṣaṇabhāvinā tad dauṣṭhulyaṃ / prabhāvyate pratīyata ityarthaḥ / / tadyathā khalavilāntargataṃ bījam aṅkureṇeti /
# de bas na bde ba la sogs pa'i gnas skabs dang lhan cig pa skad cig re re la 'byung ba'i lus kyi gnas ngan len de rab tu ston te / / shes par byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / dper na myu gus gyul gyi ser ga'i nang du song ba'i sa bon mngon pa lta bu'o /
tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati / / atra kāraṇam āha - [p.127]
# de'i phyir lus la yongs su brtags pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go / / 'dir rgyu smos pa /
tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti sabījasaṃskārātmakatvād / ityarthaḥ /
# de'i mtshan nyid ni gnas ngan len dang bcas pa'i 'du byed yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste / / sa bon dang bcas pa'i 'du byed kyi bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
saṃskāraduḥkhatā hi vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatādauṣṭhulyābhyām / anugatatvāt kāraṇatvāc ca dauṣṭhulyam ityktā /
# 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid ni 'gyur ba dang sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid ngag gnas ngan len gnyis kyi rjes su song ba dang de'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal du bshad do /
ata eva saṃskāraduḥkhatayā sarvasāsravaṃ vastvāryaiḥ duḥkhatvenālokita
# de bas na 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyis zag pa dang bcas pa'i dngos po thams cad 'phags pa rnams kyis sdug bsngal nyid du gzigs so /
evaṃ kāyasmṛtyupasthānena duḥkhasatyam avataratīti /
# de ltar na lus dran pa nye bar gzhag pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go /
tṛṣṇāhetur vedanā - avidyāsaṃsparśajetyabhiprāyāt anāsravāyā atad / hetutvāt /
# sred pa'i rgyu ni tshor ba ste / / zhes bya ba ni ma rig pa'i 'dus te reg pa las byung bar dgos pa ste / / zag pa med pa ni de'i rgyu ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra sukhā vedanā tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ / / duḥkhā tad asaṃyogaviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ /
# de la bde ba'i tshor ba ni de dang ldan zhing mi 'bral bar sred pa'i rgyu'o / / sdug bsngal ni de dang mi phrad pa dang bral bar sred pa'i rgyu'o /
aduḥkhasukhā tad avasthābhir atitṛṣṇāyās tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyāś ca / kasyāṃcit samāptau hetur iti /
# sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa ni snyoms par 'jug pa 'ga' zhig la de'i gnas skabs la mngon par dga' ba'i sred pa'i rgyu dang de dang phrad cing mi 'bral par sred pa'i rgyu yin no /
sa duḥkhavedanayā spṛṣṭaḥ kāmasukham abhinandatīti vacanāt duḥkhāpi / vedanā sukhāyāḥ tṛṣṇayā hetur bhavati /
# de sdug bsngal gyi tshor bas reg na 'dod pa'i bde ba la mngon par dga'o zhes 'byung ba'i phyir / / sdug bsngal ba'i tshor ba yang bde ba la sred pa'i rgyur 'gyur te /
tat parīkṣayā samudayasatyam avatarati /
# de la yongs su brtags pas kun 'byung ba'i bden pa la 'jug go /
sa hi vedanāṃ svarūpataḥ kāraṇataḥ kāryato'nityato / duḥkhataścopaparīkṣamāṇaḥ samudayasatyam avatarati tṛṣṇāṃ tat / kāryatvenāvagacchatītyarthaḥ /
# de la tshor ba rnams la rang bzhin dang 'bras bu dang mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba nyid du nye bar yongs su rtog na kun 'byung ba'i bden pa la 'jug ste / / sred pa ni de'i 'bras bur khong du chud do zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tṛṣṇā hi sūtre samudayasatyam ityuktā /
# mdo sde las sred pa ni kun 'byung ba'i bden par gsungs te /
ko duḥkhasamudayaḥ ?
# sdug bsngal kun 'byung ba gang zhe na /
paṭhyate - tṛṣṇā paunarbhavikānandā rāgasahagateti vistaraḥ /
# yang 'byung ba'i sred pa dga' ba'i 'dod chags dang ldan pa'o zhes rgya cher 'byung ngo /
evaṃ vedanāsmṛtyupasthānena samudayasatyam avatarati /
# de ltar tshor ba dran pa nye bar gzhag pas kun 'byung ba'i bden pa la 'jug go /
ātmābhiniveśavastu cittam iti /
# bdag tu mngon par zhen pa'i gzhi ni sems te zhes bya ba la /
anyasya nityādiguṇaviśiṣṭasyātmano'bhāvād ātmābhiniveśālambanaṃ / cittam eva /
# rtag pa la sogs pa'i yon tan khyad par can gyi bdag gzhan med pas na bdag tu mngon par zhen pa'i dmigs pa ni sems nyid do /
tasmāt tat parīkṣayā nirodhasatyam avatarati śāntatvena /
# de bas na de yongs su brtags pas 'gog pa'i bden pa la zhi ba nyid du 'jug ste /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - ātmocchedabhayāpagamād iti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / bdag chad bar dogs pa'i 'jigs pa med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste /
citte hy anityatvādiparīkṣayā'tmābhiniveśo vyāvartate duḥkhasaṃjñā / pravartate /
# sems la mi rtag pa la sogs par yongs su brtags pas bdag tu mngon par zhen pa ldog cing sdug bsngal du 'du shes 'byung ngo /
ataścātmocchedabhayāpagamād duḥkhamātrasyocchedān nirodhasatyaṃ / śāntatvenāvataratīti / / evaṃ cittasmṛtyupasthānena nirodhasatyam avataratīti / / dharmaparīkṣayā sāṅkleśikavyāvadānikadharmāsaṃmohān mārgasatyam / avataratīti / / tatra sāṅkleśikā dharmāḥ kleśopakleśāḥ / / vyāvadānikās tu kleśopakleśapratipakṣabhūtāḥ premamaitryādayaḥ /
# de'i phyir bdag chad pa'i 'jigs pa med pas sdug bsngal ba tsam zhig gcod pa'i phyir 'gog pa'i bden pa la zhi ba nyid du 'jug ste / / de ltar sems dran pa nye bar gzhag pas 'gog pa'i bden pa la 'jug ces bya'o / / chos la yongs su brtags pas kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i chos la rmongs pa med pa'i phyir lam gyi bden pa la 'jug go zhes bya ba de la kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos rnams ni nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams so / / rnam par byang ba rnams ni nye ba'i gnyen por gyur pa rnams te / / mi sdug pa dang byams pa la sogs pa'o /
teṣāṃ sāṅkleśikānāṃ vyāvadānikānāñca vipakṣapratipakṣabhāvaṃ / buddhvā sarvopadravātyantaprahāṇopāye mārgasatye'bhimukhībhavati / / evaṃ dharmasmṛtyupasthānena mārgasatyam avataratīti / / avatāro'tra pratyekaṃ satye satyalakṣaṇāvabodhaḥ / / tatra kāyasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā anityato duḥkhataḥ śūnyato'nātmato'pi
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba de rnams la gnyen po dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi ngo bor shes nas gnod pa thams cad gtan du spang ba'i thabs lam gyi bden pa la mngon du phyogs par 'gyur te / / de ltar chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pas lam gyi bden pa la 'jug go / / 'jug pa ni 'dir bden pa so so la bden pa'i mtshan nyid du rtogs pa'o /
anekā'śucidravyasvabhāvato'pi aśucibījato'pi aśuciniṣyandato'pi / aśucisthitihetuto'pi aśucivikārato'pi phenabhaṅga ivāsārato'pi gatito'pi / yonito'pi /
# de la lus dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa ni mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa dang mi gtsang ba du ma'i rdzas kyi rang bzhin dang mi gtsang ba'i sa bon dang mi gtsang ba'i rgyu mthun pa dang mi gtsang ba gnas pa'i rgyu dang mi gtsang bar 'gyur ba dang dbu ba rdos pa bzhin du snying po med pa dang 'gro ba dang skye gnas yin par bsgom mo /
vedanācittadharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā punar / anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmato'pi svalakṣaṇato'pi hetuto'pi phalato'pi / dhātubhūmigatito'pi kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtato'pi vipakṣapratipakṣato'pi / / bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanā evañcānupalambhākāreṇa / ca vikalpaprahāṇārthaṃ / / smṛtyupasthānānāṃ tu prajñāsvābhāvye'pi smṛtyupasthānavacanaṃ / smṛtibalenopasthānād etāsāṃ prajñānāṃ smṛtyupasthānam ucyate //4-1// [p.128]
# tshor ba dang sems dang chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams bsgom pa yang mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa dang spyi'i mtshan nyid dang rang gi mtshan nyid dang rgyu dang 'bras bu dang khams dang sa dang 'gro ba dang dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po yin par bsgom mo / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa ni 'di lta bu yang yin la rnam par rtog pa spangs pa'i phyir mi dmigs pa'i rnam par yang bsgom mo / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams shes rab kyi rang bzhin yin du zin kyang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa'i tshig ni dran pa'i stobs kyis nye bar gnas pa'i phyir ram / / 'di dag gis dran pa nye bar gnas pas dran pa nye bar gzhag pa zhes bya'o /
{ catvāri samyakprahāṇāni } / smṛtyupasthānabhāvanānantaraṃ samyakprahāṇabhāvanoktā / / kiṃ kāraṇam ata āha / yasmāt - / parijñāte vipakṣe ca / iti vistaraḥ / / smṛtyupasthānabhāvanayeti /
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa'i 'og tu yang dag par spong ba bsgom pa bshad de / / de ci'i phyir zhe na / / de'i phyir 'di ltar / / mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po rnams / / rnam pa thams cad yongs shes nas / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
aviśeṣābhidhāne'pi dharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanayaiveti veditavyaṃ / / dhātubhūmyavakāśaiḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇādyākārais tathā
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgoms nas zhes khyad par med par brjod kyang chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa nyid yin par rig par bya'o /
sāsravānāsravanadhātubhūmi-śaikṣāśaikṣādyākārais tathā / sāsravānāsravadhātubhūmi-śaikṣāśaikṣādibhedena ca vipakṣe pratipakṣe / ca sarvaprakāra parijñāte / / vipakṣāgamāyeti / / vipakṣāpagamamo'trotpannānāṃ prabandhacchedo'nutpannānāṃ cānutpādaḥ / / pratipakṣopagamāya ceti /
# khams dang sa'i spangs pa dang spyi'i mtshan nyid la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang de bzhin du zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa dang khams dang sa dang slob pa dang mi slob pa la sogs pa'i bye brag gis mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po rnam pa thams cad du yongs su shes na mi mthun pa'i phyogs gsal ba ni 'dir skyes pa rnams kyi rgyun chad pa dang ma skyes pa rnams mi skyed pa'o / / gnyen po bskyed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba la /
pratipakṣāgama utpannānāṃ prabandhānuvṛttir anutpannānāñcotpādaḥ / / vīryaṃ caturdhā pravartata iti vipakṣapratipakṣayor utpanānutpannabhedena / caturdhā vīryasya pravṛttiḥ / / utpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ prahāṇāyeti vistara / itīdam āgamena vīryasyaiva caturdhā pravṛttiṃ darśayati /
# gnyen po bskyed pa ni skyes pa rnams kyi rgyun gyis rjes su 'jug pa dang ma skyes pa rnams skyed pa'o / / brtson 'grus rnam pa bzhi rab tu 'byung zhes byang ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po gnyis skyes pa dang ma skyes pa tha dad pas brtson 'grus rnam pa bzhi 'byung ste / / sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams spang ba'i phyir zhe rgya cher 'byung ngo zhes bya ba 'dis ni lung gis brtson 'grus nyid rnam pa bzhi 'byung bar ston to /
vistaravacanena śeṣagranthābhisambandhaḥ / / tatrāyāṃ śeṣo granghaḥ - prahāṇāya chandaṃ janayati vyāyacchate vīryam
# rgya cher zhes bya ba ni tshig lhag ma dang sbyar ba'o / / de la 'di ni tshig lhag ma ste sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams spangs pa'i phyir 'dun pa skyed do / / 'bad do /
ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samyakpradadhātīti / / evam anutpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām anutpādāya / chandañjanayatīti vistaraḥ /
# brtson 'grus rtsom mo / / sems rab tu 'dzin to / / yang dag par rab tu 'jog go zhes bya ba dang de bzhin du sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa rnams mi bskyed pa'i phyir 'dun pa bskyed do zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o /
evam anutpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām utpādaya chandañjanayatīti / vistaraḥ /
# de bzhin du dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa rnams bskyed pa'i phyir 'dun pa bskyed do zhes rgya cher bya'o /
utpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sthitaye bhūyobhāvatāyai / asampramoṣāya paripūraṇāya chandañjanayati vyāyacchate vīryam
# dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams gnas pa dang phyir zhing 'byung ba dang yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir 'dun pa bskyed do / / 'bad do / / brtson 'grus brtsam mo /
ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti / / samyak pradadhāti / / utpannānāṃ sthitir aparihāṇiḥ / / bhūyobhāvaḥ prabandhenotpādaḥ / / paripūriḥ prakarṣagamanaṃ /
# sems rab tu 'dzin to / / yang dag par rab tu 'jog go zhes bya ba'o / / skyes pa rnams gnas pa ni yongs su mi nyams pa'o / / phyir zhing 'byung ba ni rgyun du skye ba'o / / yongs su rdzogs par bya ba ni phul du phyin par 'gyur ba'o /
chandañjanayatīti sagauravodyaktavīryasamṛddhiṃ darśayati /
# 'dun pa skyed ces bya ba ni gus par brtson 'grus bsgom pa'i sbyor ba ston to /
vyāyacchata iti kausīdyaprahāṇāya kāyacitte'bhimukhīkarotītyarthaḥ /
# 'bad ces bya ba ni le lo spangs te / / lus dang sems mngon du byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
vīryam ārabhata iti layauddhatyāpakarṣaṇārthaṃ /
# brtson 'grus rtsom zhes bya ba ni bying ba dang rgod pa bsal ba'i phyir ro /
katham ārabheta ?
# ji ltar rtsom zhe na /
līnaṃ cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samvejanīyapramodānīyadharmamanaskāraiḥ / / uddhataṃ cittaṃ tasminnevālambane samyak pradadhāti / samvejanīyapramodanīyadharmamanaskārair dhārayatītyarthaḥ / / evañca [p.129] / samyakpradhānāni vīryātmakānīti jñāpitam bhavati / / samyag ebhiḥ kāyavāṅmanāṃsi dhārayantīti samyakpradhānāni //4-2// / { catvāraḥ ṛddhipādāḥ } / karmañatā sthites tatra
# yang dag pa shes par bya ba dang dga' bar bya ba'i chos yid la byed pas bying ba'i sems rab tu 'dzin to / / sems rgod par gyur na dmigs pa de nyid la yang dag par rab tu 'jog ste / / 'dzin zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de ltar yang dag par spong ba rnams ni brtson 'grus kyi rang bzhin du bstan pa yin te / / 'di rnams kyis lus dang ngag dang yid yang dag par 'dzin pas na yang dag par 'dzin pa rnams so /
iti vistaraḥ / / tatreti tasyāṃ vipakṣapratipakṣāyāpagamavīryabhāvanāyāṃ /
# der gnas las su rung ba nyid / / ces rgya cher 'byung ba la der zhes bya ba ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs bsal ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom pa de la'o /
karmaṇyatā cittasthiteḥ sarvārthasamṛddhiyogyatā /
# sems gnas pa'i las su rung ba nyid ni don thams cad 'byor par nus pa nyid de las su rung ba nyid do /
sā ca karmaṇyatā chandavīryacittamīmāṃsādhipatyaprabhavetyata āha -
# las su rung ba de yang 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems pa dang dpyod pa'i dbang gis byung bas na de'i phyir /
karmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā iti / / sarvasyābhijñādikasyārthasya samṛddhi ṛddhiḥ / / tasyāḥ pratiṣṭhārthena ṛddhipādā ṛddhihetava ityarthaḥ / / ata evāha - sarvārthasamṛddhihetutvād iti / / te punaścandasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādaḥ / vīryasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādā cittasamādhiḥ / prahāṇasaṃskārasamanavāgata ṛddhipādaḥ mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ
# las su rung ba nyid ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi po dag ste zhes bya ba smos so; / / mngon par shes pa la sogs pa don thams cad 'grub par byed pa ni rdzu 'phrul lo / / de'i gnas yin pa'i phyir rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa zhes bya ste / / rgyu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de bas na don thams cad 'byor pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro zhes smos te / / de dag kyang 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang sems kyi ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa zhes bya ba'o /
prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipāda iti / / tatra cchandsamādhir yadā chandādhipatyād vīryabhāvanāyāṃ sagauravaṃ
# de la 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe 'dun pa'i dbang gis brtson 'grus rtsom pa la gus par 'jug pa na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
pravartamānaḥ spṛśati cittasyakāgratāṃ / / vīryasamādhir yadā vīryam ārabhamāṇaḥ sātatyaprayogāt spṛśati / cittasyaikāgratāṃ / / cittasamādhir yadā pūrvasamādhibījam āgamya citta eva cittaṃ dhārayan / spṛśati cittasyaikāgratāṃ / / mīmāmsāsamādhir yadālambanapravicito'nuspṛśati cittasyaikāgratām iti / sthitiratra cittasthitiḥ samādhir veditavya iti samādhigrahaṇaṃ
# brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe brtson 'grus rtsom pa na rtag par sbyor bas sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o / / sems kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe sngon gyi ting nge 'dzin gyi sa bon la brten nas sems 'dzin cing gang sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o / / dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe dmigs pa rab tu rnam par 'byed pa na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o / / gnas pa ni 'dir sems gnas pa ste / / ting nge 'dzin du rig par bya'o zhes bya ba la /
saṃskṛtalakṣaṇād vyavacchedārthaṃ /
# ting nge 'dzin smos pa ni 'dus byas kyi mtshan nyid las dbye ba'i phyir ro /
yata ārabdhavīryasya cittakarmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā bhavanti ataḥ / samyak prahāṇānantaraṃ ṛddhipādā nirdiṣṭāḥ / / sā punaḥ karmaṇyatā [p.130] / kim prayojanā kiṃ hetukā cetyata āha - / pañcadoṣaprahāṇāyāṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārabhāvanānvayā videtavyeti / / anvayo hetuḥ //4-3// / { pañca doṣāḥ }
# 'di ltar brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni sems las su rung ba nyid rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhir gyur pa de'i phyir yang dag par spong ba'i 'og tu rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams bstan to / / las su rang ba de yang dgos pa ni gang / / rgyu ni gang zhe na de'i phyir / / nyes pa lnga spang ba'i phyir 'du byed bsgom pa'i rgyu las byung bar rig par bya'o zhes bya ba smos so /
te ca pañcadoṣā na vijñāyanta ityataḥ pṛcchati katame pañca doṣā iti / / tat pradarśayann āha - / kausīdyam avavādasya sammoṣo laya udbhavaḥ / / iti vistaraḥ /
# nyes pa lnga po de dag mi shes nas / / de'i phyir / / nyes pa lnga po de dag gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang de dag bstan pa'i phyir / / le lo dag ni gdams ngag rnams / / brjed dang bying dang rgod pa dang / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / de dag ni nyes pa drug tu 'gyur ro snyam pa la / / de'i phyir /
ete hi ṣaḍdoṣā ityata āha - tatra layauddhatyam eko doṣaḥ kriyata iti / pañca bhavanti /
# de la bying ba dang rgod pa ni nyes pa gcig tu bsdu'o zhes bya ba smos te / / de'i phyir lngar 'gyur ro /
tatra kausīdyaṃ prayogakāle doṣas tenāprayogāt /
# de la le lo ni sbyor ba'i tshe na nyes pa ste / / des mi sbyor ba'i phyir ro /
udyuktasyāvavādasammoṣo doṣas tena cittasamādhānabhāvāt /
# brtson pa'i tshe gdams ngag brjed pa ni nyes pa ste / / des sems mnyam par gzhag pa med pa'i phyir ro /
samāhitasya layauddhatyaṃ doṣastena cittakarmaṇyatā'bhāvāt /
# mnyam par gzhag pa la bying ba dang rgod pa ni nyes pa ste / / des sems las su rung ba med pa'i phyir ro /
anabhisaṃskāro layauddhatyapraśamanakāle doṣaḥ /
# bying ba dang rgod par gyur pa'i tshe mngon par 'du mi byed pa nyes pa'o /
anabhisaṃskāra upekṣā tayā tad dvayāśamanāt / / abhisaṃskāraḥ praśāntau doṣa iti / / abhisaṃskāraścetanā /
# mngon par 'du mi byed pa ni btang snyoms te / / des de gnyis rab tu zhi bar mi byed pa'i phyir ro / / rab tu zhi ba'i tshe ni mngon par 'du byed pa'o zhes bya ba ni nyes pa zhes bya bar snyegs so / / mngon par 'du byed pa ni sems pa'o /
layauddhatyavigamāddhi samatāprāptatvāt praśāntam ity ucyate //4-4// / { aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ } [p.131] / prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ prahāṇāya saṃskārāḥ / / kasya prahāṇāya ?
# bying ba dang rgod pa dang bral bas mnyam pa nyid du gyur pa'i phyir rab tu zhi ba zhes bya'o / / spang bar bya ba'i phyir 'du byed rnams ni spong ba'i 'du byed rnams so / / gang spang ba'i phyir zhe na /
anantaroktānāṃ pañcānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ prahāṇāya /
# bshad ma thag pa'i nyes pa lnga rnams spang ba'i phyir ro /
yadyevaṃ tena vaktavyam eṣāṃ prahāṇāya katham aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārā
# gal te de lta na des de dag spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad ji ltar rnam par gzhag pa brjod dgos so /
vyavasthāpyanta iti / / tatra kausīdyaprahāṇāya catvāraś chandavyāyāmaśraddhāprasrabdhayaḥ /
# de la le lo spang ba'i phyir bzhi ste / / 'dun pa dang rtsol ba dang dad pa dang shin tu sbyangs pa'o /
tatra cchando'bhilāṣaḥ / / vyāyāmo vīryaṃ / / śraddhā'bhisampratyayaḥ / / prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatā /
# de la 'dun pa ni 'dod pa'o / / rtsol ba ni brtson 'grus so / / dad pa ni mgon par yid ches pa'o / / shin tu sbyangs pa ni las su rung ba nyid do /
kathaṃ punar ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya vyavasthāpyanta ityata āha - te
# ji ltar na le lo spang ba'i phyir de dag rnam par gzhag ce na / / de'i phyir /
punar yathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ / / āśrayo'rthāśritas tasya nimittaṃ phalam eva ca / iti /
# de dag kyang go rims bzhin du rig par bya ste / / gnas dang de la gnas pa dang / / rgyu dang 'bras bu nyid du'o /
ato'nyonyaprabhāvitatvād ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya samvartanta iti / darśayati - āśrayaśchando vyāyāmasya āśrito vyāyāmaḥ /
# zhes bya ba smos so / / de dag gcig las gcig 'byung bas na le lo spong bar 'gyur ba ston to / / rtsol ba'i gnas ni 'dun pa'o / / gnas pa ni rtsol ba ste /
abhilāṣasya vyāyāmapūrvakatvāt / / tasyāśrayasya chandasya nimittaṃ śraddhā /
# 'dod pa ni rtsol ba'i sngon du 'gro ba'i phyir ro / / gnas 'dun pa'i rgyu ni dad pa ste /
katham ityato bravīti - sampratyaye saty abhilāṣād iti /
# ji lta zhe na / / de'i phyir / / yid ches par gyur na 'dod pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
śraddadhānasya hi hetuphale kriyābhilāṣo bhavati /
# rgyu dang 'bras bu la dad pa dang ldan pa ni bya ba la 'dod par 'gyur ro /
tasyāśritasya vyāyāmasya phalaṃ prasrabdhiḥ /
# gnas pa rtsol ba de'i 'bras bu ni shin tu sbyangs pa ste /
katham ityata āha - prārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣā'dhigamād iti /
# ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / brtson 'grus brtsams na ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par thob pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
samādhiviśeṣagamanaṃ hi prasrabdhinimittaṃ /
# ting nge 'dzin khyad par du 'gro ba ni shin tu sbyangs pa'i rgyu'o / / de'i phyir /
ata ārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣagamanāt prasrabdhir vyāyāmaphalam
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa'i ting nge 'dzin khyad par du 'gro bas shin tu sbyangs pa ni rtsol ba'i 'bras bur bshad do /
ityuktaṃ / / tathā hy ārabdhavīryasya dauṣṭhulyavitarkādyapakṣālavigamāt pramoda
# de ltar brtson 'grus brtsams pa gnas ngan len gyi rnam par rtog pa'i nyes pa dang bral bas dga' ba skye'o /
utpadyate / / manaḥpramodāt kāyacittayoḥ prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatālakṣaṇatā /
# yid dga' bas lus dang sems gnyis shin tu sbyangs te las su rung ba nyid kyi mtshan nyid do /
tataḥ samādhiviśeṣagamanam iti /
# de bas na ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par thob pa'i phyir zhes bya ba'o /
atra ca vīryaṃ sahetukaṃ saphalaṃ ca kausīdyapratipakṣeṇoktaṃ /
# 'dir ni brtson 'grus rgyu dang bcas shing 'bras bu dang bcas pa le lo'i gnyen por bshad do /
caturṇāṃ doṣāṇāṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ pratipakṣa iti / / tatra smṛtir avavādasammoṣasya pratipakṣaḥ / / samprayojanyaṃ layauddhatyasya / / cetanā'nabhisaṃskārasya /
# nyes pa bzhi'i gnyen por grangs bzhin no zhes bya ba de la / / dran pa ni gdams ngag brjed pa'i gnyen po'o / / shes bzhin ni bying ba dang rgod pa'i gnyen po'o / / sems pa ni mngon par 'du mi byed pa'i gnyen po'o /
abhisaṃskārasyopekṣeti saṃskāropekṣā'tra veditavyā /
# btang snyoms ni mngon par 'du byed pa'i gnyen po ste / / 'dir 'du byed kyi btang snyoms su shes par bya'o /
smṛtyādīnāṃ punar lakṣaṇavivakṣayedam āha - te punaḥ smṛtyādayo / veditavyā yathākramam iti /
# dran pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid brjod par 'dod pa'i phyir / / de dag kyang ngan pa la sogs pa rig par bya ste go rims bzhin zhes bya ba 'di smos so /
smṛtir ālambane'sammoṣa iti / [p.132]
# dran pa ni dmigs pa ma brjed pa'o zhes rgya cher 'byung ba la /
vistarīkṛtamālambanam iti cittasthāpanīyam avavādavastv abhilapanam / ityartaḥ /
# dran pa ni dmigs pa ma brjed pa'o zhes bya ba ni sems gnas par bya ba'i gdams ngag yid kyis brjod ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
samprajanyaṃ smṛtyasampramoṣe sati layauddhatyāvabodha iti / / upasthitasmṛtir hi samprajanyavān bhavatyevetyata āha - smṛtyasampramoṣe / satīti / / anubuddhyā layauddhatyaṃ śamathavipaśyane yuganaddhādaprayatnena
# shes bzhin ni dran pa ma brjed par gyur na bying ba dang rgod pa rtogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni dran pa nye bar gnas pa shes bzhin dang ldan par 'gyur ro / / de'i phyir dran pa ma brjed par gyur na zhes bya ba smos te / / bying ba dang rgod pa rtogs nas zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gnyis zung du 'brel par 'jug pa'i phyir bsgrim mi dgos par 'jug go zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
pravartetetyarthaḥ / / upekṣeti viṣayāntarānabhisaṃskāra ityarthaḥ /
# btang snyoms zhes bya ba ni yul gzhan la mngon par 'du mi byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig ste /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - sūpasthitasmṛtiravavāde līnaṃ cittam uddhtaṃ vā / yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti / / layauddhatyavigamāya ca tad abhisaṃskaroti layauddhatyavigamāc copekṣāṃ / karotīti / / evaṃ tasya cittapraśaṭhatā karmaṇyatā / / atra ca karmaṇyatāsthitir iti svārthe bhāvapratyayaḥ svapeṭatvādivat //
# de ni 'di skad du gdams ngag la dran pa shin tu nye bar gnas pa ni bying ba dang rgod pa'i sems yang dag pa ji ltar ba bzhin du shes shing / / bying ba dang rgod pa dang 'bral ba'i phyir de mngon par 'du byed la / / bying ba dang rgod pa dang 'bral na yang btang snyoms su byed do zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / de ltar na de'i sems rnal du 'jug pa las su rung ba nyid yin no /
{ pañcendriyāṇi } / ṛddhipādānantaraṃ pañcendriyāṇi śraddhādīnyuktānīti sambadhyate /
# rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa'i 'og tu dbang po lnga rnams te / / dad pa la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni bstan zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti kenārthenetyabhiprāyaḥ / / ata āha -
# de dag ji ltar rnam par gzhag ce na zhes bya ba ni gang gi phyir zhes dgongs pa'o / / de'i phyir /
ropite mokṣabhāgīye chandayogādhipatyataḥ / / iti vistaraḥ /
# thar pa'i cha dang mthun bskyed na / / 'dun dang sbyor ba dbang byed do / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
ādhipatyata iti vartata ityanena cchandayogādhipatyata / ityatrādhipatyaśabdaḥ prayukta uttaratrāpyanuvartata iti darśayati /
# dbang byed pa zhes bya bar snyegs so zhes bya ba 'dis ni 'dun pa dang sbyor ba dbang byed ces bya ba'i sgra 'dir smos pa 'og ma rnams la yang snyegs so zhes ston to /
ṛddhipādaiḥ karmaṇyacittasyāropite mokṣabhāgīye kuśalamūle iti / / karmaṇyacittasya vimokṣabhāgīyaṃ kuśalamūlaṃ cittasandhāne pratiṣṭhāṃ
# rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyis sems las su rung ba thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed nas zhes bya ba ni sems las su rung ba sems kyi rgyud la thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rab tu 'jog pa 'thob ste /
pratilabhate chandādhipatyato yāvat pravicayādhipatyataḥ na tv / akarmaṇyacittasya /
# 'dun pa ni dbang byed pa nas rab tu rnam par 'byed pa ni dbang byed pa'i bar du 'gyur gyi / / sems las su mi rung ba la ni ma yin no /
sā ca cittakarmaṇyatā ṛddhipādair bhavati /
# sems las su rung ba nyid de yang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyis 'gyur ro /
tasmād ṛddhipādānantaraṃ vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ / pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇīti vyavasthāpyante /
# de bas na rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa'i 'og tu thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa la dbang byed pas dad pa la sogs pa dbang po lnga rnams rnam par gzhag go /
chandādhipatyata iti kāraṇe kāryopacārāśchraddhaivātra / chandaśabdenoktā /tadyathā dadhatrapuṣaṃ sadyojvara iti /
# 'dun pa ni dbang byed zhes bya ba ni rgyu la 'bras bu btags nas dad pa nyid la 'dir 'dun pa'i sgrar bshad de / / dper na zho dang ga gon la 'phral du rims zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
athavāstitvaguṇaśaktiṣu yathākramam abhisampratyayaprasādābhilāṣāḥ / śraddhāyā lakṣaṇaṃ /
# yang na yod pa nyid dang yon tan can dang nus pa rnams la go rims bzhin du mngon par yid ches pa dang dang ba dang 'dod pa rnams ni dad pa'i mtshan nyid do /
ataścandagrahaṇenātrābhilāṣalakṣaṇā śraddhaiva gṛhyate na tu cchanda iti
# de bas na 'dun pa smos pas 'dir 'dod pa'i mtshan nyid dad pa smos par 'gyur gyi 'dun pa ni ma yin no /
prayogādhipatyata iti prayujyate 'neneti prayogaḥ /
# sbyor ba ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni 'dis sbyor bar byed pas na sbyor ba ste /
prayogaśabdena vīryam abhipretaṃ /
# sbyor ba'i sgra ni brtson 'grus la bya bar dgongs pa'o /
ālambanāsampramoṣādhipatyata iti smṛtīndriyādhipatyataḥ /
# dmigs pa mi brjed pa ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni dran pa'i dbang po dbang byed pa ste /
ālmbanābhilapanalakṣaṇaṃ smṛtīndriyaṃ /
# dmigs pa gsal ba'i mtshan nyid ni dran pa'i dbang po'o /
avisārādhipatyata iti samādhīndriyādhipatyataḥ / / avisāro hi samādhīndriyaṃ cittaikāgratālakṣaṇatvāt /
# mi 'phro ba ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang po dbang byed pa ste / / sems rtse gcig pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas mi 'phro ba ni ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang po'o /
pravicayādhipatyataśceti prajñendriyādhipatyataḥ /
# rab tu rnam par 'byed pa ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni shes rab kyi dbang po dbang byed pa ste /
prajñendriyasya dharmapravicayātmakatvāt /
# shes rab kyi dbang po chos rnam par 'byed pa'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
ca śabdo vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipattyāt / [p.133] / yathākramaṃ pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇi veditavyānīti darśayati /
# kyang zhes bya ba'i sgra ni thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa la dbang byed pas dad pa la sogs pa dbang po dag dang go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o zhes bya bar ston to /
śraddhadhāno hi saṃsāracārakān niḥsaraṇārthaṃ vīryam ārabhate /
# dad par gyur pa ni 'khor ba'i btson ra nas 'byung bar 'gyur bas de'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo /
ārabdhavīryasya triśikṣāniṣpattiḥ smṛtisamādhiprajñendriyāṇi / yathākramaṃ /
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa bslab pa gsum sgrub ste / / dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi dbang po rnams go rims bzhin no /
evaṃ darśanamārgaprayogabhūmāv indriyāṇāṃ prādhānyam iṣyate /
# de ltar mthong ba'i lam la sbyor ba'i sa la dbang po di rnams gtso bor 'dod do /
anye tvāhuḥ - na mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ / śraddhādīnām indriyatvaṃ /
# gzhan dag na re thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa la dbang byed pa la dad pa la sogs pa'i dbang po zhes mi bya'o /
kiṃ tarhi ropite mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūle chandādīnām ādhipatyata / etānīndriyāṇy ucyante /
# thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed nas 'dun pa la sogs pa la dbang byed pas na 'di dag dbang po zhes bya'o /
etad eva pradarśayann āha - chandādhipatyataḥ śraddhāyā indriyatvam iti / sambadhyate / / prayogo vyāpāraḥ / / asammoṣa ālambanavipraṇāśaḥ / / avisaraṇam avisāraḥ / / pravicayanaṃ pravicayaḥ /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir 'dun pa ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba smos te / / dad pa'i dbang po zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro / / sbyor ba ni byed pa'o / / mi brjed pa ni dmigs pa chud mi za ba'o / / 'phro ba med pas na mi 'phro ba'o / / rab tu rnam par 'byed pas na rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'o /
teṣāṃ prayogasammoṣāvisārapravicayānām ādhipatyād / vīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñākhyaścaittā indriyākhyaṃ bhavantīti /
# sbyor ba dang mi brjed pa dang mi 'phro ba dang rab tu rnam par 'byed pa de dag la brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab ces bya ba'i sems las byung ba rnams dbang bas na / / dbang po rnams zhes bya bar gyur zhes zer ro /
