# de gnyi ga dang ldan pa su yang med pa'i phyir ro / / gang gi phyir de dag ni de lta ma yin pas de la nga'i 'di med do zhes skrag par 'gyur du'ang ci yod /
kim iti māno bhavaty ayaṃ me viśeṣa iti / [p.169] / apare tu manyate - pudgalas tāvan naivāsti /
# nga'i khyad par ni 'di yin no zhes nga rgyal du 'gyur du yang ci yod ces zer ro / / gzhan dag ni 'di snyam du sems te / / gang zag ni med pa nyid do /
dharmo'pi naivāsti / / avasthādvayaṃ yo'nubhavati yasyaitad dvayaṃ kalpyeta / / kiṃ tarhi pratītyasamutpādamātram etat saṅkleśavyavadānam iti /
# gang gnas 'di gnyis myong ba dang 'di gnyis gang la brtag pa'i chos de yang med pa nyid do / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba 'di dag ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba nyid du zad do snyam mo /
ayam api saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpakatvāt /
# 'di yang kun rdzob tu'o don dam par ni ma yin te / / de ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro /
anena cāviparyāsena kṣayavṛddhyasadbhāvād avikāritvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ / pratividhyatīti /
# phyin ci ma log pa 'dis chos kyi dbyings zad pa dang 'phel ba med pa'i phyir 'gyur ba med par rab tu rtogs par 'gyur ro /
anena cāviparyāsena sarvam āvaraṇaṃ prahāya nirāvaraṇo niryātītyanye / atha vānena saṃvṛtyātmakena daśaviparyāsena paramārthāviparyāso'tra / sūcitaḥ tasyānyathā nirdeśānupapatteḥ / / anyaḥ punar āha - ya ete vyañjane'rthe manaskāre'visāre svalakṣaṇe
# gzhan na re phyin ci ma log pa 'dis sgrib pa thams cad / / spangs te / / sgrib pa dang bral ba'i nges par 'byung ngo zhe'o / / yang na kun rdzob kyi bdag nyid phyin ci ma log pa 'di bcus / / don dam pa'i phyir ci ma log pa 'di bstan te / / gzhan du ni bstan pa mi 'thad pa'i phyir ro /
sāmānyalakṣaṇe'śuddhau śuddhāvāgantuke'trāse'nunnatau cāviparyāsāḥ / kalpitā āśrayās te svabhāvatrayam adhikṛtyeti /
# gzhan na re gang dag yi ge dang don dang yid la byed pa dang mi 'phro ba dang rang gi mtshan nyid dang spyi'i mtshan nyid dang ma dag pa dang dag pa dang glo bur dang mi skrag pa dang khengs pa med pa la phyin ci ma log pa de dag ngo bo nyid gsum gyi dbang du byas pa'o zhe'o /
tatra vyañjanārthāviparyāsāv atra parikalpitaṃ svabhāvam adhikṛtya /
# de la yi ge dang don la phyin ci ma log pa ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi dbang du byas pa ste /
saṃyogino dvayapatitasya cārthasya kalpitatvāt /
# 'brel pa dang gnyis su ltung ba'i don ni brtags pa'i phyir ro /
atattvaviṣayatve'pi satyevaṃ tad dvayam aviparyāsa eva / / aviparyāsas tathaiveti /
# de kho na'i yul ma yin du zin kyang / / de bzhin du phyin ci ma log pa de bzhin nyid kyi phyir te / / de gnyis phyin ci ma log pa nyid do /
manaskāre'viparyāsaḥ paratantrasvabhāvam adhikṛtya /
# yid la byed pa la phyin ci ma log pa ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid kyi dbang du byas pa ste /
jalpamanaskārasya prakṛtyā ālayavijñānātmakatvāt /
# rtog pa dang yid la byed pa gnyis rang bzhin gyis kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
avisāre'viparyāsaḥ pariniṣpannasvabhāvam adhikṛtya /
# mi 'phro ba la phyin ci ma log pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi dbang du byas pa ste / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
kuta etan nirvikalpasya jñānasya bhāvābhāvayor vikṣepavigatatvād / aviparyāsapariniṣpattyā ca pariniṣpannasvabhāvasaṃgṛhītatvāt / / svasāmānyalakṣaṇayor aviparyāso dharmadhātā meva tasya
# rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes ni / / yod pa dang med pa la gyeng ba dang bral ba'i phyir dang phyin ci ma log par yongs su grub pas yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid du bsdus pa'i phyir ro / / rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log pa ni chos kyi dbyings nyid la ste /
vikalpaviśayātikrāta svarūptvāt/
# rnam par rtog pa'i yul las 'das pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi phyir ro /
aśuddau śuddau caviparyāso dharma(dhāto)avasthāviśeṣe / / āgantuke'viparyāso dharmadhātāv eva tasya hy ākāśavat
# ma dag pa dang dag pa la phyin ci ma log pa ni chos kyi dbyings nyid kyi gnas skabs kyi bye brag la'o / / glo bur la phyin ci ma log pa ni chos kyi dbyings nyid la ste /
prakṛtiviśuddhasya cittasaṅkleśāc cittaviśuddhyā cāgantukam etad ubhayaṃ / vyavasthāpyate /
# nam mkha' bzhin du rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa de la / / sems kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba 'di gnyis ni glo bur yin par rnam par gzhag go /
atrāsānunnabhāvāviparyāso dharmadhātāv eva tasyākāśavad / akṛtrimatvād hāniviśeṣābhāvāt / / evam ete daśa viparyāsāḥ svabhāvatraye veditavyāḥ / / { daśa vajrapadāni } [p.170]
# mi skrag pa dang khengs pa med pa la phyin ci ma log pa ni chos kyi dbyings nyid la ste / / de nam mkha' bzhin du bcos ma ma yin pa'i phyir 'bri ba dang khyad par du gyur pa med pa'i phyir ro / / de ltar phyin ci ma log pa bcu po 'di dag ngo bo nyid gsum du rig par bya'o /
ete cānantaroktā daśaviparyāsāḥ sūtrokteṣu daśasu vajrapadeṣu / yathākramaṃ yojayitavyāḥ /
# bshad ma thag pa'i phyin ci ma log pa bcu po 'di dag ni mdo sde las gsungs pa'i rdo rje'i tshig bcu dag dang go rims bzhin du sbyar bar bya ste /
daśa vajrapadāni katamāni ?
# rdo rje'i tshig bcu po gang zhe na /
sadasattā'viparyāsaḥ āśrayaḥ māyopamatā avikalpanatā / prakṛtiprabhāsvaratā saṅkleśo vyavadānaṃ ākāśopamatā ahīnatā
# yod pa dang med pa dang phyin ci ma log pa dang gnas dang sgyu ma lta bu nyid dang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid dang rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba nyid dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang nam mkha' lta bu dang 'grib pa med pa dang khyad par du 'phags pa med pa'o /
aviśiṣṭatā ceti / / tatra vajramiva vajraṃ sarvaviparyāsabheditvāt taiścābhedyatvāt /
# de la phyin ci log thams cad 'joms pa dang de dag gis mi choms pa'i phyir rdo rje dang 'dra bas na rdo rje zhes bya ba ste /
anantaroktam aviparyāsajñānaṃ tac ca vajram ebhiḥ pratīyate avagamyata / iti vajrapadāni / / vajravyākhyānam ityarthaḥ /
# bshad ma thag pa'i phyin ci ma log pa'i shes pa'o / / rdo rje de ni 'di dag gis rtogs par byed / / khong du chud par byed pas rdo rje'i tshig rnams te / / rdo rje'i rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
atha punarvyañjanārthamanaskārādaya eva padaśabdhenocyante tato vajrasya / padānyālambanānityarthaḥ /
# ji ste na yang yi ge dang don dang yid la sogs pa nyid la tshig ces bya ba'i sgrar brjod de / / de'i phyir rdo rje'i tshig rnams te /
athava durbhedatayā vajravadetānyeva padāni vajra padānītyuccayante /
# dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / yang rdo rje bzhin du mi choms pa'i tshig de dag ni rdo rje'i tshig rnams zhes bya'o /
atrāviparyāsānāṃ sūtrayojanārthaṃ vajrapadopanyāsaḥ /
# 'dir phyin ci ma log pa rnams mdo sde dang sbyar bar bya ba'i phyir rdo rje'i tshig rnams bkod do /
vajrapadānāṃ va daśavidhāviparyāsamukhenedaṃ vyākhyānam iti
# yang na rdo rje'i tshig rnams ni phyin ci ma log pa rnam pa bcu'i sgo nas bshad par bstan pa'o /
pradarśanārthaṃ / / tatra vyañjanānām arthasattvam asattvañca sadasattetyato vyañjaneṣv / aviparyāso vajrapadeṣu sadasattayā veditavyaḥ /
# de la yi ge rnams kyi don yod pa dang med pa ni yod pa dang med pa ste / / de bas na yi ge rnams la phyin ci ma log pa ni / / rdo rje'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas yod pa dang med par rig par bya'o /
dvayaprabhāsaḥ parikalpitaḥ sa cātrārthaḥ /
# gnyis su snang ba kun brtags pa de ni 'dir don yin te /
sa ca tathā na vidyata ityayam atrāviparyāsa ityarthāviparyāso / vajrapadeṣv aviparyāse yojayitavyaḥ /
# de yang de ltar yod pa ma yin zhes bya ba 'di ni 'dir phyin ci ma log pa ste / / de ltar don la phyin ci ma log pa ni rdo rje'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas phyin ci ma log pa dang sbyar bar bya'o /
jalpamanaskāra evātrāśraya ityato manaskāre'viparyāso / vajrapadeṣvāśraye yojayitavyaḥ /
# rtog pa'i yid la byed pa nyid 'dir gnas te / / de bas na yid la byed pa la phyin ci ma log pa ni rdo rje'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas gnas zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
māyādyupamayā yaścetaso'visāre'viparyāsaḥ sa vajrapadeṣu / māyopamatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ / / dharmadhātusvalakṣaṇam eva kalpanārahitatvād avikalpanatā /
# sgyu ma la sogs pa lta bur gang sems mi 'phro ba la phyin ci ma log pa 'di ni / / rdo rje'i tshig gi nang nas sgyu ma lta bu nyid dang sbyar ro / / chos kyi dbyings kyi rang gi mtshan nyid ni rtog pa dang bral bas rnam par mi rtog pa ste /
tena svalakṣaṇāviparyāso nirvikalpatvena draṣṭavyaḥ / / dharmadhātusāmānyaṃ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvaṃ /
# de bas na rang gi mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log pa ni rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du blta'o / / chos kyi dbyings kyi spyi ni rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba ste /
tena sāmānyalakṣaṇāviparyāsaḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratayā saṅgṛhītaḥ /
# de bas na spyi'i mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log pa ni rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal bar bsdus so /
dharmadhātor aviśuddhiviśeṣo viśuddhiviśeṣaśca saṅkleśo [p.171]
# chos kyi dbyings rnam par ma dag pa'i bye brag dang rnam par dag pa'i bye brag ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba ste /
vyavadānañcetyato'śuddhau viśuddhau cāviparyāsaḥ / saṅkleśavyavadānāntare saṅgṛhyate /
# de'i phyir ma dag pa dang dag pa la phyin ci ma log pa ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i nang du 'dus so /
dharmadhātoḥ saṅkleśavyavadānayor / āgantukatve'viparyāso'sāvapyākāśopamatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ /
# chos kyi dbyings la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa gnyis glo bur du byung ba la phyin ci ma log pa 'di yang nam mkha' lta bu nyid dang sbyar bar bya'o /
saṅkleśavyavadānāvasthayor dharmadhātoḥ kṣayavṛddhyabhāvād
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i dus gnyis na / / chos kyi dbyings zad pa dang 'phel ba med pas /
atrāse'nunnatau cāviparyāso vajrapadeṣv ahīnāviśiṣṭatāyāṃ
# mi skrag pa dang khengs pa med pa la phyin ci ma log pa ni rdo rje'i tshig rnams kyi nang nas /
yojayitavyaḥ / / evam ete daśāviparyāsā daśasu vajrapadeṣu yathākramaṃ yojayitavyāḥ /
# 'grib pa med pa dang khyad par du 'phags pa med pa dang sbyar ro / / de ltar phyin ci ma log pa bcu po 'di dag ni / / rdo rje'i tshig bcu po dang go rims bzhin du sbyar ro /
vajrapadānāṃ śarīravyavasthānam iti yānārthānadhikṛtya vajrapadānāṃ
# rdo rje'i tshig rnams kyi lus rnam par gzhag pa zhes bya ba ni don gang dag gi dbang du byas te /
pravṛttis te'rthās teṣāṃ śarīraṃ /
# rdo rje'i tshig rnams 'jug pa'i don de rnams de dag gi lus so /
teṣāntu caturdhā vyavasthānaṃ svabhāvataḥ ālambanataḥ avikalpanataḥ / codyaparihārataś ca /
# de dag kyang rnam pa bzhir gzhag ste ngo bo nyid dang dmigs pa dang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid dang brgal ba dang lan no /
tatra trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ pariniṣpannaparikalpitaparatantrākhyā ādyais
# de la ngo bo nyid ni gsum ste yongs su grub pa dang kun brtags pa dang gzhan gyi dbang zhes bya ba dag ste /
tribhiḥ padair yathākramam iti / / tatrādau bhavānyādyāni tāni punaḥ sadasattā'viparyāsa āśrayaśceti /
# tshig dang po gsum dang go rims bzhin no zhes bya ba de la / / dang po ni yod pa dang med pa dang phyin ci ma log pa dang gnas zhes bya ba'o /
tatra sadasattayā pariniṣpanna uktaḥ /
# de la yongs su grub pa ni yod pa dang med par bshad do /
aviparyāsena parikalpita uktaḥ /
# kun brtags pa ni phyin ci ma log par bshad do /
āśrayatvena paratantra uktaḥ / / katham iti ?
# gzhan gyi dbang ni gnas su bshad do / / ji ltar zhe na /
pariniṣpannasya sadasattāyā sadasattayā nirdeśa iti kecit /
# kha cig na re yongs su grub pa ni yod pa dang med pa'i phyir yod pa dang med par bstan pa yin no zhe'o /
kathaṃ sadasal lakṣaṇatvāt pariniṣpannasya sadasattayā'bhidhānam ityeke /
# ji ltar yod pa dang med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir yongs su grub pa zhe na / / kha cig na re yod pa dang med par brjod pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
saṃyogāt saṃstavācākṣarāṇāṃ kalpitenārthena sārthakatvaṃ paśyan / viparyayāc ca nirarthakatvaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvo'nabhilāpya iti / avagamyate / / atas tat sadasattā pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ity uktam ityanye /
# gzhan dag na re yi ge rnams 'brel pa dang 'dris pa'i phyir rnam par brtags pa'i don gyis don yod pa dang bzlog na don med par mthong bas yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid brjod du med par rtogs par 'gyur te / / de bas na de yod pa dang med pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid du bshad do zhe'o /
mahāyānadeśanādharmaḥ suviśuddhadharmadhātuniṣyandatvād / viparyāsapratipakṣālambanatvāc ca pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ity ucyate /
# gzhan na re theg pa chen po bstan pa'i chos ni shin tu rnam par dag pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyu mthun pa dang phyin ci log gi gnyen po'i dmigs pa yin pa'i phyir / / yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bya ste /
so'rthaḥ kalpitasvabhāvasya bhavati na tu parikalpitaḥ /
# rnam par brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi don yin du zin kyang kun brtags pa ma yin te /
ataḥ sadasattā pariniṣpanna ityuktam ityapare /
# de'i phyir yod pa dang med pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid du bshad do zhe'o /
anye tv āhuḥ - sadasattā'viparyastatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ukta iti
# gzhan dag na re yod pa dang med par phyin ci ma log pa'i phyir yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid du bshad do zhe'o /
aviparyāsena parikalpitas tasyāvidyamānena dvayarūpeṇa prakhyāti / lakṣaṇāt / / āśrayeṇa paratas tasyābhidhānaṃ /
# phyin ci ma log pa ni kun brtags pa ste / / yod pa ma yin yang gnyis po med pa'i ngo bor snang ba'i mtshan nyid du gyur pa'i phyir ro / / gnas ni gzhan gyi dbang ste /
hetutvād āśraya ity ucyate phalatvāt paratantra iti /
# de ni rgyu yin pas na gnas zhes bya'o; / / 'bras bu yin pas na gzhan gyi dbang zhes bya'o /
etad eva svabhāvatrayam ālambanato jñeyaṃ /
# ngo bo nyid gsum po 'di dag nyid shes par bya ba yin pas dmigs pa'o /
avikalpanata ityatra vigrahabhedād āha - yena ca vikalpayati nirvikalpena
# rnam par mi rtog pa nyid ces bya ba ni 'dir tshig rnam par sbyar ba'i bye brag gis na / / gang gis rnam par mi rtog ce na / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis so /
jñānena yac ca na vikalpayati prakṛtiprabhāsvaratāṃ / / tatrārya vigrahabhedaḥ - na vikalpayatyanenetyavikalpanaṃ na vikalpyate / tadityavikalpanaṃ / / tad bhāvo'vikalpanatā /
# gang la rnam par mi rtog ce na / / rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba la'o zhes bya ba smos so / / de la tshig rnam par sbyar ba'i bye brag ni 'di yin te / / 'dis rnam par mi rtog pas na rnam par mi rtog pa dang de rnam par rtog par bya ba ma yin pas na / / rnam par mi rtog pa ste / / de'i dngos po ni rnam par mi rtog pa nyid do; / / de ltar rnam par mi rtog pa nyid ni /
evam avikalpanatā dvābhyāṃ vajrapadābhyāṃ paridīpiteti darśayati / / tad anena jñeyajñānavyavasthānaṃ yathākramaṃ veditavyaṃ yad uta tribhiḥ / svabhāvair avikalpanatayā ceti /
# rdo rje'i tshig gnyis kyis brjod par bstan to / / de bas na 'di shes bya dang shes pa rnam par gzhag pa 'di lta ste / / ngo bo nyid gsum dang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid dang go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o /
tatra tribhiḥ svabhāvair jñeyavyavasthānaṃ grāhyatvāt /
# de la ngo bo nyid gsum ni gzung ba yin pa'i phyir shes byar rnam par gzhag go /
avikalpanatayā jñānavyavasthānaṃ grāhakatvāt /
# rnam par mi rtog pa nyid ni 'dzin pa yin pa'i phyir shes par rnam par gzhag go /
codyaparihārata upayuktebhyaḥ śiṣṭāni vajrapadāni / / atra kiñcid vajrapradaṃ codyasya parihāra eva /
# brgal ba dang lan ni rdo rje'i tshig bshad zin pa'i lhag ma rnams so / / 'di la rdo rje'i tshig kha cig ni brgal ba'i lan nyid de /
tadyathā māyopamatā ākāśopamatā ahīnāviśiṣṭatā ceti / [p.172] / kiñcit punaścodyam eva / / tadyathā saṃkleśo vyavadānam iti / / tasmācodyaparihāraś ca codyasya parihāraś ca codyaparihārau / asarūpaikaśeṣaṃ kṛtvā /
# 'di lta ste / / sgyu ma lta bu nyid dang nam mkha' lta bu nyid dang 'grib pa med pa nyid dang khyad par du 'phags pa med pa zhes bya'o / / kha cig ni brgal ba nyid de / / 'di lta ste / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba zhes bya'o / / de bas na brgal ba'i lan dang brgal ba ni /
tatra codyaṃ yadyete parikalpitaparatantralakṣaṇā dharmā na saṃvidyante
# brgal ba dang lan te mi mthun pa gcig ma bcug pa'o / / de la brgal ba ni gal te kun brtags pa dang gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid kyi chos de dag med na /
grāhyagrāhakatveneti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa nyid du zhes bya ba'i tshig gi lhag ma'o /
katham upalabhyante grāhyagrāhakatvenetyabhiprāyaḥ /
# ji ltar dmigs par 'gyur / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa nyid du zhes bya bar dgongs so /
ata saṃvidyante dharmāṇāṃ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratā na yujyate / grāhyagrāhakatvātmanā vidyamānatvāt / / etac codyaṃ /
# ji ste yod na de lta na go chos rnams rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba nyid du mi rung ste / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid du yod pa'i phyir ro / / 'di ni brgal ba'o /
tanmāyopamatayā pariharati /
# de'i lan ni sgyu ma lta bu nyid yin te /
yathā māyākṛtaṃ na saṃvidyata upalabhyate ceti /
# dper na sgyu ma byas pa lta bu ni med kyang dmigs pa lta bu'o zhes bya ba ste /
na hi māyopalabhyatayā saṃvidyate tato'pyevaṃ saṃvidyata iti jñātuṃ
# sgyu ma ni dmigs su yod kyang de'i phyir de bzhin du yod do zhes bya bar shes par mi nus so /
śakyate / / yadi parkṛtiprabhāsvaratā dharmāṇāṃ tat kathaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃkleśaḥ paścād / vyavadānam iti codyaṃ /
# gal te chos rnams rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba nyid yin na / / ji ltar sngar kun nas nyon mongs pa phyis rnam par byang zhes brgal te /
nahi prakṛti viśuddhe kadācid saṃkliṣṭatopapadyate / / asya parihāraḥ saṅkleśavyavadānam ākāśopamatayā veditavyaṃ /
# rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa yin na / / nam du yang kun nas nyon mongs pa mi 'thad do zhes bya ba de'i lan ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba nam mkha' lta bur rig par bya ba yin te /
yathā ākāśaṃ prakṛtipariśuddham āgantukenopakleśenasaṃkliśyate tad
# dper na nam mkha' rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa la / / glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pas kun nas nyon mongs so /
apagamād vyavadīyate ceti / / evaṃ dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiviśuddhatvepyāgantukair upakleśaiḥ saṃkleśaḥ / / tad apagamāc ca vyavadānam iti yadyaprameyabuddhotpāde satyaprameyāṇāṃ / sattvānāṃ kleśapraśamastat kathamanādisaṃsāre pratyekasyāpi
# de dang bral ba rnam par byang ngo zhes pa de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa yang glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyis kun nas nyon mongs so / / de dang bral na rnam par byang ngo / / gal te sangs rgyas dpag tu med pa byung ste / / sems can dpag tu med pa dag gi kun nas nyon mongs pa bsal te /
buddhotpādasyāprameyāṇāṃ satvānaṃ saṃsārāpagamān nirvāṇapraveśāc
# thog ma med pa'i 'khor bar sangs rgyas 'byung ba re res kyang sems can dpag tu med pa dag 'khor ba dang phral te / / mya ngan las 'das par btsud na /
ca na saṃsārasamucchedo na nirvāṇavṛddhri veti codyaṃ / / asyāhīnāviśiṣtatayā parihāraḥ / / aprameyatvāt sattvadhātor vyavadānapakṣasya ceti /
# de'i phyir / / ji ltar 'khor ba rgyun chad par mi 'gyur zhing mya ngan las 'das pa 'phel bar mi 'gyur zhes brgal ba de'i lan ni 'grib pa med pa dang khyad par du 'phags pa med pa nyid yin te /
parimāṇavato hi vastuno hāniḥ samucchedo vā prajñāyate aprameyaś ca / sattvadhātuḥ / / tasya hānir api na prajñāte kuta eva samucchedaḥ prajñāsyeta ākāśavat
# sems can gyi khams dang rnam par byang ba'i phyogs dpag tu med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste / / tshad dang ldan pa'i dongs po ni 'grib pa'am rgyun chad par sngon gyi sems can gyi khams dpag tu med pa de la ni / / 'grib par yang mi mngon na rgyun chad par ltag la mngon te nam mkha' bzhin no /
vyavadānasyāpyaprameyatvād viśeṣa eva nāsti tasya kathaṃ vṛddhir / bhaviṣyati ākāśavat /
# rnam par byang ba yang dpag tu med pa'i phyir khyad par nyid kyang med na / / de 'phel bar ji ltar 'gyur te /
tasyāvaraṇāpagād āvaraṇābhāvāc ceti / / dvitīyaṃ śarīravyavasthānam iti vajrapadānām ity adhikṛtaṃ / / yatra yā ca yato bhrāntir abhrāntir yā ca yatra ca / / bhrāntyabhrāntiphale caiva paryantaś ca tayor iti //
# nam mkha' sgrib pa dang bral ba dang sgrib pa 'byung ba bzhin no / / lus rnam par gzhag pa gnyis ni zhes bya ba ni rdo rje'i tshig rnams kyi zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / gang la gang zhig gang las 'khrul / / ma 'khrul gang zhig gang la dang / / 'khrul dang ma 'khrul 'bras bu nyid / / de nyid kyi ni tha ma'o /
vajrapadair bhrāntiviṣayo bhrāntisvarūpatā bhrāntihetur bhrāntiphalaṃ / bhrāntiparyantaśca nirdiṣṭaḥ /
# zhes bya ba ni rdo rje'i tshig rnams kyis 'khrul pa'i yul dang 'khrul pa'i rang gi ngo bo nyid dang 'khrul pa'i rgyu dang 'khrul pa'i 'bras bu dang 'khrul pa'i 'bras bu mthar phyin pa bstan to /
tathā'bhrāntisvarūpam abhrāntiviṣayo'bhrāntiphalaṃ tatparyantaś ceti /
# de bzhin du ma 'khrul pa'i rang gi ngo bo dang ma 'khrul ba'i yul dang ma 'khrul pa'i 'bras bu dang de'i mthar phyin pa yang bstan to /
tatra yatra bhrāntir iti sadasattāyāṃ vyañjanānāṃ
# de la gang la 'khrul zhes bya ba na / / yod pa dang med pa la ste /
sārthakatvanirarthakatvalakṣaṇāyām abhidhānābhidheyayos tat / sambandhasya ca bhāvasvarūpeṇa parikalpitatvāt / / yā ca bhrāntir iti viparyāso bhrāntiḥ / / svātmanyavidyamānena dvayākāreṇa prakhyānāt / / yato bhrāntir ityāśrayād bhrāntir āśrayaḥ punar jalpaparibhāvito / manaskāra ālayavijñānātmakaḥ /
# yi ge rnams kyi don yod pa dang med pa'i mtshan nyid la rjod pa dang brjod par bya ba dang de'i 'brel pa ni dngos po'i ngo bor kun brtags pa'i phyir ro / / gang zhig 'khrul ces bya ba la / / phyin ci log ni 'khrul pa ste / / bdag nyid la yod pa ma yin par / / gnyis kyi rnam par snang ba'i phyir ro / / gang las 'khrul zhes bya ba ni / / gnas las 'khrul pa ste / / gnas ni rtog pas yongs su bsgos pa'i yid la byed pa kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i bdag nyid do /
abhrāntir yā ceti māyādivad arthataḥ sadasattāvisāro'bhrāntiḥ /
# ma 'khrul gang zhig ces bya ba ni / / sgyu ma la sogs pa lta bur don gyi yod pa dang med par mi 'phro ba ni ma 'khrul pa'o /
bhāvābhāvābhiniveśabhrāntipratipakṣaś cābhrāntiḥ /
# dngos po dang dngos po med pa la mngon par zhen pa 'khrul pa'i gnyen po yang ma 'khrul pa ste /
sā yathākramaṃ māyopamatayā'vikalpanatā ca nirdiṣṭā / / yatra ceti yatra ca [p.173] / sā'bhrāntiḥ /
# de ni sgyu ma lta bu nyid dang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du go rims bzhin du bstan to / / gang la zhes bya ba ni gang la de sems ma 'khrul ba'o / / de yang rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba nyid la ste /
sā punaḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratāyāṃ pariniṣpannasvabhāvalakṣaṇāyāṃ / / bhrāntyabhrāntiphale caiveti tatra bhrāntiphalaṃ hi saṅkleśaḥ / / bhrāntiniṣyanda iti vākyaśeṣaḥ / / abhrāntiniṣyandānāyā bhrānter abhrāntiphalatvāt / / abhrāntiphalaṃ vyavadānaṃ sasamprayogam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ / / evakārakaraṇaṃ tat phale saṅkleśo vyavadānam ityanenaivokte / ākāśopamatayā tu paśyati dharmadhātor yasya bhrāntyabhrāntiphalaṃ tat / saṅkleśavyavadānātmakaṃ / / nedaṃ tat prakṛtikam iti pradarśanārthaṃ / / paryantaś ca tayor iti saṅkleśavyavadānayoḥ paryanto nirvāṇaṃ / / taccahīnānadhikatvena paryantam uktam ityeke / / anye tvāhuḥ - saṃsārasyāprameyatayā'pacayābhāvād ahīnatāyuktaḥ / saṅkleśaparyantaḥ / / nirvāṇasyāprameyatayopacayābhāvād aviśiṣṭatāyukto vyavadānaparyanta  iti / / etāni daśa vajrapadāny aviparyāsaprasaṅgadvāreṇoktāni / / na tu sūtritānītyatas tānyantaraślokābhyāṃ saṅgṛhītāni - / sadasattā'viparyāsa āśrayo māyayopamā / / akalpanā prakṛtyā ca bhāsvaratvaṃ sadaiva hi // / saṃkleśo vyavadānañca ākāśopamatā tathā / / ahīnatvādhikatvañca daśa vajrapadāni hi // / atra ca pariniṣpannaśabdārthasambandhadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ / / yathā pratyavabhāsate tathā 'rthānāṃ svabhāvasattādarśanaṃ / viparyāsaḥ / / tad arthapravṛttikāraṇadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ / / arthasamāropāpavādadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ / / yathānām arthasvabhāvadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ / / bhāvānāṃ svasāmānyalakṣaṇayor vastutvena darśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ / / svastyasvastisañcārād viśuddhir aviśuddhiśceti darśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ / / ekasyaivāśuddhiviśuddhidarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ / / saṅkleśavyavadānaprahāṇapratilambhayor hāniviśeṣadarśanāt / trāsamānapravṛttir viparyāsaḥ / / ityete daśa viparyāsāḥ /
# yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid mtshan nyid la'o / / 'khrul dang ma 'khrul 'bras bu nyid / / ces bya ba de la / / 'khrul ba'i 'bras bu ni kun nas nyon mongs pa ste / / 'khrul pa'i rgyu mthun pa'i zhes bya ba'i tshig gi lhag ma'o / / ma 'khrul ba'i rgyu mthun pa'i ma 'khrul ba ni / / ma 'khrul pa'i 'bras bu'i phyir ma 'khrul ba'i 'bras bu ni rnam par byang ba ste / / mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'i zhes bya ba'i tshig gi lhag ma'o / / nyid ces bya ba brjod pas de'i 'bras bu kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba zhes bya ba 'dis bshad de / / nam mkha' lta bu nyid ces bya bas ni chos kyi dbyings gang gis 'khrul ba dang ma 'khrul pa'i 'bras bu de dag kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i bdag nyid yin gyi / / de de'i rang bzhin ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir ro / / de gnyis ni mtha' ma'o zhes bya ba ni / / kha cig na re kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba gnyis kyi mtha' ni mya ngan las 'das pa ste / / de yang 'grib pa med pa dang lhag pa med pas mthar thug pa med pa'i phyir bshad do zhe'o / / gzhan dag na re 'khor ba dpag tu med pa'i phyir / / 'bri ba med pas 'grib pa med pa dang ldan pas ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtha' ma'o / / mya ngan las 'das pa dpag tu med pas 'phel ba med pa'i phyir / / khyad par du 'phags pa med pa dang ldan pa ni rnam par byang ba'i tha tshig go zhes zer ro / / rdo rje'i tshig bcu po 'di dag ni phyin ci ma log pa'i zhar la bshad kyi mdor byas pa las ni mi 'byung ngo / / de bas na / / yod med phyin ci ma log dang / / gnas dang sgyu ma lta bu nyid / / mi rtog pa dang rang bzhin gyis / / rtag bar 'od gsal nyid dang ni / / kun nas nyon mongs rnam byang dang / / de bzhin nam mkha' lta bu nyid / / 'grib dang med pa lhag med pa / / rdo rje'i tshig ni bcu zhes bya'o / / zhes bya ba bar gyi tshigs su bcad pa gnyis kyis sdud do / / 'di la yongs su grub pa'i sgra dang don 'brel par lta ba'i phyin ci log dang don rnams ji lta bur snang ba de lta bur ngo bo nyid du yod par mthong ba'i phyin ci log dang don de 'byung ba'i rgyu la phyin ci log dang don la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs par lta ba'i phyin ci log dang ming ji lta ba bzhin du don gyi ngo bo nyid du lta ba'i phyin ci log dang dngos po rnams kyi rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid la dngos po nyid du phyin ci log dang bkra shis pa dang bkra shis pa ma yin pa kun du spyod pas las rnam par dag pa dang rnam par ma dag par lta ba'i phyin ci log dang gcig kho na la rnam par ma dag pa dang rnam par dag par lta ba'i phyin ci log dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba spang ba dang 'thob pa dang 'grib pa dang khyad par du lta bas skrag pa dang brgyal ba 'byung ba'i phyin ci log ste / / 'di dag ni phyin ci log bcu'o /
bodhisattvasya tad abhāvādaviparyāsāvasthitasya / yathokteṣvartheṣvariṇatā vidarśanā bhāvanā veditavyā / / uktā'nudharmapratipattiḥ // / { antadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ }
# byang chub sems dpa' la de dag med pas / / ji skad bshad pa'i don rnams la phyin ci ma log par gnas pa ni lhag mthong bsgom pa yin par rig par bya'o /
[p.174] / anudharmapratipattyantaram antadvayavarjane pratipattir vaktavyetyataḥ
# rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa bshad zin to / / rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa'i 'og tu mtha' gnyis spang ba sgrub pa brjod par bya ste / / de'i phyir /
pṛcchati - antadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ katametyata āha - yā ratnakūṭe / nāmadharmaparyāyeṇa samyak pratipatteḥ svabhāvapratipādanārthaṃ / madhyamā pratipadupadiṣṭā /
# mtha' gnyis spang ba sgrub pa gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir gang dkon mchog brtsegs pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs las yang dag par sgrub pa'i ngo bo nyid bstan pa'i phyir / / dbu ma'i lam bshad do zhes bya ba smos so /
tadyathā - kāśyapa iha mahāratnakūṭe dharmaparyāye śikṣitukāmena / bodhisattvena yoniśodharmaprayuktena bhavitavyaṃ /
# 'od srungs 'di lta ste / / dkon mchog brtsegs pa chen po chos kyi rnam grangs la slob par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpas tshul bzhin du rab tu chos la sbyar bar bya'o; /
katamaśca yoniśodharmaprayogaḥ ? / yaduta - sarvadharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣā /
# tshul bzhin du chos la sbyor ba gang zhe na 'di lta ste / / chos rnams la yang dag par so sor rtog pa ste /
yā nātmapratyavekṣā na / sattvanajīvanapoṣanapudgalanamanujanamānavapratyavekṣā / / iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā [p.175] / pratipaditi vistareṇa yāvad dvitīyapradīpodāharaṇaparyantaḥ paṭhyate /
# gang bdag med par rtog pa dang sems can med pa dang srog med pa dang gso ba med pa dang skyes bu med pa dang gang zag med pa dang shed las skyes med pa dang shed bu med par so sor rtog pa 'di ni / / 'od srungs dbu ma'i lam mo zhes bya ba nas / / mar me'i dpe gnyis pa la thug gi bar du rgya cher 'byung ngo /
kasyāntasya varjanādasau veditavyā ? / katam asyāntasya varjanān madhyamā pratipatter jñātavyetyarthaḥ / / ata āha -
# mtha' gang spangs pas de rig par bya zhe na zhes bya ba ni mtha' gang spangs pas dbu ma'i lam shes par bya zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de'i phyir /
pṛthaktvaikatvam antaś ca tīrthyaśrāvakayor api // / iti vistaraḥ /
# tha dad pa dang gcig mtha' dang / / mu stegs nyan thos gnyis ka dang / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
ayaṃ pañcadaśavidho'ntadvayabhedaḥ /
# bco lnga po 'di dag ni mtha' gnyis dbye ba ste /
asya varjanāt sā veditavyā /
# 'di dag spangs pas de rig par bya'o /
atra pṛthagādidarśanamantaḥ / / ekaikapakṣābhiniviṣṭatvāt kārye kāraṇopacāraṃ kṛtvā / / tatra rūpādibhyaḥ pṛthaktvam ātmana ityantaḥ ekatvam ityantaḥ /
# 'dir tha dad pa la sogs par lta ba'i mtha' ni phyogs re re la mngon par zhen pa'i phyir 'bras bu la rgyu gdags par byas pa'o / / de la gzugs la sogs pa dang bdag tha dad ces bya ba yang mtha'o /
tatra ye rūpādīn sknadhānāyatanāni dhātūṃś ca nityātmana / upabhogavastutvena kalpayanti tad rūpādibhyaḥ pṛthaktvamātmana ityantaḥ /
# gcig ces bya ba yang mtha'o zhes bya ba de la / / gzugs la sogs pa phung po rnams dang skye mched rnams dang khams rnams ni bdag rtag pa'i spyad par bya ba'i 'os su rtog pa gang yin pa de dag ni gzugs la sogs pa dang bdag tha dad do snyam pa'i mtha'o /
ye punar ādhyātmikān saṃskārān rūpādīnām ātmatvena pratipannā yaḥ
# nang gi 'du byed gzugs la sogs pa la bdag tu 'du shes nas gang mthong ba dang thos pa dang shes pa de ni bdag yin la /
paśyati śṛṇoti jānāti sa ātmeti bāhyāṃścātmīyatvena kalpayanti tad / rūpādibhya ekatvam ātmana ityantaḥ yat sūtryate - sa jīvas taccharīram / anyo jīvo'nyaccharīram iti darśanaṃ tadevātrāntaśabdenoktaṃ /
# phyi'i rnams ni bdag gi ba yin par rtog pa gang yin pa de ni gzugs la sogs pa dang bdag gcig go zhes bya ba'i mtha' ste / / gang mdo sde las srog kyang gzhan la lus kyang gzhan pa dang srog de lus de yin zhes bya bar lta ba nyid 'dir mtha' zhes bya ba'i sgrar bstan to /
tat parivarjanārtham iti rūpādibhyas tattvānyatvāntaparivarjanārtham / ātmanaḥ /
# de yongs su spang ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni gzugs la sogs pa dang bdag de nyid dang gzhan gyi mtha' yongs su spang pa'i phyir ro /
madhyamā pratipad yad dharmātraṃ viṣayabhūtaṃ jñānaṃ /
# dbu ma'i lam gang chos tsam zhig yul du gyur pa'i ye shes so /
etad eva pradarśayann āha - yā nātmapratyavekṣā / yāvannamānapratyavekṣeti /dharmamātradarśanāddhi vandhyāpurtravad / ātmā nāstītyavagacchan nātmānaṃ pratyavekṣate nānusaratītyarthaḥ /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir gang bdag med par so sor rtog pa nas shed bu med par so sor rtog pa'i bar du'o zhes bya ba smos so / / chos tsam du mthong bas ni bdag mo gsham gyi bu bzhin du med par khong du chud nas bdag med par so sor rtog ste /
kuta eva tasya rūpādibhyas tattvam anyatvaṃ vā gṛhyata iti ?
# rjes su rtogs zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de dang gzugs la sogs pa de nyid dam gzhan du 'dzin par lta ga la 'gyur /
ātmaśabdenaiva tadarthe'vagamyamāne kimarthaṃ
# bdag ces bya ba'i sgra nyid kyis de'i don khong du chud par 'gyur na /
sattvādiparyāyaviśeṣābhidhānaṃ ?
# ci'i phyir sems can la sogs pa rnam grangs kyi bye brag smos she na /
na sarvasya sarvaparyāyavyutpattir ityataḥ sarveṣāṃ tadarthāvabodhārthaṃ / paryāyāntaranirdeśaḥ /
# thams cad kyis rnam grangs thams cad khong du chud par mi 'gyur te / / de'i phyir thams cad kyis de'i don khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir rnam grangs gzhan bshad do /
tat kālavikṣiptānāṃ vā paryāyāntareṇa tadarthaprāpaṇārthaḥ / / tenaivābhidhānenocyamāne'nyeṣāṃ prāpaṇāt / / nityaṃ rūpam iti tīrthikāntaḥ /
# yang na de'i dus su gyengs pa rnams la rnam grangs gzhan gyis de'i don rtogs par bya ba'i phyir te / / brjod par bya ba de nyid brjod na ni gzhan dag gis brnyas par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
te hi parikalpitarūpān vastutvenābhiniveśya nityatvena kalpayanti / nityaviparyāsopahatatvāt / / anityam iti śrāvakāntaḥ /
# gzugs la sogs pa rtag go zhes bya ba ni mu stegs can gyi mtha' ste / / de dag ni rtag par phyin ci log gis non pa'i phyir kun brtags pa'i gzugs la sogs pa la dngos po kho nar mngon par zhen nas rtag pa nyid du rtog go / / mi rtag go zhes bya ba ni nyan thos kyi mtha' ste /
tair api kalpitasvabhāvānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ vasturūpeṇānityatvena / samāropaṇādantatvaṃ /
# de dag kyang kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi gzugs la sogs pa la dngos po'i ngo bor mi rtag pa nyid du sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir mtha' nyid de /
atyantasaṃsārodvegakarān nirvāṇasya cāntapātanād / anityadarśnasyāntatvaṃ /tad ubhayaparivarjanārtham iti / nityānityadarśanaparivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad yā rūpādīnāṃ / nanityapratyavekṣā nānityapratyavekṣeti / / tat punaḥ kiṃ /
# shin tu 'khor ba las skyo bar byed pa dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i mthar ltung bar byed pas mi rtag par lta ba'i mtha'o / / de gnyi ga yongs su spang ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni rtag pa dang mi rtag par lta ba yongs su spang ba'i phyir dbu ma'i lam ste / / gang gzugs la sogs pa la rtag par yang mi rtog / / mi rtag par yang mi rtog pa'o /
nirvikalpajñānaṃ / / yan na rūpādīn rūpādiṣv eva nityatvenānityatvena cānugacchati / / rūpādīnām ityādiśabdena
# de yang gang zhe na / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes te / / gang gzugs la sogs pa la gzugs la sogs pa nyid du rtag pa'am / / mi rtag pa mi rtog pa'o /
vedanā-saṃjñā-saṃskāra-vijñāna-skandhānāṃ / pṛthivy-ap-tejo-vāyv-ākāśa-dhātūnāṃ / cakṣuḥ-śrotra-ghrāṇa-jihvā-kāya-mana-āyatanānāṃ ca grahaṇaṃ / [p.176] / ātmeti śabdena pudgalasamāropānta iti skandhadhātvāyatana vyatiriktam
# gzugs la sogs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i sgras ni tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa'i phung po rnams dang sa dang chu dang me dang rlung dang nam mkha'i khams rnams dang mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi skye mched rnams bsdu'o / / bdag yod ces bya ba'i sgras ni gang zag tu sgro 'dogs pa'i mtha'o zhes bya ba ni phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams dang tha dad pa'am /
avyatiriktaṃ vā vandhyāputravad asantam ātmānaṃ dravyataḥ paśyataḥ
# tha dad pa ma yin pa'ang rung ste / / bdag mo gsham gyi bu bzhin du rdzas med par mthong yang /
pudgalasyātmano vasturūpasamāropaṇam antaḥ /
# gang zag la bdag tu dngos po'i ngo bor sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir mtha'o /
nairātmyam ityapavādāntaḥ / / apavādo hi sato'sattva parikalpa ityuktaḥ /
# bdag med ces bya ba ni skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' ste zhes bya ba ni yod pa la med par yongs su rtog pa ni skur pa 'debs pa zhes bya na /
ātmanastv asattvāt kathaṃ nairātmyam ity apavādānta āpadyata ityata
# bdag ni med pas ji ltar bdag med ces bya ba la skur pa 'debs pa'i mthar 'gyur zhe na / / de'i phyir /
āha - prajñaptisato'pyapavādāt nairātmyam apavādānta iti sambadhyate
# btags pa'i yod pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te / / bdag med par skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
sa punar dharmāṇāṃ santāno yasmin hetuphalasambandhaḥ prajñāyate / / samudayo vā yatra devamanuṣyaprajñaptiḥ /
# de yang chos rnams kyi rgyun te / / gang la rgyu dang 'bras bu 'brel par mngon pa'o / / yang na spyir gang du lha dang mir gdags pa'o /
tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad ityātmanaḥ / sadasattādarśanaparivarjanārthaṃ / / tasyāḥ punar yasyā madhyamāyāḥ pratipado nirūpaṇārtham āha -
# de yongs su spang ba'i phyir dbu ma'i lam ste zhes bya ba ni bdag yod pa dang med par lta ba yongs su spang pa'i phyir ro / / da ni dbu ma'i lam gang yin pa brtag par bya ba'i phyir ro /
yadātmanairātmyayor madhyamam iti /
# gang bdag dang bdag med pa de gnyis kyi dbus zhes bya ba smos so /
kiṃ punas tan madhyaṃ / / nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ /
# de'i dbus ci zhig ce na / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes so /
grāhyārthavikalpasyāntatvaṃ darśayitvā
# gzung ba'i don la rnam par rtog pa mtha'o nyid du bstan nas /
grāhakārthavikalpasyāntatvapradarśanārtham āha - bhūtaṃ cittam ityādi
# 'dzin pa'i don la rnam par rtog pa mtha' nyid du bstan pa'i phyir / / sems yang dag pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
athavā pudgalasya samāropāpavādāntatvaṃ darśayitvā dharmasya / samāropāpavādāntadarśanārtham āha - bhūtaṃ cittam ityādi /
# yang na gang zag la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' bstan nas / / chos la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' bstan pa'i phyir / / sems yang dag pa'o zhes bya ba ni zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
yathā pratibhāsate yathā vā'bhilapyate cittaṃ tathaiva bhūtaṃ vidyata / iti /ayaṃ dharmasamāropāntaḥ abhūtasya cittasvabhāvabhūtatvena
# sems ji ltar snang ba dang ji ltar brjod pa de bzhin du yang dag par yod do zhes bya ba 'di ni / / chos la sgro 'dogs pa'i mtha' ste sems kyi ngo bo nyid yang dag pa ma yin pa la yang dag pa nyid du sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
samāropāt / / abhūtaṃ cittam ityapavādāntaḥ /
# sems yang dag pa ma yin no zhes bya ba ni skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha'o /
tasya hi grāhyagrāhakarahitātmanā nirabhilāpyena ca vidyamānam / apyabhūtam iti paśyataḥ sarvātmanā dharmasvabhāvāpavādād / apavādāntaḥ /
# de ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba'i bdag nyid brjod du med par yod kyang med par mthong ste / / chos kyi ngo bo nyid la rnam pa thams cad du skur pa 'debs pas na skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha'o /
tat parivarjanārtham iti samāropāpavādarahitasya dharmanairātmyasya / pravitedhārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad /
# de yongs su spang ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pa dang bral ba la chos bdag med par rtogs par bya ba'i phyir / / dbu ma'i lam ste /
sā yatra nacittaṃ na cetanā na mano na vijñānam iti / / abhiniveśā na pravartanta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
# de ni gang la sems med pa dang yid med pa dang rnam par shes pa med pa zhes bya ba ni mngon par zhen pa 'byung ba med do zhes bya ba'i tshig gi lhag ma'o /
yatra vā viṣaye na cittaṃ sāsravavāsanābhiścittātmakaṃ pravartate na / cetanā'bhisaṃskāralakṣaṇā na mano manyanākāraṃ na vijñānañca / vikalpanam iyaṃ madhyamā pratipad ityucyate / / tatra cittam ālayavijñānaṃ sarvasrāvadharmavāsanābhiścittatvāt / / cetanā manaskarma kuśalākuśalāvyākṛteṣu cittapreraṇakarmikā /
# yang na yul gang la zag pa dang bcas pa'i bag chags bsags pa'i bdag nyid kyi sems mi 'jug pa dang mngon par 'du byed pa med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi sems pa med pa dang rlom sems kyi rnam pa'i yid med pa dang rnam par rtog pa'i rnam par shes pa med pa 'di ni dbu ma'i lam zhes bya'o / / de la sems ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ste / / zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad kyi bag chags bsags pa'i phyir ro / / sems pa ni yid kyi las te / / dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams la sems 'jug par byed pa'i las can no /
manaḥ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ / / vijñānaṃ ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥ /
# yid ni nyon mongs pa can gyi yid do / / rnam par shes pa ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug go /
akuśalādayo dharmāḥ saṃkleśa iti vipakṣāntaḥ /
# mi dge ba la sogs pa'i chos rnams ni / / kun nas nyon mongs pa'o zhes bya ba ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi mtha'o /
kuśalādayo vyavadānam iti [p.177] / pratipakṣāntaḥ /
# dge ba la sogs pa ni rnam par byung ba'o zhes bya ba ni gnyen po'i mtha'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i sgras ni /
ādiśabdena / sāvadya-anavadyalaukika-lokottara-sāsravānāsrava-saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtādayo / nirdeśāḥ sambadhyante / / tatra yathaivākuśalāḥ kuśalāś ca dharmāḥ pratibhāsante'bhilapyante ca / tathaiva saṃkleśo vyavadānañceti darśanaṃ vipakṣāntaḥ pratipakṣāntaś ca
# kha na ma tho ba dang bcas pa dang 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa dang zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa dang 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas la sogs pa bstan par 'gyur ro / / de la dge ba dang mi dge ba'i chos ji ltar snang ba dang brjod pa de bzhin du kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar lta ba ni / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi mtha' dang gnyen po'i mtha'o /
tatrā'kuśalā akṣemārthatvāt / / sāvadyā duścaritasamutthāpakatvāt /
# de la mi dge ba ni mi bde ba'i don to / / kha na ma tho ba dang bcas pa ni nyes par spyod pa kun nas slong ba'i phyir ro /
laukikā viparyastatvāt / / sāsravā āsravānuśayitatvāt /
# 'jig rten pa ni phyin ci log gi phyir ro / / zag pa dang bcas pa ni zag pa rgyas par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
saṃskṛtāḥ pratyayotpāditvāt /
# 'dus byas ni rkyen rnams kyis bskyed pa'i phyir ro /
tad viparītās tu kuśalādayo veditavyāḥ / / tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad iti / / vipakṣapratipakṣayors tacchavdenābhisambandhaḥ / / na madhyamā'tra pratipaj jñāyata ityata āha - / yo'syāntadvayasyā'nupagamo'nudāhāro'pravyāhāra iti /
# de las bzlog pa ni dge ba la sogs par rig par bya'o / / de yongs su spang ba'i phyir dbu ma'i lam ste zhes bya ba la / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po ni de zhes bya ba'i sgra dang sbyar ro / / dbu ma'i lam mi shes nas / / de'i phyir / / gang mtha' de gnyis khas mi len cing mi brjod mi smra'o zhes bya ba smos so /
tatrā'nupagamo vipakṣapratipakṣayor anabhiniveśaḥ /
# de khas mi len pa ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po la mngon par zhen pa med pa'o /
anudāhāras tasmin vipakṣapratipakṣānte pareṣām asamādāpanāt / / apravyāhāro vipakṣapratipakṣāntayor asaṃvarṇanāt /
# mi brjod pa ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po'i mtha' de la gzhan dag yang dag par 'dzin du mi 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / mi smra ba ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po gnyis mi brjod pa'i phyir ro /
tīrthikaśrāvakāntapratipakṣeṇa madhyamāṃ pratipadaṃ deśayitvā / bodhisattvāntapratipakṣeṇa madhyamāṃ pratipadaṃ pratipādayann āha -
# mu stegs can dang nyan thos kyi mtha'i gnyen por dbu ma'i lam bstan nas / / byang chub sems dpa'i mtha'i gnyen por dbu ma'i lam bstan pa'i phyir /
astīti śāśvatāntaḥ nāstītyucchedāntaḥ tayor eva pudgaladharmayoḥ /
# gang zag dang chos de gnyis yod do zhes bya ba ni rtag pa'i mtha'o / / med do zhes bya ba ni chad pa'i mtha'o zhes bya ba smos te /
sarvadā svalakṣaṇasamārupād astīti śāśvatāntaḥ /
# rang gi mtshan nyid la rtag par sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir / / yod do zhes bya ba ni rtag pa'i mtha'o /
sarvathā svarūpāpavādān nāstītyucchedāntaḥ /
# rang gi ngo bo la rnam pa thams cad du skur pa 'debs pa'i phyir med do zhes bya ba ni chad pa'i mtha'o /
tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad yad anayor antayor madhyamiti/ / ubhayāntavigamo'tra madhyamabhipretamityeke /
# de yongs su spang ba'i phyir dbu ma'i lam ste / / mtha' de gnyis kyi dbus gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba la / / kha cig na re mtha' gnyi ga dang bral ba ni 'dir dbu mar 'dod do zhe'o /
ubhaya lakṣanamatra dvayorantayo madhyamityapare / / kathaṃ kṛtvā ?
# gzhan dag na re 'di gnyi ga'i mtshan nyid ni 'dir mtha' gnyis kyi dbus so zhe'o / / ji lta zhe na /
yo'hyabhūtaparikalpavad dharmadhātuvadvā jñeyamn abhidheyaṃ ca vastu / dravyataḥ paramārthataścāstītyabhiniveśaḥ sa śāśvatāntaḥ / / tasya tahā'sattvāt /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa lta bu'am / / chos kyi dbyings lta bur shes bya dang brjod par bya ba'i dngos po rdzas nyid dang don dam par yod do zhes mngon par zhen pa de ni rtag pa'i mtha' ste / / de ni de bzhin du med pa'i phyir ro /
tadvā śaśaviṣāṇavan nāstyeveti darśanam ucchedāntaḥ / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ? / tasya prajñaptito'stitvāt /
# de ltar ri bong gi rva bzhin du med pa nyid du lta ba ni chad pa'i mtha' ste / / ci'i phyir zhe na / / de rtag par yod pa'i phyir ro /
atas tan nirākaraṇenocchedānta ucyate /
# de bas na de bstsal bar bya ba'i phyir chad pa'i mtha' zhes bya'o /
ataścāstitva nāstitvayor madhyaṃ dravyaḥ paramārthaś ca nasti / prajñaptito'stītyubhayalakṣaṇaṃ bhavati /
# de'i phyir yod pa nyid dang med pa nyid kyi dbus rdzas nyid dang don dam par med pa la btags par yod do zhes bya ba ni gnyi ga'i mtshan nyid yin no /
vipakṣapratipakṣayoḥ samāropāntam adhikṛtyāha - avidyā grāhyā / grāhakā cetyantaḥ /
# de mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po la sgro 'dogs pa'i mtha'i dbang du mdzad de ma rig pa la gzung ba'o / / 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba ni mtha' ste /
evaṃ vidyā saṃskārā asaṃskṛtañca tat pratipakṣo grāhyaṃ / grāhyakañcetyantaḥ /
# de bzhin du ma rig pa dang 'du byed rnams dang de'i gnyen po 'dus ma byas la gzung ba'o / / 'dzin pa'o zhes pa yang mtha' ste /
atra ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇam iti paryantagrahāṇād / vijñānanāmarūpādayo'dhyākṣipyante /
# 'dir rga shi'i bar la zhes bya ba'i mtha' smos pa ni rnam par shes pa dang ming dang gzugs la sogs pa yang bsdu'o /
vijñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañcetyantaḥ /
# rnam par shes pa la gzung ba'o 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba yang mtha'o /
evaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā tṛṣṇā upādānaṃ bhavo / jāti-jarā-maraṇaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañcetyantaḥ /
# de bzhin du ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug dang reg pa dang tshor ba dang sred pa dang len pa dang srid pa dang skye ba dang rga shi la gzung ba'o 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba yang mtha'o /
tatrā'vidyā satyaratnāsaṃprakyānātmikā / / punyā punyānijñjasvabhāva cetanā sa punarbhāvabhisaṃskaraṇāt / saṃskārāḥ /
# de la ma rig pa ni bden pa dang dkon mchog mi shes pa'i bdag nyid do / / 'du byed rnams ni bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i ngo bo nyid de / / zag pa dang bcas pa'i sems pas yang srid pa mngon par 'du byed pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ saṃkleśalakṣaṇavyākhyānānusāreṇa vijñānādayo'pi vistareṇa / vaktavyāḥ / / vidyā'nāsravaṃ jñānaṃ /
# de bzhin du kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid bshad pa'i tshul du rnam par shes pa la sogs pa yang rgya cher brjod par bya'o / / rig pa ni zag pa med pa'i ye shes so /
saṃskārāṇāṃ jñānamevā'saṃskṛtaṃ pratipakṣaḥ /
# 'du byed rnams kyi gnyen po ni 'dus ma byas kyi ye shes so /
atha vā'nyasmād asaṃskṛtād [p.178] / vyavacchedārtham āha - tat pratipakṣa iti /
# de nyid kyi phyir 'dus ma byas gzhan las dbye ba'i phyir gnyen po zhes bya ba smos so /
anye tv anutpattimatvād asaṃskṛtam aṣṭavidham apyatra manyante /
# gzhan dag ni mi skye ba can yin pas na / / 'dus ma byas rnam pa brgyad car yang 'dir 'dod do /
pratipakṣastvanāsravā cetanā punar bhāvanabhisaṃskaraṇād iti /
# gnyen po ni zag pa med pa'i sems pa ste / / yang srid pa mngon par 'du mi byed pa'i phyir ro snyam du sems so /
tan nirodho grāhyo grāhako vetyantaḥ /
# de 'gog pa la gzung ba'o 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba yang mtha' ste zhes bya ba la /
tac chabdena vijñānādayo jarāmaraṇaparyavasānāḥ sambadhyante / / nirodho na vijñāyate kiṃ bhāvaḥ kāraṇaṃ vetyāha - yena tan nāmarūpaṃ / nirudhyata iti / / kena punas tan nāmarūpaṃ nirudhyate /
# de zhes bya ba'i sgras ni rnam par shes pa la sogs pa nas rga shi la thug gi bar du sbyar ro / / 'gog pa la yang ngo bo nyid dam rgyu yin pa mi shes nas / / de'i phyir / / lam gang gis ming dang gzugs 'gag pa'o zhes bya ba smos so / / gang gis ming dang gzugs de 'gag par 'gyur zhe na /
nāmarūpapratipakṣeṇā'nāsraveṇa mārgeṇa / / vidyā cā'vidyā cādvayam etad advaidhīkāram ityetad evātra jñānaṃ
# ming dang gzugs kyi gnyen po zag pa med pa'i lam gyis so / / rig pa dang ma rig pa de ni gnyis su med de gnyis su byar med do zhes bya ba de ni /
saparivāraṃ mārgaḥ /
# 'dir ye shes 'khor dang bcas pa ste lam mo /
ataś ca nirudhyate'neneti nirodhaḥ / / kaḥ punar atrāntaḥ / / ayam eva grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśaḥ / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# de'i phyir 'dis 'gag par byed pas 'gog pa'o / / de la mtha' gang zhe na / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa 'di nyid do / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
advayaprakṛtiṣv avidyādiṣv avidyamānadvayādhyāropapravṛttavāt /
# ma rig pa la sogs pa gnyis med pa'i rang bzhin dag la med bzhin du gnyis su sgro 'dogs pa 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ grāhyagrāhakānto dvidhā - kṛṣṇaśuklapakṣabhedeneti /
# de bzhin du nag po dang dkar po'i phyogs kyi bye brag gis /
tatra kṛṣṇapakṣe dvādaśabhavāṅgāni avidyā yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i mtha' rnam pa gnyis so zhes bya ba de la / / nag pa'i phyogs ni ma rig pa nas rga shi'i bar srid pa'i yan lag bcu gnyis so /
evaṃ śuklapakṣe'pyvidhyādinirodhabhedena dvādaśaprakāra / evāvidhyānirodho yāvaj jarāmaraṇanirodha iti /
# de bzhin du dkar po'i phyogs kyang ma rig pa la sogs pa 'gag pa'i bye brag gis ma rig pa 'gag pa nas / / rga shi 'gag pa'i bar rnam pa bcu gnyis so /
atra ca nirydhyante'enā'vidyādaya iti tat pratipakṣabhūto mārga eva / nirodhaśabdenoktaḥ /
# de la 'dis ma rig pa la sogs pa 'gag par 'gyur bas na / / de'i gnyen por gyur pa lam nyid la 'gog pa'i sgrar brjod do /
tat parivarjanārtham iti grāhyagrāhakāntaparivarjanārthaṃ / madhyamāpratipad uktyabhisambadhyate /
# de yongs su spang ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i mtha' yongs su spang ba'i phyir dbu ma'i lam bstan to zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
sā ca na vijñāyata ityata āha - vidyā cā'vidyā cādvayam etad iti /
# de yang mi shes te / / de'i phyir rig pa dang ma rig pa 'di ni gnyis su med ces bya ba smos so /
kathaṃ vidyā cāvidyā ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ tan nirodhaścā'dvayam ityata
# ji ltar na rig pa dang ma rig pa nas / / rga shi dang rga shi 'gag pa'i bar du gnyis su med ce na /
āha - vidyāvidyādīnāṃ grāhyagrāhakatvābhāvād iti /
# de'i phyir rig pa dang ma rig pa la sogs pa gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
tad abhāvastv avidyādīnām advayaprakṛtitvāt / / athavā vidyā'vidyeti parikalpitasvabhāvo'taś ca parikalpitasvabhāvayor
# de'i dngos po med pa ni ma rig pa la sogs pa gnyis su med pa'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro / / yang na rig pa dang ma rig pa ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid de /
vidyā'vidyayorabhāvasamatayā vidyā cā'vidyā cādvayam iti /
# de'i phyir kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid rig pa dang ma rig pa dngos po med par mtshungs pas / / rig pa dang ma rig pa gnyis su med do /
evaṃ saṃskārāṇām asaṃskṛtasya ca vijñānasya tan nirodhasya ca yāvaj / jarāmaraṇasya tannirodhasya ceti vaktavyaḥ / / kā punar atra madhyamā pratipat /
# de bzhin du 'du byed rnams dang 'dus ma byas dang rnam par shes pa dang de 'gog pa nas 'gog pa dang rga shi zhes bya ba'i bar du brjod par bya'o / / 'dir dbu ma'i lam gang zhe na /
etad eva jñānaṃ vidyā cāvidyā cādvayam etadavaidhīkāram iti na / vidyotpādayitavyā nā'vidyā nirodhayitavyā / / na saṃskārādayaḥ praheyāḥ / / na tannirodhaḥ prāptavya iti yadevaṃ jñānam etadavaidhīkāraṃ // [p.179]
# rig pa dang ma rig pa 'di ni gnyis su med de gnyis su byar med par shes pa de nyid de'i rig pa bskyed par bya ba yang med cing ma rig pa dgag par byar yang med pa dang 'du byed rnams spang bar bya ba yang med la / / de 'gog pa thob par bya ba yang med pa de ltar shes pa gang yin pa de ni gnyis su dbyer med pa'o /
trividhaḥ saṅkleśa iti / / tatra kleśaḥ karmajanmasaṃkleśanimittatvāt svayañca kliṣṭatvāt
# kun nas nyon mongs pa ni rnam pa gsum ste zhes bya ba de la; nyon mongs pa rnams ni las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa'i rgyu yin pa dang bdag nyid kyang nyon mongs par gyur pas kun nas nyon mongs pa zhes bya'o /
svaparātmanor vyābādhahetutvād vā saṃkleśa ucyate /
# yang na bdag dang gzhan la gnod par byed pa'i rgyu yin pas kun nas nyon mongs pa zhes bya'o /
karmāpi kleśādhipatyanirvṛttatvāj janmahetutvāt svayam api ca kasyacit / kliṣṭatvāt saṃkleśa ucyate /
# las kyang nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis byung ba dang tshe'i rgyur gyur pa dang bdag nyid kyang kha cig nyon mongs par gyur pas kun nas nyon mongs pa zhes bya'o /
janmāpi karmakleśanimittatvāt sarvopadravāspadabhūtatvāc ca saṃkleśaḥ /
# tshe yang las dang nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis byung ba dang gnod pa thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pa'i phyir kun nas nyon mongs pa zhes bya'o /
punaḥ kleśasaṅkleśasya tridhā bhedapradarśanārtham āha -
# yang nyon mongs pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa gsum du dbye ba bstan pa'i phyir /
kleśasaṅkleśastrividha iti vistaraḥ /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa yang rnam pa gsum ste zhes rgya cher smos so /
tatra dṛṣṭayaḥ pañca satkāyadṛṣṭyādikāḥ /
# de la lta ba ni lnga ste / / 'jig tshogs la lta ba la sogs pa'o /
rāgadveṣamohā eva nimittaṃ śokādihetutvāt punar bhavahetutvāc ca /
# 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug nyid rgyu ste / / mya ngan la sogs pa'i rgyu dang yang srid pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
anye tvāhuḥ - rāgādīnāṃ nimittaṃ tad anukūlā indriyārthāḥ ayoniśo / manaskāraḥ rāgādivāsanā ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā /
# gzhan dag na re 'dod chags la sogs pa'i rgyu ni de'i rjes su mthun pa dbang po dang don dang tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa dang 'dod chags la sogs pa'i bag chags kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa'o zhes zer ro; /
evantu varṇayanti - rāgādinimittaṃ tadābhāsa iti /
# der snang ba ni 'dod chags la sogs pa'i rgyu'o zhes de skad kyang 'dzer to /
punar bhavapraṇidhānaṃ punar bhavaprārthanā /
# yang srid pa la smon pa ni srid pa phyi ma 'dod pa'o /
yasya pratipakṣo jñānaśūnyateti vistaraḥ / / tatra dṛṣṭānāṃ jñānaśūnyatā pratipakṣaḥ /
# de'i gnyen po ni stong pa nyid shes pa zhes rgya cher 'byung ba de la lta ba rnams kyi gnyen po ni stong pa nyid shes pa ste /
śūnyatāviṣayaṃ jñānamātra jñānaśūnyatā /
# stong pa nyid kyi yul la shes pa ni 'dir steng pa nyid shes pa'o /
rāgādinimittapratipakṣo jñānā'nimittaṃ sarvanimittavigamāt /
# 'dod chags la sogs pa'i rgyu'i gnyen po ni mtshan ma med pa shes pa ste / / mtshan ma thams cad dang bral pa'i phyir ram /
animittaviṣayaṃ vā jñānam jñānānimittaṃ /
# mtshan ma med pa yul du gyur pa'i shes pa ni mtshan ma med pa shes pa ste /
parikalpitarāgādiśūnyatāviṣayatvāt punarbhavapraṇidhānapratipakṣo / jñānāpraṇihitaṃ /
# kun brtags pa 'dod chags la sogs pa'i stong pa nyid yul du gyur pa'i phyir ro / / yang srid par smon pa'i gnyen po ni smon pa med pa shes pa ste /
punarbhavapraṇidhānavigataṃ punarbhavaśūnyatāviṣayaṃ vā jñānaṃ / jñānapraṇihitaṃ /
# yang srid par smon pa dang bral ba 'am / / yang srid pa'i stong pa nyid yul du gyur pa shes pa ni smon pa med pa shes pa'o /
karmasaṅkleśaḥ śubhāśubhakarmābhisaṃskāraḥ punarbhavākṣepakayoḥ / śubhāśubhayoḥ karmaṇor upacayo'bhinirvṛttir abhisaṃskāraḥ /
# las kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las mngon par 'du byed pa'o zhes bya ba ni srid pa la 'phen pa'i las dge ba dang mi dge ba gnyis sogs pa dang mngon par 'grub pa mngon par 'du byed pa'o /
yasya pratipakṣo jñānā'nabhisaṃskāraḥ /
# de'i gnyen po ni mngon par 'du mi byed pa shes pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
yena jñānena karma punarbhavann asya nā'bhisaṃskaroti taj jñānaṃ / jñānābhisaṃskāraḥ /
# shes pa gang gis las kyis de'i yang srid pa mngon par 'du mi byed pa shes pa ste /
tat punasthathatāviṣayaṃ / / janmasaṅkleśaḥ punarbhavajātiḥ pratisandhicittaṃ /
# de'ang de bzhin nyid yul du gyur pa'o / / tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ni yang srid par skye ba zhes ba ba ni nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i sems so /
jātasya cittacaittānāṃ pratikṣaṇotpādaḥ pratisandhibandhād ūrdhvam / āmaraṇāt /
# skyes pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams skad cig re re la 'byung ba zhes bya ba ni nyid mtshams sbyor ba phan chad ma shi tshun chad do /
punarbhavaprabandha iti kleśasahito maraṇabhavaḥ / / tasmād anantaram antarbhāvaḥ / / tataś ca punarpyupapattibhavaḥ / / ārūpyasamāpattilābhinantu maraṇabhavād evānantaram upapattibhāvaḥ /
# yang srid pa'i rgyun to zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa dang bcas pa'i 'chi ba'i srid pa dang de'i 'og tu bar ma do'i srid pa dang de nas yang skye ba'i srid pa'o / / gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa thob pa rnams kyi ni 'chi ba'i srid pa de nyid kyi 'og tu skye ba'i srid pa'o /
yasya pratipakṣo jñānā'jātir jñānānutpādo jñānāsvabhāvatā ca / / tatrājātāḥ sarvadharmāḥ prikalpitātmktveneti yaj jñanaṃ
# de'i gnyen po ni skye ba med pa shes pa dang 'byung ba med pa shes pa dang ngo bo nyid med pa shes pa'o zhes bya ba de la chos thams cad kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid kyis ma skyes par shes pa dang stong pa nyid yul du gyur pa'i shes pa gang yin pa de ni skye ba med pa shes pa'o /
śunyatāviṣayaṃ vā taj jñānajātiḥ / / parikalpitadharmaśūnyatāviṣayaṃ  jñanaṃ jṇanutpādaḥ tena / tadanutpādprativedāt /
# kun brtags pa'i chos rnams kyi stong pa nyid yul du gyur pa'i shes pa ni 'byung ba med pa shes pa ste / / des de dag gis 'byung ba med pa rtog pa'i phyir ro /
vandhyāputravad asattvād asvabhāvo bhāvaprabandha iti yaj jñānaṃ taj / jñānāsvabhāvatā /
# mo bsham gyi bu bzhin du med pa'i phyir dngos po'i rgyun ngo bo nyid med par shes pa gang yin pa de ni ngo bo nyid med pa shes pa'o /
etaj jñānaśūnyatādikaṃ saptavidhajñānaṃ yathoktasya saptavidhasya / dṛṣṭyādivipakṣasya pratipakṣaḥ /
# stong pa nyid shes pa la sogs pa shes pa rnam pa bdun po de dag ni ji skad du bshad pa mi mthun pa'i phyogs lta ba la sogs pa rnam pa bdun gyi gnyen po'o /
etasyaiva trividhasya kleśakarmajanmasaṅkleśasya saptadhābhinnasyā'pagamo / vyavadānaṃ / / apagamaḥ prahāṇaṃ /
# nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa de gsum / / rnam pa bdun du ta dad par gyur pa de dag dang bral ba ni rnam par byang ba ste / / bral ba ni spangs pa'o /
anye tu manyante tathatā mārgo nirvāṇañca vyavadānaṃ / / apagacchatyasminn anevāpagatiścetyevaṃ vigrahabhedāt tathatādayo / vyavadānam iti / / tatra jñānaśūnyatādibhir iti ādiśabdāj jñānaśūnyatā
# gzhan dag ni de bzhin nyid dang lam dang mya ngan las 'das pa ni rnam par byang ba ste / / 'di la lam 'dis bral ba ni bra ba ste / / de ltar tshig rnam par sbyar ba tha dad pa'i phyir / / de bzhin nyid la sogs pa ni rnam par byang ba'i snyam du sems so / / de ltar stong pa nyid shes pa la sogs pas zhes bya ba la /
jñānānimittaṃ jñānāpraṇihitaṃ jñānābhisaṃskāro jñānājātir / jñānānutpādo jñānāsvabhāvatā ca parigṛhyante /
# sogs pa'i sgras ni stong pa nyid shes pa dang mtshan ma med pa shes pa dang smon pa med pa shes pa dang mngon par 'du mi byed pa shes pa dang skye ba med pa shes pa dang 'byung ba med pa shes pa dang ngo bo nyid med pa shes pa yongs su bsdu'o /
jñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmā iti /
# shes bya stong pa nyid la sogs pa'i chos rnams zhes bya ba ni /
atrāpyādiśabdena jñeyaśūnyatā jñeyanimittaṃ jñeyānabhisaṃskāro / jñeyājātir jñeyānutpādo jñeyāsvabhāvatā ca pariniṣpannalakṣaṇāḥ
# 'di la yang sogs pa'i sgras ni zhes bya ba stong pa nyid dang shes bya mtshan ma med pa nyid dang shes bya smon pa med pa nyid dang shes bya mngon par 'du mi byed pa nyid dang shes bya skye ba med pa dang shes bya 'byung ba med pa dang shes bya ngo bo nyid med pa yongs su grub pa'i mtshan nyid rnams yongs su bsdu'o /
parigṛhyante / / etena trividhena saṅkleśena yathāyogaṃ yāvan na śūnyatādayaḥ kriyanta  iti /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa gsum po de dag dang ci rigs par stong pa nyid la sogs pa'i bar du mi byed de zhes bya ba ni /
anantaroktena [p.180] / kleśakarmajanmasaṃkleśena pṛthagbhūtajñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmā / jñānaśūnyatādibhir na kriyante / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ na kriyante / / yasmāt te prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādaya iti / / prakṛtyaivā'dṛṣṭyādisvabhāvā ityarthaḥ / / kuta etat ? / ata āha - dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtyasaṃkliṣṭatvāt / / ato jñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmāḥ prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādaya iti / jñānaśūnyatādibhir na kriyante / / yathāyogam ityayam atra yathāyogārthaḥ / / jñānaśūnyatayā jñeyaśūnyatā dṛṣṭisaṃkleśena vimuktā virahitā na
# shes bya stong pa nyid la sogs pa'i chos rnams ni bshad ma thag pa'i nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa dag tha dad par gyur pa'o / / rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni / / stong pa nyid shes pa la sogs pas stong pa nyid du mi byed pa'o / / ci rigs par zhes bya ba la / / 'dir rigs pas ni 'di yin te / / stong pa nyid shes pa shes bya stong pa nyid lta ba'i kun nas nyon mongs pa dang mi ldan zhing bral bar mi byed de /
kriyante dṛṣṭiśūnyatāyāḥ svayam evādṛṣṭisvabhāvatvāt / / evaṃ jñānānimittena jñeyānimittaṃ rāgādinimittair virahitaṃ na / kriyate rāgādinimittaiḥ śūnyatāyāḥ svayam evānimittatvāt /
# lta ba'i stong pa nyid ni bdag nyid kyi lta ba'i ngo bo nyid ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / de bzhin du mtshan ma med pa shes pas shes bya mtshan ma med pa 'dod chags la sogs pa'i mtshan ma rnams dang bral bar mi byed de / / 'dod chags la sogs pa'i mtshan ma'i stong pa nyid ni /
jñānāpraṇihitena jñeyāpraṇihitaṃ na kriyate praṇidhānaśūnyatāyāḥ / prakṛtyaivāpraṇidhānalakṣaṇatvāt /
# bdag nyid kyi mtshan ma med pa'i phyir ro / / smon pa med pa shes pas shes bya smon par mi byed de / / smon pa'i stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis smon pa med pa'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
jñānānabhisaṃskāreṇa jñeyānabhisaṃskāro na kriyate
# mngon par 'du mi byed pa shes pas shes bya mngon par 'du mi byed par mi byed de /
abhisaṃskāraśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivānabhisaṃskāralakṣaṇatvāt /
# mngon par 'du byed pa'i stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis mngon par 'du mi byed pa'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
jñānājāthyā jñeyajātirṇaṃ kriyate, jātiśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛutyai vā / jāti lakṣaṇatvāt /
# skye ba med pa shes pas shes bya skye ba med par mi byed de / / skye ba stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis skye ba med pa'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
jñānānutpādena kriyānutpādo na kriyate
# 'byung ba med pa shes pas shes bya 'byung ba med par mi byed de /
cittacaittapratikṣaṇotpādaśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivānutpādalakṣaṇatvāt /
# sems dang sems las 'byung ba skad cig re re la 'byung ba'i stong pa nyid ni / / rang bzhin gyis 'byung ba med pa'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
jñānasvabhāvatayā jñeyāsvabhāvatā na kriyate punarbhavaśūnyatāyāḥ / prakṛtyaivāsvabhāvatvāt /
# ngo bo nyid med par shes pas shes bya'i ngo bo nyid med par mi byed de / / yang srid pa'i ngo bo nyid ni rang bzhin gyis ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir ro /
athavā trividhena saṃkleśena yathāyogam iti vistaraḥ /
# yang na kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa gsum po de dag dang ci rigs par zhes rgya cher smos pa ni /
kleśakarmajanmasaṃkleśena saptadhābhinnena jñeyaśūnyatādīnāṃ
# nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa bdun du phye ba dang shes bya stong pa nyid la sogs pa'i chos rnams kyi nang nas /
dharmāṇāṃ yasya dharmasya yena saṃkleśabhedena yogaḥ sa dharmo na
# chos gang kun nas nyon mongs pa tha dad pa gang dang sbyar bar rigs pa'i chos de ni /
jñānaśūnyatādibhiḥ kriyate kiṃ tarhyadhigamyate /
# stong pa nyid shes pa la sogs pas stong pa nyid du mi byed kyi shes par bya ba nyid do /
tatra dṛṣṭisaṃkleśena jñānaśūnyatāyogaḥ evaṃ yāvat
# de la lta ba'i kun nas nyon mongs pa ni stong pa nyid shes pa dang sbyar ro /
punarbhavaprabandhena jñānāsvabhāvatāyogaḥ /
# de bzhin du yang srid pa'i rgyun ni ngo bo nyid med pa shes pa dang sbyar ba'i bar du'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ na kriyate ? / yasmāt te prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādayo dharmā dharmadhātoḥ / prakṛtyaivāsaṃkliṣṭatvād iti /
# ci'i phyir mi byed ce na 'di ltar / / chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin gyis kun nas nyon mongs pa can du ma gyur pa'i phyir / / de dag rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid la sogs pa'o /
tatra dṛṣṭayo na jñānaśūnyatayā śūnyāḥ kriyante tāsāṃ prakṛtyaiva / śūnyatā lakṣaṇatvāt /
# de la ta ba rnams ni stong pa nyid shes pas stong par mi byed de / / de dag ni rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
rāgādinimittaṃ jñānānimittena nānanimittaṃ kriyate dharmadhātoḥ
# 'dod chags la sogs pa'i mtshan ma med pa shes pas mtshan ma med par mi byed de /
prakṛtyaivānimittatvāt /
# chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin gyis mtshan ma med pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ yāvat punar bhavaprabandho jñānāsvabhāvatayā nāsvabhāvaḥ
# de bzhin du yang srid pa'i rgyun ni ngo bo nyid med par shes pas ngo bo nyid med par mi byed pa'i bar du ste /
kriyate yato'nutpanne'pi pratipakṣe parikalpitaḥ svabhāvo'sanneva /
# 'di ltar gnyen po ma skyes kyang kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid yod pa ma yin pa nyid do / / de dag gi phyir da lta bur gyur pa de'i phyir /
yataścaitad evam ato yadi dharmadhātuḥ saṃkliśyate vā viśuddhyate veti / kalpayatyam antaḥ /
# gal te chos kyi dbyings kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba'am / / rnam par dag par 'gyur ba'i snyam du rtog pa 'di ni mtha' ste / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
kiṃ kāraṇam ityato bravīti - prakṛtyasaṃkliṣṭasya saṃkleśaśuddhyabhāvād
# de'i phyir / / rang bzhin gyis kun nas nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa la ni nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
ākāśavad iti /
# nam mkha' bzhin no /
etasyāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamāpratipad yan na śūnyatāyā / vidyātmikāyā dharmānajñeyaśūnyatādīn pariniṣpannasvabhāvātmakaṃ
# mtha' de gnyis yongs su spang bar bya ba'i phyir dbu ma'i lam ste gang stong pa nyid rig pa'i bdag nyid kyis shes bya stong pa nyid la sogs pa'i chos yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi bdag nyid rnams /
tad vipakṣeṇa paratantrasvabhāvena dṛṣṭyādikena śūnyān virahitān karoti
# de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid lta ba pa la sogs pa dang bral bar stong par mi byed kyi /
api tv anutpannāyām api vidyāyāṃ parikalpitena svabhāvena / dṛṣṭisvarūpeṇa dharmā eva śūnyāḥ /
# rig pa ma skyes su zin kyang lta ba'i ngo bo nyid kyi chos rnams nyid kyis kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis stong ngo /
evaṃ yannānimittena dharmānanimittān karoti dharmā evānimittāḥ
# de bzhin du gang mtshan ma med pas chos rnams mtshan ma med par mi byed de / / chos rnams nyid kyis mtshan ma med pa nas /
yāvadyannāsvabhāvatayā dharmānasvabhāvān karoti dharmā / evāsvabhāvā iti /
# ngo bo nyid med pas chos rnams ngo bo nyid med par mi byed de / / chos rnams nyid kyis ngo bo nyid med pa'i bar du'o /
yaivaṃ pratyavekṣā iyam ucyate kāśyapa dharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣeti /
# gang dag de ltar so sor rtog pa 'di ni 'od srungs chos rnams la yang dag par so sor rtog pa zhes bya'o /
evaṃ vidyāstitvaṃ tad vipakṣāstitvāṃ ca parikalpitasvabhāvavigataṃ / paridīpayann adhyāropāpavādāntapratikṣepaḥ kṛto bhavati // [p.181]
# de bzhin du rig pa yod pa dang de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs yod pa yang kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid dang bral bar bstan pas / / sgro btags pa dang bskur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' spangs pa yin no /
yo'yam anukrānto vikalpaprabhedastasmād ayam aparaḥ saptavidho / vikalpadvayāntaḥ /
# gang rtag tu 'das pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i rab tu dbye ba de las 'di ni gzhan yin te rnam par rtog pa'i mtha' gnyis rnam pa bdun no /
vikalpaprabhedapradarśanārtham āha - tadyathā bhāve'pi vikalpo'ntaḥ / abhāve'pi vikalpo'nta iti /
# rnam par rtog pa'i rab tu dbye ba bstan pa'i phyir ro / / 'di lta ste / / dngos po yod par rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o / / dngos po med par rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o zhes pa smos te /
katham ityato bravīti - pudgalo'sti yasya vināśāya śūnyatā nairātmyam / api vā nāstīti vikalpanāt /
# ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / gang zag yod de de gzhig pa'i phyir stong pa nyid do / / yang na bdag med pa yang med do snyam du rtog pa'i phyir te zhes bya ba smos so /
yadi śūnyatayā dharmān prakṛtiśūnyatvān na śūnyān karoti tena tarhi
# gal te chos rnams rang bzhin gyis stong pa'i phyir stong pa nyid kyis stong par mi byed na /
pudgalo'sti yasya vināśāya śūnyatā / / nairātmyam api vā nāsti pudgalābhāvāt /
# des na gang zag yod de de gzhig pa'i phyir stong pa nyid do / / yang na gang zag med pa'i phyir bdag med pa yang med par 'gyur te /
na hi pratipakṣo nirvipakṣo'sti /
# gnyen po ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs med pa ma yin no /
tasmād avaśyaṃ pudgalāstitvaṃ vā nairātmyaṃ bhāvo vā pratipattavya iti
# de bas na gdon mi za bar gang zag yod pa'am / / bdag med pa yang med par shes par bya'o zhe na /
tadbhāvābhāve vikalpo'ntaḥ / / etasya bhāvābhāvavikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārtham iyaṃ madhyamā / pratipat / / na khalu punaḥ kāśyapa pudgalavināśāya śūnyatā /
# de med pa yang rnam par rtog pa'i mtha'o / / yod pa dang med par rnam par rtog pa'i mtha'i 'di gnyis spang ba'i phyir dbu ma'i lam 'di lta ste / / 'od srung gang zag rnam par gzhig pa'i phyir /
api tu śūnyataiva śūnyeti vistareṇa sūtrapāṭhaḥ /
# stong pa nyid ma yin gyi stong pa nyid kyis stong ngo zhes mdo las rgya cher 'byung ba'o /
tatra na saṅkliṣṭa pudugalavināśāya na oyavadānpudgalothpādāya / śūnyatā /senādivatprajñaptisatvāt pudgalasyotpādavināśābhāvād api / tu śūnyataiva śūnyā na tu pudgalena satkāyadṛṣṭisamāropitena
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa can gyi gang zag rnam par gzhig pa dang rnam par byang ba'i gang zag bskyed par bya ba'i phyir stong pa nyid ma yin gyi gang zag bskyed par bya ba dang gzhig par bya ba'i dngos po med pa'i phyir / / dmag la sogs pa bzhin btags par yod pas stong pa nyid kyis stong gi / / 'jig tshogs la lta bas gang zag tu sgro btags pas ni ma yin te /
tasyātyantam asattvāt /
# de ni gtan med pa'i phyir ro /
evañca kṛtvā pudgaladharmātmanā na bhāvaḥ śūunyatā tad rahitatvāt /
# de ltar byas na gang zag dang chos kyi bdag nyid kyis stong pa nyid dngos po ma yin gyi de dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
pariniṣpannena nābhāvaḥ tac ca śūnyatāyāḥ pariniṣpannātmakatvaṃ / pratipādayann āha - pūrvāntaśūnyatā aparāntaśūnyatā
# yongs su grub pa'i bdag nyid kyis ni dngos po med pa ma yin no / / stong pa de yongs su grub pa'i bdag nyid du bstan pa'i phyir / / sngon gyi mtha' stong pa / / phyi ma'i mtha' stong pa /
pratyutpannaśūnyateti kālatraye'pi tathaivāstitvapratipādanāt /
# da ltar byung ba stong pa zhes bya ba smos te / / dus gsum char du yang de bzhin du yod pa bstan pa'o /
athavā pṛthagjanāśaikṣaśaikṣāvasthāsu tathaivāstitvapratipādanāt /
# yang na so so'i skye bo dang slob pa dang mi slob pa'i dus dag na'ang de bzhin du yod par bstan pa ste /
tatra pṛthagjanāvasthā pūrvāntaḥ aśaikṣāvasthā'parāntaḥ / śaikṣāvasthā pratyutpanna iti /
# de la so so'i skye bo'i dus ni sngon gyi mtha'o / / mi slob pa'i dus ni phyi ma'i mtha'o / / slob pa'i dus ni da ltar byung ba'i mtha'o /
yasmāc caivaṃ bhāvābhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā tasmād āha - śūnyatāṃ / kāśyapa pratisarateti nirvikalpajñānaviṣayatvāt na pudgalam / ityabhidhānamātratvād iti / [p.182]
# gang gi phyir de ltar yod pa dang med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid yin pa de'i phyir 'od srungs stong pa nyid la brten par bya'i zhes gsungs te / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi yul yin par bstan to / / gang zag la ni ma yin no zhes bya ba ni brjod pa tsam du zad pa'i phyir ro /
śāmye'pi vikalpo'ntaḥ śamane'pi vikalpo'nta ityanuvartate /
# zhi bar bya bar rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir /
katham ityata āha - praheyaprahāṇakalpanayā śūnyatāyās trasanāditi /
# spang bar bya ba dang spong bar byed par rtog pas stong pa nyid kyis skrag pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra śāmyaṃ praheyaṃ praśamanaṃ prahāṇaṃ / / dharmān praheyatvena śūunyatāñca prahāṇatvena kalpayitvā / śūnyatāyāmuttrāso jāyate / / kathaṃ ? / trividho hi saṅkleśaḥ praheyaḥ /
# de la zhi bar bya ba ni spang bar bya ba'o / / zhi bar byed pa ni spong bar byed pa ste / / chos rnams ni spang bar bya ba nyid / / stong pa nyid ni spong bar byed pa brtags nas stong pa nyid la skrag pa skye'o / / ji lta zhe na / / kun nas nyon mongs pa rnam pa gsum ni spang bar bya ba yin na /
sa yadi prakṛtiśūnyaḥ tataḥ pudgalavan na praheyaḥ syāt /
# gal te de rang bzhin gyis stong pa lta na go / / de'i phyir gang zag spang bar bya ba ma yin par 'gyur ro /
tataś ca praheyābhāvāt prahāṇābhāva iti śūnyatāyām uttrāso jāyate / ayam apyanta eva / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# spang bar bya ba med na spong bar byed pa yang med do zhes stong pa nyid kyi skrag pa skye ste 'di yang mtha' nyid du / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
rūpavedanādayo hi dharmā yathaiva vijñānātmani viparivartante tathaiva / te dravyataḥ santītyabhiniviṣṭāḥ teṣāṃ kalpitarūpāṇāṃ rūpādīnām / ātmavat prakṛtyaivāsattvam ajānānās tacchūnyatāyā bibhyati /
# gzugs dang tshor ba la sogs pa'i chos ji ltar rnam par shes pa'i bdag nyid la snang ba de bzhin du de dag rdzas su yod do zhes mngon par chags te / / kun brtags pa'i ngo bo'i gzugs la sogs pa de dag bdag bzhin du rang bzhin gyis med par ma shes nas stong pa nyid kyis skrag go /
tasmād etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārtham ākāśadṛṣṭāntaḥ /
# de bas na rnam par rtog pa'i mtha' de gnyis yongs su spang bar bya ba'i phyir / / dpe nam mkha' ste /
tadyathā - kāśyapa kaścid eva puruṣa ākāśajo bhītaḥ sorastāḍaṃ / krandedevañca vaded apanayatadākāśam iti / / takiṃ manyase kāśyapa śakyam ākāśam apanetuṃ ? / āha - no hīdaṃ bhagavan /
# 'od srungs 'di lta ste / / dper na / / mi la la nam mkha' la skrag cing 'jigs nas brang rdung zhing du ste / / nam mkha' ni sol zhes de skad zer na / / 'od srungs de ji snyam du sems / / nam mkha' de bsal bar nus sam / / gsol pa / / bcom ldan 'das de ni rngo mi thogs lags so /
bhagavān āha - evam eva kāśyapa ete śramaṇabrāhmaṇāḥ śūnyatāyām
# bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa / / 'od srungs de bzhin du dge sbyong ngam bram ze gang dag stong pa nyid kyis skrag rab tu skrag na /
utttrasanti tān ahaṃ mahāvikṣepaprāptānīti vadāmi / / tat kasmād hetoḥ ? / śūnyatāyām eva hi te kāśyapa vicaranti tasyā eva bibhyantīti /
# de dag ni sems 'khrugs pa chen por gyur to zhes nga smra'o / / de ci'i phyir zhe na 'od srungs de dag stong pa nyid la spyod na / / de nyid kyis 'jigs pa'i phyir ro zhes 'byung ba'o /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - yathākāśaṃ sarvarūpānugatatvād apanetum aśakyam
# de ni 'di skad du bstan par 'gyur te / / ji ltar nam mkha' gzugs thams cad kyi rjes su song bas bsal bar mi nus pa de bzhin du /
evaṃ sarvadharmeṣu sarvakālaṃ śūnyatā vyavasthitetyapanetuṃ na śakyate /
# chos thams cad la stong pa nyid dus thams cad du gnas par bsal bar mi nus te / / chos ma spangs pas stong pa nyid gnas pa las bsal bar yang mi nus la /
na ca dharmaprahāṇena śūnyatā vyavasthāpayitum ataścāyam / asthānasaṃtrāsa iti darśayati /
# chos bsal bas stong pa nyid gzhag pa yang ma yin no / / de'i phyir 'di ni skrag pa'i gnas ma yin no zhes ston to / / skrag par bya bar rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o /
trāsye'pi kalpo'ntaḥ tataś ca trāsyād bhaye'pi / / kiṃ ? / vikalpo'nta ityadhikṛtaṃ / / yatastrāsaḥ sambhavati tat trāsyam ucyate / / bhīyate'smād iti bhayaṃ /
# skrag par bya ba de las 'jigs par rnam par rtog pa yang mtha' ste / / gang la 'jigs par 'gyur ba de ni skrag par 'gyur ba'o zhes bya'o / / de las 'jigs pa byang bas na 'jigs pa ste /
tasmād yad aniṣṭaphalaṃ tasmin strāsye tasmiṃśca bhaye yo vikalpayati / so'ntaḥ /
# de las mi 'dod pa'i 'bras bu'o / / skrag par bya ba de dang 'jigs pa de la gang rnam par rtog pa de ni mtha' ste / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir /
katham ityato bravīti - parikalpitarūpāditrasanāt duḥkhabhīrutayeti / / bālā hi parikalpitarūpādīn vastutaḥ kalpayitvā tebhyo bhayam aniṣṭaṃ / phalaṃ ca kalpayanti /
# sdug bsngal gyis khong sngangs pas kun brtags pa'i gzugs la sogs pa la skrag pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / byis pa ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo gzugs la sogs pa la dngos por kun brtags nas / / de dag la mi 'dod pa'i 'bras bu 'jigs par rnam par rtog go /
tataśca duḥkhabhīrutayā tebhyo rūpādibhyas tan nimittebhyaś ca bhayāt / trasantīti /
# de'i phyir sdug bsngal gyis khong sdangs [*sdang?] pas / / gzugs la sogs pa de dag dang de'i mtshan ma rnams kyis 'jigs shing skrag par 'gyur ro /
etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ [p.183] / citrakaradṛṣṭāntaḥ /
# rnam par rtog pa'i mtha' de gnyis yongs su spang ba'i phyir dpe ri mo mkhan te / / 'od srungs 'di lta ste /
tadyathā - kāśyapa citrakaraḥ svayam eva bhīṣaṇaṃ yakṣarūpaṃ kṛtvā / tasmād eva bhītasrasto'dhomukho nipatya sammohaṃ nigacchet / / evam eva kāśyapa sarvabālapṛthagjanāḥ svayam eva
# dper na ri mo mkhan zhig bdag nyid kyis gnod sbyin gyi gzugs 'jigs 'jigs lta zhig bris nas / / des 'jigs skrag ste / / kha bub tu 'gyel nas brgyal bar gyur pa de bzhin 'od srungs byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams /
rūpaśabdagandharasasparśān kṛtvā tebhyaḥ saṃsāre bhrāmyanti na ca tān / dharmān yathābhūtaṃ prajānantīti /
# gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg pa bdag nyid kyis byas pa de dag gis 'khor ba na 'khor yang / / chos de dag yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mi shes so zhes 'byung ba'o /
yathā ca citrakaraḥ svayaṃkṛte bhīṣaṇake yakṣarūpe mithyāvikalpena
# ji ltar ri mo mkhan zhig bdag nyid kyis gnod sbyin gyi gzugs 'jigs 'jigs lta zhig bris pa la log par rnam par rtog pas /
bhūtayakṣabhāvam adhyāropya tasmād bhītaḥ sammoham āpadyate /
# gnod sbyin gyi dngos po yang dag pa'o snyam du sgro btags te / / des skrag nas brgyal bar 'gyur ba de bzhin du /
evaṃ sarva eva bālā mithyāvikalpaprasrutāḥ svayaṃ kṛtair iti vikalpitaiḥ / saṃsāre bhrāmyante kṣaṇāvasthānikāyasabhāgānavasthitatvāt /
# byis pa log par rnam par rtog pa la zhugs pa skad cig gi gnas skabs thams cad ni / / bdag nyid kyis byas pa zhes bya ba bdag nyid kyi rnam par rtog pa dag gis 'khor ba na 'khor te / / rigs mthun par skad cig kyang mi gnas pa'i phyir ro /
pūrvako dṛṣṭāntaḥ śrāvakānadhikṛtyāyantu bodhisattvān iti /
# dpe snga ma ni nyan thos la sogs pa las brtsams pa'o / / 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams las brtsams pa'o zhes bya ba la /
śrāvako hi śūnyatāyām akṛtaparicayatvāc chūnyatāyās trasyati /
# kha cig na re nyan thos ni stong pa nyid yongs su 'dris par ma byas pas stong pa nyid kyis skrag go /
bodhisattvas tu parikalpitadharmavikalpena saṃkliśyate
# byang chub sems dpa' ni kun brtags pa'i chos la rnam pa kun nas nyon mongs pa ste /
vikalpakleśatvādityeke /
# rnam par rtog pa ni nyon mongs pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
nānayor arthaviśeṣo'styapi tu vargadvayavaśād dvayābhidhānam ityanye /
# gzhan dag na re 'di gnyis la don du bye brag med mod kyi ris gnyis kyi dbang gis gnyis su brjod do zhe'o /
śrāvakaḥ śūnyatātrāsādadhigantavyaṃ nādhigacchati bodhisattvaḥ punar / vikalpitadharmatrāsād ityapare /
# gzhan dag na re nyan thos ni stong pa nyid kyis skrag pa'i phyir rtogs par bya ba ma rtogs so / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni rnam par brtags pa'i chos kyis skrag pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
pūrvaka ātmagrāhapratipakṣeṇa ayaṃ punar dharmagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti kecit / grāhye'pi vikalpo'nto grāhake'pi / / vikalpo'ntaḥ ityadhikṛtaṃ /
# kha cig na re snga ma ni bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o / / 'di ni chos su 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o zhe'o / / gzung bar rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o /
katham ete grāhyarūpādayas tad grāhakāśca vijñānakāyāḥ / svalakṣaṇataḥ kāryataś ca gṛhyamāṇā ātmādivad adhyāropitātmāno
# 'dzin par rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o / / gzung ba gzugs la sogs pa dang de la 'dzin pa rnam par shes pa'i tshogs de dag rang gi mtshan nyid dang 'bras bus shes par byar yod bzhin du / / bdag la sogs pa dang 'dra bar sgro btags pa'i bdag nyid du ji ltar 'gyur zhes /
bhaviṣyantītyevaṃ grāhyagrāhakayor vastutaḥ parikalpo'nto'bhipretaḥ /
# de ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis la dngos por yongs su rtog pa ni 'dir mthar 'dod do /
etasya [p.184] / vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ māyākāradṛṣṭāntaḥ /t / tadyathā kāśyapa māyākāraḥ puruṣo māyākṛtaṃ nirmimīti /
# rnam par rtog pa'i mtha' de gnyis yongs su spang ba'i phyir / / dpe sgyu ma bye ba pa ste; 'od srungs 'di lta ste / / dper na sgyu ma byed pa'i mi zhig gis sgyu ma sprul pa sprul nas /
atha sa māyānirmitas tameva māyākāraṃ khādet /
# sgyu ma sprul ba des sgyu ma byed pa de nyid zos pa de bzhin du /
evam eva kāśyapa yogācāro bhikṣur yadyadevārambaṇaṃ manaskaroti tat / sarvam asya riktam eva khyātīti vistaraḥ /
# 'od srungs dge slong rnal 'byor spyod pa dmigs pa gang dang gang yid la byed pa da dag thams cad de la gsog tu snang ngo zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o /
katham anenaivaṃ vidhaṃ vikalpadvayāntaṃ parivarjayantīti ?
# ji ltar 'dis rnam par rtog pa'i mtha' 'di gnyis yongs su spong zhe na / / de'i phyir /
ata āha - vijñaptimātrajñānakṛtaṃ hy arthābhāvajñānaṃ /
# rnam par rig pa tsam du shes pas don dngos po med par shes par byas nas /
tac cārthābhāvajñānaṃ tadeva vijñaptimātrajñānaṃ nivartayati /
# don dngos po med par shes pa des kyang rnam par rig pa tsam du shes pa de nyid rnam par bzlog go /
arthābhāve vijñaptyasambhavād ityetad atra sādharmyam iti /
# don dngos po med na rnam par shes pa mi srid pa'i phyir te / / de ltar na 'di ni 'dir mtshungs so zhes bya ba smos te /
māyākārasthānīyaṃ vijñaptimātratājñānaṃ /
# sgyu ma byed pa lta bu ni rnam par rig pa tsam du shes pa'o /
nirmitayakṣasthānīyam arthābhāvajñānaṃ /
# sprul pa'i gnod sbyin lta bu ni don dngos po med par shes pa ste /
vijñaptimātrajñānaprabhāvitatvād arthābhāvajñānasya / / yathā nirmito nirmātāraṃ bhakṣyedevam arthābhāvajñānaṃ tadeva / vijñaptimātrajñānaṃ bhakṣyati / / asatyarthe vijñaptimātrasyāsaṃbhavād arthopalabdhir vijñaptir iti / kṛtvā / / samyaktve'pi vikalpo'nto mithyātve'pi vikalpo'nta ityadhikṛtaṃ / / nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ samyaktvena vā / vikalpayato mithyātvena vā 'ntadvayaṃ / / kathaṃ ? / samyaktvamanāsravā dharmā mithyātvaṃ sāsravāḥ / / tatra yadi bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ samyaktvenaivādhyavastyatyevaṃ
# don dngos po med par shes pa ni rnam par rig pa tsam du shes pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro / / ji ltar sprul pa byed pa sprul pa zos pa de bzhin du / / don dngos po med par shes pas kyang rnam par rig pa tsam du shes pa de nyid zos te / / don la dmigs pa ni rnam par rig pa zhes bya bas / / don med na rnam par rig pa tsam yang med pa'i phyir ro / / yang dag pa nyid du rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o / / log pa nyid du rnam par rtog pa yang mtha' ste / / nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dus na yang dag par so sor rtog pa na yang dag pa nyid du'am / / log pa nyid du rtogs pa'i mtha' gnyis so / / ji lta zhe na / / yang dag pa nyid ni zag pa med pa'i chos rnams so / / log pa nyid ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams so / / de la gal te yang dag par so sor rtog pa na dag pa nyid du chags na /
kuśalasāsravā na bhūtapratyavekṣā syāt / / atha punar asamyaktvalakṣaṇam eva evam api mithyātvam evopapadyate / traidhātukapratisaṃyuktakuśalavad iti /
